
-----title
泉州 (出生地)
-----detail

/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　幼颖异，有大志。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　少学章句翰墨，皆母陈氏亲授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1092')">1085-1092年</a>　居乡泉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年</a>　少在郡斋，拟草制词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1095')">1094-1095年</a>　居乡泉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1096&endYear=1096')">1096年</a>　习举子业成，得《春秋》、《左传》及《汉书》，读而好之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　居乡泉州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4d82b9e6a2474d6daeb7e04b993a4211_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4d82b9e6a2474d6daeb7e04b993a4211");'><span id='4d82b9e6a2474d6daeb7e04b993a4211_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1143')">1141-1143年</a>，63-65岁</div><div id='4d82b9e6a2474d6daeb7e04b993a4211' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年7月16日</a>　在徽州，移知泉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　抵达泉州任所后，上谢表。作品：谢泉州到任表。<div id='poem_1222671' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222671' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222671?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢泉州到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222671")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222671_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222671'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222671'>恭承休命，就易名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222671_comment'></div>去父母之邦，接淅敢同于他国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222671_comment'></div>问蛮夷之俗，褰帷如在于中州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222671_comment'></div>责重扪心，恩深陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222671_comment'></div>伏念臣昨从祠馆，叨领守符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222671_comment'></div>素号迂疏，无问马及羊之智；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222671_comment'></div>乃蒙安便，得维桑与梓之州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222671_comment'></div>二年而劳力劳心，一身而畏首畏尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222671_comment'></div>力祈罢免，反冒迁除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222671_comment'></div>虽卖剑买牛，老犹堪于渤海；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222671_comment'></div>然举头见日，身益远于长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222671_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下总覈百工，照临万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222671_comment'></div>眷方隅之濒海，须师帅之得人，故遣近臣，往绥遐俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222671_comment'></div>况今闽徼，莫盛泉山，既旁接书文之同，当尤惩狱市之扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222671_comment'></div>臣敢不仰遵宽大，俯厉衰残？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222671_comment'></div>讲求百粤之宜，参诸禹贡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222671_comment'></div>奉上三年之计，对以春秋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1222671_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222671'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二九，《唐宋元名表》卷下之二，《新安文献志》卷四○，《文章辨体汇选》卷一三八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222671_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　抵达泉州任所后，上谢执政启。作品：帅到任谢执政启。<div id='poem_1222820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>帅到任谢执政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222820")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222820'>由散秩而启专城，三周岁籥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222820_comment'></div>无微劳而叨易地，四拜除书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222820_comment'></div>蒙记录之不忘，知生成之笃厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222820_comment'></div>伏念满盈小器，衰朽馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222820_comment'></div>早怀许国之忠，妄希前辈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222820_comment'></div>终乏适时之用，可谓腐儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222820_comment'></div>会中兴修复于官仪，许末路追参于人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222820_comment'></div>中荐扬于清贯，外遍历于名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222820_comment'></div>顾饕荣已飒于二毛，戒之在得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222820_comment'></div>愿投老归安于三径，乐以忘忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222820_comment'></div>方拟上于囊封，复改膺于阃寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222820_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官两仪间气，百世真儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222820_comment'></div>人甘傅说之盐梅，莫知所作；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222820_comment'></div>天与仲尼之日月，孰得而踰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222820_comment'></div>辅成历数以方閒，立尽功名而未老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222820_comment'></div>俯怜孤迹，尝近清光，每因泚笔之馀，靡惜分符之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222820_comment'></div>第南徐之大府，连北固之通津，以地为雄，于今为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222820_comment'></div>宜英豪之是任，岂绵薄之能胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222820_comment'></div>大惧疾颠，仰烦严谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222820_comment'></div>敢不铭藏埏埴，鞭策罢癃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222820_comment'></div>国家之号令文章，既闻耳矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222820_comment'></div>州县之簿书期会，愿尽心焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1222820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222820'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷二三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷七○。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222820_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　汪藻知泉州，张元干有贺启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　在泉州，尝上书乞宫祠。作品：谢乞宫祠降诏不允表。乞祠与宰相书。<div id='poem_1222675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢乞宫祠降诏不允表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222675")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222675'>上需头之奏，具述土思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222675_comment'></div>奉方底之函，未容家食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222675_comment'></div>拜恩深厚，省己衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222675_comment'></div>伏念臣一去阙廷，四叨民社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222675_comment'></div>虽竭从补外，屡膺符竹之颁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222675_comment'></div>然靡称在前，宜被玺书之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222675_comment'></div>既力求于置散，乃犹许于饕荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222675_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下受命宅中，隆宽尽下，不替惟良之选，猥私亡益之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222675_comment'></div>一心而同三千，幸逢兴运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222675_comment'></div>百里而半九十，敢爱馀生？</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1222675_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222675'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三六。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222675_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　在泉州，有詹太和墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>詹太和墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十一年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222953")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222953'>左朝请大夫、直显谟阁、知虔州詹君讳太和，字甄老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222953_comment'></div>曾祖瑀、祖諴、父时，世为严州遂安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222953_comment'></div>时以君故，赠朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222953_comment'></div>君擢政和八年进士第，官自迪功郎八迁为左朝请大夫，职自直秘阁再迁为显谟阁，尝历真州扬子县尉、监泗州粮料院、河北河东路宣抚司书写机宜文字、尚书水部员外郎、淮南路转运使、知江、虔、抚三州，再知虔州以殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222953_comment'></div>君年十八，秀出其乡，有司以君应诏，后数年解褐调扬子尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222953_comment'></div>扬子濒江，雅多盗，君能得名，捕者十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222953_comment'></div>改承务郎，以母忧归里中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222953_comment'></div>会方腊起清溪，方千里皆震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222953_comment'></div>君家距清溪不百里，里豪余熙者欲连众应贼，君挺身见熙，熙严兵待之，几不得脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222953_comment'></div>君无惧色，徐以祸福譬之，熙矍然悟，愿并力讨腊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222953_comment'></div>君为徒步越境，见熙于官军，表其忠以徇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222953_comment'></div>当是时，承平久，贼振臂一呼，州县皆没，朝廷意严民皆盗，欲荡平之，得君书乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222953_comment'></div>君因率诸豪道官军，径趋贼巢，擒腊以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222953_comment'></div>是役也，严民微君，几不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222953_comment'></div>幕府上功，拜熙武义大夫，并官其民百馀人，而君止授宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222953_comment'></div>众恨待君薄，君笑而不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222953_comment'></div>以会课转奉议、承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222953_comment'></div>渊圣登极，转朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222953_comment'></div>上皇幸东南，事出非常，泗州当孔道，守臣皆惶恐称病，君以监粮料院领州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222953_comment'></div>一日行宫关白，士卒若送文书如京师者悉还之，且毋给其廪，官吏莫知所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222953_comment'></div>君请白之朝，众持不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222953_comment'></div>君乃自为奏，间道蜡书以闻，朝廷嘉其敏，录付行宫，上皇为之切责左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222953_comment'></div>或谮君「小臣离间当诛」，上皇曰：「彼尊朝廷也，何罪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222953_comment'></div>君由是知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222953_comment'></div>先是契丹归我之人分隶诸州，朝廷用议者将悉还之，君曰：「敌以此曹叛己，日须其至甘心，奈何使之趋死？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222953_comment'></div>愚谓不若留为腹心便」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222953_comment'></div>从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222953_comment'></div>后契丹人见君扬州，罗拜马前以泣曰：「非君，吾属无类矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222953_comment'></div>右丞李公宣抚河东，辟君为属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222953_comment'></div>未行，朝廷欲夺君使金，君谢不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222953_comment'></div>今丞相秦公为御史中丞，谓君曰：「今国难如巨石蔽天而下，壮士试出力当之，或百万生灵可活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222953_comment'></div>此何时而君辞难乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222953_comment'></div>君感其言，惶恐听命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222953_comment'></div>会兵部尚书王云使还，以不及期而止，遂从宣抚使出关见李公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222953_comment'></div>明日请辞，李公愕然问其故，君曰：「太和寒士，宣抚不知其不可收之，必以太和为有补秋毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222953_comment'></div>今候三日始见，见与客俱，宣抚不问，客亦无关白者，何以留为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222953_comment'></div>李公改容谢，与语大奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222953_comment'></div>宣抚罢，归遂安，道除尚书水部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222953_comment'></div>归未及家，邑人倪从度乱，浙西骚然，人皆推君，浙西帅叶公因请于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222953_comment'></div>君为斩内应者五十馀人，且塞其饷道，贼即日降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222953_comment'></div>时上在维扬，得奏良悦，进君朝请郎，趣之还省，转朝奉、朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222953_comment'></div>丁外艰，诏起为直秘阁，淮南路转运使枢密张公使川陕，亦辟君以从，皆不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222953_comment'></div>终丧，即慨然请老，时年未四十也，士大夫莫不高之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222953_comment'></div>居数年，以廉直为乡人之平，而与尉曹锄其强梗难治者，一邑为清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222953_comment'></div>绍兴六年，给事中吕祉等荐君可用，诏复故官，诣行在所，君犹不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222953_comment'></div>久之，过临安，见留守，吕丞相谓坐客曰：「诸君识詹直阁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222953_comment'></div>天下奇士，颐浩不及也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222953_comment'></div>时有饭蔬惑众者，君亟请除之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222953_comment'></div>未数日，果有以此谋乱者，丞相太息曰：「君可谓有先见之明矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222953_comment'></div>其策虑过人类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222953_comment'></div>枢密张公为相，以君见上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222953_comment'></div>君首陈强兵选将之说，上深以为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222953_comment'></div>时方议迁都，集近臣于前，各以意对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222953_comment'></div>上曰：「朕欲以詹太和守九江，如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222953_comment'></div>众杂然曰善，遂知江州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222953_comment'></div>先是诸将部曲往来九江者率为奸利，莫敢问，有王玮者尤专恣，民厌苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222953_comment'></div>君械致诸狱，自是过九江者莫能犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222953_comment'></div>治最闻，擢直显谟阁、知虔州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222953_comment'></div>贼黄细三等暴甚，君欲诱降之，提点刑狱赵涣规以为功，督兵往捕，君争不能得，果大败而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222953_comment'></div>诏罢涣，专诿君，君示以威信，平其尤剧者二十馀辈，渠魁皆生致戏下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222953_comment'></div>于是汀、吉、循、梅数州皆倚君为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222953_comment'></div>转朝请大夫，移抚州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222953_comment'></div>到官扩廪济饥民，所活以万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222953_comment'></div>召对，复知虔州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222953_comment'></div>又召对，卒于临安客舍，年四十八，时绍兴十年十月癸未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222953_comment'></div>君刚勇高明，见事立行，未尝犹豫，故所向有功，而居官皆可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222953_comment'></div>方朝廷多事，君未尝不在选中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222953_comment'></div>议者谓少假之年，其施设何如也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222953_comment'></div>君娶陈氏，封宜人，生一男二女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222953_comment'></div>男柬之，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222953_comment'></div>女适进士汪量，次甫数岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222953_comment'></div>柬之将以绍兴十一年九月某甲子，葬君于其县霞山之北，以君兄左中奉大夫、直秘阁至之状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222953_comment'></div>藻与直阁，同年进士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222953_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1222953'>人之才能，患无位以施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222953_comment'></div>得其施矣，患不逢其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222953_comment'></div>君班内朝，持节而使，剖符而守，位不为卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222953_comment'></div>以应变之长，投功名之会，又得时以为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222953_comment'></div>十年之间，所成就者如此，亦少发胸中之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222953_comment'></div>曾未及中寿而殁，此识与不识，皆为君悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222953_comment'></div>君之可书者多矣，姑掇其大者而志之，于以伸君未卒之志，而慰后人之思。</div><div id='poem_sentence_79_1222953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年8月29日</a>　在泉州，有表贺徽宗皇帝梓宫还阙。作品：徽宗皇帝梓宫还阙慰表。<div id='poem_1222655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽宗皇帝梓宫还阙慰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年8月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222655")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222655'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222655'>舆卫遐征，千年厌世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222655_comment'></div>衣冠永閟，万里还京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222655_comment'></div>痛缠宸极之尊，哀被海隅之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222655_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下躬承龟鼎，慕见羹墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222655_comment'></div>龙髯既绝于中天，蜃路尝淹于异域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222655_comment'></div>虽迎瞻引綍，动一人罔极之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222655_comment'></div>然归祔庙祧，实千古非常之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222655_comment'></div>愿宽圣抱，俯慰群心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222655_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1222655_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年8月29日</a>　在泉州，有表贺徽宗显肃皇后梓宫还阙。作品：显肃皇后梓宫还阙慰表。<div id='poem_1222656' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222656' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222656?labeling=true' target='_blank'>显肃皇后梓宫还阙慰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年8月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222656")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222656_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222656'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222656'>慈极终天，灵輴返国，凡居持载，孰不哀摧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222656_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下功懋承祧，孝深陟屺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222656_comment'></div>念昔从周狩，莫陪八骏之归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222656_comment'></div>幸今祔汉陵，当乐千人之聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222656_comment'></div>孺慕虽钟于此日，母仪如见于平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222656_comment'></div>愿抑圣情，少安群下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1222656_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年8月29日</a>　在泉州，有表贺徽宗懿节皇后梓宫还阙。作品：懿节皇后梓宫还阙慰表。<div id='poem_1222657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>懿节皇后梓宫还阙慰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年8月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222657")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222657'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222657'>騩驾当还，龙輴乃至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222657_comment'></div>变俄生于坤载，哀尤切于宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222657_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下运启中兴，教先内治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222657_comment'></div>汲汲方求于故剑，迢迢已隔于灵津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222657_comment'></div>瞻六引之来归，抚九嫔而增恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222657_comment'></div>然数存修短，而礼极哀荣，愿裁临感之悲，永副苍生之望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1222657_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在泉州，侄汪恺卒于饶州德兴县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在泉州，有诗题止戈堂。作品：题止戈堂二首。<div id='poem_528422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题止戈堂二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528422")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528422'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528422'>此老胸中百万军<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，暂劳试手犬羊<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>群。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528422'>山头不复望廷尉，柱后何须用惠文。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528422'>解带为城聊戏剧，卖刀买犊便耕耘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528422'>三山胜处开华屋，千载人传旧使君。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528422'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_528422'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_528422_0'>⑴ 原作兵，据《永乐大典》卷七二四二改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_528422_0'>⑵ 原作虎狼，据《永乐大典》改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_528422_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_528423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528423?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528423'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528423'>千里闽山驿骑飞，天书趣解海边围。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528423'>异军方逐苍头起，元帅徐将白羽挥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528423'>翻就铙歌春举酒，收还烽火夜开扉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528423'>向来万事关兵气，却作风光坐上归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528423'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528423_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在泉州，作晁氏墓志铭。作品：孺人晁氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孺人晁氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222955")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222955_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222955'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222955'>绍兴十二年八月，姨母之孙孙镇元朴以书抵余曰：「吾妇晁氏禀和于天，承庥于大族，受训于贤父母，其端柔明庄，类非世间女子所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222955_comment'></div>故吾母得之而知天下之有贤妇，吾得之而知天下之有良配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222955_comment'></div>盖吾妻奉吾母与所以事吾者，无秋毫不用其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222955_comment'></div>今不幸死矣，吾母悼之至不能独存，而弃吾之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222955_comment'></div>吾方哀吾母，不暇他哀，而念吾妻常戚戚于中而不能已也，君其为我书其生平，以泄其思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222955_comment'></div>并授其家爵里一通」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222955_comment'></div>云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222955_comment'></div>孺人出济北诸晁，尚书虞部郎中、赠金紫光禄大夫仲冬之曾孙，朝散郎致仕、赠大夫端知之孙，而右朝请大夫、提举两浙市舶贲之之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222955_comment'></div>初提举止一女，与宜人程氏爱之尤笃，常抚而示族姻曰：「此闺房之秀也，孰能当吾女者乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222955_comment'></div>时元朴好学清修，名声藉藉士大夫间，事母夫人孝，求所以奉温凊者，闻晁氏女佳，乃往聘焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222955_comment'></div>提举曰：「是上饶孙令耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222955_comment'></div>吾知之久矣，兹可依也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222955_comment'></div>以女与孙氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222955_comment'></div>家素贫，孺人安之，无不足之色，与元朴相敬如宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222955_comment'></div>从元朴官湖南，无何遇疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222955_comment'></div>疾之三日，谓其保母曰：「吾且死，不得终吾姑之养矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222955_comment'></div>琅然诵佛书而绝，无一字差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222955_comment'></div>得年二十一，时绍兴十年十月某甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222955_comment'></div>孺人得疾，保母欲呼巫觋禳禬，孺人遽止之，曰：「吾夫得禄奉旨甘耳，奈何以儿故他费乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222955_comment'></div>既卒，元朴闻之恸曰：「姆独不素告我乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222955_comment'></div>盖其不能忘者，大率如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222955_comment'></div>元朴以某年某月某日，举孺人之丧，葬于饶州馀干县斛塘之原，从吉卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222955_comment'></div>元朴尝为上饶令，有绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222955_comment'></div>今为左宣教郎、主管台州崇道观云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222955_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1222955'>承也厚而得也多，不为松柏而为蕣也，嘻，其奈何！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1222955_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在泉州，李正民有诗记汪藻赠荔子蕉乾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　在泉州，有诗题叶份普光明庵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在泉州，春，徙知宣州。<br /></div>

/><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　在开封。琼林宴赐冰，状元霍端友属汪藻表谢。汪藻授纸笔，立就，如素习之，一坐叹惊。作品：琼林苑宴颁冰谢表（不全）<span class='inlineComment2'>（谢表不见于本集、《浮溪文粹》、《浮溪集拾遗》，部分见于张邦基《墨庄漫录》卷十：“江彦章四六之工，自少年即妙。崇宁三年霍端友榜琼林苑宴谢颁冰，彦章作谢表有云：‘使嗽润而吮清，得除烦而涤秽。顺时致养，俯同豳雅之春开；受命知荣，固异卫人之夕饮。’又云：‘深防履薄之危，不昧至坚之渐。子孙传诵，记御林金碗之香；生死不忘，动宫井玉壶之洁。’”）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='61d080ac015f495580c6d8a8b1be0df8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("61d080ac015f495580c6d8a8b1be0df8");'><span id='61d080ac015f495580c6d8a8b1be0df8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1115')">1112-1115年</a>，34-37岁</div><div id='61d080ac015f495580c6d8a8b1be0df8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　秩满，代还，至京师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在开封，徽宗亲制《君臣庆会阁诗》，群臣进和。汪藻之篇，众莫能及。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　除九域图志所编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　在开封，任九域图志所编修官。与刘滂过从甚密。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　在开封，任九域图志所编修官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年1月29日</a>　在开封，母陈氏卒于京师汪藻居所。汪藻丁忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　作吴夫人墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和五年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222958")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222958'>夫人吴氏，新安郡人，为同郡崔光弼少李妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222958_comment'></div>年五十七，以政和四年十一月某甲子，卒于广州其子耀卿之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222958_comment'></div>明年十二月壬申，耀卿护丧归葬郡之长南三十里永丰乡鸾坑原，始叙夫人之行实，求予铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222958_comment'></div>夫人之先世以力田为家，居乡称善人长者，未尝出而求仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222958_comment'></div>其父瀚，始以赀交结贤士大夫，名有器识，所为多可纪，一时衣冠喜从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222958_comment'></div>夫人生而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1222958", 1222958, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>丰端</span>奇颖，瀚教以诗书笔墨而黜女工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222958_comment'></div>居无何，夫人于笔墨女工皆善，诸豪争聘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222958_comment'></div>瀚笑曰：「吾有一女，爱甚于男，所不足者非财也，何至与儿曹为偶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222958_comment'></div>立谢聘者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222958_comment'></div>会少李蚤孤，以身归其伯父驾部君，至新安而驾部以前死，留不得去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222958_comment'></div>瀚一见喜曰：「吾阅人多矣，无如崔君者，必以为婿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222958_comment'></div>父老谏曰：「君求婿久矣，今妄得一游士，初昧平生，独奈何予之女」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222958_comment'></div>瀚曰：「吾极知崔君人材足依，毋多言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222958_comment'></div>归夫人崔氏，厚以金缯田宅畀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222958_comment'></div>故少李从学四方二十馀年，未尝以家事关心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222958_comment'></div>而岁时烝尝庆吊，晨昏饮食起居，于流寓中孑然自表白崔氏之门者，皆夫人力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222958_comment'></div>及少李两荐有司，不报，倦游而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222958_comment'></div>夫人益倾赀供宾客费，日进诸子于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222958_comment'></div>岁晚或几于不足，人以为忧，而夫人处之自如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222958_comment'></div>逮崇宁初，天子新学校法，次子耀卿以文学知名，中进士科，为施州州学教授、广南东路提举学事司管勾文字，奉夫人以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222958_comment'></div>人谓且享于报，而夫人卒矣，距少李卒之八年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222958_comment'></div>夫人资宽厚，孝于亲，顺于夫，慈于子，睦于宗族，而仁于僮使，静专婉娈，无一不宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222958_comment'></div>晚喜释氏书，薰祓精甚，或日一食，门内之治，绝不经意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222958_comment'></div>间用声乐自娱，若淡然于世无情者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222958_comment'></div>子四人，曰栎、曰耀卿、曰夏卿、曰真卿，皆力学如夫人教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222958_comment'></div>女三人，适进士汪某、李天贶、汪文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222958_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222958_comment'></div>夫人始嫔崔氏而亢其宗，晚从子养而遗其累，终始皆合于义，是宜为铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222958_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1222958'>壸则母训，古必能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222958_comment'></div>后专组紃，鲜克承之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222958_comment'></div>懿此硕媛，学而明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222958_comment'></div>夫曰匪妇，余孰成之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222958_comment'></div>子曰匪母，余孰荣之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222958_comment'></div>宜老宜寿，福禄盈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222958_comment'></div>百未酬一，神遽倾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222958_comment'></div>令龟崇冈，室且城之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222958_comment'></div>孰贻无穷，歌以永之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1222958_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='89e1c831f6084768a454010a61f8084d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("89e1c831f6084768a454010a61f8084d");'><span id='89e1c831f6084768a454010a61f8084d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1119')">1117-1119年</a>，39-41岁</div><div id='89e1c831f6084768a454010a61f8084d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年11月</a>　在开封，除秘书省校书郎，有谢宰相余深启。作品：除馆职谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1222858' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222858' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222858?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除馆职谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222858")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222858_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222858'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222858'>沈迹下僚，分无它望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222858_comment'></div>受知英相，恩匪素谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222858_comment'></div>从稠人忽被于诏除，岂薄伎可堪于时用！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222858_comment'></div>盖师席托十年之旧，谓书林叨一日之先，猥以名闻，使之序进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222858_comment'></div>伏念某起家寒甚，承学缺如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222858_comment'></div>早慕功名，未叹儒冠之误；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222858_comment'></div>晚谙梦幻，方惊客枕之迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222858_comment'></div>三陪御府之英，五见长安之闰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222858_comment'></div>华发骎骎而欲雪，故人落落以如星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222858_comment'></div>自笑蠹鱼，生死不忘于文字；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222858_comment'></div>有同凫雁，去来谁计于江湖！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222858_comment'></div>甘为襆被之行，少逭怀铅之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222858_comment'></div>孰云误宠，更及微躯，守是正之遗篇，参编摩之载笔，既润久枯之辙，仍安屡绕之枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222858_comment'></div>厚德难名，当于古人求耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222858_comment'></div>馀生未泯，期以国士报之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222858_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇特进少宰相公，伟业格天，宏材周物，人臣名世之盛者，天子举国而听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222858_comment'></div>位虽次于周公，美实专于伊尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222858_comment'></div>制作悉还于邃古，经纶盖积于平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222858_comment'></div>吴邑纵囚，异政流传于父老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222858_comment'></div>虞庠讲艺，微言厌服于豪英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222858_comment'></div>铨曹力挽于羁单，宪府靡谈于阴伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222858_comment'></div>洎陟纲维之地，尤输药石之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222858_comment'></div>沙合南台，知千载真贤之出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222858_comment'></div>春回东阁，喜四时元气之新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222858_comment'></div>凡负器以怀奇，皆愿忠而望赐，有如孤进，兹为曲成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222858_comment'></div>虽大钧播物以无垠，宁私小己；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222858_comment'></div>然飞鸟依人而向爱，敢有它肠！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1222858_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年12月14日</a>　在开封，汪藻奉旨与校书郎孙觌、刘彦适，著作郎刘倪涛共同编次《秘书总目》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在开封，迁著作佐郎，任职期间，曾参与修徽宗日历。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年闰9月1日</a>　在开封，以秘书省日历案首进崇宁日历推恩，再迁符宝郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在开封，张扩有诗留别汪藻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　在开封，梁师成使人致意，许以侍从之官，汪藻谢而不往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　在开封，春，通判宣州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='42336689c5b94ee9aec14c9bd3b50bc7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("42336689c5b94ee9aec14c9bd3b50bc7");'><span id='42336689c5b94ee9aec14c9bd3b50bc7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>，49岁</div><div id='42336689c5b94ee9aec14c9bd3b50bc7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年1月10日</a>　钦宗被金兵所迫，复至青城。汪藻与同僚扈驾随行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在青城。金帅授意加金主徽号，汪藻被命草定册文。作品：册文（不存）<span class='inlineComment2'>（汪藻草定册文之事，未载于《宋史》本传及《建炎以来系年要录》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年1月11日</a>　钦宗在青城，金人令众亲王、宰执侍从留城外，余令归。汪藻亦被留。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年1月14日</a>　钦宗夜召从臣赋诗以遣忧，汪藻亦与之。作品：虏帐梦回惊日处，都城心切望云时（存句）<div id='poem_528564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>句<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年1月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528564")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528564'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528564'>虏帐梦回惊日处，都城心切望云时<span class='inlineComment2'>（应制）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528564'></div><div id='poem_sentence_1_528564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_528564'><span class='label'>宋徐莘《三朝北盟会编》卷七四　《三朝北盟会编》引《痛定录》：</span>前此上在青城斋宫无聊，何𣓨奏宜赋诗以遣兴，乃出征孙觌、汪藻应制。上诗用时字韵，藻诗云云。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_528564_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

宣州
