ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　任宣州教授。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f3ad471db3da450bbff7101a6bc0c0ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f3ad471db3da450bbff7101a6bc0c0ef");'><span id='f3ad471db3da450bbff7101a6bc0c0ef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>，41岁</div><div id='f3ad471db3da450bbff7101a6bc0c0ef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　在宣州，年底，上书请祠，得提点江州太平观。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5ceb7b82ef0b47c083903837c9e67808_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5ceb7b82ef0b47c083903837c9e67808");'><span id='5ceb7b82ef0b47c083903837c9e67808_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>，65岁</div><div id='5ceb7b82ef0b47c083903837c9e67808' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　到宣州任，上到任谢表。作品：谢宣州到任表。<div id='poem_1222674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢宣州到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222674")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222674'>宣为辅郡，古号名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222674_comment'></div>邈然千里之封，蒙此一麾之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222674_comment'></div>圣恩加厚，臣意知荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222674_comment'></div>伏念臣昨自禁严，叨分忧顾，违天威而寖远，惊星纪之忽周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222674_comment'></div>虽中解于印章，亦屡更于符竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222674_comment'></div>比祗明诏，往守遐陬，顾期年何补于秋毫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222674_comment'></div>恐一旦溘先于朝露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222674_comment'></div>力陈诚恳，仰渎听闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222674_comment'></div>班超求入于边关，本缘衰病；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222674_comment'></div>韩愈召还于海道，喜见华风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222674_comment'></div>况承流密迩于行朝，而上冢经过于旧里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222674_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下得天人之助，成宗社之安，混殊俗以为家，视群臣而若子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222674_comment'></div>念年迫桑榆之吏，乃日陪羁绁之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222674_comment'></div>新建武之官仪，不图重见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222674_comment'></div>数贞元之朝士，今已无多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222674_comment'></div>特予便安，稍令亲近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222674_comment'></div>臣敢不布宣宽大，招复流逋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222674_comment'></div>课农桑阡陌之间，庶为乐土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222674_comment'></div>誇觞咏溪山之上，肯效前人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1222674_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222674'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二九。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222674_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在到宣州前，有词与黄公度。作品：点绛唇（新月娟娟）<div id='poem_132800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_132800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/132800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>点绛唇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_132800")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_132800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_132800'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_132800'>新月娟娟，夜寒江静山衔斗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_132800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_132800'>起来搔首，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_132800", 132800, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>梅影</span>横窗瘦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_132800_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_132800'>好个霜天，闲却传杯手。<div id='poem_sentence_2_132800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_132800'>君知否？<div id='poem_sentence_3_132800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_132800'>乱鸦啼后，归兴浓如酒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_132800_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_132800'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(132800)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　在宣州，李正民有诗寄之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　至宣州方一月，即改镇江府。上到镇江任谢表。作品：谢镇江府到任表。<div id='poem_1222673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢镇江府到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222673")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222673'>起废江湖，甫三周于岁籥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222673_comment'></div>疏荣观阙，凡四易于州麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222673_comment'></div>嗟治迹之无闻，辱除书之屡至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222673_comment'></div>人微责重，天大恩深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222673_comment'></div>伏念臣积冒宠荣，寖成衰朽，咸谓陈人之安用，独蒙圣主之不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222673_comment'></div>念尝陪扈于初年，未忍弃捐于中道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222673_comment'></div>适当盛际，遍历名藩，深行百粤之区，远薄三吴之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222673_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下厉精求治，虚己受言，择循良共理之人，先悃愊无华之吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222673_comment'></div>故如臣等，亦在选中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222673_comment'></div>臣敢不恭布诏条，具宣德意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222673_comment'></div>坐揽淮山之形胜，深究古今；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222673_comment'></div>心如江水之朝宗，靡忘夙夜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222673_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222673'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二四。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222673_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年9月</a>　罢知镇江府。上谢表。作品：谢罢知镇江府除宫观表。<div id='poem_1222679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢罢知镇江府除宫观表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222679")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222679'>愿投散地，屡奏囊封，惧速烦言，卒蒙薄责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222679_comment'></div>荷圣恩之深厚，矜微物之衰残，特与便安，何胜感涕！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222679_comment'></div>伏念臣早缘薄技，误简渊衷，当乘舆巡幸之时，历行阙高华之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222679_comment'></div>一麾而临千里，违颜坐见于周星；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222679_comment'></div>半岁而阅三州，奔命几驰于百舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222679_comment'></div>食息未容于黔突，姓名已挂于丹书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222679_comment'></div>既屈刑诛，仍捐稍廪，俾脱剧烦之地，永全孤陋之身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222679_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下子视群臣，天临万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222679_comment'></div>浩浩陶镕之大，拳拳簪履之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222679_comment'></div>而臣生也有涯，身其馀几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222679_comment'></div>俟河清而已见，幸同父老之歌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222679_comment'></div>去日近以虽荣，无复轩墀之望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222679_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222679'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222679_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年9月</a>　罢知镇江府。上谢丞相启。作品：解镇江任谢丞相启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年9月</a>　罢知镇江府。上宫观表。作品：谢再任宫观表。<div id='poem_1222678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢再任宫观表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222678")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222678'>参华法从，均秩仙祠，本清朝优老之恩，岂愚者养疴之地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222678_comment'></div>猥蒙申命，弥愧素餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222678_comment'></div>伏念臣阻远清光，侵寻衰朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222678_comment'></div>中华未复，当先多士以著鞭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222678_comment'></div>众杰并驰，乃效庸夫而高枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222678_comment'></div>负国涵养，为时指名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222678_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下笃孝于亲，择贤而辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222678_comment'></div>念搢绅之长物，为羁靮之旧臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222678_comment'></div>忍令中道之弃捐，姑使全家之饱煖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222678_comment'></div>臣敢不偷安圣日，待尽馀年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222678_comment'></div>挂神武之冠，敢言长往；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222678_comment'></div>刻浯溪之石，愿颂中兴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222678_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
德兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4d2ad5f2d9384b07852ad699b9f129dc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4d2ad5f2d9384b07852ad699b9f129dc");'><span id='4d2ad5f2d9384b07852ad699b9f129dc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1108')">1105-1108年</a>，27-30岁</div><div id='4d2ad5f2d9384b07852ad699b9f129dc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年6月</a>　父榖卒于家。丁父忧，作父行状。作品：奉议公行状。<div id='poem_1222919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉议公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222919")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222919'>公讳谷，字次元，姓汪氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222919_comment'></div>汪氏、轩辕，皆古国名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222919_comment'></div>春秋时，童子踦以功显鲁，孔子韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222919_comment'></div>中间谱系不传，至五季有自歙之黄墩徙婺源还珠者，于公为九世祖，子孙因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222919_comment'></div>用高资为江左著姓，至公之父子，始以进士继踵起家，知名一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222919_comment'></div>如文正范公、韩康公、王文公，雅相知友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222919_comment'></div>年位皆不满其德，搢绅悼叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222919_comment'></div>公皇祐五年及第，一命抚州宜黄县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222919_comment'></div>少年明锐，遇事莫为持难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222919_comment'></div>盗杀里中民，胥惮于捕鞫，则为虎伤以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222919_comment'></div>公一见辄穷其伪，曰：「凡兽食人不容偏齧，今迹如此，谓之虎伤，何哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222919_comment'></div>胥不意情得，即叩头吐实，一邑以为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222919_comment'></div>移泰州泰兴令，会中遣御史按水灾，他邑长以裁减民赋不均，诉者纷然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222919_comment'></div>及被诘，莫知所为，独泰兴有经式，公私交便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222919_comment'></div>御史以公为能，喜甚，召与语，大奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222919_comment'></div>坐公堂上，庭折诸邑长，指泰兴为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222919_comment'></div>当是时，汪泰兴名闻淮东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222919_comment'></div>公进曰：「此未足为御史言也，县濒江，民依沙为田，出租赋，岁久沙溃，民抱虚责，阅数十吏无告，害莫大此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222919_comment'></div>愿益得为民除去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222919_comment'></div>于是奏可，蠲复者无算，讫今泰人诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222919_comment'></div>丁外艰，以长孙承祖母万年君忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222919_comment'></div>改建康节度推官，知汉阳军汉阳、润州金坛县、泉州晋江县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222919_comment'></div>元丰初，县官立法，期会旁午，晋江雅多权右，前为丞者，熟视强梗莫敢治，以故给纳常殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222919_comment'></div>公至，则系执政家吏一人，曰：「咎当归我，不诿他人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222919_comment'></div>调太平州军事推官、庐州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222919_comment'></div>部使者怒旁郡守，谋以危法中伤，鞫者莫敢直，直者辄以罪去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222919_comment'></div>最后请公，公曰：「祸人自免，岂吾心耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222919_comment'></div>考正于理，不为屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222919_comment'></div>使者大怒，亟劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222919_comment'></div>公益不能夺，则以狱上刑部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222919_comment'></div>至刑部，则以公言为当，乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222919_comment'></div>闻者壮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222919_comment'></div>有新贵人如京师，厚征从兵之食者，众多附之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222919_comment'></div>公曰：「国家之著挈令也，日给粮如所给之秩，否则有刑，费则有偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222919_comment'></div>今日汝何令之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222919_comment'></div>惟吾之所从，欲他日刑吏而偿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222919_comment'></div>无乃不可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222919_comment'></div>且何必剥贱媚贵」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222919_comment'></div>不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222919_comment'></div>后果及于败，皆以公为知言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222919_comment'></div>初令泰兴，以材敏称，至荐者一日倍当迁之数人，谓公且显矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222919_comment'></div>无何忧患十年，仅得一幕吏，汉阳以县省去官，金坛以避仇称病免官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222919_comment'></div>当公之免也，法以期叙，而遽踵新令告满二年，其为幕吏，法当减举将之半，而又以坐免沮格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222919_comment'></div>居晋江日，有哀公者，骤荐于朝，皆为公庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222919_comment'></div>会盗起闽中，按察者多得罪，复报闻罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222919_comment'></div>呜呼，可谓穷矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222919_comment'></div>公亦自以直道孤立，知者不为无人，然动辄跋疐，若阴有柅之者，乃益退缩，不为表暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222919_comment'></div>欲为地者，皆推而不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222919_comment'></div>一旦弃官，老于故居龙溪之上，治田桑、保坟墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222919_comment'></div>客至则酾酒击鲜，剧谈竟日，为温厚长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222919_comment'></div>无纤介隐衷，然于亲疏，曲有礼意，各得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222919_comment'></div>虽面刺人过，而受者更以为喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222919_comment'></div>与人说理，道成败，反覆曰「后当如是」，初若阔疏，事验皆信服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222919_comment'></div>间则翻诗书，铅椠不释手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222919_comment'></div>凡经抄录者，无不精审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222919_comment'></div>岁时书问，无贵贱必亲治惟谨，未尝敕子弟占答，故辞翰可师，人皆藏之以为珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222919_comment'></div>有诗百篇，意深语典，因事立诫，要不虚发，而不以示人，其隐德如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222919_comment'></div>家居十有二年，以致仕恩转通直郎，以覃恩转奉议郎，赐五品服，盖晚而子孙取科第，仍祖孙五世，基绪不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222919_comment'></div>人方以鲜俪为荣，而公卒矣，享年八十，寔崇宁乙酉六月某甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222919_comment'></div>曾祖某，故不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222919_comment'></div>祖某，任司封员外郎，赠光禄少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222919_comment'></div>父某，任都官员外郎，以公故赠中散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222919_comment'></div>妻开封陈氏，永嘉县君，继室寿光县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222919_comment'></div>男六人，槃、棐、槩、楶、藻、汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222919_comment'></div>楶，先公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222919_comment'></div>藻，从事郎、宣州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222919_comment'></div>公清慎刚介，出于天资，终始完节，不以势利毫发干挠，质之神明无愧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222919_comment'></div>乞身强健，时优游自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222919_comment'></div>常曰：「吾先世以才短年，今奇拙而寿足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222919_comment'></div>其退居龙溪，家日益贫，或以赂怵公者，曰：「吾宁贫，忍为此耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222919_comment'></div>官闽日，僧居岁熟荔支自守贰而下皆馈焉，无虑万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222919_comment'></div>公曰：「是豢吏也夫」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222919_comment'></div>独斥还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222919_comment'></div>后有坐是而黜者，人方服公之廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222919_comment'></div>王文公于公为父执，方用事时，汲汲于人物，诸附丽者多贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222919_comment'></div>有劝公以异时所得缄尺为献者，公笑而不答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222919_comment'></div>虽缘吏事，一再造请，谆谆道旧故，而卒无一语及私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222919_comment'></div>建昌李公常治湖，公以故人子往依焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222919_comment'></div>常屡以美官勉公，公不屑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222919_comment'></div>渤海张公择宾、南剑陈公称一见公于稠人，即嗟重论荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222919_comment'></div>公曰：「不缘介绍而能然，真知我者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222919_comment'></div>录其讳日，岁蔬食以报之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222919_comment'></div>公尤善摄生，至老精神容貌不少衰，时与壮者角膂力起步为笑乐，往往多不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222919_comment'></div>常诵佛书，愿脱疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222919_comment'></div>方与亲串命酒如平时，神识不谬，俄侧身而逝，众以为获报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222919_comment'></div>诸孤期以某月某日，奉公葬于龙溪源冕木坞，永嘉夫人祔焉，从公卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222919_comment'></div>谨录公行事如此，以待立言者图不朽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222919_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_87_1222919_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1107')">1106-1107年</a>　居德兴。丁父忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年1月</a>　正月，蔡京加太师。有诗贺其生辰。作品：上蔡太师生辰二首。<div id='poem_528447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上蔡太师生辰二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528447")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_528447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528447'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528447'>万古<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>储英气，生贤镇庙祧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528447'>方春回暖律，随帝下神霄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528447'>早岁陪兴运，清忠服迩僚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528447'>三篇俱命说<span class='inlineComment2'>（《诗渊》作说命）</span>，两纪独承尧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528447'>为国隆堂陛，中天斡斗杓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528447'>光华归使牒，宁谧载民谣。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528447'>九牧金成鼎，三山石峙桥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528447'>元圭来旧锡，神宝献新雕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528447'>堂起房心次，音谐角徵韶。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528447'>车书人一统，符瑞岁千条。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528447'>璧海材逾盛，沙场虏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>不骄。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528447'>献琛皆累译，入彀有垂髫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_528447'>郭解双封国，班超五日朝。<div id='poem_sentence_12_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_528447'>嘉谋从昔合，奕业更谁昭。<div id='poem_sentence_13_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_528447'>眷礼群臣异，恩光此日饶。<div id='poem_sentence_14_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_528447'>授图开地壮，傍阙筑堤遥。<div id='poem_sentence_15_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_528447'>供帐移金屋，歌钟实绮寮。<div id='poem_sentence_16_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_528447'>名园藏茂密，华阁耸岧峣。<div id='poem_sentence_17_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_528447'>诏跸纡临幸，宸毫纪宴招。<div id='poem_sentence_18_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_528447'>弟兄联衮绣，孙子列蝉貂。<div id='poem_sentence_19_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_528447'>印琢金为彩，鱼悬玉在腰。<div id='poem_sentence_20_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_528447'>中姻连筑沁，外族缀涂椒。<div id='poem_sentence_21_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_528447'>帝子传杯勺，宫墙有鼓箫。<div id='poem_sentence_22_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_528447'>果新无独享，羹美或亲调。<div id='poem_sentence_23_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_528447'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_528447_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_528447'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_528447_0'>⑴ 《诗渊》册六页四四九六作尊□</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_528447_0'>⑵ 原作敌，据《诗渊》改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_528447_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_528448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528448?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_528448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528448'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528448'>宇宙将昭泰，风云必会同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528448'>帝师黄阁老，人羡黑头公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528448'>庆节同尧历，新阳应嶰筒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528448'>仪韶来彩凤，占梦得真熊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528448'>寿考天资鲁，神灵岳降嵩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528448'>曲仪尊赤舄，歌咏美彤弓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528448'>夷险无殊节，诚明信保躬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528448'>济川先众楫，遵渚集飞鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528448'>炳炳丹青笔，堂堂社稷忠。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528448'>斗杓还列宿，廉陛倚层穹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528448'>文武俱为宪，诗书孰比隆。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528448'>规模三代远，谋略万夫雄。<div id='poem_sentence_11_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_528448'>字画诸王品，文章两汉风。<div id='poem_sentence_12_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_528448'>早登青琐闼，频入紫微宫。<div id='poem_sentence_13_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_528448'>器敏无馀刃，才豪妙吐虹。<div id='poem_sentence_14_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_528448'>声光连日月，气概俯华戎。<div id='poem_sentence_15_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_528448'>天上经纶合，人间制作工。<div id='poem_sentence_16_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_528448'>向来凝庶绩，谁复简清衷。<div id='poem_sentence_17_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_528448'>弦诵三雍富，舟车四海通。<div id='poem_sentence_18_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_528448'>地归铜柱北，春满玉关东。<div id='poem_sentence_19_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_528448'>养士菁莪盛，论才骏马空。<div id='poem_sentence_20_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_528448'>圣时方密勿，贤业助昭融。<div id='poem_sentence_21_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_528448'>螭纽乾符正，龙文帝鼐崇。<div id='poem_sentence_22_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_528448'>伊汤咸有德，房杜不言功。<div id='poem_sentence_23_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_528448'>礼秩群臣异，恩波此日丰。<div id='poem_sentence_24_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_528448'>宸章颁琬琰，相第列帡幪。<div id='poem_sentence_25_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_528448'>东壁文昭烂，西昆气郁葱。<div id='poem_sentence_26_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_528448'>节旄藏棨戟，茅土启龟蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_27_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_528448'>衮绣卿云里，貂蝉瑞霭中。<div id='poem_sentence_28_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_528448'>御奁金宝带，神厩玉花骢。<div id='poem_sentence_29_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_528448'>蓬岛波全阔，天钧乐未终。<div id='poem_sentence_30_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_528448'>禁香纷缥缈，朝佩杂玲珑。<div id='poem_sentence_31_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_528448'>芝草盈田紫，蟠桃照海红。<div id='poem_sentence_32_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_528448'>后彫凝秀发，难老湛方瞳。<div id='poem_sentence_33_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_528448'>冰质期姑射，丹砂唤葛洪。<div id='poem_sentence_34_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_528448'>潜机神宇定，睟表德符充。<div id='poem_sentence_35_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_528448'>瑞鹤千年羽，灵蓍五色丛。<div id='poem_sentence_36_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_528448'>旧传调鼎客，今识钓璜翁。<div id='poem_sentence_37_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_528448'>世世联台衮，年年拱帝聪。<div id='poem_sentence_38_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_528448'>欲知耆算永，元气等无穷。<div id='poem_sentence_39_528448_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_528448'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_528448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年8月</a>　服除。授从事郎荆南府掌书记，不赴。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c9cdbaea6797447a8c31331473eda0a0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c9cdbaea6797447a8c31331473eda0a0");'><span id='c9cdbaea6797447a8c31331473eda0a0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1117')">1116-1117年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='c9cdbaea6797447a8c31331473eda0a0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　居德兴，丁母忧，作许几墓志铭。作品：户部尚书许公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222932' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222932' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222932?labeling=true' target='_blank'>户部尚书许公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和六年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222932")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222932_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222932'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222932'>政和五年四月甲寅，中大夫、提举洪州玉隆观许公卒于袁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222932_comment'></div>公以文学起家，以材力结人主之知，为世名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222932_comment'></div>当朝庭建立法度之时，所更皆其要剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222932_comment'></div>凡事纷于前，众人圜视莫知所为，公独从容处决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222932_comment'></div>初若不以经意，退而视其规模，条析明甚，有深思熟虑不能至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222932_comment'></div>用此四历大镇，五为户部侍郎，一为尚书，官至中大夫，职至枢密直学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222932_comment'></div>虽间用言者数出，然天子思公，不逾时辄召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222932_comment'></div>故卒之日，贤士大夫皆衋然悲伤，以用公之材为未究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222932_comment'></div>公讳几，字先之，世居饶之馀干，至高祖始占籍信州贵溪，故今为贵溪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222932_comment'></div>曾祖待用、祖尧卿，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222932_comment'></div>皇考宗举，举进士，卒官秘书丞，以公故赠光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222932_comment'></div>公儿时有大志，出语惊人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222932_comment'></div>大丞相韩公琦镇大名，公在大名以诸生见，独伟视公，为加礼，遣诣太学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222932_comment'></div>未冠，擢上第，调筠州高安主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222932_comment'></div>光禄公间往视之，会摄邑事，规画良善，光禄喜曰：「儿能尔，吾何忧」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222932_comment'></div>为之信宿而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222932_comment'></div>丁光禄公忧，起主饶州乐平簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222932_comment'></div>已而为其令，大兴学校，课士习经，亲与之酬酢，虽旁邑亦遣子弟从学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222932_comment'></div>浚陂池利于民者，责其寮分任之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222932_comment'></div>独练湖之役为大，则躬按行其地，为之区处，溉田无虑万计，民刻石纪功，治行为江东第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222932_comment'></div>用荐者改宣德郎、知宣州南陵县，还民之托僧尼为奸者数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222932_comment'></div>勾当开封府右厢公事，尹高其能，虽府事亦关决公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222932_comment'></div>会复常平官，大臣首荐公，擢提举京西南路常平等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222932_comment'></div>奉使有旨，为开封府推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222932_comment'></div>丁普安太夫人忧，免丧除虞部、金部、户部员外郎，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222932_comment'></div>今上即位，有以永兴等路馈饷为言者，遣公驰视，数月毕，财以不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222932_comment'></div>馆北使，除大府少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222932_comment'></div>先是吏俸不时得，贫者患之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222932_comment'></div>公能使利无遗入，用品秩高下，分日而给，未几以均足闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222932_comment'></div>为提举南郊事务官，除将作监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222932_comment'></div>吏与工比为奸，盘结牢甚，如斲削涂塈丹雘之工，当以次用，而吏于役初，概给其廪，故浮耗不赀，且閒剧不均，诉者纷然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222932_comment'></div>公以楹数逆为之程，使未役其役者不食其食，费省而功倍，遂为永法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222932_comment'></div>除大理卿，改太仆，马政蕃息，入户部为侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222932_comment'></div>公前为郎多在户部，其财用出纳敛散，铢分缕析，皆有成法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222932_comment'></div>及莅官左曹，益当天下之剧，夙夜尽瘁，讲求利病罢行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222932_comment'></div>其大者必反复议论，务合熙宁、元丰之法，毅然不可回夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222932_comment'></div>上亦知公忠，乃多见纳用，议者以异时居大农无与公比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222932_comment'></div>除显谟阁待制、知郓州、充京东西路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222932_comment'></div>盗倚梁山为薮，害所被甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222932_comment'></div>公籍渔者十人为保，晨肆其出，夕责其归，否则同保以闻，自是穷治无脱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222932_comment'></div>汶上多衣冠，其嚚子憸孙，惟怙势横闾里，善良苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222932_comment'></div>公刑其尤者以徇，风俗为变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222932_comment'></div>迁显谟阁直学士、知成都府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222932_comment'></div>入见，除户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222932_comment'></div>以子丧乞外，上曰：「卿宣力久，其少安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222932_comment'></div>复除直学士、知成都府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222932_comment'></div>言者以公摇泉布法，降充待制、提举亳州明道宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222932_comment'></div>既投閒，筑室饶之东湖，尽江山之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222932_comment'></div>大观三年秋，亟召，除工部侍郎，数日改户部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222932_comment'></div>岁有大礼之费且倍，经人为公虑，公不取于下，不贷于中，前期而办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222932_comment'></div>会开封府李孝称领诏狱，以公摄尹事，剖决精明，廷中皆指相示曰：「是故为厢官者，其可犯耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222932_comment'></div>稍稍引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222932_comment'></div>拜本部尚书，兼详定一司敕令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222932_comment'></div>公练习邦赋，每檄在京库务及移文诸路，口授吏曰，某所为钱若干，某所为物若干，某费当取彼，某储当给彼，吏且听且书，莫知其端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222932_comment'></div>及覆视案牍，无一不如公言者，人人骇服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222932_comment'></div>言者以公治染院事不实，除龙图阁直学士、知婺州，俄降充天章阁待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222932_comment'></div>已而事白，除枢密直学士、河东路计度转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222932_comment'></div>公屡辞不获，则请广籴以绝豪右射利之奸，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222932_comment'></div>改真定府路安抚使，兼知成德军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222932_comment'></div>未逾月，徙河东路经略安抚使，兼知太原府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222932_comment'></div>河东被边，绵地数千里，公尽护诸将，纪律赫然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222932_comment'></div>及其暇时，修垦田法以利兵农，谨烽燧、明斥候，奸不得发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222932_comment'></div>或报衙头招集亡命，公用防秋法戍境上度兵官牛宗可，使用防城法，布鹿角、坏道路、为陷马坑，贼知有备，讫公去不敢窥边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222932_comment'></div>有恶少数人，结死党，号弟兄，其一犯法，悉捕治之，而流其为首者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222932_comment'></div>边郡例以抚养库钱易货他郡，公为盗欺，至乾没不可计，莫能擿其奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222932_comment'></div>公一追偿，无敢隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222932_comment'></div>以其赢劳将士，皆得其死力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222932_comment'></div>坐户部时裁减吏禄非是，夺枢密直学士，提举杭州洞霄宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222932_comment'></div>寻谪授永州团练副使，袁州安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222932_comment'></div>公屏居杖履，翛然无流落之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222932_comment'></div>既二年，上立皇太子，复中大夫、提举洪州玉隆观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222932_comment'></div>命未至而公卒，享年六十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222932_comment'></div>公于父母兄弟，慈祥孝友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222932_comment'></div>乐振人之急，成人之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222932_comment'></div>其于宗族，振之尤厚，于乡里成之尤力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222932_comment'></div>遇恩不任其子，而任其弟畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222932_comment'></div>及帅河东，辟畿自随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222932_comment'></div>终公身，五子其官者一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222932_comment'></div>故人陈于扬越客死，公为归其丧，具本业，其家至今赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222932_comment'></div>盖节义如此者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222932_comment'></div>公聪明强记，任气敢为，状貌雄伟，议论轩然，见者竦动，知其为非常人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222932_comment'></div>居官无小大久暂，要为不苟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222932_comment'></div>不以吏追民，不以狱诿吏，然民亦劝趋无敢怠，吏亦莫能窜其奸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222932_comment'></div>故去乐平、南陵且三十年，父老至今诵公怀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222932_comment'></div>于驭军理财知大体，遇事纤悉必有法度，后人用之辄享其便，虽欲出意变更，然卒不能出公之意外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222932_comment'></div>喜读书，为文立成，不属藁，亦未尝引以自名，专用缘饰吏事，故其所施为卓荦过人如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222932_comment'></div>有文集三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222932_comment'></div>妻赵氏，清献公抃之孙，封安康郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222932_comment'></div>男六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222932_comment'></div>曰璹、曰球，皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222932_comment'></div>琰，承奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222932_comment'></div>馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222932_comment'></div>女五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222932_comment'></div>适某官胡干化，亦前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222932_comment'></div>馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222932_comment'></div>琰将以政和六年九月某日，葬公饶州鄱阳县某乡里之原，以藻世姻，知公为悉，使来问铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222932_comment'></div>故掇公平生行事之大者书之，而系以铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222932_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_1222932'>天之生材，不妄付与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222932_comment'></div>惟与伟人，则莫量数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222932_comment'></div>公方妙龄，即以材著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222932_comment'></div>两乘轺车，三帅戎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222932_comment'></div>五司邦财，最久其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222932_comment'></div>事之纷来，众色疑沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222932_comment'></div>惟公怡然，麾以笑语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222932_comment'></div>孰幽无明，孰废无举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222932_comment'></div>烨如星旋，浩如川注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222932_comment'></div>旁观叹嗟，缩手无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1222932_comment'></div>出入践更，咸有誉处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1222932_comment'></div>虽班中台，十未施五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1222932_comment'></div>官三纪馀，卒以才赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1222932_comment'></div>彭蠡之南，是谓平楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1222932_comment'></div>冈峦属连，气象吞吐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1222932_comment'></div>筑宫其间，龟筮咸许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1222932_comment'></div>非公之英，孰配兹土？</div><div id='poem_sentence_113_1222932_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　居德兴，丁母忧，作胡君墓志铭。作品：主簿胡君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>主簿胡君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和六年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222943")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222943'>安定胡者，君族姓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222943_comment'></div>霖、君济者，君字名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222943_comment'></div>世家歙之婺源，尝得奉新主簿以归者，君爵里也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222943_comment'></div>曰顺宜、曰大明，居乡称善人长者，遗芳衍庆，逮其子孙者，君祖、父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222943_comment'></div>少孤，能自树立，喜读书属文，与其兄学四方，要必自我起家，虽祁寒剧暑不置者，君志操也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222943_comment'></div>以赀长雄其乡，务交结贤士大夫，间斥其馀，趋人之急，晚不乐试吏，居家以甘旨奉其亲者，君行义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222943_comment'></div>筑亭馆溪山之间，藏书万卷，以课子弟，莳花万本，以娱宾客，一时台阁之彦、戚里之贤，交口誉君，以文纪其实，至无虑数百篇者，君能自适其适而有闻于世者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222943_comment'></div>得年五十有三，以政和二年某月甲子殁牖下者，君之始终可考而无愧者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222943_comment'></div>曰清河张氏，宜家媲德，曰师礼、师雄、师愈，嶷然为举子之秀者，君之嫔、息也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222943_comment'></div>女一人，为进士张亨龙妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222943_comment'></div>孙男女若曾孙合十人者，君之后将大而无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222943_comment'></div>六年冬十有二月某甲子，卜其家百步曰西园之石者，君之葬所年月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222943_comment'></div>孔子曰：「隐居以求其志，行义以达其道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222943_comment'></div>君于志义，几于两得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222943_comment'></div>而孤师礼又能状君之行实，求铭于余，以行世传后，其言皆合理应法，此余所以为之铭而不得辞者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222943_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1222943'>德人之生，如玉粹然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222943_comment'></div>与瑑琮璧，交神享贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222943_comment'></div>宁韫诸石，辉山润川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222943_comment'></div>孰能自珍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222943_comment'></div>君实有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222943_comment'></div>不受世琢，独完其天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222943_comment'></div>徜徉林庐，匪轾匪轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222943_comment'></div>喜事如侠，遗神若仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222943_comment'></div>俯仰一世，归安九泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222943_comment'></div>绳绳诸郎，驹骏雏鹓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222943_comment'></div>尚想来世，幽光益传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222943_comment'></div>其植墓槚，清阴满阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222943_comment'></div>刻吾铭诗，信必有年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1222943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　居德兴，丁母忧，作母陈夫人行状。作品：夫人陈氏行状。<div id='poem_1222920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夫人陈氏行状<span class='inlineComment2'>（代张珌作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222920")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222920'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222920'>夫人陈氏，开封府开封人，内藏库使、遥授蔚州刺史赞之曾孙，累赠职方员外郎承道之孙，守曹州法曹参军咨之女，而奉议郎汪谷之妻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222920_comment'></div>蔚州以客从太祖汉、周间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222920_comment'></div>即位，录其劳，诸子踵入官，而承道独以病废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222920_comment'></div>生子咨、咏，始业诗书，为儒家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222920_comment'></div>咏举进士，至尚书屯田郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222920_comment'></div>咨以扈真宗祀汾阴，得试礼部，卒用其弟婿参知政事丁度恩奏初品官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222920_comment'></div>法曹之官于南也，为诸女择配，以非其士难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222920_comment'></div>闻奉议贤，曰「不可失也」，遂妻以长女，生男女八人而终，是为永嘉县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222920_comment'></div>永嘉之亡，奉议君哀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222920_comment'></div>以夫人娴内则，少孤，事其母孝，谓抚诸孤，莫宜夫人，遂聘以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222920_comment'></div>夫人内顺外严，通诗书，力勤俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222920_comment'></div>虽不逮舅姑之养，然事其像，朝夕薰修，岁时奠醊，甚于事其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222920_comment'></div>食饮不荐不先尝，踖焉如将见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222920_comment'></div>永嘉四男子，槃、棐、槩、楶，夫人鞠之尽力，自襁抱森然成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222920_comment'></div>诸子亦恩之，如实生己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222920_comment'></div>夫人既老，槃亦齿发衰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222920_comment'></div>其就养豫章，槃自子舍来省之，相持逾月不能诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222920_comment'></div>既行，以悲思卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222920_comment'></div>夫人二子，曰藻、曰汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222920_comment'></div>少学章句翰墨，皆夫人亲指授，有法度，程其日益之功，虽祁寒剧暑不置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222920_comment'></div>故藻登崇宁二年进士第，今为宣教郎，充详定《九域图志》所编修官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222920_comment'></div>奉议君与藻，仕皆小官，禄不足食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222920_comment'></div>夫人为簿其所入，铢量算计，不妄以毫发费，虽迨老不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222920_comment'></div>或谏止之，曰：「不尔无以养仕者之廉，且吾乐之，不为病也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222920_comment'></div>至宾客过从，则亲视肴醪，凡所以为甘旨之奉者，豫节而储之，以待一时之须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222920_comment'></div>故藻多得从名士游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222920_comment'></div>奉议君清修畏人，知宦不遂而归卧林壑间，以夫人生辇毂，疑于不满，夫人处之晏如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222920_comment'></div>暨藻之仕，意且讳贫矣，夫人每以奉议君所以励己者戒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222920_comment'></div>故藻亦所至自饬，不汲汲于苟进，繄夫人之训则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222920_comment'></div>然少喜佛书，母病疾，灼香于臂，无完肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222920_comment'></div>中年尤精确，晨起斋祓坐诵，虽事颠沛于前，不辍以观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222920_comment'></div>晡则置酒戏诸孙为笑乐，日以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222920_comment'></div>虽春秋高，彊健如壮者，事不少纵，阃内肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222920_comment'></div>盖主汪氏祭四十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222920_comment'></div>以今上登极恩封寿光县君，用政和三年九月制改封孺人，享年七十七，政和五年正月二十九日，卒于京师藻所居之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222920_comment'></div>于是奉议卒十年矣，棐、槩、楶、汇及诸女亦皆前死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222920_comment'></div>孙七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222920_comment'></div>恺，通仕郎、监泰州西溪盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222920_comment'></div>馀未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222920_comment'></div>卒之明年某月，合葬于饶州德兴县龙溪源冕木坞奉议、永嘉君之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222920_comment'></div>呜呼，夫人可谓贤矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222920_comment'></div>事亲孝而一之以诚，友夫义而济之以俭，抚子慈而成之以孝，卒也享寿考康宁，从禄万里而考终于其乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222920_comment'></div>呜呼，夫人其可无愧乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222920_comment'></div>诸孤不敢违杖而走请，以珌子婿，知之为详，故属书其懿范如此，以待世之立言者，图不朽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222920_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1222920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年5月</a>　居德兴，丁母忧。五月，服除。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d887df8e7ae24ac49cdfef36c0ab41ab_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d887df8e7ae24ac49cdfef36c0ab41ab");'><span id='d887df8e7ae24ac49cdfef36c0ab41ab_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1112')">1108-1112年</a>，30-34岁</div><div id='d887df8e7ae24ac49cdfef36c0ab41ab' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　年底，改江南西路提举学事司干当公事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在洪州，任江西提举学官。结识刘滂。后成多年至交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在洪州，结识徐俯、洪炎、洪刍等人，结社唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在洪州，有诗《春日》，为诗社诸公所称赏。<div id='poem_528416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和家叔春日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_528416'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528416'>晓看春水满方塘，静掩柴扉白日长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528416'>花意风光空烂漫，客愁山色对苍茫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528416'>扬州歌吹今何在，陶令田园亦就荒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528416'>试问南来米贵贱，欲随春浪过潇湘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年闰8月15日</a>　在洪州，中秋夜，与诸友登临赋咏。向子諲《水调歌头》（闰余有何好）载其事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在洪州，汪藻、张元干、徐俯、向子諲、吕本中、苏坚、苏庠诸友人结社唱和。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1111&endYear=1111')">1111年</a>　任在洪州，江西提举学官。有贺冬表。作品：江西提举司贺冬表。<div id='poem_1222624' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222624' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222624?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江西提举司贺冬表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1111年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1222624'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222624'>日官祗日于朝，告阳来复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222624_comment'></div>天子承天之意，与物咸亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222624_comment'></div>爰修亚岁之仪，茂对履时之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222624_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下诚参化育，幽赞神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222624_comment'></div>朔复朔而谨治历之端，形无形而体好生之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222624_comment'></div>推步舒长之景，数得周正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222624_comment'></div>逍遥供奉之班，心存魏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222624_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1222624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222624'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷六。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222624_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年1月</a>　在洪州，送别向子諲。<br /></div>

-----title
宁国
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0a6096763def446e953b3c9594b72f03_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0a6096763def446e953b3c9594b72f03");'><span id='0a6096763def446e953b3c9594b72f03_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>，41岁</div><div id='0a6096763def446e953b3c9594b72f03' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年6月</a>　过宁国，于传舍借观友人叶择甫所藏李伯时画，并跋。作品：跋叶择甫李伯时画。<div id='poem_1222877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋叶择甫李伯时画<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十三年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222877")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222877'>若人云亡，画笔中绝，使杜少陵见之，当复有郑公长夜之叹耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222877_comment'></div>宣和元年六月，鄱阳汪藻借观于宁国传舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222877_comment'></div>宣和初余通守宣城，时择甫官宁国，出此画，书其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222877_comment'></div>比自泉南移宣城，过福唐，择甫复以示余，则二十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222877_comment'></div>一见如隔生事，为感叹久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222877_comment'></div>绍兴癸亥季春朔，新安汪藻书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1222877_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
旌德
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a3ab586b7a214ed08555e5cf05266607_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a3ab586b7a214ed08555e5cf05266607");'><span id='a3ab586b7a214ed08555e5cf05266607_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>，41岁</div><div id='a3ab586b7a214ed08555e5cf05266607' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>盛夏，行旌德山中，有诗。作品：大热行旌德山中不可车马至凌氏林亭。<div id='poem_528256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大热行旌德山中不可车马步至凌氏林亭诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528256")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528256_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528256'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528256'>踞石休茧足，掬泉洗赪容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528256'>于何脱冠履，共指云外峰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528256'>翳彼园屋小，钩帘苍翠重。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528256'>庭空燕雀乳，树老莓苔封。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528256'>露泫过墙竹，风凄横涧松。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528256'>欣然曲肱卧，鼻息春醅浓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528256'>推床上马去，孰是陈元龙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528256_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528256'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_528256_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>初冬，复过凌氏园，有诗。作品：再过凌氏园复用前韵。<div id='poem_528276' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528276' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528276?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再过凌氏园复用前韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528276")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528276_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528276'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528276'>儿辈病元亮，斗筲羁曼容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528276'>何时跨鸿鹄，食藕莲花峰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528276'>小槛再游历，轻寒裘未重。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528276'>人家当卮黍，不愧千户封。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528276'>愿因琴高生，傥见乔与松。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528276'>从兹毁车马，永绝世味浓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528276'>岁晚复来此，清阴期箨龙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528276'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_528276_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宜兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='792e093ae3304b0b8a948318e9be6d63_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("792e093ae3304b0b8a948318e9be6d63");'><span id='792e093ae3304b0b8a948318e9be6d63_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1126')">1119-1126年</a>，41-48岁</div><div id='792e093ae3304b0b8a948318e9be6d63' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　沿水路往阳羡，有诗纪行。作品：汴中放船归阳羡。<div id='poem_528297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汴中放船归阳羡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1119年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528297")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528297'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528297'>流澌欲作环佩鸣，枯木未肯回春声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528297'>舟人坐恐雪为祟，娇鸦又舞天边城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528297'>天公知我不足厄，乞与十日霜风晴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528297'>遥遥烟堤护玉镜，滉滉云海浮金钲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528297'>揽衣坐数踵间息，窥见宇宙无馀情。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528297'>灯花也似调儿女，咄咄笑我长宵征。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528297'>我生底处不堪著，未归且杂吴儿耕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528297'>纵无邻翁饮子美，会有稚子迎渊明。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528297'>仙山况闻连洞壑，饵朮或可求长生。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528297'>闲中日月吾所有，此外付之人重轻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528297_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528297'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_528297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　春，李正民有诗送之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　寓居宜兴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　寓居宜兴。平贼乱后有文。作品：信州二堂碑。<div id='poem_1222921' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222921' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222921?labeling=true' target='_blank'>信州二堂碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222921")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222921_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222921'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222921'>宣和二年十月，盗发清溪，入睦入歙入杭，蹂十州之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222921_comment'></div>间以兵围信，不克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222921_comment'></div>天子为出禁旅，付大臣讨平之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222921_comment'></div>初，清溪民阻山为暴，吏不时制，寖剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222921_comment'></div>部使者不以闻，益放兵无所忌，至攻府寺，略人民，由是东南皆警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222921_comment'></div>时守州令邑者，疆比壤连，无一人奉尺书为朝廷言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222921_comment'></div>独信州王君曰：「贼兴篁竹间，不旬日其锋如此，势非可以朝夕破者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222921_comment'></div>今不百里俯吾境，万一不戒，如吾民何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222921_comment'></div>即斥金帛募士，增陴浚隍，修战斗具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222921_comment'></div>按蹊隧所通者二十馀所，悉以兵戍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222921_comment'></div>用通守王侯策，起其属高志临，付以军政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222921_comment'></div>条便宜，章十馀上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222921_comment'></div>且以计策告当路之用事及城守者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222921_comment'></div>十二月，贼覆浙东，军张甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222921_comment'></div>顷之焚婺源、开化，屡以兵偪信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222921_comment'></div>知有备，引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222921_comment'></div>正月，攻江山、常山，残之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222921_comment'></div>于是绕信境数百里，皆为贼区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222921_comment'></div>君居其中，部勒诸将益严，与王、高二侯，勠力缔谋，屯韩岩以托开化，屯馆头以捍常山，屯竹巘以捍江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222921_comment'></div>率深沟固垒，日扬兵境上，为不可测者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222921_comment'></div>独柳家都不为备，匿精甲数里间，志临以亲兵仆旗鼓踵其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222921_comment'></div>贼果虞三戍之众，不敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222921_comment'></div>二月，既入衢，则鼓行寇柳家都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222921_comment'></div>营崄峙枨，益驱人为兵，欲必举信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222921_comment'></div>初以偏师尝，我克之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222921_comment'></div>已而尽锐攻，号十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222921_comment'></div>志临出奇兵鏖击，贼大败，拔营去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222921_comment'></div>追奔数十里，焚荡俘馘至不可胜计，缚其伪统军以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222921_comment'></div>因分其兵为三：一自韩岩复开化，一自馆头复常山，一自柳家都复江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222921_comment'></div>长驱迅卷，遂复衢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222921_comment'></div>贼之在他境者，皆望风遁去，东南以平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222921_comment'></div>于是天子下诏曰：「信州守臣愈，斩贼有功，其进职若官殊等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222921_comment'></div>通守举舜亦裨赞之良也，增秩次之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222921_comment'></div>而以志临为衢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222921_comment'></div>君与王侯既相与侈上之赐，而喜释于守城之劳也，乃筑堂二，曰「示喜」、曰「后乐」，而书其本末来请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222921_comment'></div>藻曰：天下之事，所贵于智者，以审于祸福成败之机，而图其大者，区区一时胜负之功，不足议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222921_comment'></div>方盗奋于承平百年之馀，民不知兵，吏不知守，独君察于几微，慨然以书抵在位者，或非笑，或怒，且排妒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222921_comment'></div>卒之无一不如君策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222921_comment'></div>及情见势屈，而向之为吏者，方狃于故常，曰「吾知谨簿书期会而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222921_comment'></div>吾书生也，何以兵为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222921_comment'></div>巽懦诪张，争为完躯保妻子之计，视刈其民如草菅然，而无以善之，曾未有奉一州六县无秋毫之失归报天子如君者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222921_comment'></div>而余顾以为区区一时胜负之功，诚以信于江南为四塞地，使狺然吞噬之心西摇，抚南窥建，北扰宣饶，则虽磨以岁月，未能遽下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222921_comment'></div>惟君以方千里之地，屹然于横流奔沸之中，扼其吭，笞其背，使气夺力殚，不能尺寸进，卒夷其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222921_comment'></div>当是时，并江循海，三路三十馀州，皆坚壁清野，倚君为重，则君之建立为何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222921_comment'></div>是宜天子差功第赏，书君令甲，而信州一日暴于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222921_comment'></div>则斯堂之以喜乐名者，君与信人果得而私哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222921_comment'></div>君通经术，长于吏治，所至皆可纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222921_comment'></div>始君之至州，无十日之赢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222921_comment'></div>既二年而镪腐粒陈，以之赏功募士，调兵食，皆出于此，可谓为政知所先后，而功非偶然立者，可歌也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222921_comment'></div>乃作诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1222921'>惟帝奠治，以天为区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222921_comment'></div>藐彼南服，大江之隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222921_comment'></div>八圣休养，狃于丕平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222921_comment'></div>有不能驯，啸呼以惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222921_comment'></div>奋厥蝼蚁，敢仇王师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222921_comment'></div>帝顾在列，孰予往笞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222921_comment'></div>矫矫禁旅，统之公侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222921_comment'></div>春祃于野，旋师麦秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222921_comment'></div>囚献刑得，第勋策劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222921_comment'></div>孰固吾圉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222921_comment'></div>予其汝褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222921_comment'></div>在列咸启，信为偏城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222921_comment'></div>曰守臣愈，实能弭兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222921_comment'></div>惟昔首孽，众为不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222921_comment'></div>曰此猘者，吾疆惧纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222921_comment'></div>乃理隍壁，乃褒选锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222921_comment'></div>爰走爰集，严兵待攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222921_comment'></div>贼屡闯境，引师环之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222921_comment'></div>一遇鏖击，崩奔不支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222921_comment'></div>坐以支堞，扼其三方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222921_comment'></div>邻国仰首，如川得防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222921_comment'></div>帝曰俞哉，惟汝予力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222921_comment'></div>锡之命书，光宠而国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222921_comment'></div>愈拜稽首，敢扬王休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222921_comment'></div>乃作华屋，睇山俯流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222921_comment'></div>君在斯堂，寄适云杪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222921_comment'></div>里民户歌，杂以嬉笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222921_comment'></div>君在斯堂，宾客粥粥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222921_comment'></div>间于忧虞，起舞相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222921_comment'></div>民祝君寿，长为父师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222921_comment'></div>毋或去我，阽于垫危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222921_comment'></div>士曰君材，维试之仂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222921_comment'></div>如何此州，私我贤伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222921_comment'></div>凡厥本剽，载之民谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222921_comment'></div>来者是式，君将在朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222921_comment'></div>我为颂诗，繄史之订。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222921_comment'></div>匪民之私，天子之庆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_85_1222921_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　寓居宜兴。作张根行状。作品：朝散大夫直龙图阁张公行状。<div id='poem_1222918' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222918' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222918?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫直龙图阁张公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1121年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222918")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222918_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222918'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222918'>公讳根，字知常，姓张氏，唐宰相文瓘之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222918_comment'></div>五季时，有徙居江淮者，故今为饶州德兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222918_comment'></div>大理通直父子，以气节言行为乡人所宗，一时豪杰，皆拜其家如子姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222918_comment'></div>至中奉公始举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222918_comment'></div>公幼庄重，方髫稚已凛然有成人风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222918_comment'></div>性嗜学，扫一室独居，人不堪其忧，澹如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222918_comment'></div>饶士盛东南，应书常数千人，所取裁百一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222918_comment'></div>公以童子在选中，时年十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222918_comment'></div>入京师，补太学生，群数千人试于有司，复中第二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222918_comment'></div>自是以文居诸生右，而行独修饬，出入皆可从迹，祭酒博士欲召见之，不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222918_comment'></div>连三试礼部，以元丰五年擢进士第，年二十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222918_comment'></div>礼部尚书黄公履闻其名，以女妻之，归拜大父母、父母于堂，人以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222918_comment'></div>调临江军司理参军，迁瀛州防御推官，知处州遂昌县事，有政绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222918_comment'></div>代去，民挽留之不可，碑其事以怀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222918_comment'></div>用荐者于法应迁，以大父母年高致其仕，则恩及之，遂以通直郎致仕，时年三十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222918_comment'></div>丁令人忧，有绝人之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222918_comment'></div>葬之日，鹤翔于墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222918_comment'></div>上嗣服，问辅臣人材可用者，曾丞相布以公对，而翰林学士曾肇及部使者亦奏公节行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222918_comment'></div>于是落致仕，召对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222918_comment'></div>力辞，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222918_comment'></div>则面陈人主能不以功业之敏自矜，盈成之易自佚，守之以中，求天下无治不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222918_comment'></div>因言东南灾伤，赈给有限，愿广求所以宽恤之术，而杭州置造局可罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222918_comment'></div>「臣尝谓人主一日万几，所恃者方寸之地耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222918_comment'></div>一累于物，以失其正，则聪明志虑且耗怠，而贤不肖混淆，至于纪纲不振矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222918_comment'></div>愿陛下清心省欲，以窒祸之原，天下幸甚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222918_comment'></div>上嘉纳，将用公，而小人不利，以为昧朝廷大体，授公亲贤宅教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222918_comment'></div>未几，除通判杭州，以亲老，乞监西京东岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222918_comment'></div>丁中奉公忧，服除，提举江南西路常平等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222918_comment'></div>洎终任，田畴之垦、桑柘之植、沟防之修者，以千万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222918_comment'></div>时居养安济法行久，有司颇以浮冗，侵常平本钱，或取给于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222918_comment'></div>公约为数条上之，所节过半，大臣不悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222918_comment'></div>岁旱饥，尽发常平米及遮留上供米赈济，已旧责、蠲新赋，凡可以弭灾，无不为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222918_comment'></div>手疏力请于朝，凡八十馀上，纤悉有法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222918_comment'></div>躬遍所部，阅半岁，暑行数万里，虽瘴疫冒之而前，官吏为惶恐尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222918_comment'></div>于是方数千里，流冗悉归，施及邻壤，其全活者不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222918_comment'></div>会中贵人为走马者怙力挟私，以官吏散军衣给钱非是，举一路帅臣监司守贰而下，劾罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222918_comment'></div>公曰：「散军衣半钱，例也，况其数加旧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222918_comment'></div>祖宗置东南军伍与西北异，上下相安百五十年矣，今一旦以给散坐帅臣监司，恐军寖骄不可制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222918_comment'></div>且帅臣监司，朝廷与之分忧顾者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222918_comment'></div>政使有罪，犹当待报，直以体量尺纸罢之，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222918_comment'></div>今兹振贷，奉行尤藉官吏，乃空十郡，仅有存者，非徒无检视蹂践之患，虑别启奸倖，为朝廷忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222918_comment'></div>于是诏悉还之，官吏相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222918_comment'></div>自崇宁行盐钞法，和买民帛，率不得偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222918_comment'></div>虽朝廷令借封桩钱，而钱特空名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222918_comment'></div>公乃大发常平米，计直予民，犹不能半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222918_comment'></div>会星变大赦，则奏：「自祖宗以来，岁给蚕盐以取民输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222918_comment'></div>今民既输五年，而一县至有负民五十万缗者，将何所控告？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222918_comment'></div>谓宜因霈恩，尽给今岁租百四十万斛，给中都百二十万，而官兵度五十万，使岁入如数，犹缺四十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222918_comment'></div>旧以盐利三十馀万缗和籴，故虽凶岁不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222918_comment'></div>自更法以来，州县重取百姓耗米以给，民既不堪其苛，而和买四十万缗，复以无所从出之钱给之，民心易摇，不可不虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222918_comment'></div>议者徒谓亏榷货务额，此岂知社稷至计哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222918_comment'></div>未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222918_comment'></div>间会诏书许诸路监司实封言事，公言：「本路去岁诏蠲租四十万，而户部责发如数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222918_comment'></div>祖宗立东南上供额六百万斛，赐发运司本钱数百万缗，使岁广籴以备非常，随补随取，此万世良法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222918_comment'></div>自希恩者以为羡馀献之，故朝廷不足则下诸路补发，势必敷于民，为无穷之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222918_comment'></div>缘此漕计窘乏，无名之敛百出，臣以为补发不当复催，尽以盐额还漕司，籴本钱还发运司便」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222918_comment'></div>已而运盐复元丰法，稍以盐还民，公之力为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222918_comment'></div>洪州官没锡数万斤，系兵吏七百人于狱，株连且千计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222918_comment'></div>公曰：「十年失于讥察，有司之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222918_comment'></div>今罗取无罪之人苦之，追偿必不可得之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222918_comment'></div>方岁凶之馀，冤滥如此，何以召和气乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222918_comment'></div>朝廷为罢狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222918_comment'></div>兴国民郭友馀习妖教，郡以屡赦闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222918_comment'></div>公言：「友馀，张角术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222918_comment'></div>异时李逄尝以此惑民，请论如法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222918_comment'></div>大观四年，领广盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222918_comment'></div>入议，时上躬政事，隆宽尽下，公欲遂成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222918_comment'></div>洎对上劳苦良渥，首以江西赈济为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222918_comment'></div>公奏：「救荒，臣职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222918_comment'></div>惟本路阙乏，所请辄从，民力以纾，为大利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222918_comment'></div>若行此数年，公私自然充实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222918_comment'></div>上深然之，赐绯衣银鱼以遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222918_comment'></div>且曰：「推行法度，要在得人，不扰于民，方为利国」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222918_comment'></div>公奏：「训辞深厚，乞颁之天下，付之史官」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222918_comment'></div>从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222918_comment'></div>敕归本路，有所见，奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222918_comment'></div>公顿首谢，因言：「臣幸因天宁节随班上寿，不胜封人之祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222918_comment'></div>昔管仲祝桓公以无忘在莒时，臣亦愿陛下无忘答天戒时」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222918_comment'></div>上大悦，即日趣议盐事，得内侍省牒，事听关白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222918_comment'></div>公即奏：「陛下幸蠲烦苛、破朋党，而士大夫以大臣不和，议论不一，观望苟且，莫肯自尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222918_comment'></div>陛下毁石刻、除党籍，与天下更始，而有司以大臣仇怨，废锢自如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222918_comment'></div>为治之害，莫大于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222918_comment'></div>愿思所以协和之且，申严戒敕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222918_comment'></div>又请「限丰岁广籴之数，以毋夺民食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222918_comment'></div>精县令铨补之法，以毋失民平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222918_comment'></div>勿妄支移常平封桩钱，以志灭二敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222918_comment'></div>使中国竞、百姓富、朝廷正、群臣和，以示人主尊强隆盛之势」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222918_comment'></div>反复数千言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222918_comment'></div>时执政近臣方大为矛盾，故公言屡及之，以感悟上意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222918_comment'></div>迁转运使，人谓公德行文学，宜在朝廷，处之非其地，而公不屑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222918_comment'></div>会岁饥疫，朝廷责补发不已，又促输纳䌷绢之期，追远年无名之责，鬻官田者大亏上供之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222918_comment'></div>公历陈利害，奏罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222918_comment'></div>且言「盐法既更，其封桩盐可尽给和买，还之民」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222918_comment'></div>力陈，见听以广盐敷额，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222918_comment'></div>以直达有劳，进两官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222918_comment'></div>公于漕计，能权其赢，为转输之本，故屡办而民不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222918_comment'></div>寻徙淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222918_comment'></div>先是漕臣承抛降，虑不及事，则以浮数调民，州县递增，所取无艺，吏缘为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222918_comment'></div>或州郡以非所产，至漫数年不一输者，公令民必实，且为纳直通融之法，民欢趋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222918_comment'></div>有出非其时，地非所出者，复曲折为陈，或纾或免，其事非一，当时称便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222918_comment'></div>被旨赴阙，大臣以有亲嫌言者，令再任，除直龙图阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222918_comment'></div>岁水灾甚，民流满道，而钱法遽更，农末皆病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222918_comment'></div>公乞蠲租赋，尽散洛口米、常平、青苗斛斗赈贷，且通一路有无应办，公私为之两济，诏书褒谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222918_comment'></div>寻以江淮诸司使臣游蠹诸郡，命公按之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222918_comment'></div>公悉条其状并所自以闻，诏各驱还所役，违者从公械治，于是大失权倖意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222918_comment'></div>徙两浙，公闻苏杭局每物必十倍其费，以其一供奉，馀悉饷权倖为己私，穷之则火其籍，如苏州一日焚官物八十万是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222918_comment'></div>于是因辞免慷慨力陈，命以之寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1222918_comment'></div>复以表谢，其略曰：「虽以天下奉一人，不为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1222918_comment'></div>然得丘民为天子，顾不重哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1222918_comment'></div>搢绅诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1222918_comment'></div>小人由是得以间公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1222918_comment'></div>会盗刘五暴庐、寿，公走助宪臣破之，除秘阁修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1222918_comment'></div>以渠魁未擒，不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1222918_comment'></div>方欲条上讨贼之方，而中遣贵人董捕，欲自以为功，乃奏罢宪臣，而公亦坐降两官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1222918_comment'></div>自淮贼扰，军兴颇乏，公以为县官空匮，未有甚于此时，而当路恬不警省，万一有缓急，何以待之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1222918_comment'></div>因手诏取会漕司财用，乃言：「东南诸路阙乏之由，除拨赐、赡学、宗室等财用田产，添置官兵及朝廷非汎抛买外，一项茶盐钱并入榷货务，应和买盐并支见钱，而民卒不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1222918_comment'></div>乃至军储，亦月为之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1222918_comment'></div>稍有水旱，即干叩朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1222918_comment'></div>此大弊也，其原自榷货务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1222918_comment'></div>朝廷纵未能尽还岁额，若止分其半以助漕司，岁会天下，合得和买茶蚕盐价赐之，许折兑上供钱，以示大信于民，诸路当亦少宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1222918_comment'></div>茶盐法行十馀年，尚未立租额，岁务增羡，民穷困不聊生，可为流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1222918_comment'></div>今籴本之外，复须五百万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1222918_comment'></div>属者赵霆宣御笔，令于额外计置斛米，岁终殿最正用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1222918_comment'></div>漕司方以经入不足为忧，不知钱何所出，恐迫之即不能无骚扰之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1222918_comment'></div>今民和买既不得钱，而斛斗又非倍输不可，其间官户以倖免，豪猾以赂移，所苦者特畏法贫弱之民，可谓无名无数，高下不均之甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1222918_comment'></div>而有司方以用度不继，率取给于此，虽人知其非，苟避诛罚，莫肯为陛下言者，况复使之额外计置哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1222918_comment'></div>因进三说：一曰常平止纳息以抑兼并，二曰下户均出役钱以绝奸伪，三曰市易取净利以役商贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1222918_comment'></div>虽名非正，然与敷和买而不售其直，什一而使之倍输，额外无名无数之敛有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1222918_comment'></div>愿陛下储此钱以驭四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1222918_comment'></div>若夫理财，尤在节用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1222918_comment'></div>而节用以修造为先，修造虽于国体有不可废者，比类以此固宠市恩，不可不察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1222918_comment'></div>其次如人臣赐第、赐带、予金帛、给田屋之类，尤为泛滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1222918_comment'></div>佐命如赵普，不闻官为造第也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1222918_comment'></div>定策如韩琦，不闻彫墙峻宇僭拟宫省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1222918_comment'></div>今乃人得居而有之，奈何掠民肤髓为厮役之奉乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1222918_comment'></div>书奏，自禁中擿节用之说，付有司看详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1222918_comment'></div>而大臣及议者不察，谓公言利摇成法，章交上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1222918_comment'></div>上察其诚，不之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1222918_comment'></div>会御前人船所占留直达纲船，公以上供期迫，乞还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1222918_comment'></div>且因起发竹石，上言：「本路一竹之费，无虑五十缗，他路犹不止此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1222918_comment'></div>今不以充苑囿而入诸臣之家，民力之奉将安所涯？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1222918_comment'></div>愿示休息之期，以厚天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1222918_comment'></div>书奏，权贵积怒未发间，御笔以直达促限，令漕臣较州郡赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1222918_comment'></div>公贴黄亲书，力陈人情有大不可者，乞展限，其辞激烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1222918_comment'></div>奉御笔落职监信州酒税，有「轻躁妄言，不循分义」之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1222918_comment'></div>外廷方莫测，而台臣复论前奏常平事，责授濠州团练副使，郴州安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1222918_comment'></div>寻以讨贼功，许自便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1222918_comment'></div>更宣和改元赦，复朝奉大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1222918_comment'></div>夏祭赦，复朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1222918_comment'></div>宣和二年六月十七日，以疾终于家，享年六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1222918_comment'></div>公诚孝，甫六岁已能知母疾，疗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1222918_comment'></div>通直曰：「是必为孝子矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1222918_comment'></div>既罢临江，时中奉公客熙河未归，步驰省者再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1222918_comment'></div>冒寒暑，往返万馀里，卒御之以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1222918_comment'></div>自是专以奉亲为乐，举天下无以易其志者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1222918_comment'></div>时四亲在堂，随其意奉之，日躬仆妾之劳，有古人所难者。<div class='inline'
