id='poem_sentence_155_1222918_comment'></div>令人疾病，一夕须发为变，扶持弥月，癯然骨立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1222918_comment'></div>既卒，勺饮不入口者七日，屡绝复苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1222918_comment'></div>方哀毁甚，而奉饮食起居，无一不如生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1222918_comment'></div>啜粥寝苫，不盥不栉，不易衣，不尝味，不饮药，泣不绝声，终丧三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1222918_comment'></div>及侍祖妣疾、执父丧，亦如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1222918_comment'></div>终其身孺慕不已，言及辄声与涕俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1222918_comment'></div>初，公之请老也，年方壮，人惜其遽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1222918_comment'></div>公曰：「养及四亲，人之至幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1222918_comment'></div>万一有不及，为终身忧，其可缓乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1222918_comment'></div>是年以父母之恩及其祖妣，而以妻封及其母，乡人彭汝砺为文颂叹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1222918_comment'></div>未几，复以己得之服为祖荣，于是闻者莫不耸动，而天下人知公名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1222918_comment'></div>公居山林久，一旦为天子所知，起之召对，士大夫想闻其风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1222918_comment'></div>及对，首陈谠论，卓然以名节当上意，于出处皆合，天下益贤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1222918_comment'></div>自此三赐对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1222918_comment'></div>洎奉使十馀年，其面陈者不计，章疏凡数百上，悉天下大计，触当时之讳，诋方行之令，与大臣权倖为敌而无所阿附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1222918_comment'></div>反覆穷尽，不度可否，以身任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1222918_comment'></div>有宰执台谏所不敢言，人为股栗而公不恤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1222918_comment'></div>上亦知公精忠，每排众议用之，数加器使奖赉，于开陈多见听纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1222918_comment'></div>而小人权倖日以谗公，虽卒坐言谴死，而天下拱手推为正人钜德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1222918_comment'></div>卒之日，识与不识，皆为霣涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1222918_comment'></div>公之学不守章句，居閒十有六年，专覃思经史，务欲明圣人之道而见之行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1222918_comment'></div>故发为议论，辨博闳深，援引古今，深知治体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1222918_comment'></div>在元祐则言诋新法、置理诉司者，在建中则言不当弃地，在大观、政和则言籴本、和买、茶盐法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1222918_comment'></div>其大者欲人主正心术、去朋党、斥玩好，而于论边事尤详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1222918_comment'></div>其至自熙河，深以中国受屈为耻，得其曲折，归以告彭汝砺，使并王赡荐用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1222918_comment'></div>其说以为「二边之患，近而且遽者，惟熙河、青唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1222918_comment'></div>以其与夏人相为掎角，而国家惩宝元、元丰之失，以兵为讳，非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1222918_comment'></div>夫维大舟者必屡折其势，制猛兽者必先困其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1222918_comment'></div>彼夏贼蕞尔，政当徐以术制之，不当急与之较」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1222918_comment'></div>乃陈攻御备守策上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1222918_comment'></div>以弃熙河为持右臂授羌，将为陇蜀之害，而守熙河非灭青唐、取河南不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1222918_comment'></div>其后朝廷卒不弃熙河，王赡取青唐，悉如公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1222918_comment'></div>元符间，夏人穷蹙，藉契丹请平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1222918_comment'></div>公以为自祖宗以来，每敌犯塞，为害益深，所侵益大，所须益多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1222918_comment'></div>不取，后稍振必复为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1222918_comment'></div>不若厚礼其使，使乾顺身入朝，否则归我河南，质其大臣爱子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1222918_comment'></div>皆不从，则曲在彼，而我师有名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1222918_comment'></div>彼固已失其咽喉，若由兰会浮槎以进，一夕可至，所谓迅雷不及掩耳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1222918_comment'></div>会命已行，不果从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1222918_comment'></div>后朝廷每有事西方，未尝不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1222918_comment'></div>至论常平，则又言之，欲必取二敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1222918_comment'></div>自陈东南无事，欲行死边塞，求人可用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1222918_comment'></div>用人当如李愬缚元济之奇，不当如樊哙行匈奴之诞，人皆伟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1222918_comment'></div>公于吏治不为文具，凡劳险烦剧，人所不堪者，未尝辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1222918_comment'></div>临事强明，人不能欺，尤汲汲于恤民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1222918_comment'></div>与客论利病，常至夜分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1222918_comment'></div>有所得立陈，推见本末，能使朝廷必从己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1222918_comment'></div>其驭吏严而不伤，升黜以核实，不以偏辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1222918_comment'></div>故自为州县吏至为部使者，人皆取法，畏而服之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1222918_comment'></div>于施财乐善如嗜欲，然至宠利，则低回畏避，甚于机阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1222918_comment'></div>居太学时，得家问辄举箧授同舍之贫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1222918_comment'></div>所至坐客常满，亲友游士馆于公家者，常数十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1222918_comment'></div>葬死字孤，皆得其所求而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1222918_comment'></div>士之落南繇江西以出者，多赖公以生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1222918_comment'></div>大臣台谏以忠斥者，率数千里追赆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1222918_comment'></div>退视其奉养陋甚，死之日馀铜唾壶、书数簏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1222918_comment'></div>闻人小善，必演而成之，虽昧平生，亦拳拳慰荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1222918_comment'></div>或斥非其罪者，虽自敌以上，非职所及，亦冒为之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1222918_comment'></div>然平生未尝以私干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1222918_comment'></div>其迁官十，悉以劳以恩而不磨勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1222918_comment'></div>淮南之僚有攘公之功取优迁，而赏不及公者，人皆愤之，公未尝言及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1222918_comment'></div>坐淮贼例镌官，则乞并降己官，以除其负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1222918_comment'></div>得圭田，又损己而均之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1222918_comment'></div>其与人不校，反调护之类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1222918_comment'></div>然朝廷亦雅高其节，始以服推其祖，晚以子之官官其叔父，皆非故事，特旨从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1222918_comment'></div>平居谦厚不伐，胸中洞然，一言之出，终身可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1222918_comment'></div>喜面折人过，然退无异言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1222918_comment'></div>于人委曲成就，无所不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1222918_comment'></div>及忠义激烈，万牛莫能回其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1222918_comment'></div>居乡里，于亲疏长幼、大小厚薄，无不用其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1222918_comment'></div>盖人有一善，可以名其终身者，在公皆不足道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1222918_comment'></div>夫人黄氏，南华县君，改封宜人，知书，有贤行，先公四十日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1222918_comment'></div>子四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1222918_comment'></div>焘，太学博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1222918_comment'></div>熹，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1222918_comment'></div>煇、焕未官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1222918_comment'></div>女七人，适秘书郎黄伯思、起居郎李纲、太学博士李富国、大府寺丞薛良显、杭州监税范渭、宝应县丞虞澹，一人尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1222918_comment'></div>至老未尝释书不观，故下至天文、地理、卜筮、图纬、历数，无不精通，而尤深释氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1222918_comment'></div>其文温润纯粹，仁义之言蔼如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1222918_comment'></div>诗平澹简古似其人，乡人师之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1222918_comment'></div>随其材，或文或行，皆有可称，而其弟相、朴，遂以文学躐台省、跻侍从，为名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1222918_comment'></div>其子焘，亦以任子力学，廷中第三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1222918_comment'></div>有释《周礼》、《易》、《春秋》等书三百六十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1222918_comment'></div>公早树立，隐然有公辅望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1222918_comment'></div>自亲亡，力思所以报国，故身虽不在朝廷，而未尝一日忘君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1222918_comment'></div>尝患风俗上下相蒙以取利，每因职事所及，灾异所询，于爱君恤民之际，谆谆言之，又以告大臣亲旧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1222918_comment'></div>尝曰：「苟有以天下为度者，吾从矣，亦何常之有哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1222918_comment'></div>而妻父黄履尤器公，以为可属大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1222918_comment'></div>虽相去千里，公有言必告，有大事亦以咨公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1222918_comment'></div>如救邹浩之类，皆自公发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1222918_comment'></div>其裨益之功，阴及天下非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1222918_comment'></div>而谗者疾公不置，以天子聪明大度，知公如此，而曾不得一日立于朝廷之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1222918_comment'></div>或以时未可言，谓公少贬者，公曰：「吾以委蛇事君，虽出没风波万变之中，随宜救世，而无功名富贵之累」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1222918_comment'></div>为得圣人用心，顾世人未知之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1222918_comment'></div>使遂其志，施设何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1222918_comment'></div>闻贬郴阳，独挈其所著书以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1222918_comment'></div>及返，犹疏时事数千言，须上悟而陈之，且属弟侍御史朴诵言于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1222918_comment'></div>疾已革，其语不伦矣，而所道亦时事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1222918_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1222918_comment'></div>可谓忠义出于天性，古之全德君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1222918_comment'></div>诸孤将以某年某月某甲子，合葬公夫人于其里铸印墩，谨录其行事如右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1222918_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_257_1222918_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　寓居宜兴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　寓居宜兴。新年，有诗抒怀。作品：偶书。<div id='poem_528278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528278")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528278'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528278'>长簟北窗下，抛书任纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528278'>娟娟稚筱上，熠熠丛榴明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528278'>眷此感佳节，怊然怆平生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528278'>少年文翰场，结客俱擅名。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528278'>瑶草俟采掇，云鸿肆遐征。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528278'>如何二十载，日与忧患并。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528278'>骨肉随逝水，儿童长柴荆。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528278'>向来交臂人，接武霄汉行。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528278'>姻亲岁时会，尊酒怀抱倾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528278'>兹余岂复愿，顾影良自惊。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528278'>飞雨夜来急，涛翻江上城。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528278'>田家梦亦好，想像秋稼成。<div id='poem_sentence_11_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_528278'>新春了在眼，续我斋庖清。<div id='poem_sentence_12_528278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_528278'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_528278_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　寓居宜兴。访顾子美话旧，同游无锡县惠山，有诗。作品：次韵子美寄彦章同游惠山之作。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年4月6日</a>　寓居宜兴。为张元干题跋。作品：题跋。<span class='inlineComment2'>（张元干《芦川归来集》卷十附录汪藻题跋云：“宣和甲辰四月六日,鄱阳汪藻书。”此跋未收入汪藻《浮溪集》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年4月6日</a>　寓居宜兴。有诗送太守刘光。作品：送毗陵太守刘君受代东归。<div id='poem_528298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送毗陵太守刘君受代东归</a><span class='authorDate'>（1124年4月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528298")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528298'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528298'>往年我作新安民，人人能说刘使君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528298'>使君本一儒者耳，数十年来嗟未闻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528298'>我时屈指今州县，似此贤侯当识面。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528298'>那知漂泊千里馀，画戟清香日陪宴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528298'>使君何以人不如，胸中正有万卷书。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528298'>清真简淡乃天性，文章政事犹其馀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528298'>向来天子留君住，重与毗陵三万户。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528298'>谁教一曲渭城歌，忽作梨花枝上雨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528298'>宦游南北安得同，抚循凋郡还须公。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528298'>人生五马亦不恶，与民处处为春风。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528298_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528298'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_528298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　寓居宜兴。作嫂王文丽墓志铭。作品：安人王氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>安人王氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和七年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222956")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222956'>安人王氏，讳文丽，字幼明，其先会稽萧山人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222956_comment'></div>祖丝，以兵部员外郎事昭陵，为三司盐铁判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222956_comment'></div>子若孙踵登进士科，声闻吴中，号萧山王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222956_comment'></div>父霁，卒官太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222956_comment'></div>官于池，与中大夫汪公某僚相好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222956_comment'></div>时大夫诸孙侍旁者朝奉公某，长而贤，乃以安人妻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222956_comment'></div>朝奉之父曰中奉公某，母曰两陈令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222956_comment'></div>长令人之亡，诸幼累累肩差，朝夕孺慕，人不堪其忧，安人为收育抚携，甚于己子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222956_comment'></div>及少令人入汪氏，而髦者冠、髽者笄，交手授姑，退立堂下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222956_comment'></div>朝奉既再举进士不第，念中奉春秋高，买田筑室于故居浮溪之阳，以迟其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222956_comment'></div>安人左右赞襄，悉有条序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222956_comment'></div>洎中奉请老，果居而乐之，因敕家事勿复关我，日从宾客饮酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222956_comment'></div>朝奉益思所以奉承者，安人晨起则躬视烹庖，比珍异百须之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222956_comment'></div>每车马及门，辄举以进，老人未尝费一词也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222956_comment'></div>已而侍立少令人之侧，怡怡訚阊，若不能言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222956_comment'></div>妇姑白首相敬如宾，至今里人谈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222956_comment'></div>方安人勤舅姑之养也，诸子既兴于学矣，安人间于盥馈之事，则必临视其所习，故诸子皆嶷然成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222956_comment'></div>长子恺，擢绍圣四年进士第，安人飨其禄二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222956_comment'></div>恺于内行甚修，事安人尽礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222956_comment'></div>丐恩于朝，再锡命书，以有今封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222956_comment'></div>安人自朝奉公殁，即致家政于其妇，终日宴坐诵佛书，求出世间法，虽寒暑不置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222956_comment'></div>御僮使有恩，人皆终其身不忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222956_comment'></div>宣和六年四月壬戌遇微疾，起居如平时，越三日弃诸孤，洎属纩无一语乱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222956_comment'></div>享年七十有四，男女七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222956_comment'></div>恺，朝奉郎、知宣州宁国县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222956_comment'></div>忱，当以进士得官，病不能赴，前安人二日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222956_comment'></div>慥，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222956_comment'></div>恂，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222956_comment'></div>女适进士胡闻修、儒林郎俞积、通直郎杜璟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222956_comment'></div>孙五人，尧举、舜举、待举，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222956_comment'></div>尧举，太学内舍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222956_comment'></div>恺、忱、慥将以七年三月壬申，祔安人于宣州泾县方壶村朝奉公之茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222956_comment'></div>藻，朝奉季弟也，事安人为最久，乃再拜叙其本末，泣而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222956_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1222956'>顺于承夫，惟妇之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222956_comment'></div>孝而宜家，繄族之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222956_comment'></div>安人方处，母训则孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222956_comment'></div>来嫔汪宗，送往事居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222956_comment'></div>老人坐堂，夫奉宾谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222956_comment'></div>妇趋出房，醴胾咸列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222956_comment'></div>退视诸寝，诜然执经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222956_comment'></div>孰成其亲，有子在庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222956_comment'></div>禄养恩封，备有纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222956_comment'></div>天之报人，还以施者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222956_comment'></div>施则厚矣，报疑未酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222956_comment'></div>岂无后人，尚对厥休！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222956_comment'></div>方壶之原，下从夫子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222956_comment'></div>纳词于幽，窀穸之始。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1222956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年12月24日</a>　寓居宜兴。钦宗即位。诏有司论所以崇奉徽宗皇帝者，汪藻有文。作品：上太上道君皇帝尊号玉册文。<div id='poem_1222452' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222452' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太上道君皇帝尊号玉册文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年12月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222452")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222452'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222452'>维靖康元年，岁次丙午，八月某甲子朔，某日某甲子，皇帝臣某稽首再拜奉册言：臣闻道之大者，理谢形容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222452_comment'></div>名之尊者，言绝称谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222452_comment'></div>矧脱屣万乘，秕糠唐虞，独超希夷，事出诠表，欲赞之美，孰为端倪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222452_comment'></div>然应帝王之运者，既同乎人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222452_comment'></div>则殚臣子之诚者，乌得无述？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222452_comment'></div>恭惟太上道君皇帝陛下，席累圣之绪，辑三圣之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222452_comment'></div>爰自践履丕图，励精求治，克相民欲，纳之太和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222452_comment'></div>用能二十馀年，德业淳备，万物炊累，各成其天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222452_comment'></div>俯视区中，无足为者，乃陋神器，褰裳去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222452_comment'></div>明黄屋之非心，听玄珠之他得，全以所覆，畀之冲人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222452_comment'></div>方且高蹈殊庭，怡神秘箓，泯雷声于渊默，凝泰定之天光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222452_comment'></div>言念父有成功，必传之子，子克嗣事，敢忘所天？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222452_comment'></div>是用夙夜靡遑，力图报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222452_comment'></div>而群情虽切，伟范未昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222452_comment'></div>幸今方内底宁，岁丰兵却，车书文轨，指日可同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222452_comment'></div>岂寡昧克堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222452_comment'></div>实慈训所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222452_comment'></div>宜稽典礼，仰正鸿名，臣不胜大愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222452_comment'></div>谨奉玉宝，上尊号曰「教主道君太上皇帝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222452_comment'></div>伏惟太上皇帝陛下，与神为友，游物之初，遵汾水而憩华胥，访广成而追大隗，玩其清净，福我邦家，亿万斯年，为众君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222452_comment'></div>臣诚欣诚跃稽首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1222452_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　寓居宜兴期间，从贺铸游，借其藏书之己所未见者录藏之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　寓居宜兴期间。校定《柯山张文潜集》，并跋。作品：柯山张文潜集书后。<div id='poem_1222872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>柯山张文潜集书后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222872")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222872'>右文潜诗千一百六十有四，序、记、论、志文、赞等又百八十有四，第为三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222872_comment'></div>余尝患世传文潜诗文人人殊，屏居毗陵，因得从士大夫借其所藏，聚而校之，去其复重，定为此书，皆可缮写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222872_comment'></div>文潜名耒，谯郡人，仕至起居舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222872_comment'></div>尝为宣、润、汝、颍、兖五州太守，又尝谪居黄州、复州，最后居陈以殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222872_comment'></div>其集以《鸿轩》《柯山》为名者，居复、黄时所作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222872_comment'></div>元祐中，两苏公以文倡天下，从之游者，公与黄鲁直、秦少游、晁无咎，号四学士，而文潜之年为最少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222872_comment'></div>公于诗文兼长，虽当时鲜复公比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222872_comment'></div>两苏公、诸学士既相继以殁，公岿然独存，故诗文传于世者尤多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222872_comment'></div>若其体制敷腴、音节疏亮，则后之学公者，皆莫能仿佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222872_comment'></div>公诗晚更效白乐天体，而世之浅易者，往往以此乱真，皆弃而不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222872_comment'></div>其采获之遗者，自如别录云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1222872_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　寓居宜兴期间。代作启。作品：代宜兴宰通交代启。<div id='poem_1222799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宜兴宰通交代启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222799")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222799'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222799'>湖山信美，每虞制锦之伤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222799_comment'></div>田园将芜，惟幸及瓜而代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222799_comment'></div>与兹阖境，共伫行旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222799_comment'></div>某官拔萃诸儒，逢源六籍，凛端亮不回之操，粲深醇甚盛之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222799_comment'></div>擢殊第于早年，衮衮大庭之对；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222799_comment'></div>试长材于剧邑，洋洋载路之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222799_comment'></div>谓宜雍容以参鸳鹭之行，庶几遇合而畅夔龙之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222799_comment'></div>敢云鹏翼，尚屈鹅州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222799_comment'></div>山色溪光，可乐簿书之暇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222799_comment'></div>人情物态，尤无狱讼之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222799_comment'></div>以衰迟尚尸素其间，惟高明可笑谈而办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222799_comment'></div>正恐金马玉堂之趣召，不容铜章墨绶之久淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222799_comment'></div>某空恋稻粱，偶先糠秕，碌碌非拨繁之手，骎骎迫更成之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222799_comment'></div>虽地方一同，不减古子男之国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222799_comment'></div>惟政乏三异，亟须新令尹之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222799_comment'></div>胸臆所藏，晤言可尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222799_comment'></div>顾肇更于岁籥，宜茂拥于春祺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222799_comment'></div>尚谨节宣，即新涣渥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1222799_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年1月4日</a>　寓居宜兴。李纲除尚书右丞，汪藻有贺启。作品：贺李纲右丞启。<div id='poem_1222827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺李纲右丞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年1月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222827")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222827'>伏审躬被策书，进居丞弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222827_comment'></div>精忠贯日，正二仪倾侧之中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222827_comment'></div>凛气横秋，挥万骑笑谈之顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222827_comment'></div>国须贤立，天为时生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222827_comment'></div>恭以某官，厚德镇浮，英材经远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222827_comment'></div>得文武弛张之枢要，独运胸中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222827_comment'></div>明古今治乱之渊源，不专纸上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222827_comment'></div>爰自践扬之始，每勤献纳之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222827_comment'></div>老成尚有于典刑，天下想闻其风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222827_comment'></div>昨属殊邻之扰，上贻当宁之忧，夕烽既彻于甘泉，清跸将游于汾水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222827_comment'></div>惟公夙夜，与国存亡，挺身六品之卑，抗议九重之邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222827_comment'></div>留家誓死，镵血书词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222827_comment'></div>销大变于胚胎，转危机于呼吸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222827_comment'></div>洎干戈之指阙，援桴鼓以登陴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222827_comment'></div>义动三军，人皆奋死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222827_comment'></div>气吞异类，寇辄请盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222827_comment'></div>身且九殒以一生，国则崇朝而再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222827_comment'></div>昔李晟、子仪之功高矣，而未尝定策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222827_comment'></div>张良、谢安之谋至矣，而初不临戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222827_comment'></div>永惟元勋，夐绝前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222827_comment'></div>既名高而众媢，乃谗就而身危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222827_comment'></div>士讼公冤，亟举幡而集阙下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222827_comment'></div>帝从民望，令免胄以见国人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222827_comment'></div>荐经艰难，益见奇伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222827_comment'></div>方主上大明之今日，实邦家希阔之昌期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222827_comment'></div>欲众贤同建于事功，非雅望孰为之师表？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222827_comment'></div>将万世维持之是赖，何一时康济之足言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222827_comment'></div>藻久托馀光，欣闻盛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222827_comment'></div>虽无缘进旅退旅，陪宾客之后尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222827_comment'></div>岂不能大书特书，续山林之野史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222827_comment'></div>岩廊多暇，岁律方春，愿精寝餗之调，用副华夷之望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1222827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222827'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷二三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷五三，《翰苑新书》续集卷一，《启隽类函》卷一六，《四六法海》卷六，《新安文献志》卷四二，《奇赏斋古文汇编》卷一九八，《宋四六选》卷一二，《南宋文范》卷二九。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222827_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在宜兴，召为屯田员外郎，旋改礼部。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　应诏赴阙，自宜兴启程，途经泗州、天长、扬州、镇江等地至京城。《上宰执乞道君还阙札子》叙自宜兴启程沿途所见所闻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年3月5日</a>　在赴京途中，汪藻上宰执札子，乞迎徽宗还阙。作品：上宰执乞道君还阙札子。<div id='poem_1222765' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222765' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222765?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宰执乞道君还阙劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（靖康元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222765")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222765_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222765'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222765'>藻尝观孔子陈庶人之孝曰：「谨身节用，以养父母」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222765_comment'></div>自庶人等而上之，其位愈尊，其德愈大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222765_comment'></div>至天子则曰：「爱敬尽于事亲，而德教刑于四海」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222765_comment'></div>岂不以天子以天下为家，顾天下安否如何耳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222765_comment'></div>天下安，亲必预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222765_comment'></div>古之言孝如舜者，亦可以已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222765_comment'></div>或问孟子：「舜为天子，皋陶为士，瞽瞍杀人，则如之何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222765_comment'></div>曰：「执之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222765_comment'></div>「然则舜不禁欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222765_comment'></div>曰：「舜乌得而禁之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222765_comment'></div>夫有所受之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222765_comment'></div>有所受之云者，言受至公之道于天，以治斯人之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222765_comment'></div>舍是吾无以为治矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222765_comment'></div>然则徇一切之私，害天下之公，欲上安君亲，下治天下，古无是理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222765_comment'></div>恭惟太上皇帝以二十六年临御之尊，一旦上畏天威，举神器付之主上，此尧舜用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222765_comment'></div>是宜太平之期，自今以始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222765_comment'></div>然乘舆一出，中外怅然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222765_comment'></div>非不知天子仁孝，重违上皇之心，姑顺适之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222765_comment'></div>而议者谓庙堂诸公无一言救止，于扶颠持危之计，为不审矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222765_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222765_comment'></div>以天下养者，其虑不可以不深，而朝廷政令不可以不一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222765_comment'></div>戎狄之患，何代无之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222765_comment'></div>政使犯阙，为上皇者当痛心悔惧，与吾君共守，雪宗社之耻，慰军民之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222765_comment'></div>为主上者当迎上皇宫中，朝夕定省，以宽其危疑震扰之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222765_comment'></div>乃使仓卒南征，暴露野次，越在江海，五十馀日，未知还期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222765_comment'></div>万一先驱所至，有霜露之侵，是为人主能以天下养乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222765_comment'></div>方车驾之出也，衣冠惶骇，倾国南奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222765_comment'></div>小人之有罪者皆以扈从为名，未闻有请于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222765_comment'></div>而贵臣近侍受国厚恩者率捧头鼠窜，曾无数人在君侧为国家守者，而朝廷亦未闻呵止诘问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222765_comment'></div>是为朝廷尚有政令乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222765_comment'></div>且四海之师，使之勤王者，天子之诏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222765_comment'></div>藻比过泗州，闻上皇之诏，止勤王之师，守臣惶惑，莫知所从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222765_comment'></div>虽行宫意有所在，非道路所知，要之人情观望，不无疑恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222765_comment'></div>既藻与军士杂行天长道中，皆口语藉藉，以南幸为非，有不悦之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222765_comment'></div>所至藩篱，鸡犬萧然一空，为之寒心者数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222765_comment'></div>至扬州，闻有奉迎之诏，道路少安，旋闻渡江，无不失色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222765_comment'></div>比得镇江报，官兵日给六千馀缗，而小人献议者缮营宫室，移植花竹，购买园池，科须百出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222765_comment'></div>墨敕纷然，转易守令，迁官锡服，略无虚日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222765_comment'></div>如唐恪、翁彦国，帅也，惑于诰命并行，而莫知所守矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222765_comment'></div>嗜利苟得者干请行宫，其沸如市，不复知有朝廷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222765_comment'></div>朱勔粪除其家，率敛州县，为乘舆法物，邀请临幸者，相属于道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222765_comment'></div>昨日又闻行宫指挥，颇留勤王之师以自卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222765_comment'></div>传者汹汹，遂以为江津非给符不渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222765_comment'></div>苏常数州，居民迁徙，皆不安其居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222765_comment'></div>盖天下之弊尝极矣，幸天子儆戒，旷然大变，真千载一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222765_comment'></div>谓当继此坐薪尝胆，不容更有秋毫之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222765_comment'></div>自靖康改元，所谓慰人心者果何事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222765_comment'></div>民未见德，而自江以南，已绝维新之望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222765_comment'></div>今敌尚未在郊，此何等时，而小人已无忌惮如此，人何望耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222765_comment'></div>以镇江行宫日给计之，月当用二十万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222765_comment'></div>二浙之民将坐见涂炭，而东南和籴指挥于是废格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222765_comment'></div>民既愁怨，加以三军道路之言，惩往时青溪之役，西兵方春以瘅死，人人土思，其势必乱，则上皇岂得高枕而卧耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222765_comment'></div>藻以为上皇糠秕天下，褰裳去之，盖已超然万物之上矣，其中岂无所处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222765_comment'></div>而人不能无私忧过计者，以群小在侧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222765_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222765_comment'></div>小人平居，犹无顾惜，况自知恶稔，天下之所不赦，苟纾岁月之死，亦何所不至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222765_comment'></div>此社稷之至计，庙堂之深忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222765_comment'></div>使庙堂虑乎车驾未动之前，亦无今日之患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222765_comment'></div>不惟是而已，小人揣上皇享国之久，平时极四海之奉，方富于春秋，以龙德为隘，引周穆王瑶池之故事以劝其游，陈肃宗西内之戒以钳其返，挟此为奸，骎骎不已，则予我剑南一道之言，有时而出矣，不知何以答之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222765_comment'></div>自江以南，诏令将壅不行，而上皇晨昏之礼阙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222765_comment'></div>当是之时，天子果得为孝乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222765_comment'></div>今数小人者，斲丧国家，危辱至此，可谓天下之大恶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222765_comment'></div>上皇不归，则典刑不正，朝廷可越此而治他罪耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222765_comment'></div>在国家危疑之时，天子释位而去矣，首恶之臣乃恬不之问，又可以令天下乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222765_comment'></div>如是则所谓旷然大变者，果安在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222765_comment'></div>为今之计，莫若重为礼以必上皇之归，遣现任宰臣为奉迎上皇使，天子率百官东向临遣于庭，退而斋居，蔬食清宫以待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222765_comment'></div>且责行宫使以必死，大赏随行将士，令扈驾以归，庶几父子之诚，有所感动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222765_comment'></div>若小人尚敢牵制，则自行宫使以下，择其甚者易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222765_comment'></div>彼为奸谋者既去，直言日闻，则上皇亦不复留矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222765_comment'></div>行宫既复，二圣重欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222765_comment'></div>虽上皇翛然不复以万几关心，然阅天下理义多矣，大事应禀而后行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222765_comment'></div>志同于上，命一于下，乾坤再造，国祚无疆，天子之孝，孰大于是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222765_comment'></div>失是不图，异时追悔，恐无所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222765_comment'></div>伏望垂览而少加意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222765_comment'></div>天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222765_comment'></div>天下幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_75_1222765_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4b86e6ab8b7545d0b4cbde9d10d16136_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4b86e6ab8b7545d0b4cbde9d10d16136");'><span id='4b86e6ab8b7545d0b4cbde9d10d16136_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1129')">1128-1129年</a>，50-51岁</div><div id='4b86e6ab8b7545d0b4cbde9d10d16136' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　在宜兴，为程迈之父振作神道碑。作品：尚书刑部侍郎赠端明殿学士程公神道碑。<div id='poem_1222923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书刑部侍郎赠端明殿学士程公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222923")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222923'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222923'>靖康元年冬，金人再犯京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222923_comment'></div>明年春，天子在野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222923_comment'></div>敌索金缯无艺，府库不足，以民财继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222923_comment'></div>诏尚书梅执礼、侍郎陈知质、程振、给事安扶督民输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222923_comment'></div>一日敌帅坐城闉，猥谓四人者曰：「吾国赋羊马于民，率比屋相甲乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222923_comment'></div>若甲输而乙否，则执而诛之，谁敢违者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222923_comment'></div>意民穷且变生，将投隙而逞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222923_comment'></div>四人同辞而对曰：「今天子蒙尘，臣民皆愿前死，虽肝脑不计也，于金缯何有哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222923_comment'></div>顾诚无有塞责」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222923_comment'></div>敌帅大怒，问：「官长安在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222923_comment'></div>欲加以罪而置其馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222923_comment'></div>程公恐尚书坐之，遽前曰：「皆官长」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222923_comment'></div>敌帅不胜忿，四人皆死之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222923_comment'></div>建炎初，上即位，哀其忠，降玺书褒叹，各进官七等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222923_comment'></div>于是程公自承议郎进朝议大夫，官其子若亲属二人，下饶州给葬事，遣官护视，厚赙其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222923_comment'></div>言者谓未足酬公，复以端明殿学士告其柩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222923_comment'></div>公讳振，字伯玉，饶州乐平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222923_comment'></div>大王父承宪、大父溥、父翱，世业儒为闻家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222923_comment'></div>翱以公故，赠朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222923_comment'></div>公少有轶才，未冠，求师友四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222923_comment'></div>入京师，游太学，必秀出其辈类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222923_comment'></div>一时名士如张商英、陈瓘、张廷坚、邹浩，悉见之迎门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222923_comment'></div>崇宁三年，车驾幸孔子祠，见诸生太学，公以高第补将仕郎，除和州州学教授，留为辟雍录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222923_comment'></div>久之，迁博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222923_comment'></div>会诏近臣求人材可用者，或以公闻，召至政事堂，擢太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222923_comment'></div>以亲老丐外，得提举京东西路学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222923_comment'></div>秩满，复留居东州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222923_comment'></div>五年，奏立孟子冢祠，以公孙丑、万章从祀，皆见听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222923_comment'></div>改京西南路提举常平，入尚书为膳部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222923_comment'></div>逾年，拜监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222923_comment'></div>时大臣崇党相轧，若水火然，一时士大夫鲜不附丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222923_comment'></div>公孤立行一意，屹然其间，人服其正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222923_comment'></div>迁辟雍司业，兼太子舍人，改国子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222923_comment'></div>初，见太子东宫，言「古者大祭祀，登馂受爵，必以上嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222923_comment'></div>既礼备载，且元丰彝典具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222923_comment'></div>昨上有事明堂，而殿下不预，非所以尊宗庙、重社稷也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222923_comment'></div>太子瞿然曰：「初无人及此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222923_comment'></div>由是骤加奖重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222923_comment'></div>后每进说古今治乱，辄向纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222923_comment'></div>迁左司员外郎，兼官如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222923_comment'></div>时方腊暴浙右，声摇京师，公从容为宰相王黼言：「宜乘此时言天下弊事，庶几稍革，当天意、顺人心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222923_comment'></div>黼怏然不悦曰：「上且谓黼挟寇，奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222923_comment'></div>公知黼忌其言，不答，趋出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222923_comment'></div>然太子荐公甚力，外廷莫知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222923_comment'></div>会两省官缺，上曰：「程振老成忠实，必以为给事中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222923_comment'></div>黼衔前忿不能平，白公资浅，且雅长辞令，止除中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222923_comment'></div>已而中书侍郎冯熙载黜知亳州，黼怨熙载，甚欲公劾奏，且以丑言诋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222923_comment'></div>公不从，黼大怒，风言者论公有党，谪提举武夷山冲佑观，时宣和三年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222923_comment'></div>明年，复集贤殿修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222923_comment'></div>丁内艰，寻除徽猷阁待制、中书舍人，皆力辞不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222923_comment'></div>无几何，太子受内禅，是为渊圣皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222923_comment'></div>渊圣念公久，趣还旧班，对便朝，问劳甚渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222923_comment'></div>俄诏自中出，除尚书吏部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222923_comment'></div>公以大臣不协，议论多驳，诏令轻改，失其事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222923_comment'></div>如金人拿兵且半年，而至今不解者，以或和或战之说未一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222923_comment'></div>裁抑滥赏，如黑白易分，而数月之间三变其说者，以庙堂不能忘私而多与其党为地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222923_comment'></div>今日一人言之，以为是而行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222923_comment'></div>明日一人言之，以为非而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222923_comment'></div>或出圣断隃度而不暇畴咨，或用大臣偏辞而遂形播告，所以动未必善，处未必宜，乃辄为之反汗焉，其势不得不尔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222923_comment'></div>乃闻敌寇河北，力请合诸路兵掎角击之，以牵其势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222923_comment'></div>且曰：「彼猖獗如此，陛下犹欲守和议，而不使之少有所惩创乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222923_comment'></div>渊圣虽美其言，而夺于大臣，卒不能用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222923_comment'></div>连抗章求去，优诏不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222923_comment'></div>以吏部铨综有声，滋欲试之民事，除开封尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222923_comment'></div>先是大辟情或可矜，多取旨原贷，祖宗行之岁久，好生洽于民心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222923_comment'></div>崇宁以来，议者谓辇毂先弹压，凡情不当法，率巧请杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222923_comment'></div>公奏宜一准祖宗故事，遇得旨即著为令，令不载者，许援其比而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222923_comment'></div>自此天府之囚，全活者不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222923_comment'></div>已而诏捕亡卒，获数千人，公请充入步军司而除其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222923_comment'></div>步军司请论如法，法当尽诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222923_comment'></div>公以多事时，一日而杀千人，民必大骇，且未决，当系有司，宁无反侧之患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222923_comment'></div>渊圣大以为然，卒如公请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222923_comment'></div>除尚书刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222923_comment'></div>久之，敌邀天子幸其营，公亟白宰相何㮚，思所以折敌之语，告于上而却之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222923_comment'></div>㮚忽宣言翌日车驾出城，群臣失色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222923_comment'></div>已而敌求金不已，朝廷莫知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222923_comment'></div>公冒死直前，卒与祸会，寔靖康二年二月二十五日也，得年五十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222923_comment'></div>初，公为中书舍人，王黼以客沈积中帅河朔，欲觇敌图燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222923_comment'></div>公语积中，当思异时覆族之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222923_comment'></div>积中佩公戒，至所部首以书谢公，盛言其不可之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222923_comment'></div>公具以积中语告诸朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222923_comment'></div>洎公左迁，童贯、蔡攸卒兴是役，致变起肘腋，而公罹其凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222923_comment'></div>故闻公之丧，士无贤愚，皆为之出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222923_comment'></div>公天资乐易，与人谈笑，极酝藉风流，至论事则挺然不可回夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222923_comment'></div>宣和中，上皇崇道家之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222923_comment'></div>公至东宫，渊圣问焉，公对甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222923_comment'></div>其略曰：「周公作《鸱鸮》之诗，孔子以为知道，其言不过『迨天之未阴雨』、『绸缪牖户』而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222923_comment'></div>老子著《道经》，亦曰『为之于未有，治之于未乱』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222923_comment'></div>盖老氏与孔子合者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222923_comment'></div>今不固根本于无事之时，而徒事目前土木之工，非二圣人之意也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222923_comment'></div>他日渊圣为太上皇道之，太上皇颇欲去健羡，疏左右近习之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222923_comment'></div>而杨戬方兴龙德太乙之役，惧不得肆，因谗家令杨冯将辅太子幸非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222923_comment'></div>上皇震怒，执杨诛之，而渊圣之言亦废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222923_comment'></div>及靖康中，公尹天府，言利者颇欲离间两宫，公心独鄙之，每调娱父子之间，甚有恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222923_comment'></div>如诏鞫龙德宫近侍梁忻之类，特宽其文，由是纤介之疑不行，闻者无不叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222923_comment'></div>公居乡，专趋人之急，以急抵公者，未尝辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222923_comment'></div>族有五丧，积年不能举，命其子迈一日办之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222923_comment'></div>盖公之于书，无所不观，亦无所不学，属文敏赡，下笔不能自休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222923_comment'></div>书记翩翩，千里如对面语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222923_comment'></div>见之者把玩无斁，争藏弆为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222923_comment'></div>著《义语》及诗文七十馀卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222923_comment'></div>妻董氏，封硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222923_comment'></div>子迈，承务郎，传公学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222923_comment'></div>次未名，生公卒之某月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222923_comment'></div>迈以建炎二年十月辛酉，葬公乐平县嶂岭原太夫人茔之左，从公卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222923_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222923_comment'></div>士方平时，剧谈抵掌，以祸福死生自任，而谓人不能此直易耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1222923_comment'></div>及一旦临利害仅如秋毫，鲜不丧厥心而移其所守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1222923_comment'></div>若夫规以身免而推祸于人者，比肩接迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1222923_comment'></div>闻公之风者，亦可以少愧哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1222923_comment'></div>藻少以同郡登公之门，知公之详，宜莫如藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1222923_comment'></div>迈以国子司业程瑀之状来请，谨叙公之平昔而系之以铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1222923_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_112_1222923'>惟祝融之苗裔兮，公鼻祖曰伯休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1222923_comment'></div>越汉唐而南徙兮，家洎川之上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1222923_comment'></div>天既予公以修能兮，又重之以姱节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1222923_comment'></div>冠切云而事君兮，景忠精之前哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1222923_comment'></div>氛祲忽其蔽日兮，神龙荡而失渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1222923_comment'></div>众惮殃而逭祸兮，公踽踽而直前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1222923_comment'></div>左欃枪而右窫窳兮，公胡独罹此患！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1222923_comment'></div>苟杀身而成仁兮，齐死生于夜旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1222923_comment'></div>纷众美曾不概见兮，独令名其庶几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1222923_comment'></div>伟荡阴之节死兮，吾将从昔贤之所归。</div><div id='poem_sentence_121_1222923_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　在宜兴，作徐处仁夫人陈氏墓志铭。作品：吴国夫人陈氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴国夫人陈氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222959")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222959'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222959'>丞相彭城郡徐公处仁之夫人陈氏，以宣和五年正月己卯，薨于北都公府之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222959_comment'></div>越三年，彭城公薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222959_comment'></div>又明年，得建炎二年七月甲申，其子康、度奉公、夫人之柩，合葬于吴兴卞山之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222959_comment'></div>夫人世家严州，朝散郎、知楚州向之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222959_comment'></div>向父逸，卒官奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222959_comment'></div>楚州以进士起家，为开封令，有能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222959_comment'></div>未满岁，奏圄空者三，神宗以为材，将用之，擢尚书度支员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222959_comment'></div>永裕陵建，以本曹兼京西转运使，出奉祀江西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222959_comment'></div>徙楚州而终，翰林学士沈括识其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222959_comment'></div>夫人生有奇相，视瞻举措必端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222959_comment'></div>奉议君奇之，谓楚州曰：「此儿喜怒未尝形，言笑不妄发，使男也，吾家其兴乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222959_comment'></div>甫笄，归丞相彭城公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222959_comment'></div>时公贫甚，几无以为家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222959_comment'></div>一日，楚州持节过睢阳，盛车服遣女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222959_comment'></div>夫人庙见徐氏，乃在穷巷中，破屋数楹，太夫人坐堂上，旁无扶侍，夫人奉盥馈堂下如仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222959_comment'></div>楚州恐不堪其忧，使人察之，宴如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222959_comment'></div>已而斥卖嫁时衣被鞶帨，以太夫人之命，访族姻之贫者而赈之，人人咨嗟，以为不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222959_comment'></div>丞相为齐州掾，月俸不满万钱，惟太夫人甘脆是奉，夫人帅家人食粥无难色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222959_comment'></div>丞相预政，封安定郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222959_comment'></div>政和末，丞相自徐州朝京师，一时眷礼，群臣莫望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222959_comment'></div>夫人曰：「上恩固非常，然宠盈之戒，古人所谨，不可不思也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222959_comment'></div>每奏事归，必问见上安所陈，上开纳否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222959_comment'></div>尝诏丞相病已，无下拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222959_comment'></div>当是时，蔡鲁公耋老，徒损拜数而不得免焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222959_comment'></div>或以是为公荣，夫人愀然曰：「忌者至矣，其能久乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222959_comment'></div>未几，果坐谗出知扬州，其先见如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222959_comment'></div>夫人事姑孝，教子义，遇僮使有恩，敬夫如宾，治家如官府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222959_comment'></div>丞相曰：「吾平生以直道事君，取颠踬屡矣，而未尝置欣戚胸中者，繄室家是助」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222959_comment'></div>诸子曰：「使我学成而不堕其家声者，惟吾母之训」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222959_comment'></div>性通悟，于出世间法，得其指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222959_comment'></div>疾病，精爽如平时，谢医巫不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222959_comment'></div>属纩之夕，犹起坐若有所言，于死生盖超然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222959_comment'></div>薨，年五十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222959_comment'></div>历封温、福、陈、吴四国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222959_comment'></div>子五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222959_comment'></div>曰庚，擢进士第，仕至宣教郎、直秘阁、管勾亳州明道宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222959_comment'></div>曰廉、曰庾，承务郎，皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222959_comment'></div>曰康，今为右奉议郎、提举两浙西路茶盐常平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222959_comment'></div>曰度，为左宣教郎、尚书司封员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222959_comment'></div>孙男女合十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222959_comment'></div>男曰延老、曰同老，右承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222959_comment'></div>女适湖口主簿姚溥、丽水主簿王怡、右承事郎毛幵，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222959_comment'></div>初，楚州提举开封府界常平，宿陈留僧舍，夜闻垣外汹汹人声，起而烛之，积骸蔽野，于是奏乞官地瘗之，得骸八万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222959_comment'></div>虽位不满德，其后寖微，而庆钟夫人，作配名宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222959_comment'></div>疏封大国，始终安荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222959_comment'></div>后楚州之孙有以丞相之恩入官者，人以为积德之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222959_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1222959'>妫出舜后，胡公始侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222959_comment'></div>以国氏陈，晚闻太丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222959_comment'></div>夫人之先，南土是宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222959_comment'></div>英英度支，位止邦伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222959_comment'></div>德厚而踬，于偿不宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222959_comment'></div>集于夫人，莫贵与夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222959_comment'></div>厥初来嫔，仪则多有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222959_comment'></div>即安穷空，以服箕帚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222959_comment'></div>朝夕警戒，辅成公躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222959_comment'></div>燕及群息，亦云似公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222959_comment'></div>卞山之阳，维水㳽㳽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222959_comment'></div>与公同藏，千岁之始。</div><div id='poem_sentence_57_1222959_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　春，闻“苗、刘之变”，遂携家往宜兴西北之函山避居，有诗纪事。作品：避地函亭野步。<div id='poem_528291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>避地函亭野步</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528291")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528291'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528291'>今日幸无雨，天空出遥岑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528291'>行行不知疲，遂至春江浔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528291'>汲路转篱落，人家在桑阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528291'>平畴涨清波，陇麦如人深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528291'>沟畎戏凫鹜，新蒲映浮沈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528291'>我生本樵渔，对此谐初心。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528291'>风物岂不好，悲来自难任。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528291'>胡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>尘暗中原，四海如惊禽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528291'>黄屋狩万里，两宫隔辰参。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528291'>龙腾鼎湖阔<span id='poem_sentence_10_528291'>宇宙有倾覆，兹游岂岖嵚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528291_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528291'>消忧赖浊醪，太息谁能斟。<div id='poem_note_528291'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_528291_0'>⑴ 原作边，据遗集改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_528291_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　夏，“苗、刘之变”平定后，携家自水路返宜兴。有诗寄常州使君侄。作品：己酉乱后寄常州使君侄四首。<div id='poem_528326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528326' class='poemTitle 天长
