-----title
商丘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='92b49b712fbb4e3095467e59498830b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("92b49b712fbb4e3095467e59498830b5");'><span id='92b49b712fbb4e3095467e59498830b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1127')">1126-1127年</a>，48-49岁</div><div id='92b49b712fbb4e3095467e59498830b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　迁太常少卿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年1月4日</a>　兼权起居舍人。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1e6f49c758ed4e86b5c9d6431cdc3979_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1e6f49c758ed4e86b5c9d6431cdc3979");'><span id='1e6f49c758ed4e86b5c9d6431cdc3979_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>，49岁</div><div id='1e6f49c758ed4e86b5c9d6431cdc3979' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年3月23日</a>　应张邦昌之请，金帅遣还部分被留宋臣，汪藻亦因之得归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　尝与刘观共谋，藏九庙神主于太庙中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年4月14日</a>　在应天府。两撰劝进表，劝康王即帝位。作品：群臣上皇帝劝发第一表。上皇帝劝进表。<div id='poem_1222605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>群臣上皇帝劝发第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222605")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222605'>天命有归，将嗣兴于景运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222605_comment'></div>人心胥悦，咸昵就于至仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222605_comment'></div>虽睟表之非遥，犹鸿称之未正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222605_comment'></div>辱居近列，殊震危衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222605_comment'></div>伏念臣叨受国恩，早居法从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222605_comment'></div>方百六朝廷之厄会，偶二三辅弼之无人，猥以庸虚，参其谋议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222605_comment'></div>旋属敌情之变，遽成天步之艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222605_comment'></div>二帝出郊，既蒙尘而不返；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222605_comment'></div>九祧乏祀，将摄祼以为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222605_comment'></div>所宜引死以力争，顾独包羞而苟活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222605_comment'></div>生虽可耻，志则甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222605_comment'></div>盖天下屯危，方苦存亡之未定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222605_comment'></div>而古人事业，惟观济否之如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222605_comment'></div>使生灵相顾以无归，虽沟渎自经而奚益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222605_comment'></div>辄慕周勃安刘之计，庶伸程婴存赵之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222605_comment'></div>傥奉真人，光膺神器，嗣一祖八君之传序，慰四方万里之讴吟，誓伏欧刀，敢烦司败？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222605_comment'></div>幸率土相从而归启，且诸侯不辍以事周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222605_comment'></div>虽国鸿休，实臣素志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222605_comment'></div>愿假须臾之死，前瞻咫尺之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222605_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下中奋英明，外符信顺，受图高邑之壝，趣驾未央之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222605_comment'></div>盛九宾之礼以见群臣，辑六献之仪而朝清庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222605_comment'></div>时方多故，幸少留黄屋之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222605_comment'></div>臣既无功，愿自谨清宫之职。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1222605_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222605'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷四，《建炎以来系年要录》卷四，《中兴两朝圣政》卷一，《唐宋元名表》卷下之二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222605_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1222606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上皇帝劝进表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222606")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222606'>天人同心，方嗣兴于有德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222606_comment'></div>宗社重事，可久旷于常尊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222606_comment'></div>虽恳款以乐推，犹逡巡而牢避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222606_comment'></div>凡兹俟命，安可措躬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222606_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下，识照几微，诚参化育，早毓神明之胄，茂昭文武之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222606_comment'></div>有开必先，既讼狱讴歌之毕集；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222606_comment'></div>惟德是辅，将神祇祖考之咸安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222606_comment'></div>当承再造之休，乃守一谦之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222606_comment'></div>三灵交徯，四海畴依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222606_comment'></div>惟圣人所贵于因时，凡天下莫先于定分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222606_comment'></div>今九庙尚虚于祼献，两河未入于舆图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222606_comment'></div>继体守文，当亟收于众俊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222606_comment'></div>宅中图大，宜深究于远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222606_comment'></div>傥差一日之几，孰启千龄之运？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222606_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下俯占舆诵，光御法宫，涖中国而抚四夷，履至尊而制六合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222606_comment'></div>虽以位为乐，非尧舜之本心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222606_comment'></div>然其命维新，盖周邦之旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222606_comment'></div>瞻威在望，得请为期。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1222606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222606'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷四。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222606_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年4月15日</a>　在应天府。元祐皇后手书诏告天下，拥康王即位事，汪藻受命草书。作品：皇太后告天下手书。<div id='poem_1222453' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222453' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇太后告天下手书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年4月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222453")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222453'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222453'>比以敌国兴师，都城失守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222453_comment'></div>祲缠宫阙，既二帝之蒙尘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222453_comment'></div>诬及宗祊，谓三灵之改卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222453_comment'></div>众恐中原之无统，姑令旧弼以临朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222453_comment'></div>虽义形于色，而以死为辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222453_comment'></div>然事迫于危，而非权莫济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222453_comment'></div>内以拯黔首将亡之命，外以舒邻国见逼之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222453_comment'></div>遂成九庙之安，坐免一城之酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222453_comment'></div>乃以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1222453", 1222453, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>衰癃</span>之质，起于閒废之中，迎置宫闱，进加位号，举钦圣已行之典，成靖康欲复之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222453_comment'></div>永言运数之屯，坐视邦家之覆，抚躬独在，流涕何从？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222453_comment'></div>缅惟艺祖之开基，实自高穹之眷命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222453_comment'></div>历年二百，人不知兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222453_comment'></div>传序九君，世无失德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222453_comment'></div>虽举族有北辕之衅，而敷天同左袒之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222453_comment'></div>乃眷贤王，越居近服，已徇群情之请，俾膺神器之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222453_comment'></div>繇康邸之旧藩，嗣我朝之大统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222453_comment'></div>汉家之厄十世，宜光武之中兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222453_comment'></div>献公之子九人，惟重耳之尚在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222453_comment'></div>兹为天意，夫岂人谋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222453_comment'></div>尚期中外之协心，共定安危之至计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222453_comment'></div>庶臻小愒，同底丕平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222453_comment'></div>用敷告于多方，其深明于吾意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1222453_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年4月25日</a>　在应天府。张邦昌诣南京见康王，且待罪，汪藻同行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年5月1日</a>　在应天府。高宗即位。汪藻上贺表。作品：群臣贺皇帝登宝位表。<div id='poem_1222607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>群臣贺皇帝登宝位表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222607")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222607'>天启昌期，御萝图而出震；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222607_comment'></div>人瞻睟表，负黼扆以当阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222607_comment'></div>既三灵宗社之有归，将万世人民之永赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222607_comment'></div>窃考帝王之受命，殆将今古以同符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222607_comment'></div>必国步艰难，始天地出非常之主；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222607_comment'></div>及治功宏济，乃子孙承罔极之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222607_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下，勇智自天，英明冠古，躬返朴还淳之俭，奋兴衰拨乱之刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222607_comment'></div>方率土之讴吟，共思刘氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222607_comment'></div>宜昊穹之历数，专在舜躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222607_comment'></div>爰除高邑之坛，俯应大横之兆，取炎精用事之月，即艺祖兴王之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222607_comment'></div>有三千同德之臣，共扶鸿业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222607_comment'></div>用七百卜年之数，重立丕基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222607_comment'></div>方图政事之修，独运神明之断，岂止两河之复，即观二圣之还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222607_comment'></div>臣等幸备周行，获逢嘉会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222607_comment'></div>接千岁之统，交侵行殄于四夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222607_comment'></div>盛九宾之仪，率舞但同于百兽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1222607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222607'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222607_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年5月28日</a>　在应天府。除起居舍人，兼权中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年6月1日</a>　在应天府。兼检讨官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年6月12日</a>　在应天府。有状奏论赵士瑗高邮军再任不当。作品：奏论赵士瑗高邮军再任不当状。<div id='poem_1222747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222747' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222747?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论赵士𤥙高邮军再任不当状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年6月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222747")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222747'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222747'>臣准中书省送到词头一道，奉圣旨，知高邮军赵士𤥙因发运司举留，令依旧在任，其稽违朝命，特降两官，苏迟别与差遣，令臣撰词进入者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222747_comment'></div>右，臣窃以人主之柄，赏罚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222747_comment'></div>赏必及善，然后人知所劝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222747_comment'></div>罚必及恶，然后人知所惩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222747_comment'></div>未闻且赏且罚，而可以为政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222747_comment'></div>谨按赵士𤥙，始以苏迟赴官，不肯受代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222747_comment'></div>朝廷怒其稽违，朝命特降两官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222747_comment'></div>又缘自陈四任堂除，粗有劳效，乃发运使李祐劄子保奏，复令在任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222747_comment'></div>臣不知朝廷以士𤥙为是耶，为非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222747_comment'></div>若以为非，则方命不从者，尧四凶之罪也，不应使之在任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222747_comment'></div>若以为是，则借留在任者，汉循吏之恩也，不应使之降官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222747_comment'></div>以一士𤥙之身，而一日之间可赏可罚，臣窃惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222747_comment'></div>且士𤥙自陈历任有劳，至据其所临，推之不去，公违诏条，不顾义理，亦可谓无廉耻甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222747_comment'></div>纵方今乏材，岂无一人可治高邮如士𤥙者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222747_comment'></div>况新除人别与差遣，在任人迁延依旧，使有力者交结当权，无日不居官，无援者待阙及期，辄为人所夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222747_comment'></div>有十年不沾一日之禄者，宣和之风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222747_comment'></div>今陛下中兴，当痛革此弊，奈何因士𤥙复启侥倖之门耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222747_comment'></div>臣以为不罢士𤥙，恐人人效其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222747_comment'></div>茍欲贪禄，则冒耻自陈，及计会监司，侥倖保奏者，皆得之矣，此风渐不可长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222747_comment'></div>伏望圣慈别择能吏知高邮军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222747_comment'></div>或且令苏迟赴任，斥去士𤥙，为后来鄙夫之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222747_comment'></div>所有赵士𤥙依旧在任降两官词头，臣未敢撰进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1222747_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月12日</a>　在应天府。上奏论宋晦落职不当行词状。<div id='poem_1222749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222749' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222749?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论宋晦落职不当行词状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年8月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222749")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222749_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222749'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222749'>臣昨论王革等不当因赦复职，陛下亲降德音，以为王革等系参酌元犯，降等升叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222749_comment'></div>今来臣寮论列，若全不叙复，即不沾登极赦恩，可于逐官更行减等降职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222749_comment'></div>臣狂瞽之言，既蒙陛下留听，又烦圣训，委曲开谕如此，臣虽至愚，岂不知幸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222749_comment'></div>然臣区区，犹有不能已者，敢因宋晦，再为陛下陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222749_comment'></div>臣闻庆赏刑威曰君，言赏而人不以为庆，刑而人不以为威者，非人君之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222749_comment'></div>陛下自临御以来，半年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222749_comment'></div>宵衣旰食，侧躬修行，非不励精焦劳，是宜天下之人无不畏威而怀德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222749_comment'></div>然兵出则叛，将用则北，士大夫方命，偃蹇莫知听上，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222749_comment'></div>以赏不当功、罚不当罪故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222749_comment'></div>其赏罚不当，莫甚于因赦复职之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222749_comment'></div>昔齐侯之郭问父老曰：「郭何故亡」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222749_comment'></div>曰：「以其善善恶恶也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222749_comment'></div>曰：「若子之言，贤君也，何至于亡」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222749_comment'></div>父老曰：「郭君善善而不能用，恶恶而不能去，所以亡也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222749_comment'></div>自崇宁以来，纲纪日紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222749_comment'></div>其兼官据势者，非赀结权倖，则权倖之亲也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222749_comment'></div>非误国开边以取赏，则奴事阉官以进身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222749_comment'></div>如此等辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222749_comment'></div>皆仆厮之材，本非士类，乘时悖谬，攘取公器，如盗贼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222749_comment'></div>考其平生，一无分毫可得之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222749_comment'></div>以此清议不伸，搢绅道丧，天下切齿，驯致今日之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222749_comment'></div>幸陛下中兴，清议亦望稍伸，搢绅亦望行志，承平之风，庶几可复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222749_comment'></div>彼一时饕窃之人，虽尽行削夺，适还其素分耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222749_comment'></div>况名位已极矣，家赀已积矣，子弟已官矣，亲戚已显矣，士大夫犹谓有已不可追夺者，为国家之恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222749_comment'></div>今日陛下亦既深知其非，乃徒以赦恩之故，复使累累然玷汗清贯，将使终身保其宠荣，一何小人常幸而君子常不幸耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222749_comment'></div>臣恐蹈郭君不能去恶之戒，而四方解体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222749_comment'></div>或谓登极赦者，人主非常之恩也，于此而不复，非所谓旷然一新者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222749_comment'></div>臣以为赦所当复者，复其阶官耳，职不当复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222749_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222749_comment'></div>阶官者，积岁月可至，而职名者，人主所以待天下英俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222749_comment'></div>一时甄擢之权，苟非其人，终身莫得而至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222749_comment'></div>且谓之复者，言其才足以当此，偶缘过失夺之，今赦其过失复之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222749_comment'></div>既止缘侥倖，初无当得之理，何名为复哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222749_comment'></div>若小人其初得之如此其易，既得之后夺之如此其难，则英俊之人，有以相谓矣，曰「我何以砥砺为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222749_comment'></div>正使褒迁不过与此曹等耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222749_comment'></div>欲望风节之彊，事功之立，岂不难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222749_comment'></div>议者又谓「彼职名者，朝廷既已与之矣，若夺而不还，如咨怨何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222749_comment'></div>臣以为人主与夺，但问其当与不当而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222749_comment'></div>昔管仲夺伯氏骈邑三百，饭蔬食，没齿无怨言，以其公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222749_comment'></div>李吉甫相宪宗，省冗官八百员、吏千四百员，亦不闻其咨怨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222749_comment'></div>彼管仲、吉甫，人臣耳，犹能使人退听如此，岂陛下以人主权势之利，革数十年名器之滥，而忧此数鄙夫不乐哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222749_comment'></div>臣以为如宋晦辈治之不胜其多，何足一一烦朝廷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1222749", 1222749, "Clauses/139/Comments/0")'>词命</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222749_comment'></div>伏望陛下诏有司，取会凡有职名者，自观文殿学士而下，直秘阁而上共若干人，每职分为一等，每等集为一类，各具得职夺职因依及其人劳效过恶申三省，用祖宗旧法，每等止留数人，无其人则阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222749_comment'></div>其馀取旨，虽未夺者，悉行追夺，不止于不叙复而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222749_comment'></div>又有虽尝落职，而寄禄官叨窃至银青或通奉、正议、正奉者，皆前日奸凶邪佞之人非所当得，亦乞降至中大夫而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222749_comment'></div>臣又闻昨降指挥，前宰执子弟因恩泽带贴职及待制以上者并罢，而近日郑修年、亿年公然以杂学士乞见，朝廷亦不问而许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222749_comment'></div>钱盖以诞谩落职，初未尝复也，而于奏状擅带龙图阁待制，而群臣亦无一言及此者，臣窃未喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222749_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞如修年、亿年，并明降指挥，孰为当得，孰为当罢，指定姓名，镂版施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222749_comment'></div>如钱盖者，问其何以复职，如无所因，即重行黜窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222749_comment'></div>庶几卿士大夫共为陛下守此名器，辅成中兴之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222749_comment'></div>所有宋晦落职词头，臣未敢撰进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1222749_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年8月27日</a>　在应天府。迁中书舍人，上谢表。作品：谢除中书舍人表。<div id='poem_1222664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除中书舍人表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年8月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222664")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222664'>朝廷有命，莫严内史之赞书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222664_comment'></div>沟渎何知，遽补甘泉之法从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222664_comment'></div>既冒久虚之选，仍叨不试之除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222664_comment'></div>伏念臣居世寡谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222664_comment'></div>资身无策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222664_comment'></div>一官平进，安知巧宦之机？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222664_comment'></div>半世倦游，长在穷愁之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222664_comment'></div>昨幸蒙于起废，恩复许于参华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222664_comment'></div>适值时艰，俄遭敌变，身将沦于异域，望已绝于中天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222664_comment'></div>岂意生还，复膺器使？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222664_comment'></div>备史职中兴之始，摄词臣多士之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222664_comment'></div>所忧芜累之陈，不堪代匮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222664_comment'></div>乃误便蕃之及，遂使为真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222664_comment'></div>过分所期，循名而惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222664_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下兼收群策，光复丕图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222664_comment'></div>谓聪明睿智之有临，须号令文章之可述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222664_comment'></div>故于掌制，必以能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222664_comment'></div>而臣学昧渊源，文惟雕篆，况齿发早衰于多病，而精神新耗于百忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222664_comment'></div>大惧旷瘝，上孤甄擢，虽不能草诏，使武夫悍卒之涕流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222664_comment'></div>然常愿输忠，俾君子小人之情得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222664_comment'></div>倘酬鸿造，何有馀生？</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1222664_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222664'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一六，《古今事文类聚》遗集卷七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222664_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年11月2日</a>　在应天府。草李纲落职鄂州居住制。<div id='poem_1222429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李纲落职鄂州居住制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年11月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222429")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222429'>朋奸罔上，有虞必去于驩兜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222429_comment'></div>欺世盗名，孔子首诛于正卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222429_comment'></div>肆朕纂承之始，昧于考慎之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222429_comment'></div>相靡有终，刑兹无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222429_comment'></div>具官某空疏而不学，凶愎而寡谋，志轻天下而自谓无人，权震朝廷而不知有上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222429_comment'></div>靡顾国家之大计，但营市井之虚名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222429_comment'></div>专杀尚威，伤列圣好生之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222429_comment'></div>信狂喜佞，为一时群小之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222429_comment'></div>比再被于延登，朕颇怀于虚伫，而果于修怨，奸以事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222429_comment'></div>庇己姻亲，至擅刊夫诏令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222429_comment'></div>括民财力，曾罔恤于基图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222429_comment'></div>念存体貌之恩，姑解钧衡之任，虽居远外，犹极优崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222429_comment'></div>谓上印以投閒，能阖门而讼过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222429_comment'></div>乃倾家积，阴与贼通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222429_comment'></div>伊举错之非常，于听闻而实骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222429_comment'></div>宜镌宠秩，移寘偏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222429_comment'></div>昔汉弃京房，罪本繇于不道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222429_comment'></div>唐诛元载，恶盖在于罔悛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222429_comment'></div>往革乃心，毋忘予戒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1222429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年11月25日</a>　在应天府。上奏乞修军政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　在应天府。作王愈父王公权墓志铭。作品：朝散郎致仕王君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散郎致仕王君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222942")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222942'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222942'>建炎元年，朝请大夫、秘阁修撰王愈以书走广陵，属其邑人汪藻曰：「愈不天，不能事亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222942_comment'></div>先人弃诸孤，将以明年某月某甲子，葬德兴县灵湖之王塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222942_comment'></div>惟先人束发读书立训，故为后学宗，抱能不施，以不大振耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222942_comment'></div>惟不肖孤材下，不能嗣事，使其名声显闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222942_comment'></div>今既返九原，若不刻藏，惧日远日忘，终泯泯无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222942_comment'></div>惟夫子赐之铭，以宠绥其殁，假王氏无穷之休，敢请」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222942_comment'></div>藻曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222942_comment'></div>是吾邑老成，望其貌如东郭顺子，听其言如仲长公理，叩其学如皇甫士安者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222942_comment'></div>铭其可辞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222942_comment'></div>君讳某，字公权，其先琅琊王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222942_comment'></div>晋渡江，居江南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222942_comment'></div>讫唐广明之乱，有徙名数于婺源者，于君为九世祖，以力田遗子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222942_comment'></div>至君大父，始释耒为儒家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222942_comment'></div>君儿时颖甚，得书敏视若流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222942_comment'></div>游太学，籍籍诸生间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222942_comment'></div>以父老丐归，从乡举，州再上其名，再不中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222942_comment'></div>父丧，既除，即慨然有高世意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222942_comment'></div>或勉之仕，泣曰：「吾所为汲汲者，以亲在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222942_comment'></div>今亲逝矣，奚仕为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222942_comment'></div>乃杜门息交，著书数万言，言覈而理申，要必自己出，不借他人一词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222942_comment'></div>愈用君学，擢绍圣元年进士丙科，调建昌令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222942_comment'></div>时江南荐饥，县无储，独经廪厚藏，吏守文不敢发，君亟以书抵愈曰：「令活民而黜，职也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222942_comment'></div>愈禀行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222942_comment'></div>由是建昌之民居数千里，流殍少间，不知其无岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222942_comment'></div>已而愈守信，会贼方腊寇城，危甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222942_comment'></div>君索橐得白金数千两，间道资愈饷军，且戒之死，闻者无不感奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222942_comment'></div>以故兵焚残十馀州，惟信屹然无秋毫之失，盖君明于事机以成其子者类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222942_comment'></div>建中靖国初，以进士久次得官，不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222942_comment'></div>用愈恩，累官朝散郎，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222942_comment'></div>以某年某月某甲子，卒于家，春秋八十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222942_comment'></div>曾祖某、父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222942_comment'></div>妻余氏，封安人，先公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222942_comment'></div>二男子，其一愈也，次曰慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222942_comment'></div>孙六人，德昭，迪功郎，馀尚幼，而德昭前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222942_comment'></div>君居乡，博施兼容，岁折券以为常，而与人未尝校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222942_comment'></div>于治心养性，皆得其要，盖不读释老之书，而闇与之合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222942_comment'></div>古所谓耄期称道者，如君非也耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222942_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1222942'>晋之王姓两族蕃，至唐独有琅琊孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222942_comment'></div>公家江南乃其昆，以学自表为清门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222942_comment'></div>著书上与千古论，材虽不施闻则尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222942_comment'></div>遣子出仕乘朱轓，叶膏既沃还流根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222942_comment'></div>暮年章绂荣诏恩，奄蜕寿骨归丘原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222942_comment'></div>灵湖有阜如鹄鶱，君手自竁非承言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222942_comment'></div>我书其实要不烦，刻著玄石期长存。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1222942_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5fe9a96732714ce98521e24bb0dd117d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5fe9a96732714ce98521e24bb0dd117d");'><span id='5fe9a96732714ce98521e24bb0dd117d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>，50岁</div><div id='5fe9a96732714ce98521e24bb0dd117d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年1月25日</a>　在扬州行在。汪藻应诏取当转资人数。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年1月</a>　在扬州行在。因以隆祐太后兄孟忠厚及皇后父邢焕任侍从官，大臣论奏，汪藻亦奏论除授不当。作品：奏论邢焕孟忠厚除授不当状。<div id='poem_1222748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论邢焕孟忠厚除授不当状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222748")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222748'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222748'>臣闻人主之政，公与私不并行，恩与法不两立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222748_comment'></div>以公灭私、以法夺恩者治，以私害公、以恩挠法者乱，此古今不易之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222748_comment'></div>陛下以邢焕为中宫之父，易文资从武，中外之人莫不以为当而称赞圣德不已者，以其出于公法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222748_comment'></div>至以孟忠厚为系隆祐太后之亲，令依旧文资，中外之人，哄然不息，致臣僚交章论奏，虽烦圣训谆谆诲谕，终莫能弭者，以其出于私恩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222748_comment'></div>昔汉明帝马后为章帝之母，帝欲封其家，太后屡辞不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222748_comment'></div>帝重请曰：「汉兴舅氏之封侯，犹皇子之为王者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222748_comment'></div>太后诚存谦虚，奈何令臣独不加恩三舅乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222748_comment'></div>其言可谓切至，而后终不从，至数年，仅许封关内侯而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222748_comment'></div>彼外戚封侯，汉法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222748_comment'></div>而明德拳拳如此，岂不以妇人内夫家、外父母家，宗族太宠非己之福耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222748_comment'></div>故自古欲观母后之贤否者无他，在于能远外家之宠与不能耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222748_comment'></div>隆祐太后盛德著闻天下，三十年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222748_comment'></div>今一旦以忠厚之故，使陛下屈公法而隆私恩，臣恐海内之人非特得以议陛下，而于隆祐亦不能无疑，非所以成隆祐远嫌之德而全陛下孝养之诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222748_comment'></div>此事所系非轻，臣不敢缄默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222748_comment'></div>伏乞睿慈检会以前臣僚章疏，详加省览，早赐施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222748_comment'></div>所有邢焕、孟忠厚书牍行下指挥，臣未敢施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1222748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年2月7日</a>　在扬州行在。奏论不当除吕源两浙转运使及姜仲谦转运副使之职。作品：奏论除吕源两浙转运使姜仲谦转运副使不当状。<div id='poem_1222744' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222744' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222744?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论吕源除两浙转运使姜仲谦除转运副使不当状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年2月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222744")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222744_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222744'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222744'>臣窃惟国家自军兴以来，纪纲日失其序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222744_comment'></div>陛下赫然中兴，凡民物之利害、官吏之黜陟、法令之当否，所恃者郡守监司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222744_comment'></div>郡守休戚止于一州，监司实通一路，苟非其人，产祸召乱，有不可胜言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222744_comment'></div>今两浙密迩行在，盖一时根本之地，新经兵火，郡县疮痍，大半未复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222744_comment'></div>议者谓朝廷必留意监司，慎择人材，非他路比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222744_comment'></div>及除目之出，乃用吕源、姜仲谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222744_comment'></div>是二人者，其操行污浊略同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222744_comment'></div>一旦并制选除，且同为一路，以此士论沸腾，相视窃笑，茫然莫知其端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222744_comment'></div>臣谨按吕源，升卿之子，家富于财，专以包苴交结权倖为进身之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222744_comment'></div>初自常调，结林灵素、孟昌龄而得监司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222744_comment'></div>未几罢黜，复结王黼而得旧物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222744_comment'></div>黼败，人为源危之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222744_comment'></div>方是时，李邦彦当国，知赵子崧者，邦彦所厚之客也，遽以女妻子崧之子，厚其奁具，即除军器少监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222744_comment'></div>意犹未已，遂倾赀结梁师成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222744_comment'></div>无何，除职帅广西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222744_comment'></div>及赐对便朝，一日而获恩数者八，进职、进官、进赐名、锡章服、父赠待制、所生母封夫人、诸弟补官之类，皆人臣非常之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222744_comment'></div>盖师成极力荐援，称其所赂而为之报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222744_comment'></div>比者源被召赴阙，士大夫谓朝廷必深知其所为且斥而不用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222744_comment'></div>曾未阅月，为两浙转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222744_comment'></div>夫两浙，名部也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222744_comment'></div>转运使，崇资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222744_comment'></div>平时进擢能臣，不过为副使而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222744_comment'></div>吕源何人，辄当此选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222744_comment'></div>若仲谦，则甘心为谭桢之奴者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222744_comment'></div>桢之讨方腊也，仲谦以官从军，秃巾小带，身杂胥吏，趋走桢前，倚托权势，傲睨视人，施施然自以为得计，而忘其身之丑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222744_comment'></div>自后除延阁、典大藩，对宾客辄言：「仲谦卵翼，皆显之之赐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222744_comment'></div>显之，桢字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222744_comment'></div>此浙人熟闻而亲见，指名而嗤侮者，奈何使之持节，居其士民之上乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222744_comment'></div>若朝廷以二人者沾沾自喜似敏，敢为诞谩似才，奋当剧烦似有风力，以为足以办两浙之事，臣窃以为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222744_comment'></div>今两浙人心未安，缓之则凌迟，急之则纷乱，正当得老成而知大体者，威惠兼行，庶几稍定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222744_comment'></div>当此之时，岂堪二小子重扰之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222744_comment'></div>况近者臣僚论列自崇宁以来谄附非类得官得职者，并行追夺，且镂板籍、记姓名，为万世奸邪之戒，蒙陛下开纳施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222744_comment'></div>今源由灵素、昌龄、师成而得直龙图阁，仲谦由谭桢而得直秘阁，皆当在夺职籍名之数者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222744_comment'></div>既未扫除，乃同时升擢，不知朝廷好恶安在，无怪士论之纷纷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222744_comment'></div>伏望睿慈连罢源、仲谦，别选修饬廉平之吏，毋使十四州之民谓朝廷用人，复如前日之谬，善人闻之解体，奸人得以乘间窥伺，其害非细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222744_comment'></div>所有吕源除两浙转运使、姜仲谦除两浙转运副使词头，臣未敢撰进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1222744_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年2月18日</a>　在扬州行在。被劾落职，罢为集英殿修撰、提举江州太平观，上谢表。作品：谢罢中书舍人除集英殿修撰宫祠表。<div id='poem_1222676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢罢中书舍人除集英殿修撰宫祠表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年2月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222676")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222676'>臣藻言：准尚书省劄子，臣僚上言，以臣考试潭州进士何烈卷子内称臣，并不举觉回避，特罢臣中书舍人，准告授前件差遣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222676_comment'></div>臣子事君，当谨嫌疑之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222676_comment'></div>圣人容物，止从黜免之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222676_comment'></div>既联秘殿之班，仍赋殊庭之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222676_comment'></div>惟天假宠，何地酬恩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222676_comment'></div>伏念臣朴樕常材，蹉跎半世，遇陛下作兴之始，在群臣推择之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222676_comment'></div>念平生值主之难，常思奇节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222676_comment'></div>耻私智容身之陋，复踵前规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222676_comment'></div>故因词命之行，务极论思之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222676_comment'></div>庶丝毫之小益，非虫篆之空文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222676_comment'></div>而臣意广于才，宠逾其分，乃昧严恭之礼，自投卤莽之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222676_comment'></div>如孟郊之应答参差，唐人或有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222676_comment'></div>若何武之荐扬盘辟，汉法岂容？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222676_comment'></div>置散已优，饕荣何幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222676_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下隆宽尽下，观过知仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222676_comment'></div>谓子路使门人为臣，虽诚悖理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222676_comment'></div>而徐邈云酒中有圣，初亦何心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222676_comment'></div>程文尚许于兼收，考吏奚妨于末减？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222676_comment'></div>谳为失职，斥使去朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222676_comment'></div>臣敢不追讼悔尤，过为兢慎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222676_comment'></div>画马者并尾而五，常负谴忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222676_comment'></div>网禽而去面之三，永衔生赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1222676_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222676'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222676_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年2月18日</a>　在扬州行在。被劾落职，罢为集英殿修撰、提举江州太平观，上谢宰相启。作品：奉祠谢宰相启。<div id='poem_1222823' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222823' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222823?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉祠谢宰相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年2月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222823")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222823_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222823'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222823'>久宦涂之寥落，倍费陶镕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222823_comment'></div>邈祠宇之邃幽，初勤香火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222823_comment'></div>叨饩廪于啼饥之日，齿簪缨于讼过之馀，喜不自胜，惭无以喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222823_comment'></div>伏念藻寖已迫桑榆之暮，非惟惊蒲柳之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222823_comment'></div>念平日之所遭，咸其自取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222823_comment'></div>收众人之共弃，独赖并容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222823_comment'></div>每跋前疐后之自怜，荷右挈左提之曲尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222823_comment'></div>顷栖异县，擢预佐州，望恩门而知归，顾官曹而无补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222823_comment'></div>漫谤谗之四起，继抨弹之上闻，蕞尔一身，宁甘百谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222823_comment'></div>亡中流之维楫，坠矣何言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222823_comment'></div>索大寒之衣裘，悔焉已晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222823_comment'></div>回阳春之浩荡，藉白日之辉光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222823_comment'></div>非我公加意怜之，顾此生自分已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222823_comment'></div>四稔于此，一饭不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222823_comment'></div>无路酬恩，蛇雀之心犹在；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222823_comment'></div>全家待哺，糟糠之腹未充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222823_comment'></div>仰首一鸣，求哀再造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222823_comment'></div>惟奉祠之旧制，本均劳之异恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222823_comment'></div>顾惟今日临政之清明，非若异时权宜而猥受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222823_comment'></div>饥寒所迫，揣贱分敢有谒焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222823_comment'></div>罪戾尚多，将何修可以称此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222823_comment'></div>豫切负空餐之愧，惟知衔洪造之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222823_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官，道济人寰，勋隆帝室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222823_comment'></div>唐虞致主，垂万世无疆之基；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222823_comment'></div>子弟视民，均一人有庆之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222823_comment'></div>凡今旂常之所纪，皆昔简策之未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222823_comment'></div>当宁何为，垂拱视天民之阜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222823_comment'></div>寰区自幸，须臾观德化之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222823_comment'></div>有如至愚，曾不遐弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222823_comment'></div>舂粮百里，独未敢顺风而前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222823_comment'></div>饮酒满堂，不忍终向隅而泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222823_comment'></div>赐以无功之食，略其不赦之愆，非但赋粟以代耕，将使回心而向道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222823_comment'></div>恩深赐厚，感极涕洟，敢不戒多事而多言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222823_comment'></div>誓寡尤而寡悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222823_comment'></div>黄卷青箱，以理平生之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222823_comment'></div>琼函云笈，以收方外之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222823_comment'></div>益观蘧伯玉四十九年之非，仰赞广成子千二百岁之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222823_comment'></div>徐君解季札之剑，宁负初期？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222823_comment'></div>象罔得元水之珠，深加自勉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1222823_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
