href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年6月23日</a>　以中书舍人兼直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年6月</a>　在建康，有高宗移跸建康起居表。作品：车驾移跸建康起居表。<div id='poem_1222609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾移跸建康府起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222609")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222609'>江山地险，将定厥居，舆卫天行，先巡所守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222609_comment'></div>会公侯方岳之下，览形势帝王之州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222609_comment'></div>宇宙清明，华夷震叠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222609_comment'></div>伏以盘庚五迁而商人卒服，重耳三驾而楚子莫争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222609_comment'></div>方宏远之是图，非宴安而孰戒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222609_comment'></div>矧谋旧物之复，可讳属车之劳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222609_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下孝通神明，诚配高厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222609_comment'></div>虽居万乘，躬曾闵之至哀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222609_comment'></div>爰整六师，摅高文之宿愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222609_comment'></div>既王者不闻于有外，故春秋尤大于复雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222609_comment'></div>臣方奉真祠，莫居官守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222609_comment'></div>兴琅琊而续晋之祀，窃陋前规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222609_comment'></div>游云梦而缚信以归，愿求故事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1222609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月7日</a>　在建康，依诏草降夏国书、降尼玛哈书。作品：赐夏国主诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《赐夏国主诏》，当为国书之一，余不见《浮溪集》、《浮溪文粹》及《浮溪集拾遗》）</span><div id='poem_1222470' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222470' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222470?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐夏国主诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年7月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222470")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222470_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222470'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222470'>敕夏国主：世守封陲，心驰观阙，比属屯危之会，致疏问讯之通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222470_comment'></div>缅想提封，同膺袭吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222470_comment'></div>兹俯临于凉序，宜益护于生经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222470_comment'></div>今赐某物，具于别录，至可领也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222470_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1222470_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月24日</a>　在建康，试给事中，仍兼直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月1日</a>　在建康，召至都堂，令作国书。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='53a2fb45252d4c77afe59d83acc5d3c9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("53a2fb45252d4c77afe59d83acc5d3c9");'><span id='53a2fb45252d4c77afe59d83acc5d3c9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，51岁</div><div id='53a2fb45252d4c77afe59d83acc5d3c9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月11日</a>　在平江，受命草高丽答诏。作品：坏晋馆以纳车，庶无后悔；闭玉关而谢质，匪用前规（不全）<span class='inlineComment2'>（诏书原文不见于《浮溪集》、《浮溪文粹》及《浮溪集拾遗》，唯《宋史·高丽传》保存有一段文字可窥其全貌。）</span><div id='poem_1222917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郭永传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222917")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222917'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222917'>郭永，大名府元城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222917_comment'></div>少刚明勇决，身长七尺，须髯郁然，望之如神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222917_comment'></div>以祖任为丹州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222917_comment'></div>守武人，为奸利无所忌，永数引法裁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222917_comment'></div>守大怒，盛威临永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222917_comment'></div>永不为动，则缪为好言荐之朝，永因尽忠以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222917_comment'></div>后守欲变具狱，永力争不能得，袖举牒还之，拂衣去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222917_comment'></div>擢清河丞，寻知太原府大谷县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222917_comment'></div>太原帅率用重臣，每宴飨，费千金，苛取诸县以给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222917_comment'></div>大谷民富，其敛尤亟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222917_comment'></div>永以书抵幕府曰：「非什一而取，皆民膏血也，以资觞豆之费，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222917_comment'></div>脱不获命令，有投劾而归耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222917_comment'></div>府不敢迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222917_comment'></div>县有潭，出云雨，岁祷水旱为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222917_comment'></div>县祷未应，乘此哗民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222917_comment'></div>永杖巫身，暴日中，雨立至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222917_comment'></div>县人刻碑记其异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222917_comment'></div>府遣卒数辈，号警盗，刺诸县短长，游蠹不归，莫敢迕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222917_comment'></div>永械致之府，府为并他县追还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222917_comment'></div>于是府檄及部使者文移有不便于民者，必条利病反复，或遂寝而不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222917_comment'></div>客谓永世方雷同，毋以此贾祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222917_comment'></div>永曰：「吾知行吾志而已，遑恤其他」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222917_comment'></div>大谷人安其政，以为自有令来，无永比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222917_comment'></div>既去数年，复过之，则空一邑遮留，如永始去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222917_comment'></div>调东平府司录，府事无大小，决永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222917_comment'></div>吏有不能办者，私相靳曰：「尔非郭司录耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222917_comment'></div>除通判郑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222917_comment'></div>燕山之役，以永为其路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222917_comment'></div>郭药师屯边，怙恩暴甚，与民市不偿其直，复殴之，非坏目折支不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222917_comment'></div>安抚使王安中莫敢问，永白安中：「不治且难制，永请见而显责之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222917_comment'></div>不从则取其尤者磔之市，无辞也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222917_comment'></div>乃见药师曰：「朝廷负将军乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222917_comment'></div>药师惊曰：「何谓也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222917_comment'></div>永曰：「前日将军杖策归朝廷，上推赤心，置将军腹中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222917_comment'></div>客遇之日，无所不至，而将军未有尺寸功报上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222917_comment'></div>今方倚将军为重，乃纵部曲，戕民不禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222917_comment'></div>平居尚尔，如缓急何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222917_comment'></div>药师谢，无愧容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222917_comment'></div>永谓安中曰：「他日乱吾边者，必此辈也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222917_comment'></div>已而安中罢，永亦辞去，移河北西路提举常平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222917_comment'></div>会金人趋京师，所过城邑，欲立取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222917_comment'></div>是岁大寒，城池皆冰，敌率藉冰梯城，不攻而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222917_comment'></div>永适在大名，闻之，先弛壕渔之禁，人争出渔，冰不能合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222917_comment'></div>敌至城下，睥睨久之，叹息而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222917_comment'></div>迁河北东路提点刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222917_comment'></div>时车驾在维扬，命宗泽守京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222917_comment'></div>泽厉兵积粟，将复两河，以大名当冲要，檄永与帅桂充、漕臣张益谦相掎角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222917_comment'></div>永得檄大喜，即朝夕谋战守具，因结东平权邦彦为援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222917_comment'></div>不数日，声惊河朔，已没州县皆叛敌来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222917_comment'></div>敌亦畏之，不敢动，远近宴然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222917_comment'></div>居无何，宗泽死，充守京师，以张益谦代之，而裴亿为转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222917_comment'></div>益谦、亿，龌龊小人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222917_comment'></div>会范琼胁邦彦南去，刘豫举济南来寇，大名块然孤城居其间，敌以十倍之师攻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222917_comment'></div>永率士昼夜乘城，伺间则出兵徂击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222917_comment'></div>或劝益谦委城遁者，永曰：「北门所以蔽遮梁、宋，敌得志则席捲而南，朝廷危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222917_comment'></div>借力不敌，犹当死守，徐挫其锋，待外援之至，奈何弃之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222917_comment'></div>因募士赍帛书，夜缒城出，告急朝廷，且请朝廷先为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222917_comment'></div>敌攻益急，俘东平、济南人大呼城下：二郡已降者富贵，不降无噍类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222917_comment'></div>益谦辈相顾色动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222917_comment'></div>永大言曰：「今日正吾侪尽节之时」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222917_comment'></div>又行城抚将士曰：「王师至矣，吾城坚完可守，汝曹努力，敌不足畏也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222917_comment'></div>众感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222917_comment'></div>质明大雾四塞，敌以车发断碑残础掷城中，楼橹皆坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222917_comment'></div>左右蒙盾而立，多碎首者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222917_comment'></div>良久城陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222917_comment'></div>永坐城楼上，或掖之以归，诸子环泣请去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222917_comment'></div>永曰：「吾世受国恩，当以死报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222917_comment'></div>然巢倾卵覆，汝辈亦何之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222917_comment'></div>兹命也，奚惧」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222917_comment'></div>益谦、亿率众迎降，敌曰：「城破始降，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222917_comment'></div>杂然以永不从为辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222917_comment'></div>敌遣骑召永，永正衣冠南向再拜讫，易幅巾而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222917_comment'></div>敌曰：「阻降者谁」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222917_comment'></div>永熟视久之，曰：「不降者我，尚奚问」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222917_comment'></div>敌见永状貌魁杰，且夙闻其贤，乃自为好语数十言，欲以富贵啖永而降之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222917_comment'></div>永嗔目唾骂曰：「无知丑类，恨不醢尔以报国家，何说降乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222917_comment'></div>敌令译者申谕不已，永戟手怒骂不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222917_comment'></div>敌讳其言，麾之使去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222917_comment'></div>永复厉声曰：「胡不速我死？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222917_comment'></div>我当率义鬼灭尔曹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222917_comment'></div>大名人在絷者，无不以手加额，为之出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222917_comment'></div>敌令断所举手，并其家害之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222917_comment'></div>时年五十三，建炎二年十一月甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222917_comment'></div>即日语传城中，虽素不与永合者，皆相向恸哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222917_comment'></div>敌去，相与负其尸瘗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222917_comment'></div>永博古通今，得钱即买书，家藏书万卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222917_comment'></div>因事为文，皆可录，而不求人知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222917_comment'></div>见古人立名节者，未尝不慨然掩卷终日，而尤慕颜鲁公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222917_comment'></div>为人喜面折人过，退无异言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222917_comment'></div>闻秋毫之善，必咨嗟奖成如不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222917_comment'></div>士友以此严惮而归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222917_comment'></div>杜充守大名，名称甚盛，永尝画数策见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222917_comment'></div>他日问其目，曰：「未暇读也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222917_comment'></div>永数充曰：「人有志而无才，好名而遗实，骄蹇自用而得名声，以当大任，鲜不颠沛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222917_comment'></div>公等足与治乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222917_comment'></div>充大惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222917_comment'></div>靖康冬，敌犯京师，中外阻绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222917_comment'></div>或以两宫北狩告永者，永号绝仆地，家人舁归，不食者数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222917_comment'></div>闻元帅檄，始勉强一餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222917_comment'></div>其忠谊盖天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222917_comment'></div>若夫事亲孝，与人忠，轻财笃义，而于吏治精明，皆永馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222917_comment'></div>其大节如此，他不足为永道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222917_comment'></div>绍兴初，始赠永中大夫、资政殿学士，谥「勇节」，官其族数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222917_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_103_1222917'>赞曰：呜呼，靖康之祸，岂不哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222917_comment'></div>以二百年全盛之中国，而在位皆拘挛章句之徒，谓名节为非所急，士之精锐，销耎尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222917_comment'></div>一旦为敌所乘，无不全躯保妻子，奉头鼠窜，或甘心污辱之地而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222917_comment'></div>永以身徇国，至勉其家必死，非所谓烈丈夫而不为世所推移者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1222917_comment'></div>当是时，以节死者虽不为无人，若刘韐、李若水、向子韶、霍安国、张克戬、杨邦乂，皆其章章尤著者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1222917_comment'></div>然骂敌不屈，无如永者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1222917_comment'></div>故掇永平生行事著于篇，有以见永立大功名而奋不顾身者，有所从来，非偶然发也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_109_1222917_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年10月1日</a>　在平江，转对。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月3日</a>　在平江撰德音。作品：建炎三年十一月三日德音。<div id='poem_1222460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建炎三年十一月三日德音</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222460")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222460'>御敌者莫如自治，动民者当以至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222460_comment'></div>朕自缵丕图，即罹多故，昧绥怀之远略，贻播越之深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222460_comment'></div>虽眷我中原，汉祚必期于再复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222460_comment'></div>而迫于强敌，商人几至于五迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222460_comment'></div>兹缘仗卫之行，尤历江山之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222460_comment'></div>老弱扶携于道路，饥疲蒙犯于风霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222460_comment'></div>徒从或苦绎骚，程顿不无烦费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222460_comment'></div>所幸天人协相，川陆无虞，仿治古之时巡，即奥区而安处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222460_comment'></div>言念连年之纷扰，坐令率土之流离，乡闾遭焚劫之灾，财力困供输之役，肆夙宵而轸虑，如冰炭之交怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222460_comment'></div>嗟汝何辜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222460_comment'></div>由吾不德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222460_comment'></div>故每畏天而警戒，誓专克己以焦劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222460_comment'></div>欲睦邻休战，则卑辞厚礼以请和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222460_comment'></div>欲省费恤民，则贬食损衣而从俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222460_comment'></div>苟可坐销于氛祲，殆将无爱于发肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222460_comment'></div>然边陲岁骇，而师徒不免于屡兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222460_comment'></div>馈饷日滋，而征敛未遑于全复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222460_comment'></div>惟八世祖宗之泽，岂汝能忘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222460_comment'></div>顾一时社稷之忧，非予获已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222460_comment'></div>少俟寇攘之息，首图蠲省之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222460_comment'></div>况昨来蒙蔽之俗成，致今日凌夷之祸亟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222460_comment'></div>虽朕意日求于民瘼，而人情终壅于上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222460_comment'></div>主威非特于万钧，堂下自遥于千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222460_comment'></div>既真伪有难凭之患，则遐迩衔无告之冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222460_comment'></div>已敕辅臣，相与虚怀而听纳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222460_comment'></div>亦令在位，各须忘势以咨询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222460_comment'></div>直言者勿遣危疑，忠告者靡拘微隐，所期尔众，咸体朕怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222460_comment'></div>尚虑四民兴失职之嗟，百姓有夺时之怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222460_comment'></div>科需苛急，人心难俟于小康；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222460_comment'></div>犴狱繁滋，邦法有稽于末减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222460_comment'></div>乃用迎长之节，特颁在宥之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222460_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222460_comment'></div>王者宅中，夫岂甘心于远狩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222460_comment'></div>皇天助顺，其将悔祸于交侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222460_comment'></div>惟我二三之臣，与夫亿兆之众，亟攘外侮，协济中兴。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1222460_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1c041228d9be4c4fa571252c9ef41119_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1c041228d9be4c4fa571252c9ef41119");'><span id='1c041228d9be4c4fa571252c9ef41119_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，51岁</div><div id='1c041228d9be4c4fa571252c9ef41119' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月20日</a>　在越州，与李正民议移跸平江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月22日</a>　在越州，决议移跸浙西，汪藻草诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年12月16日</a>　高宗乘舟至定海。汪藻以不便海舶，请陆行以从。许之。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2374d1a02ce74577a2ebdd3ba3b855c4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2374d1a02ce74577a2ebdd3ba3b855c4");'><span id='2374d1a02ce74577a2ebdd3ba3b855c4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1131')">1130-1131年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='2374d1a02ce74577a2ebdd3ba3b855c4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在越州行在，有金人留建康乞分张浚兵马策应状。作品：奏论金人留建康乞分别张浚兵马策应状。<div id='poem_1222750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论金人留建康乞分张浚军马策应状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222750")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222750'>右，臣昨自三月末得之传闻，云金人在建康筑城，为度夏计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222750_comment'></div>臣虽幸其不然，然心窃忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222750_comment'></div>以为中国困于强敌而得少休息者，正赖其不能触热，故常已寒方至，未暑先归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222750_comment'></div>吾于半年间，汲汲措画，犹每岁奔命不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222750_comment'></div>今若纵其度夏，则长为巢穴，无所忌惮，不知朝廷何以枝梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222750_comment'></div>洎到行在，闻韩世忠列战舰江中，遮其归路，日有所获，且言金人穷蹙之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222750_comment'></div>臣窃欣幸，以为三月所传诞妄耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222750_comment'></div>续观黄榜，备录韩世忠捷奏，又谓朝夕必可扫除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222750_comment'></div>今近二十日矣，其耗寂然，未必皆实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222750_comment'></div>兼数日人自常、润来者，皆云敌于蒋山、雨花台各劄大寨，抱城开河两道以护之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222750_comment'></div>及穴山作小洞子，以为逃暑之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222750_comment'></div>陆增城垒，水造战船，而采石金人已渡复回者累累不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222750_comment'></div>今且五月矣，比常年去已月馀，乃反去而复回，其欲留建康明甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222750_comment'></div>如此，则与三月所传，又似符合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222750_comment'></div>臣闻金人动设诡诈，尤喜为穷蹙之状以疑我师，我师堕其计中者，前后非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222750_comment'></div>今安知其本为度夏计而阳为穷蹙者，特以疑我师耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222750_comment'></div>建康为东南咽喉，国之门户也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222750_comment'></div>天下转输、朝廷号令，未有不由此而通者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222750_comment'></div>若金人果据此为巢穴，则东南馈饷遂绝，如人扼其咽喉，守其门户，果得高枕而卧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222750_comment'></div>不知群臣日至上前，亦尝有反复及此者否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222750_comment'></div>岂遂以为无事，而所当讲者承平之先务乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222750_comment'></div>抑揣陛下非所乐闻而不以闻也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222750_comment'></div>不惟是而已，人既扼我咽喉、守我门户，则群盗亦将视我缓急，以为向背，国家果有力能使之退听屏息乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222750_comment'></div>况又有意外之忧所难言者，不得不虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222750_comment'></div>臣愚以为此事所系非细，庙堂当若救焚拯溺然，朝夕在念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222750_comment'></div>及五六月间，我师便利之时，会诸将与世忠一举扫除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222750_comment'></div>非特去目前之患，将使惩创终身，不敢复南，其利害岂不相万哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222750_comment'></div>虽闻近遣张浚提兵过江，节制浙西人马，迤逦前去，以为策应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222750_comment'></div>此固陛下长算也，不知张浚果能为陛下有慨然立功之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222750_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞专差得力使臣数人，赍陛下宸翰，星夜兼程，自襄、邓、荆、湖以来迎张浚军，令分数万人顺流而下，仍于上流自计置粮斛，载以自随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222750_comment'></div>彼张浚军既皆新人，必精锐可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222750_comment'></div>且敌人见上流之师突然而至，莫知其数，必破胆奔溃，此制敌一奇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222750_comment'></div>如其不然，八九月间，气候稍凉，彼得时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222750_comment'></div>机会一失，虽悔何追？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222750_comment'></div>伏望睿慈不以臣言为愚，轻此贼，忽此事，特加采纳，不胜幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1222750_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月11日</a>　在越州行在，以给事中试兵部侍郎，兼直学士院。上谢表。作品：谢除兵部侍郎表。<div id='poem_1222665' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222665' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222665?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除兵部侍郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222665")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222665'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222665'>东省瘝官，方祈病免；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222665_comment'></div>中台分职，乃误优迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222665_comment'></div>资逢世以非宜，宠逾涯而益惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222665_comment'></div>伏念臣江湖遐裔，章句小儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222665_comment'></div>材不过庸，仅及下中之品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222665_comment'></div>学虽忘老，安知左右之原？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222665_comment'></div>偶随多士之游，幸备公朝之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222665_comment'></div>遍誇清贯，遂缀迩联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222665_comment'></div>旋遭值于干戈，获奉承于羁靮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222665_comment'></div>才因事见，初无横草之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222665_comment'></div>灾与衰期，乃有负薪之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222665_comment'></div>屡投诚于魏阙，将归卧于漳滨，猥蒙内史之书，俾贰文昌之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222665_comment'></div>戎昭所系，儒绂奚堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222665_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下睿智有临，忧勤无逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222665_comment'></div>光复祖宗之旧，既已配天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222665_comment'></div>兼收文武之长，未尝愒日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222665_comment'></div>惟臣琐质，负国明恩，竭股肱之力而徒有此心，譬腹背之毛而何裨于用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222665_comment'></div>耗糜廪食，羞愧神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222665_comment'></div>不辞勉效于秋毫，顾恐溘先于朝露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222665_comment'></div>周六典治凡之职，虽幸叨居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222665_comment'></div>汉九卿赐告之恩，终期得请。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1222665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在越州行在，时行在除台谏外，只有汪藻与綦崇礼二人为曹，其它在道未至也。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月</a>　在越州行在，上札子言淮南归正人事。作品：论侨寓州郡札子。<div id='poem_1222746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论侨寓州郡劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222746")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222746_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222746'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222746'>臣闻自东晋以来，累朝皆治金陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222746_comment'></div>当时中原为五姓所据，于江南北侨立州郡，纳其流亡之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222746_comment'></div>故江都谓之南兖州，则兖州之人所居也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222746_comment'></div>京口谓之南徐州，则徐州之人所居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222746_comment'></div>以至南豫州、南司州亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222746_comment'></div>比金人入寇，多驱两河人民，列之行阵，号为「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1222746", 1222746, "Clauses/13/Comments/2")'>签军</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222746_comment'></div>彼以数百年祖宗涵养之恩，一旦与我为敌者，岂其本心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222746_comment'></div>特妻子、父兄为其劫质，以死胁之，出于不得已而然耳，固未尝一日忘宋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222746_comment'></div>今年建康、镇江为韩世忠、岳飞所招，遁归者无虑万人，其情可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222746_comment'></div>臣愚以为莫若因此时用六朝侨寓法，分浙西诸县，悉以两河州郡名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222746_comment'></div>假如金坛，权谓之南相州，许相州之人皆就金坛而居，其他类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222746_comment'></div>无事之时，多印文榜，先行散布，使皆明知国家优恤之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222746_comment'></div>俟其入寇，徐以旗帜招之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222746_comment'></div>彼既知所居各有定处，粗成井邑，父兄骨肉、亲戚故旧皆在，其有无足以相通，祸患足以相救，与乡居无异，亦何为而不居乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222746_comment'></div>况浙西州县，昨经焚劫之后，人遭杀戮，户绝必多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222746_comment'></div>如令有司籍定田产顷数，以待侨寓之人，计口而给，与土人杂耕，抚存老幼，系累其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222746_comment'></div>俟稍安居，料其丁壮，教以战阵，皆精兵也，必争先用命，永无溃散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222746_comment'></div>与夫从彼驱掳、反为我敌者，其利害岂止相万哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222746_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1222746_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月15日</a>　在越州行在，奏言遏赃吏之法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在越州行在，有诏于来年三月上旬择日殿试。作品：绍兴元年科举诏。<div id='poem_1222467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绍兴元年科举诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222467")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222467'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222467'>朕宵衣图治，仄席思贤，昨诏谕于绵区，俾宾兴于髦俊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222467_comment'></div>兹阅贤书之献，将偕计吏之来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222467_comment'></div>言念杪秋，适当大飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222467_comment'></div>有司较艺，于祀事以或妨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222467_comment'></div>多士在涂，恐行期之靡逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222467_comment'></div>姑从近制，分试外台，用比岁之彝章，临大廷而亲策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222467_comment'></div>既克成于朕志，亦良便于尔私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222467_comment'></div>可将省额合取分数下诸路提刑司，差官于转运司所在州类试，就今年八月上旬内择日引试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222467_comment'></div>其馀应合行事件，并令礼部比附建炎三年十二月二日指挥，条具申尚书省，于来年三月上旬择日殿试。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1222467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年12月13日</a>　在越州行在，尚书兵部侍郎兼权直学士院汪藻为翰林学士，上谢表。作品：谢除翰林学士表。<div id='poem_1222667' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222667' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222667?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除翰林学士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年12月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222667")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222667_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222667'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222667'>非才冒宠，久誇文石之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222667_comment'></div>优诏传恩，趣上玉堂之直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222667_comment'></div>既假朝章之焕，仍分御府之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222667_comment'></div>逊避莫从，叨尘为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222667_comment'></div>伏以文章虽本一技，命令实行四方，故自古禁林之除，极当时儒者之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222667_comment'></div>矧今多士，尤重他官，内敷帝制之坦明，外应军书之警急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222667_comment'></div>学非闳博，难酬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1222667", 1222667, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>跋烛之咨</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222667_comment'></div>思或淹迟，将误掣铃之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222667_comment'></div>当得瑰杰，来承燕閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222667_comment'></div>如臣者，猥以诸生，起于遐裔，首尾策名之二纪，中间不调者十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222667_comment'></div>会真人光复之初，陪列辟骏奔之后，骤膺间拔，遍历高华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222667_comment'></div>既时巡清跸之屡移，方驿召群英之未至，执羁在道，视草无人，姑从东省之联，兼候北门之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222667_comment'></div>尝因多病，不胜狗马之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222667_comment'></div>愿赐宽恩，任逐桑榆之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222667_comment'></div>孰云代匮，遂使为真？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222667_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下志靖华夷，忧深宵旰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222667_comment'></div>励精于学，每求稽古之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222667_comment'></div>罪己以言，欲致销兵之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222667_comment'></div>治虽得要，人岂当材？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222667_comment'></div>敢不仰佩眷知，力思补报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222667_comment'></div>丝纶行远，顾奚俟于丹青；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222667_comment'></div>海岳居微，或有资于尘露。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1222667_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222667'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一七，《古今事文类聚》新集卷一四，《渊鉴类函》卷七二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222667_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在越州行在，因草高丽答诏，高宗以所御白团扇，亲书“紫诰仍兼绾，黄麻似六经”以赐。缙绅荣之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年12月22日</a>　在越州行在，冬至，上表。作品：庚戌年冬至表。<div id='poem_1222626' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222626' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222626?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚戌年冬至表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年12月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222626")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222626_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222626'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222626'>伏以三微肇序，方迎舜日之长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222626_comment'></div>万类倾心，同望尧云之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222626_comment'></div>恭惟太上道君皇帝陛下功齐列圣，道冒群伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222626_comment'></div>温柔宽裕而足有容，夙谐民愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222626_comment'></div>进退存亡而不失正，允合天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222626_comment'></div>理极屯艰，时当亨复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222626_comment'></div>臣久违温凊，徒轸夙宵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222626_comment'></div>听嶰谷之新筒，于占则吉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222626_comment'></div>知襄城之法驾，不日而旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222626_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1222626_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222626'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷六。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222626_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在越州行在，年底，上奏论淮南屯田。<div id='poem_1222745' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222745' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222745?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论淮南屯田</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222745")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222745_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222745'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222745'>臣窃惟国家遭金人之祸，于今五年，无岁无兵，而去冬之役，振古未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222745_comment'></div>乃者盘礴之师，至江壖不渡，此陛下忧勤上通于天而天赞我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222745_comment'></div>然臣尝观古者两敌相持，所贵者机会，此胜负存亡之分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222745_comment'></div>敌兵既退，国家非暂都金陵不可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222745_comment'></div>而都金陵，非尽得淮南不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222745_comment'></div>淮南之地，金人必不能守，若为刘豫经营，不过留签军数万人而已耳，盖可驱而去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222745_comment'></div>淮南荐罹金人蹂践，且群盗继之，民去本业，十室而九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222745_comment'></div>其不耕之田，千里相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222745_comment'></div>流移之人，心已弃决，非朝夕可还也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222745_comment'></div>国家欲保淮南，势须屯田，则此田皆可耕垦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222745_comment'></div>臣愚以为正、二月间，可便遣刘光世或吕颐浩率诸头领招安人马，过江营建寨栅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222745_comment'></div>除现存人户田产不可借外，其馀流移未还者，明降指挥，各借五年，使诸军分地而耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222745_comment'></div>俟粮食充盈，规模已定，然后徐步而图中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222745_comment'></div>既固行在藩篱，且清东南群盗，此万世一时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222745_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1222745_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　在越州行在，作吴圣与墓志铭。作品：左中大夫致仕吴公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左中大夫致仕吴公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222931")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222931'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222931'>崇宁初，制诏以尚书左丞为丞相，天子虚己而听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222931_comment'></div>丞相因得操其权，进退天下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222931_comment'></div>诸附丽者，自布衣不旋踵至大官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222931_comment'></div>或舍己而从他，则中以危法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222931_comment'></div>于是一时嗜进之徒，莫不希其声光于顾盼间，諰諰然惟恐不得当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222931_comment'></div>当是时，太仆寺丞吴公点雅为相所知，相敬畏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222931_comment'></div>耻以其党进，力从之求去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222931_comment'></div>相嘻笑曰：「君欲首为去国之人耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222931_comment'></div>嗛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222931_comment'></div>自是相持国柄二十馀年，士大夫不堪其专且久，挠节从之多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222931_comment'></div>惟公卒不求合以死，天下莫不高之，虽阿相之人，亦自以为莫及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222931_comment'></div>公字圣与，其上世占籍光州，于唐为闻家，后徙闽之邵武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222931_comment'></div>至公之高祖沇，仕南汉为循州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222931_comment'></div>曾祖汉卿、祖颙，皆以行高其州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222931_comment'></div>皇考诏益务修饰，教诸子以经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222931_comment'></div>子四人，踵登进士科，兄弟竞爽，知名当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222931_comment'></div>累赠其官，为少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222931_comment'></div>公少持重寡言，人未之奇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222931_comment'></div>总角以文见乡先生黄履，进退如成人，问皆可观，履叹赏弥日，曰：「子必为令器」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222931_comment'></div>闻王文公修经金陵，负笈从之，繇是学益进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222931_comment'></div>元丰五年，擢进士第，调舒州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222931_comment'></div>年少，人或易之，有市医砭人死，系月馀莫能决，公一见曰：「此非律所谓误不如方者耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222931_comment'></div>老吏相顾大惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222931_comment'></div>移英州真阳令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222931_comment'></div>岭海去朝廷远，吏多版授，守率以胥遇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222931_comment'></div>始至，风公庭趋，公不为屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222931_comment'></div>守大怒，欲诬以事，久而知其贤，反荐诸朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222931_comment'></div>丁内艰，免丧监建州买纳茶务，守正无所阿徇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222931_comment'></div>用荐者改宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222931_comment'></div>韩宗道知杭州，奏知富阳县，政绩为一路最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222931_comment'></div>时孙杰察访东南，官吏重足事之，独荐公为可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222931_comment'></div>徽宗登极，转奉议郎，赐绯衣银鱼，签书常州判官厅公事，州倚以为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222931_comment'></div>擢太仆寺丞，相憾其去，出通判婺州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222931_comment'></div>行未半涂，差拨发福建路钱物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222931_comment'></div>凡当是选者，事已必归报求美官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222931_comment'></div>至陈留，以记白曹，不见宰相而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222931_comment'></div>相滋不悦，下除通判睦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222931_comment'></div>秩满，移越州，遂请老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222931_comment'></div>贫不能归，客婺州兰溪，四壁萧然，处之晏如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222931_comment'></div>御史中丞吴执中知其贤，起之再任，公不得已至京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222931_comment'></div>会同年生在庙堂，欲以公见上，公固辞曰：「吾尝谢事矣，岂可复见上乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222931_comment'></div>得通判洪州，径出关不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222931_comment'></div>时茶法初下，责有司奉行，郡以丞领之，敢议者斥，吏奔走不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222931_comment'></div>公独条不便于民数事上之，人为寒心，公不恤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222931_comment'></div>已而朝廷施行其说，至今赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222931_comment'></div>秩将满，报政或欲召公，公闻，即以病告，得提点衡州露仙观，继领亳之明道宫、建之冲佑观、南京之鸿庆宫，奉祠十馀年，卧家不复出，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222931_comment'></div>渊圣皇帝受内禅，转中大夫，擢知漳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222931_comment'></div>于是公无意于世矣，复请老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222931_comment'></div>以建炎四年十一月某甲子卒于家，春秋七十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222931_comment'></div>官自宣德郎十一迁至中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222931_comment'></div>有文集三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222931_comment'></div>娶同里黄氏，封令人，先公二十年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222931_comment'></div>二男四女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222931_comment'></div>男曰延年，朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222931_comment'></div>次早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222931_comment'></div>女适从政郎广德县汪诗、迪功郎长沙县尉张某、朝散大夫徐敏中、朝散郎直徽猷阁范浩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222931_comment'></div>孙男女各一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222931_comment'></div>男曰祐，迪功郎、南剑州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222931_comment'></div>女适从政郎、建昌军教授李汝翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222931_comment'></div>公退然如中人，而操履刚方，其坚如金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222931_comment'></div>与人言，虽面目严冷，而衮衮皆可书绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222931_comment'></div>少清苦，一毫不取诸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222931_comment'></div>其举进士、出京师也，仆遭疠焉，人皆恶之，欲委诸道，公辍己舆以载，徒走千里而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222931_comment'></div>晚读佛书，益翛然有遗世意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222931_comment'></div>其于简淡，盖往复而身安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222931_comment'></div>凡世间所谓矫揉以钓声名者，公无以焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222931_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222931_comment'></div>慕富贵而仕者，固人之常情，守道而不求，亦士夫之所当务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222931_comment'></div>然利害陈于前而为举世之所熏灼，其不从者几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222931_comment'></div>若夫屹然如砥柱，立于颓波之中，久而不为之动，盖今人所未见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222931_comment'></div>至终始完洁如公者，殆百年所无也，可不谓贤哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222931_comment'></div>藻少从公游，服膺最久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222931_comment'></div>延年既以公卒之年十一月葬公于其居之西若千里王公岭之下，乃属藻识其墓，藻于是叙公之实而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222931_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1222931'>古之仕者惟己责，于遭穷通我何择？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222931_comment'></div>世衰鄙夫乃求获，相时射利规什伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222931_comment'></div>伟哉吴公挺松柏，力排冰霜傲堙阨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222931_comment'></div>世方贤愚糅黑白，朝为之徒暮隆赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222931_comment'></div>幸公来游重其客，疾趋而逃远瑕谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222931_comment'></div>终身轩裳不能迫，浮沈数州下膏泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222931_comment'></div>晚归遐陬与世隔，竟全孤高返真宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222931_comment'></div>向来公卿愧方册，揭兹铭诗告阡陌。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1222931_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月1日</a>　在越州行在，上表。作品：辛亥年正旦表。<div id='poem_1222627' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222627' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222627?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛亥年正旦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222627")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222627_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222627'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222627'>伏以接千载之统，推神筴以膺期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222627_comment'></div>上万年之觞，御端朝而受祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222627_comment'></div>若稽故实，遥企清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222627_comment'></div>恭惟太上皇帝陛下体道粹精，怡神冲漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222627_comment'></div>方席宗祧之庆，遽成国步之艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222627_comment'></div>帝尧游汾水之阳，久忘天下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222627_comment'></div>文王遇明夷之卦，益见圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222627_comment'></div>臣自远威颜，荐更时序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222627_comment'></div>当玑衡之载复，怅旒扆之犹赊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222627_comment'></div>鸿雁虽宾，莫附帛书于沙漠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222627_comment'></div>风涛中阻，徒瞻云气于蓬莱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222627_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222627_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年2月2日</a>　在越州行在，兼侍讲。上谢表。作品：谢兼侍讲表。<div id='poem_1222666' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222666' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222666?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除兼侍讲表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222666")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222666_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222666'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222666'>视草禁严，谈经閒燕，兼近侍进言之责，极儒臣稽古之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222666_comment'></div>拜命以还，抚躬而惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222666_comment'></div>臣尝谓天纵将圣，奚须博学以成名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222666_comment'></div>王求多闻，盖欲取人而为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222666_comment'></div>故自古右文之世，必留心讲艺之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222666_comment'></div>如臣至愚，何以仰称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222666_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下卓然上智，济以克勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222666_comment'></div>同汉祖之英，论道不忘于息马；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222666_comment'></div>笑齐侯之陋，读书见议于斲轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222666_comment'></div>而臣猥以非才，膺兹遴选，第竭简编之习，仰承帷幄之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222666_comment'></div>虽海岳深崇，顾何取涓埃之细；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222666_comment'></div>然圣贤闻见，或不如农婢之专。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222666_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222666'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二一，《唐宋元名表》卷下之二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222666_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年2月26日</a>　在越州行在，上驭将三说。作品：行在越州条具时政。<div id='poem_1222741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222741' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222741?labeling=true' target='_blank'>行在越州条具时政</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年2月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222741")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222741_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222741'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222741'>臣窃惟人君当承平之时，中原无犬吠之惊，人臣以未见未然之事，自下劘上，甘心蹈鈇钺之诛，义士犹不以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222741_comment'></div>今国家之危，如坐烧屋之下、漏船之中，陛下宵旰忧勤，未知所以拯救之术，而求言于臣等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222741_comment'></div>傥犹狃习故态，用猥并之辞，取塞诏旨而已，岂臣等事君之义而陛下所以望臣等之意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222741_comment'></div>况陛下诏臣等以当今保民弭盗、遏寇生财之要，而卒曰当虚己而力行之，此正臣等惓惓效忠于陛下之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222741_comment'></div>臣昨扈跸温州，尝蒙陛下赐以条对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222741_comment'></div>臣以为方今所急者，惟驭将一事，更无他说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222741_comment'></div>譬御饥者当用食，舍食之外，皆非所急也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222741_comment'></div>已疾者当用医，舍医之外，皆非所急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222741_comment'></div>陛下不以臣为愚，虽不施行，然颇加采纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222741_comment'></div>臣今日区区之愚，犹守前见，敢再为陛下陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222741_comment'></div>古之进说者曰，人君恭俭爱人、清心省事、建立法度、制礼作乐，岂非甚盛之举而至美之谈欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222741_comment'></div>是数者，固人君不可须臾而忘，然今日用此，则未足以解纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222741_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222741_comment'></div>敌骑充斥于中原，群盗跳梁于诸路，陛下专于恭俭爱人、清心省事而已，为足以却之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222741_comment'></div>建立法度、制礼作乐而已，为足以却之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222741_comment'></div>是必陛下能使诸将、能使士卒，为足以却之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222741_comment'></div>而陛下诸将，爵禄已极，家赀已盈，习成悍骄，无复斗志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222741_comment'></div>一方有警，辄狐疑相伏，无一人奋然为国请行者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222741_comment'></div>或敦迫不得已而行，则邀例外之赏，肆无名之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222741_comment'></div>上不恤国，下不恤民，使朝廷为之黾勉曲从，不啻如奉骄子，是岂为国家平祸乱、立功名之人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222741_comment'></div>臣于此有驭将之说三焉，惟陛下留神省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222741_comment'></div>一曰示之以法，二曰运之以权，三曰别之以分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222741_comment'></div>何谓示之以法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222741_comment'></div>古者人君之于将帅，未尝一日废赏，亦未尝一日废刑，如冬夏寒暑然，相须而成，岂有独恩无威，漫然略不绳治，如今日之甚者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222741_comment'></div>议者谓承平之时，朝廷尊荣，操纵由我，故武夫提兵者，可予可夺，可生可杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222741_comment'></div>今溥天抢攘，国难未已，方藉此曹为腹心，孜孜拊循，犹惧不济，奈何欲咈其心，将谁肯前死？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222741_comment'></div>且今诸将悍骄已成，虽朝廷有法，果能一一治之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222741_comment'></div>此言是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222741_comment'></div>然臣所谓治之以法者，岂欲明主自亲其文哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222741_comment'></div>古者人君以恩结人，必有人臣为朝廷任其责者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222741_comment'></div>肃宗在灵武，广平王以兵二十万复长安，其权可谓重矣，先驱不肃，颜真卿劾之，王为之不敢当阙而乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222741_comment'></div>李祐夜入蔡州，缚吴元济，其功可谓大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222741_comment'></div>违诏进马，温造劾之，祐曰「今日胆落于温御史」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222741_comment'></div>夫先驱不肃、违诏进马，于军政未有害也，而二臣已不贷如此，盖小过不贷，则恶之大者，知朝廷有人，不复敢萌于胸中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222741_comment'></div>今诸将虽骄，然臣得之传闻，亦尚知畏朝廷之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222741_comment'></div>而陛下群臣，方平居时，聚谈切齿，无不以诸将负国为言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222741_comment'></div>及进言陛下，不过掎摭目前，为逭责进身之资而已，至此事则未尝有一言及之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222741_comment'></div>岂以为细故而不足言也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222741_comment'></div>揣陛下非所乐闻而不以告耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222741_comment'></div>殊不知陛下专于用恩，恩过而骄，有司时一警焉，是使陛下结其心者愈固而愈深也，何不乐闻之有哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222741_comment'></div>何谓运之以权？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222741_comment'></div>臣闻驭将如驭马，必驭者之力足以胜马，然后周旋曲折，惟我之听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222741_comment'></div>不然，窃衔诡辔，毁首碎胸，虽跬步之间，不能使之前矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222741_comment'></div>高祖之诸将，其枭雄而难制者莫如韩信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222741_comment'></div>方其围于荥阳，汉固危甚，人人怀去就之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222741_comment'></div>高祖一旦入其军中，自称使者，即卧内夺其印符，麾召诸将易置之，信盖不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222741_comment'></div>及信下魏代，辄收其精兵以距楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222741_comment'></div>既项羽死垓下，则又尽夺其军，徒为楚王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222741_comment'></div>以信之材，而周旋曲折惟高祖之听者，岂不以其智足以胜之故耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222741_comment'></div>故信尝曰：「陛下不善将兵而善将将」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222741_comment'></div>是信自知其材惟高祖足以制己，故甘心俛首为之用而不辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222741_comment'></div>大抵人君之于将帅，必有得其要领而使之心畏诚服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222741_comment'></div>谓解衣推食便足以得其欢心者，果非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222741_comment'></div>唐宪宗时，刘辟叛蜀，宰相杜黄裳度惟高崇文足以破之，而崇文素惮刘澭，使人谓曰：「公不奋命，当以澭代」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222741_comment'></div>崇文惧，尽力缚贼以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222741_comment'></div>是以澭代崇文者，黄裳得其要领也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222741_comment'></div>高祖之用韩信，其术岂亦出此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222741_comment'></div>今陛下诸将，仓卒之时，可收其精兵而用以自卫乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222741_comment'></div>于立大功之时，可夺其全军而使之归镇乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222741_comment'></div>臣有以知陛下不能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222741_comment'></div>幸今诸将皆龌龊常才，固不足深忌，万一有如韩信者，不知陛下何以待之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222741_comment'></div>如此，则平居之时，亦当深察其奸，如以刘澭代崇文之术，不可不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222741_comment'></div>何谓别之以分？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222741_comment'></div>汉高祖谓功臣曰：「诸君知猎乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222741_comment'></div>夫猎，追杀兽者，狗也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222741_comment'></div>而发纵指示兽处者，人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222741_comment'></div>今诸君徒能走得兽耳，如萧何则发纵指示者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222741_comment'></div>盖古者用兵，谋臣坐于帷幄之中，以出筹策，而将帅则听命于前，为之役使，此命之所以一而功之所以成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222741_comment'></div>高祖之所与谋者，萧何、张良、陈平而已，黥、彭之徒不得而预也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222741_comment'></div>蜀先主所与谋者，诸葛武侯而已，关、张之徒不得而预也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222741_comment'></div>唐太宗所与谋者，房乔、杜如晦而已，英、卫之徒不得而预也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222741_comment'></div>今谋臣之任宰相，执政而已，陛下以为谋之不臧欤，慎择而易之可也，独不可使武夫参预其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222741_comment'></div>窃观陛下对大臣不过数刻，而诸将皆得出入禁中，是大臣见陛下有时，而诸将无时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222741_comment'></div>臣非不知艰难之时，陛下欲得其心，姑与之无间，然此曹何所知识，必不能上补聪明，不过入则希求恩泽，出则凭藉权势而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222741_comment'></div>比道路流传，遂以为陛下进退人材，诸将或预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222741_comment'></div>以陛下英睿，择善而从，顾于此曹何有，然致是言者，恐必有可疑之迹，不可不慎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222741_comment'></div>又庙堂者，具瞻之地，大臣为天子建立政事，以号令四方者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222741_comment'></div>今诸将率骤谒径前，便衣密坐，视大臣如僚友，百端营求，期于必得而后已，朝廷岂不惧卑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222741_comment'></div>祖宗时，武臣莫尊三衙，见大臣必执梃趋庭，肃揖而退，非文具也，以为等威不如是之严，不足以相制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222741_comment'></div>以今观之，一何陵夷之甚耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222741_comment'></div>兼国家出师遣将，诏侍从集议者，所以慎之重之，博众人之见也，而诸将必在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222741_comment'></div>夫诸将者，听命于朝廷而为之使者也，乃使之从容预谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222741_comment'></div>彼既各售其说，则利于公而不利于私者，必不肯以为可行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222741_comment'></div>便于己而不便于国者，必不肯以为可罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222741_comment'></div>欲责其冒锋镝、趋死地，难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222741_comment'></div>臣愚以为，自今诸将，当律以朝廷之仪，每有奏陈，必使之如有司之式，毋数燕见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222741_comment'></div>其至政事堂，亦有祖宗故事，且毋使参议论之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222741_comment'></div>庶名分不至混淆，而可以责其功效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222741_comment'></div>是三说者果行，足以驾驭诸将矣，何忧乎保民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222741_comment'></div>何难乎弭盗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222741_comment'></div>何患乎遏寇哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222741_comment'></div>若夫国财之生，则臣愿陛下毋以生财为言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222741_comment'></div>自五六十年来，士大夫喜操生财之说，民穷至骨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222741_comment'></div>今四方莽为盗区，国家所有不过数路数十州而已，所谓生者，必生之于此数十州之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222741_comment'></div>古者以暴赋横敛为非，尚有赋敛之名也，今则直夺而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222741_comment'></div>古者以收大半之赋为非，尚有其半也，今则直尽而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222741_comment'></div>南亩之民，寒耕暑耘，黧面涂足，终岁劳苦而不厌糟糠者，陛下不得而见也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222741_comment'></div>胥吏坐门，朝暮不得休息，愁叹之声日与死比者，陛下不得而闻也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222741_comment'></div>贴妻卖子，至无地可容其身者，陛下不得而知也，尚何以生财为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222741_comment'></div>惟有痛加裁损，庶几乎其可耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222741_comment'></div>外之可以裁损者，军中之冒请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222741_comment'></div>内之可以裁损者，禁中之汎取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222741_comment'></div>何谓军中之冒请？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222741_comment'></div>朝廷不得已而取民之财，当一铢一缕一粒以养战士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222741_comment'></div>今一军之中，非战士者率三居其二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222741_comment'></div>有诡名而请者，一人而挟数人之名是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222741_comment'></div>有以使臣之名而请者，一使臣之俸，实兼十人战士之费，而行伍中使臣大半，是养兵十万，而止获万兵之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1222741_comment'></div>有借补官资而请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1222741_comment'></div>异时借补，犹须申禀朝廷，谓之真命，今则一军之出，四方游手者无不窜名军中，既得主帅借补，便悉支行禄廪，与命官一同，无有限极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1222741_comment'></div>访闻岳飞军中，如此类者几数百人，州县惧于凭陵，莫敢诃诘，其盗支之物，至不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1222741_comment'></div>不惟是而已，自军兴以来，州县贪残之吏，惟患盗贼之不来，一闻入境，则便置军期司率敛民财，无复稽考，恣为侵渔，与盗无异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1222741_comment'></div>此而不治，虽财赋日生，于国家果有秋毫之益哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1222741_comment'></div>何谓禁中汎取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1222741_comment'></div>臣窃观国家军兵之饷、百官之廪、乘舆之俸，悉在有司，而禁中时有须索，如户部银绢以万计，礼部度牒以百计者，月有进焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1222741_comment'></div>以陛下清心寡欲，必无嫔嫱横给、宴游侈费也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1222741_comment'></div>以陛下恭勤节俭，必无营缮浮耗，使令妄予也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1222741_comment'></div>然人主用财，要须有名，使有司预闻，用而无名，是取民膏血掷而弃之沟中耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1222741_comment'></div>至于度牒，则国家以虚名而权天下之实利，陛下用之以重则重，陛下用之以轻则轻，免一时掊敛之疮痍，而实济军兴之用，诚非小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1222741_comment'></div>幸毋以为方寸之纸，捐以予人而不知惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1222741_comment'></div>若内外并加裁损，大农之计，虽未知有馀，其视不知节用而专务生财者有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1222741_comment'></div>陛下所以诏臣者，臣固已毕陈于前矣，而臣有私忧过计者，敢复言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1222741_comment'></div>臣闻《坤》之初六曰：「履霜坚冰至」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1222741_comment'></div>《象》曰：「履霜坚冰，阴始凝也，驯致其道，至坚冰也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1222741_comment'></div>盖患之不可不豫防者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1222741_comment'></div>自古以兵权属人，久而未有不为患者，岂不以予之至易，收之至难，不蚤图之，后悔无及耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1222741_comment'></div>晋以六卿帅师，而卒于分晋者，六卿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1222741_comment'></div>鲁以三家帅师，而卒于弱鲁者，三家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1222741_comment'></div>汉自元、成，兵在外戚，而汉由是以亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1222741_comment'></div>唐自中叶，兵在神策，而唐由是以乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1222741_comment'></div>古今一同，此必然之理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1222741_comment'></div>国家以三衙管军，而一兵之出，必待枢密院之符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1222741_comment'></div>祖宗于兹，盖有深意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1222741_comment'></div>今诸将之骄，密院已不得而制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1222741_comment'></div>臣恐寇平之后，方有劳圣虑，孔子所谓「吾恐季孙之忧，不在颛臾而在萧墙之内也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1222741_comment'></div>臣尝观自古偏方霸国提兵者未尝乏人，岂以国家四海之大，虽曰多故，而将帅之材遂至寥寥如此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1222741_comment'></div>意偏裨之中，必有英豪，特为二三大将抑之而不伸耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1222741_comment'></div>臣以为及今之时，当用汉建诸侯之法，众建之而少其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1222741_comment'></div>精择偏裨十馀人，人裁付兵数千，直隶御前而不隶诸将，合为数万，以渐销诸将之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1222741_comment'></div>此万世计也，惟陛下毋以臣人微而忽其言，不胜幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_138_1222741_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年4月9日</a>　在越州行在，高宗赐御书扇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年5月</a>　在越州行在，隆祐皇太后崩，汪藻有挽词五首。作品：隆祐太后挽词。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《浮溪集》卷三十有《隆祐太后挽词》二首，《浮溪集拾遗》卷三又有《隆祐太后挽词》三首。）</span><div id='poem_528364' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528364' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528364?labeling=true' target='_blank'>隆祐太后挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528364")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528364_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528364'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528364'>庆源由魏国，奉祀及宣仁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528364'>盛德仪中壸，私恩绝外亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528364'>长秋期不老，厚夜忽无晨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528364'>来岁柔桑绿，谁临茧馆春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528364_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528364'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528364_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_528365' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528365' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528365?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年5月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528365'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528365'>朔漠遐征后，南州俶扰时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528365'>人心忧社稷，天意属帘帷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528365'>拥佑千龄主，图回万世基。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528365'>中兴能事毕，倏与帝乡期<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《浮溪集》卷三○）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528365_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年5月25日</a>　在越州行在，上隆祐皇太后谥议。作品：恭上隆祐皇太后谥议。<div id='poem_1222756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恭上隆祐皇太后谥议</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年5月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222756")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222756_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222756'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222756'>臣伏奉敕命，礼部状，据太常寺申，今来大行隆祐皇太后崩，合差谥议官，差臣撰谥议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222756_comment'></div>臣谨上议曰：臣闻承天者地也，所以函六气而熙岁功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222756_comment'></div>配阳者阴也，所以分四时而成物化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222756_comment'></div>俪宸极者后也，所以奉宗社而隆化基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222756_comment'></div>故古之母仪天下者，生也荐之尊名，终而述其大行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222756_comment'></div>三代尚矣，靡得而详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222756_comment'></div>在汉则明德、和熹著称于前，在唐则文德、懿安垂纪于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222756_comment'></div>皆所以揭椒涂之范，炳彤管之辉，巍巍乎与帝德并隆，不可贬已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222756_comment'></div>洪惟大行隆祐皇太后，躬圣善之德，茂柔明之资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222756_comment'></div>粤自先正魏王，有功仁祖之世，王室所赖，旂常纪之，其泽深庆绵，用集我太母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222756_comment'></div>惟我太母，基迹元祐，嫔于泰陵，逮事宣仁、钦圣两宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222756_comment'></div>禀二《南》之规，兼四教之善，正位宫掖，三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222756_comment'></div>含洪广大而体坤道之常，进退存亡而得圣人之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222756_comment'></div>及靖康初载，天割我家，二帝出郊，中原无统，列辟相视，莫知所图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222756_comment'></div>我太母起于危疑之中，自任以天下之重，手援大宝，授之圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222756_comment'></div>当方隅倾侧之时，序璇历纂承之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222756_comment'></div>虽文母以十乱兴周，不能过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222756_comment'></div>已而六飞南渡，按跸武林，元凶窥朝，宄自内作，天下之势，甚于缀旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222756_comment'></div>我太后投袂而履祸机，立谈而销逆祲，坐使天地复正，三辰复明，四方元元，悉免涂炭，虽娲皇以鍊石补天，不能过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222756_comment'></div>既勋猷崇极如此，而乃抑华敦俭，率礼蹈和，塞私谒之涂，裁外家之宠，清净谦冲而以道为本，沈潜刚克而与神为谋，拥佑圣躬，殚诚尽爱，煌煌乎度越《麟趾》《思齐》之上矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222756_comment'></div>方期清我甸服，驾旋旧京，虔奉翟车，谒款宗庙，极四海之养，即东朝之安，而昊天不辰，祸结慈极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222756_comment'></div>亲蚕告毕，方开盛夏之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222756_comment'></div>隙驷难留，遽掩长秋之御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222756_comment'></div>兹天子追慕，悼心失图，叹厚载之中倾，痛仙游之不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222756_comment'></div>虽遂服不可，勉从期岁之丧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222756_comment'></div>而兴哀无时，每过举音之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222756_comment'></div>由是命有司考易名之典，懋饰终之仪，告于神明，节以四惠，庶几有以彰淑则而畅徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222756_comment'></div>谨按《谥法》：「明德有功曰昭，视民如子曰慈，聪明睿智曰献，安民有功曰烈」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222756_comment'></div>若乃两值时变，当阳御帘，基图既安，即复明辟，泽及万世，与天无穷，非明德有功耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222756_comment'></div>寝兴焦劳，言动恳恻，冒风涛兵革之险，济宇宙生灵之艰，非视民如子耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222756_comment'></div>察兴替之端，知变通之利，亲庶政以任溥天之责，奉真人以膺神器之归，非聪明睿智耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222756_comment'></div>中微之绪而我振之，大乱之原而我窒之，从容房帷，密斡鸿造，非安民有功耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222756_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222756_comment'></div>道之大者，理谢形容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222756_comment'></div>名之尊者，言绝称谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222756_comment'></div>故古者贱不诔贵，幼不诔长，而皇后之谥则请之于庙，示虽天子，必有尊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222756_comment'></div>况我太后盛德元功，夐无前比，岂承学之臣，所能拟议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222756_comment'></div>意者必受成于宗庙，为足以对在天之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222756_comment'></div>大行隆祐皇太后谥议，宜以祖宗之命，锡之曰「昭慈献烈皇后」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222756_comment'></div>臣谨议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1222756_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年5月26日</a>　在越州行在，因入学士院需经隆祐皇太后攒宫门，而攒宫不日动工，不便出入，奏请本家供职。诏从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在越州行在，代高宗悼隆祐皇太后。作品：绍兴元年追严隆祐皇太后诏。<div id='poem_1222469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绍兴元年追严隆祐皇太后诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222469")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222469'>朕惟隆祐皇太后，母仪后德，夙表宫闱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222469_comment'></div>圣烈神功，实施社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222469_comment'></div>自遭罹于多故，尤眷佑于眇躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222469_comment'></div>方期孝养于无穷，忽痛仙游之不返。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222469_comment'></div>念欲追严于景福，莫如溥降于隆宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222469_comment'></div>乃眷囚拘，或忧疾疢，爰挺桁杨之系，庶臻囹圄之空，以伸过隙之哀，以慰在天之监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222469_comment'></div>其行在并诸路州军，见禁公事，如大情已明，小节未圆，并免取会，先此结断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222469_comment'></div>行在令御史台、诸路州军令提点刑狱官检察，无令少有冤滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222469_comment'></div>应缘干證非本犯人，如已供證了毕，即时放出，不得苛留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222469_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1222469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年7月8日</a>　在越州行在，上奏文武官滥赏事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年7月29日</a>　在越州行在，草范宗尹免宰相之职制。作品：范宗尹特授观文殿学士提举临安府洞霄宫依前通议大夫食邑实封如故任便居住制。<div id='poem_1222432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范宗尹特授观文殿学士提举临安府洞霄宫依前通议大夫食邑食实封如故任便居住制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年7月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222432")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222432'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222432'>朝廷隆钧轴之任，去留虽别于二涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222432_comment'></div>王者待股肱之臣，终始盖如于一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222432_comment'></div>朕懋建台弼，甫更岁时，力辞柄任之烦，屡上囊封之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222432_comment'></div>姑从雅志，用锡湛恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222432_comment'></div>具官某蚤以时髦，仪于禁路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222432_comment'></div>钦王如孟子，特高台谏之称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222432_comment'></div>选众举皋陶，首冠丞疑之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222432_comment'></div>方倚俟巨川之济，乃寖乖岩石之瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222432_comment'></div>日者轻用人言，妄裁官簿，以庙堂之尊而负天下之谤，以人主之孝而暴君亲之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222432_comment'></div>朕既丁宁德意，而申命于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222432_comment'></div>汝方废格诏书，而持必于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222432_comment'></div>属上还于相绂，愿休养于祠庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222432_comment'></div>详览所陈，重违其请，解冢司之要务，加秘殿之隆名，曾弃瑕疵，盖全体貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222432_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222432_comment'></div>畴若予采，尝膺同德之求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222432_comment'></div>式遄其归，终听乞身之去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222432_comment'></div>往服朕命，永孚于休。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1222432_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年8月23日</a>　在越州行在，启贺秦桧拜相。作品：贺秦丞相启。<div id='poem_1222843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺秦丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年8月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222843")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222843'>廷扬孚号，国拜元台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222843_comment'></div>有道而守四夷，方懋中兴之业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222843_comment'></div>职要而论一相，宁须夹辅之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222843_comment'></div>天意会同，人心闿怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222843_comment'></div>恭以某官运逢真主，志在生民，聚精神帷幄之中，绝礼貌簪缨之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222843_comment'></div>安危大计，孰堪举国而听焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222843_comment'></div>前后数公，方见得君之专者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222843_comment'></div>积三岁处中之望，副九重虚左之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222843_comment'></div>魁柄不移，衮衣增焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222843_comment'></div>方且收威权于王室，示风采于敌人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222843_comment'></div>取河北一百馀州，今其时矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222843_comment'></div>书汾阳二十四考，行且见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222843_comment'></div>某久托洪钧，欣闻显册，属拘縻于乘障，阻趋走于班庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222843_comment'></div>岁籥将中，庙堂多暇，冀毖鼎茵之节，永为宗社之休。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1222843_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在越州行在，除翰林学士后，张扩有诗戏之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在越州行在，在翰林院期间，尝荐徐俯。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月28日</a>　除龙图阁直学士、知湖州。上谢表。作品：谢除龙图阁直学士知湖州表。<div id='poem_1222668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除龙图阁直学士知湖州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年9月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222668")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222668'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222668'>论思无补，席宠过优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222668_comment'></div>蒙内史之赞书，预西清之更直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222668_comment'></div>载循侥冒，冞积兢危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222668_comment'></div>窃惟祖宗谟训之藏，上宪奎壁图书之象，敞禁楹而并峙，命儒学以递居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222668_comment'></div>矧接鸳鸿之游，尤高龙马之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222668_comment'></div>法从假之而出守，书生借此以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222668_comment'></div>夫岂孱庸，所能堪副？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222668_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下聪明稽古，寅畏事天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222668_comment'></div>见贤而拔其尤，每兼收于群策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222668_comment'></div>拨乱而反之正，将光复于丕图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222668_comment'></div>而臣久服周行，最为冗从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222668_comment'></div>入备内朝之供奉，出分辅郡之顾忧，虽远清光，实繄全度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222668_comment'></div>重高明之地，怅已负于明恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222668_comment'></div>践文石之班，敢遽忘于雅意？</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1222668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222668'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷一九。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222668_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　知湖州后，领日历如故。<br /></div>
-----end

宁波
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7ab235451b394d79971c6e267d3d7629_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7ab235451b394d79971c6e267d3d7629");'><span id='7ab235451b394d79971c6e267d3d7629_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年12月22日</a>　冬至日，有遥拜道君皇帝表。作品：己酉年冬至遥拜道君皇帝表本。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋庆元元年（1196），明州升格为庆元府。）</span><div id='poem_1222625' id='poem_sentence_1_1222625_comment'></div>惟亚岁之佳辰，启后天之遐福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222625_comment'></div>恭惟太上道君皇帝陛下，道隆治古，泽在生民。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年12月</a>　张元干遭馋得罪，汪藻力救得免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　自靖康以来，三年未设科举，朝廷定于明年重开，故于本年下诏，汪藻有科举诏。作品：建炎四年科举诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（南宋庆元元年（1198），明州升格为庆元府。）</span><div id='poem_1222466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222466?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建炎四年科举诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222466")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222466'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222466'>国家承百年积累之基，赖多士维持之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222466_comment'></div>每张设于科目，务收揽于人材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222466_comment'></div>为兼学业之长，用济功名之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222466_comment'></div>昨缘多故，莫守旧章，已失三年之期，遂为一切之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222466_comment'></div>与贤乡老，虽繇本郡之计偕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222466_comment'></div>较艺春官，姑付外台而类试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222466_comment'></div>幸国有从权之法，使士无失职之嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222466_comment'></div>逮亲策于明廷，果允符于众望，朅从此举，今复其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222466_comment'></div>缘敌国之尚侵，恐行期之靡定，念欲便群髦之集，莫如遵近岁之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222466_comment'></div>朕方慨慕古人，共图今日之治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222466_comment'></div>尔其各从秋赋，以待有司之公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222466_comment'></div>苟中度程，何忧爵禄？</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222466_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e70bbab7b7064041852f488a78e78b26_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e70bbab7b7064041852f488a78e78b26");'><span id='e70bbab7b7064041852f488a78e78b26_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，52岁</div><div id='e70bbab7b7064041852f488a78e78b26' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月</a>　汪藻循高宗御舟行进路线，陆从以行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年1月28日</a>　在温州，有奏论诸将无功状。<div id='poem_1222743' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222743' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222743?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏论诸将无功状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年1月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222743")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222743'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222743'>准行在御史台告报，正月三十日，三省枢密院同奉圣旨，将来敌骑北归，或尽数过江，或于建康、杭、越等州留兵占据，各当如何措画，及当于何处驻跸，除已令侍从官条具外，可更令随行在职事官各条具以闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222743_comment'></div>右，臣窃惟金人为中国患虽已五年，而自陛下即位以来，祖宗土宇，日蹙一日，生灵涂炭，岁甚一岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222743_comment'></div>臣尝稽之载籍，虽至微弱之邦，至衰闇之主，敌人临境，犹能使其国人勉强一战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222743_comment'></div>未闻以堂堂中国之大，州县所存者大半，陛下英明之资，励精求治，无失德于天下，而敌骑长驱，去巢穴万有馀里，如入无人之境，至山东则破山东，至淮南则破淮南，至浙江则破浙江，嘻笑而来，饱满而去，坐令原野厌人之肉，川谷流人之血，宗社不绝如线，以万乘之尊，至于乘桴入海，伥伥然未知税驾之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222743_comment'></div>其所以至此者何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222743_comment'></div>将帅不得其人，而陛下所以驭将帅者未得其术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222743_comment'></div>今陛下所谓将帅者谁乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222743_comment'></div>臣知之矣，不过曰刘光世、韩世忠、张俊、王𤫉之徒是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222743_comment'></div>论其官则膺节钺之除，兼两镇之重，视执政之班，在韩琦、文彦博所不敢当者，其宠可谓极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222743_comment'></div>论其家则金帛充盈，所衣者锦衣，所食者玉食，奢豪无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222743_comment'></div>虽舆台厮养，皆得以功赏补官，至一军之中，使臣反多，卒伍反少，其志可谓骄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222743_comment'></div>平时飞扬跋扈，不循朝廷法度，所至焚掠驱掳，甚于敌人者，陛下不得而问也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222743_comment'></div>拥重兵，居閒处，邀犒设锡赉者，陛下不得而吝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222743_comment'></div>然天下之人犹谓陛下宽之至此者，防秋之时，责其死力耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222743_comment'></div>及敌人之来，是数人者曾不能为陛下施一镞之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222743_comment'></div>独张俊明州，仅能少抗，若更坚守数日，待敌再来，乘其机会，极力剿除，敌必终身惩创，不敢复南，此则俊忠于陛下也，其利害岂直为今日计哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222743_comment'></div>奈何敌未退数里间，遽狼狈引军而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222743_comment'></div>其引军而行也，虽三尺童子知其不可，以为寇性强愎，不婴其锋，犹惧屠戮，况已致怨而去，既不增兵益戍，反旋军空城以挑之，是前日至小之捷，乃莫大之祸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222743_comment'></div>未几，果残明州，无噍类，是杀明州一城生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222743_comment'></div>而陛下再有馆头之行者，张俊使之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222743_comment'></div>臣尝痛念自秋以来，陛下为宗社大计，惧敌人之侵，宵旰焦劳，未尝顷刻少安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222743_comment'></div>以建康、京口、九江，皆要害之地，当宿重兵，故以杜充守建康，韩世忠守京口，刘光世守九江，而以王𤫉隶杜充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222743_comment'></div>其措置非不尽善也，若敌骑渡江，杜充、韩世忠、王𤫉并力扼其前，刘光世掩其后，可使奔北之不暇。<div class='inline'
