id='poem_sentence_22_1222743_comment'></div>洎杜充力战于前，世忠、王𤫉卒不为用，刘光世亦偃然坐视，不出一兵，方与韩梠朝夕饮宴，敌至数十里间不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222743_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222743_comment'></div>诸将已负国家，罪恶如此，谓须少畏陛下之威，惮台谏之言，日夜惶恐，席藁负质，请罪有司，谢数州生灵之死，亦知尚有朝廷之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222743_comment'></div>而张俊方且以万人杀数十人之功，冒朝廷不赀之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222743_comment'></div>自明引军至温，道路鸡犬为之一空，居民闻来，奔逃山谷，数百里间，寂无人烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222743_comment'></div>王𤫉自信州入闽，所过州县，邀索动以千计，公然移文曰「无使枉害生灵」，其志果安在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222743_comment'></div>方国家危急之时，所恃者诸将，而诸将所为如此，不知何以立国，臣窃愤之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222743_comment'></div>此事人皆知之，而无为陛下言者，岂以为不急之务哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222743_comment'></div>以天步艰难，正借此曹为重，而不敢言耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222743_comment'></div>然臣窃有惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222743_comment'></div>臣闻王者所以得天下者，以得民也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222743_comment'></div>得民者，以得其心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222743_comment'></div>兹者陛下南巡，可谓播迁之极矣，而百姓尊君亲上之志略不少衰，岂非祖宗德泽结人之深，而恃陛下为之主耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222743_comment'></div>所谓为民主者，平日取民财力以养兵，缓急之时，排难解纷，而使民安业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222743_comment'></div>今诸将闻敌人之来，则望风遁逃，反汲汲内相攻残，以为民害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222743_comment'></div>车驾所过一路，则一路罹其灾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222743_comment'></div>所过一州一县，则一州一县罹其灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222743_comment'></div>今江淮、两浙已如此矣，万一幸湖湘、幸蜀，则敌人侵其前而无人以拒，官军残其后而无法以绳，是复为江淮、两浙无疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222743_comment'></div>古者天子所临曰「幸」，言所过，人以为幸也，岂今日之所谓哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222743_comment'></div>臣恐人心一离，而陛下无所恃也，持此将安归乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222743_comment'></div>臣又闻张俊离明之时，士卒颇有愿留击敌者，俊声言陛下召之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222743_comment'></div>臣知其说矣，陛下诸将，皆本无斗志，方无事时，例先取赴行在指挥，以备警急，警急则引去，曰「朝廷召我矣」，其实欲自遁，而又假上诏令以欺其欲战之人，使归非于上及用事之臣，此尤可罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222743_comment'></div>臣比至黄岩，闻陛下使李捧屯兵县中，降指麾云俟金人至台州，则前来温州，是诸将既欲遁，而陛下又令之使遁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222743_comment'></div>夫士，驱之使斗，犹惧不前，况令之使遁耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222743_comment'></div>然则敌人长驱无所忌惮者，适其宜耳，何足怪哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222743_comment'></div>臣窃观今日诸将，在古法皆当诛，然不可尽诛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222743_comment'></div>惟王𤫉本隶杜充，充败于前，而𤫉不救，此不可赦，当先斩𤫉以令天下，其他以次重行贬降，使以功赎过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222743_comment'></div>如张俊之军，独可赏其有功将士耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222743_comment'></div>所以移军辄遁者俊也，罪亦何逃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222743_comment'></div>如此，庶几国威少振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222743_comment'></div>昔周世宗承五代之衰，将士习为骄惰，河东之败，一日而斩大将樊爱能等三十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222743_comment'></div>然后东征西讨，无不如志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222743_comment'></div>白起于秦，可谓有功矣，一不受命，赐死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222743_comment'></div>杜邮、郭元振，唐之勋臣也，明皇怒军容不整，坐之纛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222743_comment'></div>盖威克厥爱允济，爱克厥威允罔功，是数君者，其知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222743_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222743_comment'></div>人之欲无穷，恩有时而既，惟吾威足以制之，然后恤焉，足以为恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222743_comment'></div>况此曹平时厌饫于掳掠之赀矣，用几何锡赉而能满其意哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222743_comment'></div>如有赏而无刑，是姑息之政耳，自古有能以姑息而成功者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222743_comment'></div>且汉高祖之兴，所将者韩信、黥布、彭越也，以今诸将之材视之，何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222743_comment'></div>所就者，布衣而取天下也，以今诸将之功视之，何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222743_comment'></div>然高祖于是数人者，欲王则王之，欲诛则诛之，曾不少贷，此其所以为高祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222743_comment'></div>故韩信曰：「陛下不善将兵，而善将将」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222743_comment'></div>岂非将将者，人主之职耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222743_comment'></div>今陛下当以将将为职，熟视诸将悍骄如此，而无以治之，异时张俊集西兵而来，则又靡靡相效成风矣，不知生灵何时息肩，国家何时兴复！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222743_comment'></div>以臣观之，今日之兵、今日之将，玩习至此，陛下已不得而用，已不得而制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222743_comment'></div>非特无以责其至诚徇国，所至人心震恐，动有意外之忧，有之不如无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222743_comment'></div>臣愚以为敌退之后，正朝廷大明赏罚、再立纪纲、新人耳目之时，莫若择有威望大臣一人，统摄诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222743_comment'></div>虽陛下亲军，亦听其节制，稍稍以法裁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222743_comment'></div>凡军辄敢擅移屯，以护驾为名者，主将将佐僚属并论如法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222743_comment'></div>仍使于偏裨中择人材可用者，间付以方面之权，待其有功，加以爵秩，阴为诸将之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222743_comment'></div>以天下之大，岂无数人将帅之材哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222743_comment'></div>特为诸将所抑而不得伸耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222743_comment'></div>若陛下驭诸将如臣所陈，则敌或尽数过江，或于建康、杭、越等州留兵占据，守亦有功，战亦有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222743_comment'></div>车驾回临安或平江，徐议所向，留江浙亦可，幸湖湘亦可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222743_comment'></div>如其不然，虽大臣忠贯白日，谋臣如雨，言利之臣能使钱流地上，何益于事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222743_comment'></div>譬御饥者当用食，舍食之外，皆非所急也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222743_comment'></div>已疾者当用医，舍医之外，皆非所急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222743_comment'></div>今日所急，在于驭兵驭将，其他皆非先务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222743_comment'></div>惟陛下与大臣熟议断而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222743_comment'></div>臣愚狂瞽，不知忌讳，罪当万死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222743_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_84_1222743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月</a>　在温州，高宗下诏亲征，巡幸浙西，汪藻有起居表。作品：车驾亲征起居表。<div id='poem_1222610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾亲征起居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222610")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222610'>万旅戒严，六飞巡狩，法成周之时迈，张大汉之天声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222610_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下诚贯神明，资兼智勇，合群英之策虑，兴中否之基图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222610_comment'></div>念问安犹隔于鸡鸣，岂拨乱得辞于马上？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222610_comment'></div>姑从简约，用示忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222610_comment'></div>臣方远阙庭，莫供牧圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222610_comment'></div>神戈所指，方令裴度以视师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222610_comment'></div>清跸之行，将获吕嘉而名县。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1222610_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222610'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷三。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷四，《宋四六选》卷五，《江右文钞》卷二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222610_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月</a>　在温州。吕颐浩罢尚书右仆射同中书门下平章事兼御营使，汪藻草制辞。作品：吕颐浩罢尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事御营使特授镇南军节度使开府仪同三司醴泉观使食邑食实封如故任便居住制。<div id='poem_1222430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕颐浩罢尚书左仆射同中书门下平章事御营使特授镇南军节度使开府仪同三司醴泉观使食邑食实封如故任便居住制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222430")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222430'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222430'>独化钧陶之上，尝首备于弼谐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222430_comment'></div>闵劳官职之烦，宜特加于崇奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222430_comment'></div>惟时上宰，实我元勋，兹祈解于近司，爰宠颁于殊渥，诞扬大号，敷告群工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222430_comment'></div>具官某心术疏通，性资明锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222430_comment'></div>运筹泉涌，独当天下之危机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222430_comment'></div>游刃风生，能断朝廷之大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222430_comment'></div>昨属艰难之运，尤输经济之忠，冒险直前，服勤无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222430_comment'></div>取虞渊之日，重正乾坤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222430_comment'></div>问襄野之涂，卒安社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222430_comment'></div>顾在廷之莫及，方当宁以仰成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222430_comment'></div>而寖怀偏见之私，殊失大臣之体，占吏员而有亏铨法，专兵柄而几废枢庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222430_comment'></div>下吴门之诏，则虑失于先时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222430_comment'></div>请浙右之行，则力违于众议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222430_comment'></div>既人言之荐至，于物望以靡谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222430_comment'></div>屡腾引去之章，莫副挽留之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222430_comment'></div>念有铭书之伟绩，难从策免之常规，乃峻彝章，务全体貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222430_comment'></div>植牙建纛，总节制于雄藩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222430_comment'></div>执璧面槐，视班联于上衮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222430_comment'></div>假以真祠之佚，从其私计之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222430_comment'></div>皆儒臣希有之荣，盖邦国久虚之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222430_comment'></div>朕为无歉，汝亦有终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222430_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222430_comment'></div>险夷一心，非忠诚孰能至此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222430_comment'></div>进退二道，惟明哲足以尽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222430_comment'></div>矧兼将相之崇，靡缺君臣之遇，毋云去位，不我告猷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1222430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222430'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷一二。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷九○，《建炎以来系年要录》卷三二，《宋宰辅编年录》卷一四，《宋四六选》卷三。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222430_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fe7763fae3be469eb91991eadd737670_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fe7763fae3be469eb91991eadd737670");'><span id='fe7763fae3be469eb91991eadd737670_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1134')">1131-1134年</a>，53-56岁</div><div id='fe7763fae3be469eb91991eadd737670' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月3日</a>　到湖州任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在湖州，作郭永传。<div id='poem_1222917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郭永传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222917")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222917'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222917'>郭永，大名府元城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222917_comment'></div>少刚明勇决，身长七尺，须髯郁然，望之如神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222917_comment'></div>以祖任为丹州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222917_comment'></div>守武人，为奸利无所忌，永数引法裁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222917_comment'></div>守大怒，盛威临永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222917_comment'></div>永不为动，则缪为好言荐之朝，永因尽忠以报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222917_comment'></div>后守欲变具狱，永力争不能得，袖举牒还之，拂衣去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222917_comment'></div>擢清河丞，寻知太原府大谷县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222917_comment'></div>太原帅率用重臣，每宴飨，费千金，苛取诸县以给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222917_comment'></div>大谷民富，其敛尤亟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222917_comment'></div>永以书抵幕府曰：「非什一而取，皆民膏血也，以资觞豆之费，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222917_comment'></div>脱不获命令，有投劾而归耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222917_comment'></div>府不敢迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222917_comment'></div>县有潭，出云雨，岁祷水旱为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222917_comment'></div>县祷未应，乘此哗民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222917_comment'></div>永杖巫身，暴日中，雨立至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222917_comment'></div>县人刻碑记其异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222917_comment'></div>府遣卒数辈，号警盗，刺诸县短长，游蠹不归，莫敢迕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222917_comment'></div>永械致之府，府为并他县追还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222917_comment'></div>于是府檄及部使者文移有不便于民者，必条利病反复，或遂寝而不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222917_comment'></div>客谓永世方雷同，毋以此贾祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222917_comment'></div>永曰：「吾知行吾志而已，遑恤其他」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222917_comment'></div>大谷人安其政，以为自有令来，无永比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222917_comment'></div>既去数年，复过之，则空一邑遮留，如永始去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222917_comment'></div>调东平府司录，府事无大小，决永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222917_comment'></div>吏有不能办者，私相靳曰：「尔非郭司录耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222917_comment'></div>除通判郑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222917_comment'></div>燕山之役，以永为其路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222917_comment'></div>郭药师屯边，怙恩暴甚，与民市不偿其直，复殴之，非坏目折支不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222917_comment'></div>安抚使王安中莫敢问，永白安中：「不治且难制，永请见而显责之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222917_comment'></div>不从则取其尤者磔之市，无辞也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222917_comment'></div>乃见药师曰：「朝廷负将军乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222917_comment'></div>药师惊曰：「何谓也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222917_comment'></div>永曰：「前日将军杖策归朝廷，上推赤心，置将军腹中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222917_comment'></div>客遇之日，无所不至，而将军未有尺寸功报上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222917_comment'></div>今方倚将军为重，乃纵部曲，戕民不禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222917_comment'></div>平居尚尔，如缓急何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222917_comment'></div>药师谢，无愧容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222917_comment'></div>永谓安中曰：「他日乱吾边者，必此辈也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222917_comment'></div>已而安中罢，永亦辞去，移河北西路提举常平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222917_comment'></div>会金人趋京师，所过城邑，欲立取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222917_comment'></div>是岁大寒，城池皆冰，敌率藉冰梯城，不攻而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222917_comment'></div>永适在大名，闻之，先弛壕渔之禁，人争出渔，冰不能合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222917_comment'></div>敌至城下，睥睨久之，叹息而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222917_comment'></div>迁河北东路提点刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222917_comment'></div>时车驾在维扬，命宗泽守京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222917_comment'></div>泽厉兵积粟，将复两河，以大名当冲要，檄永与帅桂充、漕臣张益谦相掎角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222917_comment'></div>永得檄大喜，即朝夕谋战守具，因结东平权邦彦为援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222917_comment'></div>不数日，声惊河朔，已没州县皆叛敌来归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222917_comment'></div>敌亦畏之，不敢动，远近宴然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222917_comment'></div>居无何，宗泽死，充守京师，以张益谦代之，而裴亿为转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222917_comment'></div>益谦、亿，龌龊小人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222917_comment'></div>会范琼胁邦彦南去，刘豫举济南来寇，大名块然孤城居其间，敌以十倍之师攻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222917_comment'></div>永率士昼夜乘城，伺间则出兵徂击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222917_comment'></div>或劝益谦委城遁者，永曰：「北门所以蔽遮梁、宋，敌得志则席捲而南，朝廷危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222917_comment'></div>借力不敌，犹当死守，徐挫其锋，待外援之至，奈何弃之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222917_comment'></div>因募士赍帛书，夜缒城出，告急朝廷，且请朝廷先为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222917_comment'></div>敌攻益急，俘东平、济南人大呼城下：二郡已降者富贵，不降无噍类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222917_comment'></div>益谦辈相顾色动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222917_comment'></div>永大言曰：「今日正吾侪尽节之时」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222917_comment'></div>又行城抚将士曰：「王师至矣，吾城坚完可守，汝曹努力，敌不足畏也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222917_comment'></div>众感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222917_comment'></div>质明大雾四塞，敌以车发断碑残础掷城中，楼橹皆坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222917_comment'></div>左右蒙盾而立，多碎首者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222917_comment'></div>良久城陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222917_comment'></div>永坐城楼上，或掖之以归，诸子环泣请去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222917_comment'></div>永曰：「吾世受国恩，当以死报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222917_comment'></div>然巢倾卵覆，汝辈亦何之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222917_comment'></div>兹命也，奚惧」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222917_comment'></div>益谦、亿率众迎降，敌曰：「城破始降，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222917_comment'></div>杂然以永不从为辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222917_comment'></div>敌遣骑召永，永正衣冠南向再拜讫，易幅巾而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222917_comment'></div>敌曰：「阻降者谁」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222917_comment'></div>永熟视久之，曰：「不降者我，尚奚问」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222917_comment'></div>敌见永状貌魁杰，且夙闻其贤，乃自为好语数十言，欲以富贵啖永而降之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222917_comment'></div>永嗔目唾骂曰：「无知丑类，恨不醢尔以报国家，何说降乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222917_comment'></div>敌令译者申谕不已，永戟手怒骂不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222917_comment'></div>敌讳其言，麾之使去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222917_comment'></div>永复厉声曰：「胡不速我死？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222917_comment'></div>我当率义鬼灭尔曹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222917_comment'></div>大名人在絷者，无不以手加额，为之出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222917_comment'></div>敌令断所举手，并其家害之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222917_comment'></div>时年五十三，建炎二年十一月甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222917_comment'></div>即日语传城中，虽素不与永合者，皆相向恸哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222917_comment'></div>敌去，相与负其尸瘗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222917_comment'></div>永博古通今，得钱即买书，家藏书万卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222917_comment'></div>因事为文，皆可录，而不求人知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222917_comment'></div>见古人立名节者，未尝不慨然掩卷终日，而尤慕颜鲁公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222917_comment'></div>为人喜面折人过，退无异言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222917_comment'></div>闻秋毫之善，必咨嗟奖成如不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222917_comment'></div>士友以此严惮而归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222917_comment'></div>杜充守大名，名称甚盛，永尝画数策见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222917_comment'></div>他日问其目，曰：「未暇读也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222917_comment'></div>永数充曰：「人有志而无才，好名而遗实，骄蹇自用而得名声，以当大任，鲜不颠沛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222917_comment'></div>公等足与治乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222917_comment'></div>充大惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222917_comment'></div>靖康冬，敌犯京师，中外阻绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222917_comment'></div>或以两宫北狩告永者，永号绝仆地，家人舁归，不食者数日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222917_comment'></div>闻元帅檄，始勉强一餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222917_comment'></div>其忠谊盖天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222917_comment'></div>若夫事亲孝，与人忠，轻财笃义，而于吏治精明，皆永馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222917_comment'></div>其大节如此，他不足为永道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222917_comment'></div>绍兴初，始赠永中大夫、资政殿学士，谥「勇节」，官其族数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222917_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_103_1222917'>赞曰：呜呼，靖康之祸，岂不哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222917_comment'></div>以二百年全盛之中国，而在位皆拘挛章句之徒，谓名节为非所急，士之精锐，销耎尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222917_comment'></div>一旦为敌所乘，无不全躯保妻子，奉头鼠窜，或甘心污辱之地而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222917_comment'></div>永以身徇国，至勉其家必死，非所谓烈丈夫而不为世所推移者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1222917_comment'></div>当是时，以节死者虽不为无人，若刘韐、李若水、向子韶、霍安国、张克戬、杨邦乂，皆其章章尤著者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1222917_comment'></div>然骂敌不屈，无如永者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1222917_comment'></div>故掇永平生行事著于篇，有以见永立大功名而奋不顾身者，有所从来，非偶然发也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_109_1222917_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月14日</a>　在湖州。高宗移跸临安府，汪藻上贺表。作品：车驾移跸临安府贺表。<div id='poem_1222608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾移跸临安府贺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年1月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222608")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222608'>涓日上春，移都近甸，用虞书东狩之礼，示魏阙西归之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222608_comment'></div>国步寖康，人心胥悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222608_comment'></div>窃以用永地于新邑，盘庚所以靖民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222608_comment'></div>会诸侯于东都，宣王由之复古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222608_comment'></div>不有真王，孰恢远图？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222608_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下清明在躬，彊勉行道，自寇戎之荐入，为宗社之深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222608_comment'></div>侧身修行，而志极于艰危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222608_comment'></div>菲食卑宫，而力图于兴复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222608_comment'></div>始游襄野，卒然虽假于问途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222608_comment'></div>旋驻岐山，从者有如于归市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222608_comment'></div>既天心之悔祸，宜宇内之休兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222608_comment'></div>将返旧京，先移清跸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222608_comment'></div>越涛江而北渡，御方岳以中居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222608_comment'></div>臣蚤扈时巡，适婴郡寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222608_comment'></div>入关建策，莫输戍卒之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222608_comment'></div>望日驰诚，徒喜长安之近。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1222608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年10月</a>　在湖州，迁左朝请大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年11月25日</a>　在湖州，上奏乞修元符至建炎以来诏旨。诏从之。作品：乞修日历状。贴黄。<div id='poem_1222753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞修日历状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年11月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222753")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222753'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222753'>臣昨待罪禁林，尝于经筵面奏，本朝实录自艰难以来，金匮石室之藏无复存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222753_comment'></div>伏观列圣自哲宗皇帝而上，皆有成书，流传人间，颇有其本，朝廷已访而藏之御府矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222753_comment'></div>若太上皇帝、渊圣皇帝及陛下建炎改元，至今三十馀年，并无日历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222753_comment'></div>乞诏有司纂述，未见施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222753_comment'></div>臣窃惟自古无国无史，史未尝一日无书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222753_comment'></div>晋谓之《乘》，楚谓之《梼杌》，鲁谓之《春秋》，以此见无国无史也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222753_comment'></div>《春秋》以事系日，以日系月，以月系时，以时系年，必四时具，谓之编年，以此见史未尝一日无书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222753_comment'></div>汉法，太史公位丞相上，天下计书先上太史公，副上丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222753_comment'></div>唐及本朝，宰相皆兼史官，其重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222753_comment'></div>故书榻前议论之辞，则有时政记；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222753_comment'></div>录柱下见闻之实，则有起居注；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222753_comment'></div>类而次之，谓之日历；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222753_comment'></div>修而成之，谓之实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222753_comment'></div>所以广记备言，垂一代之典也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222753_comment'></div>若旷三十年之久，漫无一字之传，将何以示来世乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222753_comment'></div>此其不可不纂述一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222753_comment'></div>韩宣子适鲁，见《易象》与《春秋》，曰：「周礼尽在鲁矣，吾今乃知周公之德与周之所以王」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222753_comment'></div>则国家守文者，不可无史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222753_comment'></div>萧何入秦，先收丞相、御史律令图书藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222753_comment'></div>沛公具知天下阸塞、户口多少强弱处、民所疾苦，以何得秦图书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222753_comment'></div>则国家创业者，不可无史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222753_comment'></div>今陛下躬受天命，虽名中兴，实兼创业守文之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222753_comment'></div>乃一代典章，残缺如此，恐于理未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222753_comment'></div>此其不可不纂述二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222753_comment'></div>恭惟太上皇帝聪明睿哲之资，孝友温恭之德，畴咨臣下，言必成文，裁决事机，动皆合道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222753_comment'></div>在位二十馀年，未尝刑一无罪，杀一不辜，涵养生灵，耕桑万里，视唐虞三代无不及焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222753_comment'></div>渊圣皇帝恭俭忧勤，招延听纳，虽登至尊之日浅，而膏泽浃于人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222753_comment'></div>止缘奸臣误朝，驯致遐狩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222753_comment'></div>今若无书纪实，恐千载之后，徒见一朝陵迟之祸亟，不知二圣积累之功深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222753_comment'></div>兹事非轻，群臣当任其责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222753_comment'></div>此其不可不纂述三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222753_comment'></div>自古史官，无所不录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222753_comment'></div>况三十年之间，朝廷之施设、豪杰之谋谟、政事之废兴、人材之进退、礼文之因革、法度之罢行、岁事之丰凶、羌戎之服叛，有本有末，有源有流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222753_comment'></div>一法弛而不书则一法熄，一事略而不载则一事隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222753_comment'></div>且当时群臣，间有在者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222753_comment'></div>以为忠贤耶，不著其素行，安知其可嘉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222753_comment'></div>以为邪佞耶，不条其宿奸，安知其可弃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222753_comment'></div>苟因散逸，遂废其书，岂孔子及阙文之义哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222753_comment'></div>此其不可不纂述四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222753_comment'></div>《公羊传》曰：「所见异辞，所闻异辞，所传闻异辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222753_comment'></div>孔子作《春秋》，于定、哀则其事详，隐、庄则其事略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222753_comment'></div>圣人犹尔，况其他乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222753_comment'></div>中原失平，三见闰矣，及今耳目相接，尚可追求，更数年间，事将湮没，虽有良史，莫知所凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222753_comment'></div>况比年风俗之衰，公论不立，士大夫取予皆出爱憎，因一事、为一人而著书行世者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222753_comment'></div>若不乘时订正，则数世之后，信以传信，疑以传疑，是非混淆，白黑颠倒，小人之说行而君子受其诬矣，可不惧哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222753_comment'></div>此其不可不纂述五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222753_comment'></div>臣政和中为著作佐郎，修太上皇帝日历，东观凡例，臣预闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222753_comment'></div>今所领州，又幸经兵火之馀，独不残燬，视诸故府，案牍具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222753_comment'></div>如御笔手诏、赏功罚罪之文，尚班班可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222753_comment'></div>失今不辑，臣实惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222753_comment'></div>古之有国家者，虽颠沛中史官不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222753_comment'></div>况今边烽稍息，群盗屏除，正朝廷蒐讨补阙之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222753_comment'></div>伏望睿慈许臣郡政之馀，将本州所有御笔手诏、赏功罚罪文字，截自元符庚辰至建炎己酉三十年间，分年编类，仍量给官钱，市纸劄、募书工之类，缮写进呈，以备修日历官采择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222753_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1222753'>〔贴黄〕臣契勘御笔手诏、赏功罚罪文字，但见当时所颁命令，若除受差遣黜陟，与臣僚出处始终，则有所授告劄或家集行状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222753_comment'></div>今湖州土著及流寓士大夫家未尝被兵，藏书具在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222753_comment'></div>如陛下从臣纂集，乞并赐移文，于逐家取上件文字，录讫付还，庶几粗成编帙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222753_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1222753_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　在湖州，汪藻奉旨修诏旨后，吕颐浩有《与汪彦章书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　在湖州，春夏间，有诗与程瑀唱和。作品：题伯禹给事漫吾亭。<div id='poem_528259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528259?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题伯禹给事漫吾亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528259")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528259'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528259'>人生天地间，同一幻泡影。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528259'>偶然相值过，便有人与境。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528259'>那知两皆漫，直寄弹指顷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528259'>古来贤达士，物我均土梗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528259'>程侯东南俊，少日忠义秉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528259'>周旋正色地，四海惮严冷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528259'>立朝二十年，愤世欲生瘿。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528259'>班虽近日月，志则在箕颍。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528259'>中年拂衣归，绝意向钟鼎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528259'>泽幽成小筑，胜会已独领。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528259'>清寒挹湍濑，秀色揽诸岭。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528259'>聊将不羁身，对此无阏景。<div id='poem_sentence_11_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_528259'>回首浯溪老，便觉加数等。<div id='poem_sentence_12_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_528259'>从渠春风颠，那得到古井。<div id='poem_sentence_13_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_528259'>高词出胸臆，妙处如灌顶。<div id='poem_sentence_14_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_528259'>读罢眷樊笼，悠然发深省。<div id='poem_sentence_15_528259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_528259'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_528259_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　守湖州期间，因和籴米数不足，上书自劾。诏不问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　守湖州期间，得二禅老慧林、居慧，使分居道场、何山二山。有记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　守湖州期间，作庄徽墓志铭。作品：徽猷阁待制致仕赠少师谥僖庄公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽猷阁待制致仕赠少师谥僖简庄公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222935")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222935'>宣和二年九月壬寅，通奉大夫、徽猷阁待制致仕庄公卒于常州宜兴县之里第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222935_comment'></div>讣闻，天子嗟悼，诏赠光禄大夫，赙之加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222935_comment'></div>越明年八月某甲子，诸孤奉公葬其县西南三十里厚山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222935_comment'></div>既葬，太常上其状，尚书谥曰「僖简」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222935_comment'></div>又十馀年，其子左朝请大夫安常有秩于朝，累赠公为少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222935_comment'></div>于是安常与其宗老谋曰：「惟我公以经术起家，显于朝廷，尊为士大夫，寿与祉并，官至二品，殁而墓碑未刻，其何以饬来裔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222935_comment'></div>盍求能言者显书之，以垂无穷，而宠绥庄氏之祧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222935_comment'></div>乃使来请，藻辞不获命，则叙公族出官爵，与夫平生之行治而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222935_comment'></div>君讳徽，字君猷，世家扬州之江都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222935_comment'></div>曾祖馀庆、祖允明，皆居乡，称善人长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222935_comment'></div>父询，始南渡，徙居于宜兴，以公贵赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222935_comment'></div>通议卒时，有子四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222935_comment'></div>夫人某氏，贤躬门户，而纵诸子于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222935_comment'></div>由是公兄弟三人同时荐于有司，至礼部，独第公文为高等，中元丰二年进士乙科，解褐调主江宁之上元簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222935_comment'></div>王文公居金陵，四方英隽阗门，公一与之交，而非其人未尝往，繇是名声日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222935_comment'></div>授安州安陆县令，县多彊宗大姓，以侵渔闾里为能，令不之从，则持其短长以逞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222935_comment'></div>公至，一切以法裁之，诸豪皆怒，合为飞语撼公，公不为变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222935_comment'></div>既久，知其不可幸而肆也，皆靡然而服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222935_comment'></div>蔡公确以故相守安，遇僚属简严，无许可者，独期公远大而首荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222935_comment'></div>改宣德郎、知单州砀山县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222935_comment'></div>砀山在穷谷中，地偏民野，公怜其陋而以静治之，至阅旬无一人讼于庭者，与诸生终日谈经义而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222935_comment'></div>蒋公之奇尹京，辟右军巡判官，以非其官不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222935_comment'></div>无何，章丞相惇荐公于上，召对，擢提举秦凤路常平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222935_comment'></div>遭成夫人忧，免丧除提举广南西路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222935_comment'></div>象山令郑子渊，妄人也，姗常平新法，连以书抵公，有言及宗庙者，公不敢隐而以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222935_comment'></div>上曰：「远方使者能然，兹得人矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222935_comment'></div>命中书记其名，擢尚书司封员外郎，寻移金部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222935_comment'></div>上以承平久，曹多诿吏，吏缘为奸，诏左右司取诸郎勤惰各一人殿最之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222935_comment'></div>于是司金号为冗剧，公课居优，进官一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222935_comment'></div>力求补外，得提点河北西路刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222935_comment'></div>真定府判官刘曾录人阴私，为不法，至郡守监司无敢按之，公悉条具奸赃上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222935_comment'></div>曾令其子白冤，诏遣台臣就鞫，无一不如公言者，即抵曾罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222935_comment'></div>一路闻之懔然，或望风投劾而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222935_comment'></div>入为尚书度支员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222935_comment'></div>未几，除司农少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222935_comment'></div>复求补外，除江南西路转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222935_comment'></div>未行，移两浙路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222935_comment'></div>公领漕事四年，馈饷为东南之最，褒赏沓至，赐紫衣金鱼，进官者再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222935_comment'></div>明年，除直秘阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222935_comment'></div>又明年，除太府卿，遂除徽猷阁待制、知兴仁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222935_comment'></div>兴仁为辅郡，四方之戍，杂居而屯，颇悍骄难制，前为守者，惴惴然常有意外之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222935_comment'></div>公以拊摩弹压之术，时其缓急而兼用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222935_comment'></div>会偏裨刻其军，声言将为乱，阖城凶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222935_comment'></div>公钩得其情，取为首者二人治之，馀置不问，谈笑而定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222935_comment'></div>徙知平江府，郡豪朱勔挟宠张甚，视州县蔑如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222935_comment'></div>且中贵人缘勔而使者，冠盖相望，皆能祸福人于牙颊间，官吏无不倾身事之，至郡守亦有出其门者，独公不少贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222935_comment'></div>勔辈虽惮公之正，不敢谗，而讫公去，赏亦不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222935_comment'></div>方勔盛时，造乘舆服御之珍，设官于浙西诸郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222935_comment'></div>一日，上知其奸利，诏守臣悉罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222935_comment'></div>令下，郡人欢呼，而旁郡方迁延幸其必复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222935_comment'></div>公曰：「此天子盛德事也，人臣当奉承之不暇，乃顾望乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222935_comment'></div>即日结罢如诏旨，识者皆叹以为不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222935_comment'></div>留平江六年，丐閒，优诏不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222935_comment'></div>久之，除提举杭州洞霄宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222935_comment'></div>公虽七十馀，而彊健敷腴，如五六十许人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222935_comment'></div>人谓公且复起，副明天子所以委任之意，而公已翛然忘世，敕诸子勿以家事相关，筑大第荆溪之上，时从宾客倘徉溪山之间而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222935_comment'></div>以通奉大夫、徽猷阁待制致仕，得年七十八而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222935_comment'></div>娶吴氏，京口大族，有贤行，封越国夫人，先公十一年卒，祔公而葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222935_comment'></div>三男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222935_comment'></div>伯曰志行，季曰安上，皆以公任为从事郎，亦先后公数年而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222935_comment'></div>仲曰安常，擢进士第，为太常博士，历持节分符之选，今为左朝请大夫、主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222935_comment'></div>三女，长适左朝散大夫、尚书左司员外郎王冈，次适右承议郎、通判太原府方笈，次适左朝奉大夫、尚书吏部员外郎董将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222935_comment'></div>孙男女合十四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222935_comment'></div>公敦厚高明，遇人无亲疏贵贱贤不肖，一本于诚，委曲周旋，惟恐其不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222935_comment'></div>及于义当为，则其守确然，虽祸福在前，莫能为之摇夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222935_comment'></div>其使秦凤也，成夫人以远不能行，公朝夕慕怀，至忘食事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222935_comment'></div>洎执丧，癯瘁骨立，筑室冢旁，终丧而后归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222935_comment'></div>晚年得君，褒擢无虚岁，然居中则请外，居外则请閒，淹速未尝置于胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222935_comment'></div>平生无嗜好，所至左右图史，帘阁萧然，故历官四十馀年，无秋毫之累，以令名始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222935_comment'></div>少喜释氏书，晚而弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222935_comment'></div>疾革，呼子孙甥妷至前，人与之诀，无一语之乱，非有得于中者，能如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222935_comment'></div>呜呼，其贤于人远矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222935_comment'></div>藻，公妷婿也，得公之详，固无如藻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222935_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1222935'>在元丰世，英材毕臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222935_comment'></div>数十年间，国为有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222935_comment'></div>以经术进，公当是时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222935_comment'></div>圣考遗我，帝其用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222935_comment'></div>用公伊何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222935_comment'></div>维德敦厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222935_comment'></div>学为人师，材则多有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222935_comment'></div>出入四纪，绩皆可书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222935_comment'></div>儒雅饰吏，盖公之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222935_comment'></div>遂升迩联，出殿藩服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222935_comment'></div>惟皇懋功，非我求福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222935_comment'></div>终始一意，诚于事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222935_comment'></div>视富与贵，乃如浮云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222935_comment'></div>浩然而归，说此眉寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222935_comment'></div>蝉联未央，公且有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222935_comment'></div>松槚岑蔚，与家相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222935_comment'></div>尚千万年，记公之藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_89_1222935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年2月1日</a>　在湖州，郡人左朝请郎通判无为军颜经投匦诉汪藻敷籴军粮，有司查证不实。遂贬颜经二秩、停官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年3月5日</a>　在湖州，朝廷从汪藻之请，赐湖州颜真卿庙号曰“忠烈”作品：湖州奏乞修鲁公祠并赐额状。<div id='poem_1222754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州奏乞修鲁公祠并赐额状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年3月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222754")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222754'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222754'>伏见本州城东能仁院，有唐颜真卿祠堂一所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222754_comment'></div>谨按石刻，真卿以大历七年自抚州除湖州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222754_comment'></div>逮今四百馀年，州人奉祠不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222754_comment'></div>前此为湖州刺史者多矣，而此州独拳拳于真卿者，岂非以忠义感人有不能忘者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222754_comment'></div>自艰难以来，州县官吏日以军兴为忧，如真卿之祠，见为不急，栋宇倾仆，将就泯灭，臣实惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222754_comment'></div>窃谓方今多事之时，所以昭劝群伦者，忠义为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222754_comment'></div>而名节暴白，莫如真卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222754_comment'></div>昔章圣皇帝东巡，嘉张巡、许远之节，至亲幸其祠，所以旌异代之忠，示将来之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222754_comment'></div>真卿风烈，诚不在巡、远之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222754_comment'></div>幸车驾驻跸临安，真卿之祠适在旁郡，若不特加崇奖，恐无以慰邦人之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222754_comment'></div>欲望圣慈量给度牒十馀道，付臣市材葺治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222754_comment'></div>显遗直之魂，激懦夫之气，诚非小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222754_comment'></div>如蒙俞允，仍乞赐一敕额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222754_comment'></div>伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1222754_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年4月17日</a>　在湖州，上书请录故太师文彦博之孙纬世等三人为官。朝廷从其请。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1133&endYear=1133')">1133年</a>　在湖州，作蒋猷墓志铭。作品：徽猷阁直学士左宣奉大夫致仕赠特进显谟阁直学士蒋公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽猷阁直学士左宣奉大夫致仕赠特进显谟阁直学士蒋公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴三年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1133年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222950")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222950'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222950'>祖宗以来，天子与大臣论天下事，命台谏相应以义理之文，故百馀年间，朝廷清明，天下无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222950_comment'></div>熙宁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222950_comment'></div>大臣有欲更祖宗法者，恶士大夫言人人殊，始指公论为流俗，由是名节不竞三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222950_comment'></div>至政和、宣和，而天下以言为讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222950_comment'></div>当是时，丹阳蒋公兴诸生，任中执法，独信其所学，为天子辨是非，屡击权臣，皆言人所难言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222950_comment'></div>天子每改容嘉纳，许其忠精，然后天下知忠言未尝不用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222950_comment'></div>顾风俗之衰，士乐缄嘿，谓吾君不能耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222950_comment'></div>公虽以直道逡巡去国，卒老于行，不至辅相，然至今论宣和贤者，必曰蒋公云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222950_comment'></div>公讳猷，字仲远，姓蒋氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222950_comment'></div>东汉时有封义兴𠙶亭者，其后分居丹阳金坛，故公为金坛人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222950_comment'></div>曾祖郢、祖益，皆隐居不求仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222950_comment'></div>父师锡，慷慨有大节，以公故赠光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222950_comment'></div>公幼庄重如成人，力学而敏，群诸生试有司，必处其上，诸老生皆器之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222950_comment'></div>甫冠，中元丰八年进士科，调主武进簿，移巴陵令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222950_comment'></div>县介湖湘，俗习文法，喜斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222950_comment'></div>公初至，讼坌入，老吏以公年少易之，公听决如流，皆叩头服，豪右屏迹，政声流闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222950_comment'></div>改宣德郎、知江宁县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222950_comment'></div>课最，部使者以闻，迁秩一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222950_comment'></div>崇宁初，诏天下兴学，以公为信州教授，寻除监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222950_comment'></div>丁光禄忧，服除为尚书膳部员外郎，迁吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222950_comment'></div>宗子学建，除宗正少卿，兼学制参详官，改太常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222950_comment'></div>时诏原庙立僖祖殿，工既毕，言者以为当废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222950_comment'></div>朝廷下其议，公言有「其举之，莫之敢废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222950_comment'></div>今既奉安祭告矣，奈何毁之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222950_comment'></div>执政怒，送吏部，差通判南安军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222950_comment'></div>逾年，直前议，复故职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222950_comment'></div>召试中书舍人，词令一新，为学者法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222950_comment'></div>坐邓洵仁夺职不论，黜知庐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222950_comment'></div>俄除集贤殿修撰，复拜中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222950_comment'></div>召还，既对，上曰：「卿国之老成，朕未尝忘卿也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222950_comment'></div>拜御史中丞，兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222950_comment'></div>公力辞不可，则首论士风浮薄，「今群臣无他能，惟以善候伺人主，承望大臣为向背者，谓之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222950_comment'></div>其或耿介特立，守正不回，则众指为愚而非笑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222950_comment'></div>此风大不可长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222950_comment'></div>且大臣当辅佐天子，今奏事殿中，惟务雷同，略无可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222950_comment'></div>其欲稍自异者，不过退有后言，为中伤计，此不可不察」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222950_comment'></div>又言：「臣近因陪祠禁中，见路寝尚仍祖宗之旧，瓦木涂塈皆故暗，有以见陛下薄于自奉，与土阶卑宫室何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222950_comment'></div>愿推广圣心每如此，以保盈成」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222950_comment'></div>上嘉纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222950_comment'></div>在京百司，自元丰皆隶六察，崇宁中，内侍省独乞不隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222950_comment'></div>公论其非，上曰：「既名有司，不隶察何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222950_comment'></div>即以公言正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222950_comment'></div>寻察内侍省数事以闻，上寝其奏，公极论曰：「臣观古之人君，于近习有功不滥赏，有罪不废法者，皆载之信史，号为贤明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222950_comment'></div>臣职在执法，不敢缄默，以负陛下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222950_comment'></div>于是内侍刘友端等皆降官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222950_comment'></div>因命大书公疏，揭之内侍省，其徒皆侧目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222950_comment'></div>杨戬建节，公言：「祖宗时未尝有此，昨童贯首隳旧制，当时士论已不平」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222950_comment'></div>帝曰：「有非常之功，则有非常之赏，童贯有战功多，不可以人而废」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222950_comment'></div>公徐曰：「杨戬何功」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222950_comment'></div>帝曰：「自朕即位以来，制作礼乐皆其手，亦非小劳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222950_comment'></div>公曰：「事塞其源，则人无觖望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222950_comment'></div>若夫攀缘辗转，人人有意外之得，则所谓非常者，反为常矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222950_comment'></div>帝称善者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222950_comment'></div>公因言：「元丰时有选人兴水利，王安石欲改京官者，神考止令循资，于爵赏较秋毫如此，况节钺乎」」帝曰：「官爵得之易则名器卑，诚如卿言，然杨戬之命已行，当为卿杜来者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222950_comment'></div>因诏三省、御史台，当遵守弹劾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222950_comment'></div>时三省吏迁官类至四品，又近倖率请建坟寺，及彊市民居建第，公悉论之，即降诏禁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222950_comment'></div>赵良嗣献平燕书，除秘书丞，公言良嗣降敌狂妄，不宜出入禁中，后良嗣果败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222950_comment'></div>真州守贰更告讦，付公治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222950_comment'></div>守李釜雅为时宰所恶，而贰陈求道者，宰相蔡氏族婿也，帝怒甚，釜且不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222950_comment'></div>公平心处决，釜以不冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222950_comment'></div>都水使者孟昌龄议河事，久不成，费以亿万计，公私骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222950_comment'></div>公言是役有必不可成之理，愿循元丰开修二股河故事，于从臣中选忠信可托者往视，可罢罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222950_comment'></div>因言：「自陛下即位，大河轨道，何以更为劳民费财，徇虚名，亏实效，臣窃未喻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222950_comment'></div>上因震怒，曰：「朝廷事类如此，无事辄纷更，卿于台属中遣人往，具以实言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222950_comment'></div>已而为大臣沮格，识者恨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222950_comment'></div>范之才奉使淮南，还言滁水有鼎可出，诏之才求之，无所得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222950_comment'></div>惧辞窃且得罪，即督州县，发民畎水凿山，役不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222950_comment'></div>公劾之才狂妄希进，并论其出使奸利状，上大怒，投之才千里外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222950_comment'></div>公既感上知遇，遂言东南应奉且十年，如花石器用之物，输内府、入权倖之家，不为不足，殚财力，事浮靡，愿一切罢之，其言反覆深切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222950_comment'></div>因论提举两浙常平徐铸以籴本钱畀漕司制造，广东转运使徐惕以虚名羡财进奉后苑兴作，乞重寘之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222950_comment'></div>帝不从，公卧家待罪，诏起之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222950_comment'></div>因力请罢，迁兵部尚书，兼礼制局详议官，知政和七年贡举，改工部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222950_comment'></div>月馀，迁吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222950_comment'></div>吏部四选，事素繁猥，其长率怠于省治，吏得缘兹为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222950_comment'></div>公晨入坐曹，使人得自言，躬阅所诉，参稽律令可否，立疏于籍，第而行之，事以无壅，铨曹为清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222950_comment'></div>宣和二年，言者论公兼官众而事有不举者，罢吏部尚书，以徽猷阁直学士知婺州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222950_comment'></div>请投閒，改提举南京鸿庆宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222950_comment'></div>宣和四年，起知明州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222950_comment'></div>以不乐应奉事，到官数日，复请奉祠而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222950_comment'></div>七年，以刑部尚书召，兼资善堂翊善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222950_comment'></div>公再至京师，顾同列皆新进少年，益不合，日求去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222950_comment'></div>会敌骑至京师，天子内禅，上皇东巡，公率同列上章乞迁避，不从，则躬乘城昼夜守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222950_comment'></div>既解严，天子命公持表候上皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222950_comment'></div>时童贯总兵扈从，有自疑心，渊圣皇帝贬贯环卫，窜池州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222950_comment'></div>因命公持诏往，曰：「使贯退听而毋伤上皇之心，卿何以处之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222950_comment'></div>公顿首曰：「愿陛下付臣，勿以为虑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222950_comment'></div>渊圣皇帝喜，赐缣帛茗药遣行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222950_comment'></div>公及上皇于淮阴，言国事泣下，上皇亦泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222950_comment'></div>因请间言：「童贯得罪天下，今朝廷正典刑，惟陛下财幸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222950_comment'></div>上皇颔之，遂宣诏童贯即日趋贬所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222950_comment'></div>公侍上皇还京师，迁兵部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222950_comment'></div>靖康元年，复请閒，以徽猷阁直学士提举西京嵩山崇福宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222950_comment'></div>建炎三年，避兵明州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222950_comment'></div>明年属疾，上章请老，迁宣奉大夫致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222950_comment'></div>十一月某甲子，卒于昌国县蓬莱乡，春秋六十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222950_comment'></div>遗奏闻，上嗟悼，赠特进、显谟阁直学士，下所属给葬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222950_comment'></div>夫人刘氏，尚书祠部郎中淑之女，有贤行，后公二年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222950_comment'></div>二男子：曰谟，右承议郎、知封州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222950_comment'></div>曰该，右承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222950_comment'></div>三女子，长适右从政郎、龙游丞吴恢，次适右从事郎、惠安尉王悦，次尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222950_comment'></div>孙四人：台卿，右承事郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222950_comment'></div>和卿、冲卿、元卿，右承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222950_comment'></div>公资浑厚寡言笑，对家人终日如宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222950_comment'></div>平生未尝以游辞伪色借人，矫情降意徼利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222950_comment'></div>其论事上前，不为苟合，虽人主盛怒，少间复前，反覆开陈，必尽理而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222950_comment'></div>其论荐皆一时名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222950_comment'></div>平居无嗜好，未尝一日废书不观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1222950_comment'></div>有文集二十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1222950_comment'></div>其为文一本经术，无益于时者未尝言，精深简古，似其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1222950_comment'></div>以绍兴三年二月十九日，葬公明州鄞县翔凤乡隐学山之东冈，以淑人刘祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1222950_comment'></div>以左朝散郎许德之之状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1222950_comment'></div>藻尝谓名节与功利若权衡然，常相为轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1222950_comment'></div>士君子一志于功利，则名节衰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1222950_comment'></div>此岂待事至而后择哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1222950_comment'></div>必有早正素定、不与世推移者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1222950_comment'></div>方公在朝廷时，搢绅未尝有言名节者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1222950_comment'></div>公屹然特立，专以启迪人主为心，撄逆鳞、批大郤，闻者为寒心失色，而公谆谆尽言不已，不啻如父子间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1222950_comment'></div>洎岁晚困踬，一时辈流越官簿而升者踵相蹑，或以是尤公，公笑曰：「吾道犹是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1222950_comment'></div>卒未尝少贬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1222950_comment'></div>则公之所立，岂偶然者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1222950_comment'></div>藻服膺公门，知公为最详实，诸孤又以礼请，敢不叙而铭诸？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1222950_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_121_1222950'>君道主听，受言孔艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1222950_comment'></div>臣有周比，兴衰所关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1222950_comment'></div>在昔祖宗，政以言订。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1222950_comment'></div>一人垂衣，万事龟镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1222950_comment'></div>厥后靡靡，人因世移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1222950_comment'></div>安得刚者，吾其与归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1222950_comment'></div>堂堂蒋公，古之遗直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1222950_comment'></div>德为凤麟，心则金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1222950_comment'></div>见义而作，直言靡思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1222950_comment'></div>观者为栗，未尝少卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1222950_comment'></div>坐兹寡谐，材不极用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1222950_comment'></div>至今善人，徒得君重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1222950_comment'></div>国步中柅，间关异州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1222950_comment'></div>不在其位，莫如我忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1222950_comment'></div>阖棺海山，因窆其域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1222950_comment'></div>后人怀公，视此铭刻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_136_1222950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在湖州，年初，友人刘滂抵建昌军任，与汪藻书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年3月23日</a>　在湖州，上所编元符庚辰以来诏旨二百卷。诏送史馆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年3月25日</a>　在湖州，朝廷以汪藻和籴数多，进秩一等。辞不受。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年5月8日</a>　在湖州，綦崇礼奏请以彦章所编诏旨至修国史日历所，不必别设外局。诏从之。汪藻编修元符至建炎诏旨事自此时起停顿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月3日</a>　在湖州，友人知建昌军刘滂因军乱被杀害。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月14日</a>　在湖州，又上所编建炎诏旨三十七册。诏送史馆。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
临川
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fc50315d3b4449f7b55864b9c1135670_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fc50315d3b4449f7b55864b9c1135670");'><span id='fc50315d3b4449f7b55864b9c1135670_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1135')">1134-1135年</a>，56-57岁</div><div id='fc50315d3b4449f7b55864b9c1135670' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月22日</a>　移知抚州。上到任谢表。作品：谢抚州到任表。<div id='poem_1222669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢抚州到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年9月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222669")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222669'>吏最无闻，宜从黜典：戍期未毕，转畀名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222669_comment'></div>蒙拔擢之过优，惧颠隮之益速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222669_comment'></div>严程及境，涓月班春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222669_comment'></div>伏念臣蚤窃儒科，晚陪法从，久污禁林之直，寖膺州绂之除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222669_comment'></div>去国三年，长望蓬莱之气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222669_comment'></div>移官千里，遥瞻牛斗之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222669_comment'></div>矧江介之奥区，实里门之邻壤，熟知风俗，当省教条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222669_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下运属丕承，志期光复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222669_comment'></div>采薇遣戍，何昆夷、猃狁之足忧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222669_comment'></div>细柳劳军，知李牧、廉颇之可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222669_comment'></div>凡在照临之域，举怀驰骛之忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222669_comment'></div>而臣投老无堪，冒恩最甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222669_comment'></div>虽一收朝迹，无复脩门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222669_comment'></div>然两剖守符，皆非凋郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222669_comment'></div>方圣主躬巡于侯甸，宜群臣皆备于戎行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222669_comment'></div>乃从简书，莫捍牧圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222669_comment'></div>惟州县异承平之日，尤在恤民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222669_comment'></div>使里闾无愁叹之声，是为报国。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1222669_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在抚州。曾几有诗贺其守临川，汪藻和之。作品：移守临川曾吉甫以诗见寄次韵答之时吉甫除闽漕未行。<div id='poem_528391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>移守临川曾吉甫以诗见寄次韵答之时吉甫除闽漕未行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528391")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528391'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528391'>朝来剥啄叩门谁，昨夜灯花已报知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528391'>腰下方悬新守印，眼中已见故人诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528391'>十年且喜朋簪合，千里休言官牒随。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528391'>问我抽书何日竟，病来编简网蛛丝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528391'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在抚州，有启致韩驹，达敬慕之意。作品：知抚州回韩驹待制启。<div id='poem_1222810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知抚州回韩驹待制启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222810")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222810'>窃以服膺有日，识面无繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222810_comment'></div>技拙汗流，昔固惭于巧匠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222810_comment'></div>年衰气索，今复见于大巫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222810_comment'></div>未居千骑之上头，已拜双鱼之尺素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222810_comment'></div>何爱怜之及此，欲比数而收之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222810_comment'></div>恭惟宫使待制学洞古今，名垂宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222810_comment'></div>风流自命，欣如晦之得君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222810_comment'></div>谈笑多闻，恨平津之未相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222810_comment'></div>承作者百年之师友，为斯文一代之统盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222810_comment'></div>何幸馀生，获陪胜会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222810_comment'></div>载酒而问奇字，将每过于扬雄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222810_comment'></div>登楼而赋销忧，愿少留于王粲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222810_comment'></div>徂岁无几，端居有休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222810_comment'></div>愿遵六气以保调，用慰四方之倾慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222810_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1222810_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年12月</a>　在抚州，作吴懋墓志铭。作品：朝请大夫直秘阁致仕吴君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222930' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222930' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222930?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝请大夫直秘閤致仕吴君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222930")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222930_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222930'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222930'>君讳懋，字禹功，姓吴氏，其先义兴阳羡人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222930_comment'></div>世以儒名家，而不求仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222930_comment'></div>至君之父诰，始光大其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222930_comment'></div>有三子，皆授以经，其材竞爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222930_comment'></div>伯仲同时擢进士第，又同时为县令，以治行闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222930_comment'></div>士大夫言义方者，予吴氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222930_comment'></div>伯曰愈，仲即君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222930_comment'></div>诰卒，龟山先生杨时识其墓，后以君宦达，赠朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222930_comment'></div>君少有立志，风骨颀秀，望之嶷然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222930_comment'></div>尝与儿曹集外家，有以博具遗君者，君正色叱之曰：「死老奴，敢污我耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222930_comment'></div>坐客大惊，知吴氏有子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222930_comment'></div>及长，嗜学问，从先生长者游如不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222930_comment'></div>入太学，籍籍有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222930_comment'></div>既擢第，调当涂县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222930_comment'></div>时郭祥正、李之仪会当涂，皆知名士也，负才气轩轾人，不少借，一见君诗文，曰「我辈人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222930_comment'></div>会岁饥，官出粟，籴者万人，坌集于场，他吏无术，至相蹂践以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222930_comment'></div>州以命君，君布灰于地而疏其行坐，彊者东，弱者西，以五十人为甲，使听令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222930_comment'></div>间指其一曰：「给彼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222930_comment'></div>民趋而前，左受粟而右输金，各以序进，未晡而周，无一人哗者，当路交荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222930_comment'></div>县有圩田，民生理寓江，中秋大雨，圩且决，君朝夕暴露治其防，民赖以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222930_comment'></div>既去，父老指防而叹曰：「微此，吾其鱼乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222930_comment'></div>移宿松令，以简静为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222930_comment'></div>凡追逮，书县门而予之期，民信畏之，其至不差晷刻，田里间未尝识游徼啬夫之面也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222930_comment'></div>由是讼更十数令不能决者，皆立谈决之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222930_comment'></div>未几，宿松大治，门不夜阖，狱囚屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222930_comment'></div>一日，部使者按旁郡，民遮道言愿以事决宿松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222930_comment'></div>使者曰：「县各有治，汝舍汝令而从他令，岂有说乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222930_comment'></div>且道远奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222930_comment'></div>民叩头曰：「吾邑可否，视吏色辞，彼邑有令在堂，吏不能秋毫欺也，虽远奚惮」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222930_comment'></div>察访使赵默、舒州守孙杰驭下如束湿，所至人重足事之，盛威临君，君不为动，然此两人者亦卒不能使君屈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222930_comment'></div>用荐，改宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222930_comment'></div>丁外艰，服除知庐江县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222930_comment'></div>盗刘五囊橐庐、寿间，方鼓行出山，去县裁一驿，其锋锐甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222930_comment'></div>或止君毋遽行，君笑曰：「男儿当斩贼平戎，此鼠辈何为者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222930_comment'></div>今行缚之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222930_comment'></div>盗闻君来，不敢入其境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222930_comment'></div>后群盗得，吏疑独遗庐江，曰：「彼有人焉，不可图也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222930_comment'></div>召监延丰仓、知扶沟、长垣县，寻除诸王府记室兼讲书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222930_comment'></div>渊圣皇帝受内禅，金人至京师，三上书言便宜，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222930_comment'></div>后皆施行，略如君策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222930_comment'></div>入尚书为礼部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222930_comment'></div>会金人立张邦昌，法当郎草笺奏，君度不可拒，将引绳自裁，有倖非常者儳曰：「仆请为之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222930_comment'></div>君由是获免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222930_comment'></div>已而王时雍用事，坐政事堂，君发愤骂时雍曰：「反贼，吾独不能击汝如段秀实耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222930_comment'></div>时雍面颈发赤，不能对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222930_comment'></div>君因以疾求罢，不听，遂称笃病于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222930_comment'></div>今上即位，病即日愈，乃请老而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222930_comment'></div>岁馀，起公复故官，寻除司农少卿，不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222930_comment'></div>近臣交荐，擢知明州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222930_comment'></div>州承喋血馀，守将屡易，公私埽地，万目睢盱，君一调而细大咸举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222930_comment'></div>于是卫兵留戍者步军三万，陈思恭领之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222930_comment'></div>水军万艘，张公裕领之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222930_comment'></div>将騃卒骄，凌藉官府，求取无度，变生不可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222930_comment'></div>君能得榷酟之赢，给其稍廪，岁终赡足，民不知兵，治声流闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222930_comment'></div>加直秘阁，以代归，坐小法贬秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222930_comment'></div>朝廷察其枉，擢荆湖北路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222930_comment'></div>未行，改知吉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222930_comment'></div>道得病，到官病益侵，即上还印绶，六日卒，年五十五，寔绍兴四年五月某甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222930_comment'></div>积官至朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222930_comment'></div>其迁多以劳能，而不以岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222930_comment'></div>君气豪语直，遇事有不可，辄愤盈于中，虽贵人必斥其忌讳面折之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222930_comment'></div>然胸次实洞然，无城府关键，以故深中之人多不乐，而贤士亦以此归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222930_comment'></div>亲没分财，独推所得之居居其寡嫂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222930_comment'></div>恩当任子，不上其子而以其弟之子上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222930_comment'></div>内外族姻与夫平生党友，饥者食、寒者衣，病者医、死者葬、嫁其女、字其孤，至不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222930_comment'></div>有《荆溪集》及他文合三十馀卷，豪壮而赡蔚，似其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222930_comment'></div>娶同郡杨氏，封安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222930_comment'></div>两男四女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222930_comment'></div>男曰师尹、师说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222930_comment'></div>师尹好学而喜文，再任以官，再不受，其志非苟且目前者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222930_comment'></div>人谓君必有后者，其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222930_comment'></div>女曰琚，适左修职郎陆景瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222930_comment'></div>曰瑢，适左迪功郎元盥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222930_comment'></div>曰瑶，适右承务郎胡辨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222930_comment'></div>曰琬，继陆景瑞之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222930_comment'></div>师尹以君卒之年十二月某甲子，葬君其县铜棺山南笔塔之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222930_comment'></div>以藻与君厚善，来求铭，乃辑君之行治而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222930_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1222930'>呜呼禹功！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222930_comment'></div>世乘波以流，君嶪岌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222930_comment'></div>人视荫以偷，君汲汲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222930_comment'></div>文雄而气刚，见者立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222930_comment'></div>所临必恩，遗老泣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222930_comment'></div>君门洞开，胡过而不入也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222930_comment'></div>宁羸厥躬，尚后人之及也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_83_1222930_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月28日</a>　在抚州，应诏举荐右承奉郎徐度。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年3月</a>　在抚州，上奏罢抚州打造战船事。作品：抚州奏乞罢打造战船等事。<div id='poem_1222742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222742?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抚州奏乞罢打造战船等事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222742")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222742_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222742'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222742'>窃惟陛下屡降明诏求直言，欲闻民间疾苦、朝廷阙失，盛德之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222742_comment'></div>臣幸以侍从，蒙恩领州，熟视疾苦而不为陛下一言，臣则有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222742_comment'></div>臣尝闻孔子之言曰：「足食足兵，民信之矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222742_comment'></div>或问：「不得已而去，于斯二者何先」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222742_comment'></div>曰：「去兵去食」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222742_comment'></div>夫食之与兵，不可去也明矣，圣人岂不知此而顾独存区区之信哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222742_comment'></div>以为不信之祸，甚于无食无兵，不可不慎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222742_comment'></div>陛下即位以来，诏令之下，未尝不以恤民为言，恳恻丁宁，出于诚意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222742_comment'></div>官吏于常赋外，秋毫及民者，辄论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222742_comment'></div>是宜父老扶杖往听，愿少须臾毋死，思见德化之成，如《书》、《传》所载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222742_comment'></div>臣伏睹近日，百姓见朝廷命令之颁，反嘻笑咨怨，其故何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222742_comment'></div>陛下以空文示民，而民莫之信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222742_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222742_comment'></div>财利之在人间，非无量数之物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222742_comment'></div>譬一卮之水，酌之一卮则竭矣，岂复能供钟釜之用乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222742_comment'></div>国家逐路、逐州、逐县之财，皆有成数，量入为出，其理当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222742_comment'></div>今朝廷不问一路多寡有无，而责之漕臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222742_comment'></div>漕臣不问多寡有无，而责之郡守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222742_comment'></div>郡守不问一县多寡有无，而责之县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222742_comment'></div>今日移文曰为某事支系省钱若干，不管阙误，明日移文曰为某事支经制钱若干，不管阙误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222742_comment'></div>不禀承者，以威命临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222742_comment'></div>上下便文，递相逃责，至县而极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222742_comment'></div>推移不行，则浚民脂膏以应期会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222742_comment'></div>此所以陛下有爱民之心，而民莫之信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222742_comment'></div>且以臣所领一州言之，岁得酒税钱不过六万缗，而月桩、大军起纲水脚、官吏军兵请给衣赐、打箭头铁叶等钱，岁当用四十馀万缗，不知此钱从何出哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222742_comment'></div>虽积欠当催，而积欠非朝夕可得，以为不取之于民，是欺陛下耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222742_comment'></div>然尚有可议者，曰遽改之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222742_comment'></div>臣请试指目前一两事最急而病民者言之，打战船、买箭簳、翎毛是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222742_comment'></div>本州正月初六日，准安抚、转运司指挥，抚州打战船二十二只，限五月毕，出违限期，官吏并重寘典宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222742_comment'></div>臣承命惶怖，即时行下诸县，计置材植人工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222742_comment'></div>方欲施工间，二月初六日，又准安抚、转运司指挥，本州改造大样车战船二十二丈、十六丈各一只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222742_comment'></div>本州办集工料如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222742_comment'></div>三月初四日，又准安抚使指挥，分抛二十六车船各一只下抚州，候样打造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222742_comment'></div>三月初六日，又准安抚、转运司指挥，分抛二十车船一只，下抚州，候样到应期打造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222742_comment'></div>前后四牒，未尝一同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222742_comment'></div>虽其末止于打造二十车船一只，安抚、转运司每承圣旨指挥，辄有改易，民间莫知执守，数月为之骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222742_comment'></div>今方候降样，不知其样如何，岂复当改易也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222742_comment'></div>木植人工，驱而致之水滨，去州百馀里，一月馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222742_comment'></div>样未至间，势当复散，散而复集，是重扰也，不知此役何时已耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222742_comment'></div>建议者必曰：「官降度牒矣，何以民为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222742_comment'></div>不知军兴以来，度牒重重相因，虽减价不售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222742_comment'></div>今又州州承打船，抛降仓卒，安能成钱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222742_comment'></div>亦其钱岂能及朝廷所降之数哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222742_comment'></div>借使便得此钱，以官钱贴支，犹须四倍其数，民间之费，又当数倍于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222742_comment'></div>盖船之大者二十二丈，法当用材四丈有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222742_comment'></div>此材非深山穷谷中无有也，挽而致之水滨，岂一日之工、一人之力哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222742_comment'></div>船之可用不可用，非臣所敢知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222742_comment'></div>但见江西地理素薄，民生甚微，方此耕蚕之时，举家暴露视田桑，盻盻然不得为卒岁衣食之计，人人愁叹，陛下所当恤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222742_comment'></div>不知谁为陛下画此，得无用程昌县之言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222742_comment'></div>昌县人材，难逃圣鉴，是果足与参议论、共功名之人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222742_comment'></div>陛下听其言，而使数路生灵为之嗷嗷，臣窃以为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222742_comment'></div>至于箭簳、翎毛，有司当计实用之数，下所产州郡收买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222742_comment'></div>抚，小州也，岁买箭簳二百万、翎毛一百馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222742_comment'></div>一州之数如此，总诸州，盖不可胜计矣，亦安用其数如此之多乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222742_comment'></div>大抵地非所生，必求之他郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222742_comment'></div>今他郡各忧不足，安能及人，此其价所以十倍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222742_comment'></div>故一簳之直几百钱，而翎毛则尤难遽集，至有县令以翎毛决事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222742_comment'></div>诘朝讼者，执翎毛罗立于县庭之前，往往旋捕雁、雉、鹅、鹜取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222742_comment'></div>物被其毒矣，岂特民乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222742_comment'></div>夫民既无聊如此，而江西一路数千里之间，群盗处处盘结，以为劳而为民，不若安然作贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222742_comment'></div>万一群起，合而为一，岂不为陛下宵旰之忧乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222742_comment'></div>况方解严之时，尤当爱惜民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222742_comment'></div>若平居无日不扰，不知四方有警，陛下何以待之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222742_comment'></div>臣所以夙夜为国寒心者此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222742_comment'></div>此皆陛下与大臣画可帷幄之中，而臣乃以区区之愚，妄言于阙庭数千里之外，其不为下所信也必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222742_comment'></div>然事固有不可忽者，陛下胡不遣一二忠信之臣按行而巡问之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222742_comment'></div>傥不如臣言，臣当受罔上之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222742_comment'></div>万有一分可采，陛下何忍驱数州赤子，使之相延而为盗哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222742_comment'></div>臣不胜忧懑待命之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222742_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1222742_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年3月23日</a>　罢知抚州，提举江州太平观。上谢表。作品：谢提举江州太平观表。<div id='poem_1222677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢提举江州太平观表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年3月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222677")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222677'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222677'>抚凋瘵之民，常忧意外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222677_comment'></div>汰疲驽之吏，首在遣中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222677_comment'></div>虽卒抵于谴诃，然实安于分愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222677_comment'></div>感恩至骨，横涕交颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222677_comment'></div>伏念臣去国五年，分符两郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222677_comment'></div>禀生无用，嗟樗栎之漫存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222677_comment'></div>视荫几何，况桑榆之已晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222677_comment'></div>自徙江湖之外，不胜狗马之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222677_comment'></div>瞻帝所以寖遥，知人言之必至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222677_comment'></div>力陈衰惫，幸得罢归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222677_comment'></div>方负负以何言，果断断而不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222677_comment'></div>尚叨冗从，有愧空餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222677_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下祗遹祖宗，辑宁夷夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222677_comment'></div>揽英豪之策，岂止虚己而问公卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222677_comment'></div>重师帅之官，未尝单辞而专守长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222677_comment'></div>而臣自伤晚节，孤奉明恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222677_comment'></div>昔尝叨直于九重，今乃不堪于一障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222677_comment'></div>亟还印绶，甘老锄耰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222677_comment'></div>登俊良而治具毕张，生非不遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222677_comment'></div>坐软弱而终身废弃，报自无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222677_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1222677_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='644c18f179074c88be4239177210cd98_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("644c18f179074c88be4239177210cd98");'><span id='644c18f179074c88be4239177210cd98_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1139')">1135-1139年</a>，57-61岁</div><div id='644c18f179074c88be4239177210cd98' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　寓居吴兴郡长兴县。有文。作品：长兴周如愚殖斋记。长兴刘林宗养浩斋记。<div id='poem_1222881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长兴周如愚殖斋说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222881")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222881'>余少时喜之垄上，与知田者语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222881_comment'></div>其始过焉，苗之芃芃然者，若孺子之起而欲立也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222881_comment'></div>其再过焉，稼之嶷嶷然者，若成人之愿而欲进也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222881_comment'></div>三过焉，穑之肃肃然者，若壮夫之材而欲试也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222881_comment'></div>于是余三过而三有得焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222881_comment'></div>曰：「嗟乎，物化之速也如是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222881_comment'></div>其天时地利之得乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222881_comment'></div>农者曰：「吾于此致力焉，进乎天时地利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222881_comment'></div>吾自土膏之作，未尝食顷舍田而嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222881_comment'></div>于孺子也，惧其仆，日再视焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222881_comment'></div>于成人也，惧其汩，日三视焉；<div class='inline'
