id='poem_content_1222864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222864'>所贵于文者，以能明当世之务，达群伦之情，使千载之下，读之者如出乎其时，如见其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222864_comment'></div>若夫善立言者不然，文虽同乎人，而其所以为文，有非人之所得而同者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222864_comment'></div>孟子七篇之书，叙战国诸侯之事，与夫梁齐君臣之语，其辞极于辩博，若无以异乎战国之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222864_comment'></div>扬子之书数万言，言秦汉之际为最详，简雅而闳深，若无以异乎西汉之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222864_comment'></div>至其推性命之隐，发天人之微，粹然一归于正，使学者师用，比之六经，则当时所谓仪、秦、谷永、杜钦辈，岂惟无以望其门墙，殆冠履之不侔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222864_comment'></div>宋兴百馀年，文章之变屡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222864_comment'></div>杨文公倡之于前，欧阳文忠公继之于后，至元丰、元祐间，斯文几于古而无遗恨矣，盖吾宋极盛之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222864_comment'></div>于是丞相魏国苏公出焉，以博学洽闻，名重天下者五十馀年，卒用儒宗位宰相，一时高文大册悉出其手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222864_comment'></div>故自熙宁以来，国家大号令、朝廷大议论，莫不于公文见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222864_comment'></div>然公事四帝，以名节始终，其见于文者，岂空言哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222864_comment'></div>论政之得失，则开陈反覆而极于忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222864_comment'></div>论民之利病，则援据该详而本于恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222864_comment'></div>有所不言则已，既言于上矣，举天下荣辱是非，莫能移其所守，可谓大臣以道事君者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222864_comment'></div>若其讲明经术之要，练达朝廷之仪，下至百家九流、律历方技之书，无不探其源、综其妙者，在公特馀事耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222864_comment'></div>此所以一话言、一章句，皆足以垂世立教，革浇浮而已媮薄，与轲、雄之书百世相望，而非当时翰墨名家者所能彷佛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222864_comment'></div>公元丰中受诏为《华夷鲁卫录》，书成，序之以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222864_comment'></div>神宗读之，曰：「《说卦》文也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222864_comment'></div>今考其书，信然，则公之他文可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222864_comment'></div>公殁四十年，公之子携始克集公遗文，得诗若干，内外制若干，表奏、章疏、志铭、杂说若干，使藻预观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222864_comment'></div>藻少习公文，以不护拜公为恨者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222864_comment'></div>今乃尽得其书读之，可谓幸矣，故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1222864", 1222864, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>谨识</span>其端而归其书于苏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222864_comment'></div>绍兴九年三月十五日，显谟阁学士、左中大夫、提举江州太平观汪藻序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1222864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月15日</a>　居长兴，有范仲淹祠堂记。作品：范文正公祠堂记。<div id='poem_1222883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>范文正公祠堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年3月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222883")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222883'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222883'>孟子之言气曰：「至大至刚，以直养而无害，则塞乎天地之间」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222883_comment'></div>夫直之为言，大公至正之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222883_comment'></div>以大公至正之道，固守而力行之，不为富贵贫贱威武之所摇夺，虽乘田委吏之卑，亦必尽吾诚、充吾职，卒而至于立国家、定社稷、安边境、服羌戎，其功烈与日月争光，而精神折冲万里之外，谓之气塞乎天地之间可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222883_comment'></div>后世见古人功名之盛，以为类出于偶然，不知公正素定于胸中者，未尝无所从来，而其铭鼎彝、书竹帛者，非一日之积也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222883_comment'></div>文正范公自未第时，已慨然有天下之志，不以死生祸福动其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222883_comment'></div>逮遭明天子有为于时，其立朝如史鱼、汲黯，其忧国如贾谊、刘向，其守边如马伏波、羊叔子，虽庸人孺子，莫不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222883_comment'></div>独筮仕之初，有卓然大过人者，国史失其传，故不得而不纪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222883_comment'></div>公以进士释褐为广德军司理参军日，抱狱具与太守争是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222883_comment'></div>守数以盛怒临公，公未尝少挠，归必记其往复辨论之语于屏上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222883_comment'></div>比去，至字无所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222883_comment'></div>贫止一马，鬻马徒步而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222883_comment'></div>非明于所养者，能如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222883_comment'></div>狱官有亭以公名之者，旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222883_comment'></div>公卒二十年，而高邮孙觉莘老为广德军，始以诗志公之事而刻之亭中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222883_comment'></div>又六十九年，丹阳洪兴祖庆善来守，读莘老之诗而慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222883_comment'></div>初，广德人未知学，公得名士三人为之师，于是郡人之擢进士第者相继于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222883_comment'></div>庆善乃求公遗像，绘而置之学宫，使学者世祀之，而属余记其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222883_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222883_comment'></div>公之盛德，岂待文而后传，而藻亦岂记公者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222883_comment'></div>昔段秀实尽忠于唐，世徒以为一时奋取功名之人，而不知居官必有可书之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222883_comment'></div>柳宗元为摭其实，上之史官，今所以知段太尉逸事者，宗元发之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222883_comment'></div>秀实固不足以拟公，而余幸从庆善得公之详，与夫徵夏无且画工为无所愧，安知后世不采此以补史官之阙乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222883_comment'></div>然庆善为政而首及公，可谓知所本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222883_comment'></div>柔亦不茹，刚亦不吐，文正公有焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222883_comment'></div>好贤如缁衣，庆善有焉，其不可以不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222883_comment'></div>绍兴九年六月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1222883_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月15日</a>　居长兴，有高风堂记。作品：严州高风堂记。<div id='poem_1222884' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222884' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222884?labeling=true' target='_blank'>严州高风堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年3月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222884")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222884_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222884'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222884'>古之王者，取天下而天下归之，盖其功成志得之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222884_comment'></div>以功成志得而视士大夫皆可以爵禄致，必有轻天下之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222884_comment'></div>于是岩穴之间，有人主不得而臣者出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222884_comment'></div>以唐尧之圣，犹不能屈颍阳之高，况其他哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222884_comment'></div>夫士之所以自重如此，非区区为其身谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222884_comment'></div>于以厉世，则百年之风俗系焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222884_comment'></div>汉之二祖皆以布衣取天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222884_comment'></div>高祖之时，有若东园公、绮里季、夏黄公、甪里先生，世祖时，有若严子陵，皆人主不得而臣者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222884_comment'></div>园绮四人，避秦之乱，入商雒山待天下之定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222884_comment'></div>以高祖轻士善骂，义不为汉臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222884_comment'></div>帝虽高此四人，召之莫能致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222884_comment'></div>严子陵亦厌新室之暴，不肯辱其身，逮光武立，犹披羊裘钓泽中，虽三聘仅能一致，而卒不为帝留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222884_comment'></div>是五人者，其出处岂不相类哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222884_comment'></div>然园绮之徒，晚从太子之招，为太子画自安之策，正国本于谈笑，而史不记其所终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222884_comment'></div>故西汉之士，闻其风而慕之者，以计行为得，而风节减于功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222884_comment'></div>子陵本帝故人，既物色求之而来，高卧不朝，帝为亲幸其馆，漠然不应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222884_comment'></div>谯三公若奴隶然，望印绶麾而去之，终其身退耕于野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222884_comment'></div>故东汉之士闻其风而慕之者，尚风节而以功名为不足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222884_comment'></div>大抵园绮之徒学伊尹，子陵学伯夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222884_comment'></div>伊尹耕于有莘之野，曰「我何以汤之聘币为哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222884_comment'></div>卒以忧世，幡然而从汤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222884_comment'></div>伯夷遭周武王之君，犹以为薄，竟不食粟，饿死首阳之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222884_comment'></div>故孟子曰：「伯夷圣之清，伊尹圣之任」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222884_comment'></div>又曰：「闻伯夷之风，顽夫廉，懦夫有立志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222884_comment'></div>子陵世家富春，既归耕于家，后人名其钓处为严陵濑，奉祠千馀年不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222884_comment'></div>今钓濑并台俱存，而富春之境析为严州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222884_comment'></div>绍兴七年，吾友董棻令升为是州，期年政成，乃为堂于州治之左，日从宾客觞咏其上，而名之曰「高风」，以景慕子陵之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222884_comment'></div>且立文正范公所述祠堂之碑于其旁，而求予文为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222884_comment'></div>令升可谓能尚友千古矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222884_comment'></div>令升清介有守，观其所慕，足以知其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222884_comment'></div>故余述子陵出处大概以告令升，而使并刻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222884_comment'></div>绍兴九年六月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1222884_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年10月22日</a>　居长兴，除知徽州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年11月</a>　居长兴，作月观楼记。作品：镇江府月观楼记。<div id='poem_1222889' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222889' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222889?labeling=true' target='_blank'>镇江府月观记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222889")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222889_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222889'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222889'>京口以江山名天下，其来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222889_comment'></div>而为国屏蔽，尤重于晋、宋、齐、梁之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222889_comment'></div>观其千嶂所环，中横巨浸，风涛日夜，驾百川而东之，其形势之雄，实足以控制南北，岂直为骚人羁客区区登览之胜哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222889_comment'></div>州治之西有楼焉，并城而出，名曰「千秋」者，考诸图志，始于晋王恭之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222889_comment'></div>繇楼西南，循城百馀步，忽飞檐曲槛，崒然孤起于城隅之上，望数百里，见之者可观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222889_comment'></div>绍兴八年，吴兴刘岑季高来刺是州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222889_comment'></div>州承废乱之后，公私扫地，无复故时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222889_comment'></div>季高以精明彊敏之才，易民观瞻于谈笑之顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222889_comment'></div>既府寺闾井，鸠集经营，悉复其初，始暇遑于游息之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222889_comment'></div>乃即月观之址，辑而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222889_comment'></div>客有登而叹曰：呜呼壮哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222889_comment'></div>未之见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222889_comment'></div>前此颓甍圮栋，芜没于苍烟灌莽之中，虽江山不与时变迁者亦莫吾觌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222889_comment'></div>今晨霏夕霭，晴岚暖翠，复得于几席之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222889_comment'></div>而风帆浪舶，离鸿落鹜，毕陈于尊俎之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222889_comment'></div>如客得归，如蒙得发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222889_comment'></div>季高于此，可谓能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222889_comment'></div>非政有馀，力能致是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222889_comment'></div>或曰，是未足言季高之政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222889_comment'></div>季高劳于侍从之事，出分天子顾忧，方时艰难，此州实为襟要，其经理规模，必有足大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222889_comment'></div>尝与予四顾而望之，其东曰海门，鸱夷子皮之所从逝也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222889_comment'></div>其西曰瓜步，魏佛狸之所尝至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222889_comment'></div>若其北广陵，则谢太傅之所筑埭而居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222889_comment'></div>而江之中流，则祖豫州之所击楫而誓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222889_comment'></div>计其一时英雄，慷慨愤中原之未复，寇敌之末擒，欲吞之以忠义之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222889_comment'></div>虽狭宇宙而隘九州，自其胸中所积，亦江山有以发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222889_comment'></div>今揽而纳诸数楹之地，使千载之事了然在吾目中，则季高之志可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222889_comment'></div>然自有天地，则有山川，其阅人多矣，而山川胜处，非人不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222889_comment'></div>襄阳岘首，以羊叔子传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222889_comment'></div>武昌南楼，以庾元规传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222889_comment'></div>蜀之筹笔驿，以诸葛武侯传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222889_comment'></div>吾知月观与季高之名，籍籍天下矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222889_comment'></div>为书其本末，以补京口故事之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222889_comment'></div>使后人知此观复新，自吾季高始，岂不益可喜耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222889_comment'></div>季高曰：「可哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222889_comment'></div>绍兴九年十一月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1222889_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
歙县

<div class='label1' id='5d9e06b03b2d4ba38cf00c3a47cb6b0d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5d9e06b03b2d4ba38cf00c3a47cb6b0d");'><span id='5d9e06b03b2d4ba38cf00c3a47cb6b0d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1141')">1139-1141年</a>，61-63岁</div><div id='5d9e06b03b2d4ba38cf00c3a47cb6b0d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年12月29日</a>　到徽州任所。上到任谢表。作品：谢徽州到任启。<div id='poem_1222824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽州到任谢丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年12月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222824")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222824'>误膺明诏，擢领偏城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222824_comment'></div>地接行朝，盖今日股肱之郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222824_comment'></div>世联编籍，乃平生父母之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222824_comment'></div>起废恩深，叨荣愧甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222824_comment'></div>伏念一从去国，十见周星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222824_comment'></div>投迹异州，谁复过门而问字？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222824_comment'></div>疲精断简，徒知仰屋以著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222824_comment'></div>敢图三锡之馀，仍假一麾之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222824_comment'></div>遵涂挟日，入境班春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222824_comment'></div>城郭重来，疑千载去家之鹤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222824_comment'></div>交游半在，或一时同队之鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222824_comment'></div>退省惘然，曷为臻此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222824_comment'></div>惟蟠木离奇之成器，由大钧坱圠以无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222824_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官，间世真儒，中兴名相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222824_comment'></div>坐筹帷幄，收四方人物之英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222824_comment'></div>端委庙堂，复万里舆图之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222824_comment'></div>俯怜衰朽，久事退藏，爰力挽于江湖，俾再临于民社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222824_comment'></div>寻童子钓游之处，虽就荒芜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222824_comment'></div>望先人丘墓之墟，已宽梦寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222824_comment'></div>幸土思之稍慰，宜民瘼之深求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222824_comment'></div>敢不专务拊循，仰分忧顾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222824_comment'></div>褰帷问俗，姑荣衣锦之归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222824_comment'></div>上冢还家，终冀挥金之乐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1222824_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年12月29日</a>　到徽州任所。上到任谢丞相启。作品：徽州到任谢丞相启。<div id='poem_1222824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽州到任谢丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年12月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222824")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222824'>误膺明诏，擢领偏城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222824_comment'></div>地接行朝，盖今日股肱之郡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222824_comment'></div>世联编籍，乃平生父母之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222824_comment'></div>起废恩深，叨荣愧甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222824_comment'></div>伏念一从去国，十见周星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222824_comment'></div>投迹异州，谁复过门而问字？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222824_comment'></div>疲精断简，徒知仰屋以著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222824_comment'></div>敢图三锡之馀，仍假一麾之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222824_comment'></div>遵涂挟日，入境班春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222824_comment'></div>城郭重来，疑千载去家之鹤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222824_comment'></div>交游半在，或一时同队之鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222824_comment'></div>退省惘然，曷为臻此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222824_comment'></div>惟蟠木离奇之成器，由大钧坱圠以无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222824_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官，间世真儒，中兴名相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222824_comment'></div>坐筹帷幄，收四方人物之英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222824_comment'></div>端委庙堂，复万里舆图之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222824_comment'></div>俯怜衰朽，久事退藏，爰力挽于江湖，俾再临于民社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222824_comment'></div>寻童子钓游之处，虽就荒芜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222824_comment'></div>望先人丘墓之墟，已宽梦寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222824_comment'></div>幸土思之稍慰，宜民瘼之深求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222824_comment'></div>敢不专务拊循，仰分忧顾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222824_comment'></div>褰帷问俗，姑荣衣锦之归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222824_comment'></div>上冢还家，终冀挥金之乐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1222824_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在徽州，有镇江府州学重修撰记并诗。作品：镇江府重修州学大成殿记。<div id='poem_1222892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>镇江府重修州学大成殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222892")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222892'>古之有天下国家者，其世之长短，视积累之厚薄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222892_comment'></div>其祀之隆替，视子孙之兴废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222892_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222892_comment'></div>吾之所以有天下国家者，以吾有息争已乱之道，而足以庇民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222892_comment'></div>民知吾有息争已乱之道，而利加其身，则世世戴其子孙事之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222892_comment'></div>此吾所以处其庙祧之尊，而飨其岁时烝尝之奉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222892_comment'></div>苟为无以承之，祀从而隳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222892_comment'></div>惟夫子则不然，未尝有尺地一民之封也，而教实行乎天下之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222892_comment'></div>所谓息争已乱之道者，与万世共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222892_comment'></div>天下用吾说则治，不用则乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222892_comment'></div>既不用而乱矣，朝用吾说，夕治如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222892_comment'></div>天下复相率而祀之，其祀益修而严，则其道益尊而明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222892_comment'></div>此三代之子孙，于今为庶，而夫子之祀，与天地相为终始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222892_comment'></div>夫子之没，千有馀年，守文之君，当涂之士，所以讲求而祀之者不为不至，然未有如本朝之盛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222892_comment'></div>方其盛时，庙学之兴，溢乎四海之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222892_comment'></div>虽蛮夷戎狄之国，莫不知吾夫子之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222892_comment'></div>镇江有学，在州之城东南隅，经始于太平兴国八年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222892_comment'></div>后五十七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222892_comment'></div>新而广之者，文正范公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222892_comment'></div>艰难以来，镇江适当兵冲，故学宫坏为垒舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222892_comment'></div>徽猷阁直学士、新安程公来牧之数月，大成殿复及于焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222892_comment'></div>一日，公过而叹曰：「嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222892_comment'></div>释老二氏，吾儒操戈而逐之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222892_comment'></div>今道宫、佛刹，圮于戎马之馀才几日耳，已纷然相望于国都，其徒志坚而材足以有立故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222892_comment'></div>吾夫子息争已乱之道，有功于世如此，而吾徒又奉明天子之命司教于此，反熟视而不为，可愧也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222892_comment'></div>乃谋费于州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222892_comment'></div>会州豪及浮屠氏有以其赢来献者，于是鸠材庀工，诹日之良，而郡丞韩中通、葛祐之，教官邹全嗣，实左右其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222892_comment'></div>未数月而台殿成，屹然起于江山形势之中，与之相称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222892_comment'></div>其室筵屏摄、阶序门庭，与夫像设器陈，又皆秩秩绳绳，无不应图合礼，他州之祠莫及也，于是人以程公为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222892_comment'></div>呜呼，学校之事，类非俗吏之所能为也，况出于干戈之后乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222892_comment'></div>春秋二百四十二年之间，诸侯之筑宗庙、宫室、台榭、门厩，莫不为其国史所书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222892_comment'></div>而以学校见于六经者，鲁之頖宫、郑之乡校而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222892_comment'></div>岂当时以力政相高，而不暇及此耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222892_comment'></div>抑公卿士大夫知此为治乱之本者少也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222892_comment'></div>程公以经术决科，饰吏事以儒雅，而所至皆可师，宜知所本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222892_comment'></div>学将成而公去，其属刘颍士、王炳以诸生之请来告曰：「愿书以贻后人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222892_comment'></div>乃为叙而诗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222892_comment'></div>诗曰：万物一气，统于乾元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222892_comment'></div>夫子之道，与之并尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222892_comment'></div>峙山行川，莫地之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222892_comment'></div>夫子之尊，与之并久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222892_comment'></div>惟昔旬始，彗于紫微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222892_comment'></div>簠簋弃道，学门雉飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222892_comment'></div>坐令此邦，祀不蠲肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222892_comment'></div>伊谁新之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222892_comment'></div>自我贤牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222892_comment'></div>爰彻灌莽，列为飞甍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222892_comment'></div>京口之宅，曲阿之城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222892_comment'></div>弦歌在堂，一洗锋镝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222892_comment'></div>曲阿之城，京口之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222892_comment'></div>伟矣兹举，非公孰能？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222892_comment'></div>嗣我文正，百年而兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222892_comment'></div>左江右山，输秀于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222892_comment'></div>为邦生材，以笃王纪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1222892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在徽州，为汪伯彦昼绣堂作记。作品：昼绣堂记。<div id='poem_1222886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>画绣堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222886")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222886'>自古人物与山川相为轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222886_comment'></div>崧岳生甫申，淇澳生卫武，山东出相，山西出将，此人物以山川为重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222886_comment'></div>莘野以伊尹闻，磻溪以吕望闻，隆中繇诸葛亮而显，曲江繇张九龄而大，此山川以人物为重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222886_comment'></div>故为名山大川者，不以生明堂大辂之材、九鼎之金、照乘之珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222886_comment'></div>连城之璧为贵，而以毓英贤为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222886_comment'></div>为王公大人者，不以功业载旂常、铭钟鼎、书竹帛、流管弦为荣，而以归故乡为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222886_comment'></div>此古人所谓富贵而不归故乡，如衣绣夜行者，言得志而行乎四方，人孰见之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222886_comment'></div>必至吾父母之邦，然后为可乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222886_comment'></div>新安自吴为郡，今千馀年，山水峭厉而清深，故长材秀民之出，视东南为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222886_comment'></div>繇唐以来，擢高科、登显仕者，固不为无人，然未有居将相之位者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222886_comment'></div>宋兴百七十年，而大丞相汪公出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222886_comment'></div>公以诸生，徒步起家于京师数千里之外，为时伟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222886_comment'></div>遭明天子艰难之中，总州符入侍，出奇谋秘策以辅成中兴之功，遂自枢臣相天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222886_comment'></div>其精忠如金石，赫然为佐命元勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222886_comment'></div>而新安之名一日闻于天下，此新安之荣也，岂独公之荣哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222886_comment'></div>绍兴九年，公自七闽入觐，以保信之节来镇宣城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222886_comment'></div>宣城、新安、鄱阳，三州相望，皆百馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222886_comment'></div>公乃卜居鄱水之上，将归老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222886_comment'></div>建画绣之堂，而命藻记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222886_comment'></div>藻曰：公以迈往之资，应期遇运，乘风云、依日月，而正宇宙于立谈之间，虽释位而去者十年，天子未尝一日忘公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222886_comment'></div>乃建旄秉钺而兼师傅之官，亦可谓布衣之极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222886_comment'></div>公今七十馀，精明如五十许人，将复三居廊庙，坐筹帷幄，取河朔山东六十馀州归职方图籍，奉乘舆还宫阙，然后退从赤松子之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222886_comment'></div>其功名益新，则新安之名益大，藻将不一书而为天下国家庆也，又岂特为新安之荣而已哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1222886_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　在徽州，作傅楫墓志铭。作品：朝请郎龙图阁待制知亳州赠少师傅公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222933' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222933' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222933?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝请郎龙图阁待制知亳州赠少师傅公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222933")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222933_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222933'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222933'>崇宁间，钩党之论起，元祐以来士大夫为世指名者，悉堕党中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222933_comment'></div>故一时盛德精忠之人，往往赍志以没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222933_comment'></div>既没矣，子孙惧及，率秘其阀阅不敢传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222933_comment'></div>逮靖康党禁除，人人争言嘉祐、治平以前事，于是昔之悼不幸土中者，咸振耀于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222933_comment'></div>公虽没于崇宁之初，为不预其祸，然用事者犹指公为党人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222933_comment'></div>至绍兴九年公之卒葬也，三十八年矣，而墓碑未立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222933_comment'></div>公之子七人，惟诒度在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222933_comment'></div>诒度以书来乞铭，藻少仰公名，以不获拜公为恨，今乃得执笔次公之行事，幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222933_comment'></div>然藻去公几四十年，更士大夫以言为讳之时，公之行治，其详不可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222933_comment'></div>谨掇其灼然在人耳目者，序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222933_comment'></div>公讳楫，字元通，姓傅氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222933_comment'></div>傅氏系出北地，自祗、亮世仕江南，子孙因散处江淮间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222933_comment'></div>有居光州者，遭广明之乱，从王潮奔闽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222933_comment'></div>数世而至公高祖仁瑞，又徙居兴化军仙游县，故公今为仙游人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222933_comment'></div>曾大父献、大父称、皇考滋，皆以地远京师，不求仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222933_comment'></div>而皇考尤有信义，为里人所宗，以公故赠朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222933_comment'></div>公少庄重如成人，甫七岁，从乡先生学，已能痛自刻厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222933_comment'></div>他儿戏旁哗笑，如不闻，反并取其书诵读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222933_comment'></div>未冠，试广文馆第一，其文天下传诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222933_comment'></div>既不第而归，有贵人欲留公使子弟学焉者，公曰：「吾方求师友，资身未暇也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222933_comment'></div>闻孙觉、陈襄有学行，抠衣从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222933_comment'></div>襄门人有许安世、江衍之流，皆尝以文艺冠多士，襄不之取，独称公曰：「傅元通金石人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222933_comment'></div>以其女妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222933_comment'></div>擢治平四年进士第，调扬州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222933_comment'></div>守遇僚属暴甚，屡以难集事诿公而促其期，公裁决如流，未尝希意苟合，至捕其从者寘诸法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222933_comment'></div>守虽彊听而不能平，乃欲以繁剧困之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222933_comment'></div>会天长令缺，檄公摄承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222933_comment'></div>公发伏擿奸如神，猾吏恶少年皆屏迹褫气，天长大治，更以最闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222933_comment'></div>丁外艰，归里中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222933_comment'></div>里中事有不能决者，悉从公折衷，或望公门罢讼而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222933_comment'></div>调福州福清丞，帅曾巩负材倨视天下士，独与公钧礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222933_comment'></div>改苏州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222933_comment'></div>复丁内艰，免丧授太原府太谷令，白诛徙乡而还为民害者一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222933_comment'></div>于是公之仕也二十年矣，犹在吏部选，处之怡然，未尝以穷达介怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222933_comment'></div>会曾布帅太原，谒入，大惊曰：「是福清傅丞，为吾兄所知者耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222933_comment'></div>率部使者交荐，且以书言之朝廷公卿间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222933_comment'></div>改宣德郎、知吉州龙泉县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222933_comment'></div>时孙觉为御史中丞，谓公曰：「朝廷欲用公，幸少留，除书且下矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222933_comment'></div>公曰：「仕所以乐居中者，免外台督责之辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222933_comment'></div>今頫首权门，与外台奚择？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222933_comment'></div>且外官我所当得也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222933_comment'></div>径出国门不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222933_comment'></div>道除太学博士，所至学者阗门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222933_comment'></div>官太学四年，足未尝及宰相执政之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222933_comment'></div>秩满，即日诣曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222933_comment'></div>曾布知枢密院，与其副林希共荐之，宰相亦雅知公名，除太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222933_comment'></div>公长礼学，自神宗时议祠北郊，至是有诏复议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222933_comment'></div>议者多持两可，公独援经据古，损其车服、仪卫、赏赉之类，使悉得其中上之，后卒施行如公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222933_comment'></div>绍圣二年，徽宗由遂宁邸就资善堂学，诏大臣择德行老成人为傅，宰相以公名闻，除诸王府说书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222933_comment'></div>旧制，诸王课学书属文而不及经，公言王当以德义为先，区区翰墨非所急，请先讲经史以懋王德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222933_comment'></div>从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222933_comment'></div>明年，徽宗封端王，就除记室参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222933_comment'></div>又明年，为侍讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222933_comment'></div>又明年，为翊善中人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222933_comment'></div>执事王府者，例与宫僚昵，公独正色不与亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222933_comment'></div>虽一府以为介，而悉严惮之，王亦为之加礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222933_comment'></div>阅五年，移官者四而不出王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222933_comment'></div>同僚或岁中屡迁，公未尝一语及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222933_comment'></div>会谏臣邹浩以言事谴，公厚赆其行，坐是免所居官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222933_comment'></div>裁两月，徽宗即位，首问公安在，即除直秘阁，进尚书司封员外郎，擢监察御史，权殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222933_comment'></div>论内侍都知刘瑗恃宠专恣，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222933_comment'></div>移国子司业，迁起居郎，召试中书舍人，徽宗面称训词有西汉风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222933_comment'></div>于是曾布当国，以兄弟于公有汲引恩，冀其助己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222933_comment'></div>公岿然守正，凡朝廷命令有可疑，进退人材有不厌众望，如救王古、范纯礼之类，皆人所难言者，必极论之，虽屡却不为之回夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222933_comment'></div>布每以为言，不合者因是中伤公，公不恤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222933_comment'></div>徽宗顾公潜邸旧，见必咨访，公每以遵祖宗法度、安静自然为献，语宰相亦谆谆及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222933_comment'></div>归则削藁，虽至亲莫得而闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222933_comment'></div>一日李清臣劝上清心省事，徽宗曰：「近臣惟傅楫为朕言此甚详」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222933_comment'></div>然后人始知公所以启迪上心者，其卓至皆此类也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222933_comment'></div>建中靖国秋，见时事寖更张，窃叹曰：「祸其始此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222933_comment'></div>不去，楚人将钳我于市」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222933_comment'></div>闻者莫不甚其言，公笑曰：「后当以吾言为信」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222933_comment'></div>遂求补外，诏不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222933_comment'></div>恳祈不已，最后中书舍人邹浩为请，乃听除龙图阁待制、知亳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222933_comment'></div>到郡数月，属疾，易衣趺坐而卒，年六十一，寔崇宁元年二月五日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222933_comment'></div>公于孔孟之学，精思而力探之，不臻其极不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222933_comment'></div>又天资简淡，于世事无一可关心者，专用经史自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222933_comment'></div>聚书至万卷，平居正衣冠，如对大宾，否则瞑目燕坐，不妄出一语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222933_comment'></div>虽在闇室，无秋毫之欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222933_comment'></div>故能死生祸福不入胸中，视进退穷通若梦幻然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222933_comment'></div>虽当是之时，直道立朝，不为无人，若夫先见如龟蓍，卓然引去者，惟公一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222933_comment'></div>大观中，大臣屡欲以公入党籍，徽宗念公旧学之臣而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222933_comment'></div>后每因事必及公姓名，而卒不为大臣所右，故公之没，恤典不加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222933_comment'></div>公之葬在今常州宜兴县善拳山之原，累以诸子恩赠少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222933_comment'></div>妻陈氏，亦赠越国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222933_comment'></div>子谅友、谊夫，皆擢进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222933_comment'></div>谅友，仕至奉议郎、尚书膳部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222933_comment'></div>谊夫，朝请郎、尚书兵部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222933_comment'></div>谦受，朝奉大夫、夔州路转运判官，与诒微、去病、誉处，皆相继前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222933_comment'></div>诒度，今为朝请大夫、主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222933_comment'></div>有文集三十五卷，藏于家，简古而精深，世以为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222933_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_1222933'>道有所寄，千年一儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222933_comment'></div>世得而用，一人万夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222933_comment'></div>公承丘轲，知学元本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222933_comment'></div>匪惟知之，亦践其壸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222933_comment'></div>用此玉立，直哉惟清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222933_comment'></div>世无可娱，以道死生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222933_comment'></div>晚登王门，帝实知我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222933_comment'></div>擢跻近臣，初不求可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222933_comment'></div>正色凛凛，倾忠上前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222933_comment'></div>宁非大刚，吾道则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222933_comment'></div>帝知虽深，时不我与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222933_comment'></div>奉身而行，世莫能御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222933_comment'></div>竟脱党祸，归安九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222933_comment'></div>世评既公，盛德乃尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222933_comment'></div>闻风而兴，百世之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222933_comment'></div>我为铭诗，以诏来者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_106_1222933_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年3月</a>　在徽州，为曾纁作墓志铭。作品：奉议郎知舒州曾君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉议郎知舒州曾君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222946")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222946'>绍兴十年三月，故人子曾协以书抵余曰：「惟先人弃诸孤有年，惟不肖孤于窀穸事不敢缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222946_comment'></div>今岁月逝矣，所以诏后世者无传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222946_comment'></div>顾先人好友惟丈人存，敢介伯父以请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222946_comment'></div>则又为书一通，录君平生族出官阀行治，授使者速余铭，乃序而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222946_comment'></div>君讳纁，字元礼，世家建昌南丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222946_comment'></div>南丰之曾，自国初闻天下，盖君之曾祖致尧，事太宗、真宗，有大臣之言，不克施以殁，仕至户部郎中，赠谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222946_comment'></div>君之祖易占，复以议论文章名世，卒官太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222946_comment'></div>有子六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222946_comment'></div>曰巩，为中书舍人，神宗时学者宗之，号南丰先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222946_comment'></div>曰布，相徽宗皇帝，谥「文肃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222946_comment'></div>曰肇，终翰林学士，谥「文昭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222946_comment'></div>同时鼎峙为名臣，于是曾氏之名，益彰彻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222946_comment'></div>士大夫以氏族名家，皆出其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222946_comment'></div>君文昭暮子也，少警敏，自以承父祖百年馀，不痛自激昂，无以绍厥世，乃力学问，为词章，被服勤苦如寒生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222946_comment'></div>未冠试有司，已能超出其辈类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222946_comment'></div>坐党家子不得至京师，著《七志》、《鸥鸟》《老酒》二赋以自见，文昭公见而奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222946_comment'></div>年三十馀，始举进士，中其科，调主应天府虞城、明州鄞县簿，复堙阨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222946_comment'></div>久之，当路有怜其才、悼其屈者，挽为大晟府主簿，非其好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222946_comment'></div>出提举两浙河北京东路盐香，改梓州路常平，皆不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222946_comment'></div>除京畿提举学事，言者犹指君党家子免之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222946_comment'></div>得知太平州，提举两浙盐香，又皆不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222946_comment'></div>选知高邮军，移未期年，遭母兖国夫人忧，归吴中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222946_comment'></div>至毗陵卒，年四十一，官止奉议郎，时宣和五年四月五日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222946_comment'></div>娶强氏，资政殿学士、文宪公之女，兖国夫人之妷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222946_comment'></div>生子五人，曰惠、懙、剽、懻、协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222946_comment'></div>惠，迪功郎、镇江府金坛县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222946_comment'></div>懙，承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222946_comment'></div>剽、懻，皆未命，皆后君数年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222946_comment'></div>协，今为右承务郎、监临安府新城县税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222946_comment'></div>君清修谨厚，龆龀时已凝重不可干，见者无不敬异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222946_comment'></div>及长，嗜书，得一书必手钞口诵，非得其甚解不已，于《春秋》之学尤长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222946_comment'></div>平居终日寡言，淡若与世无情者，及处父母兄弟朋友之间，则能为人之所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222946_comment'></div>文章简古，似其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222946_comment'></div>议论衮衮，挟其家数世敢言之气，必有为而发，不崇空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222946_comment'></div>政和间，余始识君文宪公座上，自是日相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222946_comment'></div>每君文一篇出，读之若川增条达，莫见其止，余未尝不愧叹弥日，以为不可及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222946_comment'></div>当是时，人材盛矣，君独秀出其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222946_comment'></div>自艰难以来，典章文物委地，昔之所谓人材者，各以其所长班班见世，取能名，登显仕，而君墓上之木拱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222946_comment'></div>古人所谓人不可无年者，如君非耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222946_comment'></div>由是知君者莫不哀君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222946_comment'></div>君殁时，协未胜衣，今颀然为举子之秀，乃能数百里求文识君墓，人又莫不喜协之能绍君，如君之绍其家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222946_comment'></div>谓君有后，而曾氏世不乏人者，其在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222946_comment'></div>君墓在镇江府丹徒县丹徒乡，其葬也，以某年某月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222946_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1222946'>嗟夫子兮志莫伦，承奕世兮自发身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222946_comment'></div>佩明月兮冠切云，策坚良兮问要津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222946_comment'></div>八鸾奏兮步始陈，忽中道兮柅厥轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222946_comment'></div>成之艰兮意若勤，复夺去兮疑大钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222946_comment'></div>君有后兮将益振，谓不信兮视此文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1222946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月</a>　在徽州，为张根《春秋指南》作序。作品：吴园先生《春秋指南》序。<div id='poem_1222865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴园先生春秋指南序<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222865")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222865'>六经惟《春秋》为仲尼作，圣人见其所志之书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222865_comment'></div>学而不明乎是非，何以为人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222865_comment'></div>治而不明乎赏刑，何以为国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222865_comment'></div>此书之所以作而为万世法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222865_comment'></div>虽曰以匹夫而行天子事，有所谓婉而成章者，然其褒贬一出乎天下是非之公，岂故为殊绝甚高之论，使后人有不可及之叹哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222865_comment'></div>不知班固何所受之，立为弟子退而异言之说，开后世诸儒相诟病之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222865_comment'></div>使当时诚有异同，不应复云「游夏之徒，不能赞一辞」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222865_comment'></div>孟子去孔子百馀年，于《书·武成》、《诗·云汉》，莫不疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222865_comment'></div>至《春秋》则曰：「《诗》亡然后《春秋》作」，「孔子成《春秋》而乱臣贼子惧」，「知我者《春秋》，罪我者《春秋》」而已，未尝片言置疑于其间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222865_comment'></div>彼乱臣贼子者，岂晓然知道理之人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222865_comment'></div>一见《春秋》而知惧焉，非惧圣人之书也，惧天下是非之公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222865_comment'></div>自三《传》兴，而圣人之经始不胜其繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222865_comment'></div>好异者曰：圣人之言，窅然幽深，必有不可以近情常理度者，当冥思而力探之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222865_comment'></div>于是枝叶蕃滋，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222865_comment'></div>人人务其己说之胜，而莫知求至当之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222865_comment'></div>乃至子而以父学为非，弟子而以师说为愚，况其他哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222865_comment'></div>则《春秋》不明，三《传》乱之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222865_comment'></div>本朝自熙宁以来，学者废《春秋》不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222865_comment'></div>数十年间，笃学而好之者，盖不为无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222865_comment'></div>然一时章分句析之学胜，故虽《春秋》，亦穿凿破碎而不见圣人之浑全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222865_comment'></div>政和间，余过山阳，吴园先生张公在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222865_comment'></div>先生谓余曰：「学《春秋》而不编年，无以学为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222865_comment'></div>吾尝以诸国纵横列而类见之，圣人之意了然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222865_comment'></div>当令子见吾书」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222865_comment'></div>余未及受而先生亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222865_comment'></div>未几，先生之书盛行于士大夫间，因得伏而读之，曰：「嗟乎，圣人之意岂远人哉，曲学蔽之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222865_comment'></div>先生闭户读书二十馀年，其见于世者固已硕大光明，而所出裁一二而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222865_comment'></div>则求圣人之心而得之者，岂独此书哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222865_comment'></div>虽然，以此书考之，先生之志亦可以槩见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222865_comment'></div>绍兴十年七月，门人汪藻序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1222865_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年7月</a>　在徽州，为胡瑗《胡先生言行录》作序。作品：胡先生言行录序。<div id='poem_1222868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胡先生言行录序<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222868")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222868'>自孔子没，诸儒以学名家，固无世无人，而其间必有卓然名世者，德与言称，当时师之，后世尊之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222868_comment'></div>以汉四百年所得者扬雄，以唐三百年所得者韩愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222868_comment'></div>如董仲舒、郑康成、王通、孔颖达之徒，非无益于后世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222868_comment'></div>仲舒倡灾祥之说，王通袭圣人之迹，康成、颖达守区区训诂之文，学者疑焉，此二子所以岿然独为后世宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222868_comment'></div>宋兴八十馀年，至庆历、皇祐间，儒学无愧于古矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222868_comment'></div>当时学者，以泰山孙明复、徂徕石守道、海陵胡先生为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222868_comment'></div>而先生之门为最盛，弟子各以其经转相传授，常数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222868_comment'></div>仁义礼乐之风，蔼然被乎东南，公卿伟人由先生之门而出者接踵于时，盖数十年未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222868_comment'></div>熙宁以来，学者非王氏不宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222868_comment'></div>而先生之学，不绝如线矣，然识者知其必兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222868_comment'></div>逮今天子一新斯文，力去党锢之弊，访先生之后，得其孙涤而官之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222868_comment'></div>繇是先生之学复振耀流通，人人读先生之书，如庆历、皇祐时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222868_comment'></div>先生虽尝再至京师，为太学官，侍经天章阁，而教授吴兴为最久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222868_comment'></div>其建太学京师也，又尝下吴兴，取先生之法为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222868_comment'></div>则吴兴者，先生之洙泗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222868_comment'></div>绍兴八年，钱塘关注子东主吴兴学，而先生之孙涤在焉，相与裒先生遗书，将以布之天下，慰学者之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222868_comment'></div>得先生《易书》若干篇、《中庸义》若干篇，既藏之学宫矣，又录先生言行若干条为一帙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222868_comment'></div>孟子曰：「君子之泽五世而斩，小人之泽五世而斩，予未得为孔子徒也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222868_comment'></div>言君子小人，虽贤否不同，而泽之所施，同乎有尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222868_comment'></div>惟义理之在人心为无穷，虽传之百世可也，则先生之学复行固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222868_comment'></div>然子东所以求先生之书者，岂徒为循诵习传而已哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222868_comment'></div>将以美风俗、新人材，于是乎在，可谓知先生所以望后世之意者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222868_comment'></div>绍兴十年七月，汪藻序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1222868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年10月</a>　在徽州，为何氏书堂作记。作品：何氏书堂记。<div id='poem_1222890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222890' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222890?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何氏书堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222890")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222890_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222890'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222890'>吴兴环城皆水，独西南冈岭相属十馀里，而得浮图氏之居二焉，东曰道场，西曰何山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222890_comment'></div>何山立于宋元嘉中，道场近出于唐末五季之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222890_comment'></div>然道场踵相蹑得人，法席雄盛，钟鱼殷殷，声闻东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222890_comment'></div>何山败屋数椽，残僧数辈，望之萧然，游者弗顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222890_comment'></div>虽其兴先道场五百馀年，而衰陋反出其下远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222890_comment'></div>绍兴初，余守吴兴，得二禅老，曰慧林、曰居慧，使分居二山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222890_comment'></div>慧居何山数年，剪薙榛芜，易其圮腐而一新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222890_comment'></div>于是游道场者，如入王侯之家，其隆楼杰阁，足以吞光景而纳江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222890_comment'></div>已而过何山，则草树葱茏，轩窗窈窕，经行之地，皆雅洁幽深，如造幽人隐士之庐，至者忘归，不知雄盛移而为清胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222890_comment'></div>寺有何氏书堂，图记相承以何氏为晋何楷，楷尝读书此山，后为吴兴太守，以其居为寺而名其山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222890_comment'></div>颜鲁公书杼山碑，亦曰寺西南有何楷钓台，则楷尝居此山无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222890_comment'></div>然楷之姓名，于晋史无所见，惟《宋书》言何子平曾祖楷，为晋侍中而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222890_comment'></div>唐林宝《姓纂》亦云何睿渡江生楷，为晋侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222890_comment'></div>《晋书》称睿有子五人，独充、准有传，而不及其馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222890_comment'></div>又《括地志》谓楷为吴兴太守，《宋书》乃以楷为晋侍中，岂沈约见《晋书》，充尝除侍中，因误谓充为楷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222890_comment'></div>抑为吴兴太守，后亦至侍中耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222890_comment'></div>皆不得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222890_comment'></div>以余考之，寺有宋《禅幽寺碑》云：元嘉十四年，创立精舍于金盖山，初不言楷时有寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222890_comment'></div>且何山之名，于梁吴均诗始见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222890_comment'></div>疑楷尝学于此山，其名迹在人，后人慕之，即其处为精舍耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222890_comment'></div>谓楷以其居为寺者，非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222890_comment'></div>《禅幽寺碑》至唐会昌时已断裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222890_comment'></div>无几，有张道规者，以为式道人书，识而龛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222890_comment'></div>今碑亦不复见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222890_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222890_comment'></div>晋之士大夫，可谓求志而得其志矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222890_comment'></div>其退也，处山林而以读书为乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222890_comment'></div>其出也，居城府而以治民为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222890_comment'></div>或出或处，不过乎数十里之间，其人物风流可以想见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222890_comment'></div>楷距今几千年，此寺之废兴屡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222890_comment'></div>世以为可久者，莫如金石之传，既金石罄灭，而此山之名独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222890_comment'></div>则谓人物风流，非士大夫所先，而虚名无益于后世者，非陋欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222890_comment'></div>余老矣，方买田若溪之上，则此山将皆为吾杖屦所有，其可不留语山中，为吴兴故事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222890_comment'></div>乃订其本末而并书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222890_comment'></div>绍兴十年十月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1222890_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在徽州，冬，与赵令衿、李邴、曾开诣经山谒大慧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在徽州，有书陈尧佐逸事后。作品：书陈文惠公逸事后。<div id='poem_1222871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书陈文惠公逸事后<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222871")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222871'>文惠陈公相仁祖，每内批，夜漏下不过十刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222871_comment'></div>忽夜分有御封至私第，公不启封，来日袖至榻前屏奏曰：「今中宫虚位，张贵妃有宠，恐奸人附会，请正母仪，非陛下本意，有不得已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222871_comment'></div>若诚此事，臣不敢启封，以示同列」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222871_comment'></div>仁祖首肯曰：「姑置之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222871_comment'></div>妃即追册温成后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222871_comment'></div>当时于墓刻神道碑，不敢书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222871_comment'></div>公薨百馀年，公之曾孙右中大夫、直秘阁兖始录以示人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222871_comment'></div>呜呼，兹举也，天下之治乱系焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222871_comment'></div>文惠公不动声色，开悟转移于谈笑之顷，一旦致其主于汉唐君之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222871_comment'></div>使当时有秋毫容悦之心，其失可胜计哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222871_comment'></div>可谓仁人之言，而一言兴邦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222871_comment'></div>自古妃匹之爱，父不能得之子，君不能得之臣，所谓难言骨肉之间者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222871_comment'></div>文惠公及此，固社稷之臣，非吾仁祖有从谏之圣，亦安能容其臣如是之大乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222871_comment'></div>后世于此，可以观一时君臣之盛而为万世法矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222871_comment'></div>绍兴十年十二月，臣汪藻书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1222871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在徽州，葺徽州学舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在徽州，转左太中大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在徽州，为周之道作墓志铭。作品：尚书刑部侍郎赠通议大夫周公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书刑部侍郎赠通议大夫周公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222934")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222934'>故尚书刑部侍郎周公既葬之四十年，其嗣子石聚族之长老而谋曰：「先君以清节直道事三帝，隐然为国名臣，今墓槚成阴矣，而墓碑未立，其何以饬来裔？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222934_comment'></div>若求当世能言者，揭其一二而显诔之，岂不足以慰先君地下而宠绥周氏之祧」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222934_comment'></div>皆曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222934_comment'></div>遂相与来请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222934_comment'></div>藻读其书，曰：「噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222934_comment'></div>吾先大夫同年进士也，于藻为丈人行，铭其可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222934_comment'></div>然吾生也后，不获拜公，公之平生，藻莫得而详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222934_comment'></div>今班班在人耳目者尚多有之，姑掇其大者识之，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222934_comment'></div>石再拜曰：「幸甚」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222934_comment'></div>乃书以授石，使归而刻之墓上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222934_comment'></div>公讳之道，字觉民，世家吴兴长城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222934_comment'></div>曾祖父铤、大父仁皓、父亨，皆以修谨闻里中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222934_comment'></div>亨用公恩为光禄寺丞，赠大中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222934_comment'></div>公少寒苦，刻意于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222934_comment'></div>年十三，以文谒安定先生胡瑗，瑗奇之，因留受业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222934_comment'></div>擢皇祐五年进士第，调主杭州钱塘簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222934_comment'></div>转运司治钱塘，吏习倨骄，视州县蔑如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222934_comment'></div>转运使元绛委公督租，吏胡通者，绛任之，有田邑中，租过期不入，公执通归，杖而徇，一邑大惊，他租不日而办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222934_comment'></div>绛大喜，帅使者荐诸朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222934_comment'></div>移歙州祈门令，有政迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222934_comment'></div>改著作佐郎、知江宁府江宁县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222934_comment'></div>县素剧，更数令不能治，公视讼牒如流，庭无留事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222934_comment'></div>守知其敏，虽府事亦以委公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222934_comment'></div>于是田苦下潦与江通，公筑圩数千丈，民赖其穫，至今以公名其圩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222934_comment'></div>秩满，知遂州录事参军，改通判戎州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222934_comment'></div>初，王文公安石奉使江东，祁门其属邑也，熟知公治状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222934_comment'></div>已而寓居金陵，得公尤详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222934_comment'></div>居无何，文公当国，绛亦预政，皆言公可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222934_comment'></div>召对，擢知开封府司录参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222934_comment'></div>当是时，朝廷更法令如毛，诏之关府者日十馀下，公随事酬酢，悉得其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222934_comment'></div>且摘隐发奸如神，吏为屏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222934_comment'></div>他日以事众见，上独目公，曰「卿决狱非畏忌顾望者」，公顿首谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222934_comment'></div>除京西路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222934_comment'></div>丁外艰，服除，复提举其路常平，移成都府路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222934_comment'></div>会御史朱服言参知政事章惇交通台臣，踪迹连公，诏有司覈实，虽不尽如服言，公犹坐免所居官，废斥者累年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222934_comment'></div>元祐初，直前谩，留为大理寺丞，已而迁正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222934_comment'></div>以母老丐外，得提点江南西路刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222934_comment'></div>入尚书为刑部员外郎，以母忧去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222934_comment'></div>久之，还故职，升郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222934_comment'></div>出为江南东路转运使，移淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222934_comment'></div>岁旱饥，有司责民输如令，他官熟视莫敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222934_comment'></div>公至则除其半，民以苏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222934_comment'></div>召为大理卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222934_comment'></div>异时决狱者株连无辜，牢户皆满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222934_comment'></div>公有所讯鞫，择其诖误者先释之，廷尉省爰书，盖自公始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222934_comment'></div>擢尚书刑部侍郎，日阅具狱数百纸，无倦色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222934_comment'></div>至死生疑似之际，必反复加意，不啻如利害关身者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222934_comment'></div>每奏谳上前，或未当于法，必为上别白其是非，往往多见听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222934_comment'></div>否则抗论力陈，至漏下数刻，犹固争不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222934_comment'></div>以此出入省寺十馀年，坐狱事镌官者三，未尝有悔色，而全活者不可胜数，其详盖莫得而记也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222934_comment'></div>疾革，姆抱幼子侍前，麾而去之，曰：「吾起布衣，致位三品，尚何求」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222934_comment'></div>翛然无恋嫪之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222934_comment'></div>卒，年七十一，寔元符三年四月甲寅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222934_comment'></div>积官至朝散大夫，累赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222934_comment'></div>以其年十一月乙酉，葬其县东北五里平望乡雉山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222934_comment'></div>娶同邑袁氏，封永和县君，先公十五年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222934_comment'></div>三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222934_comment'></div>曰厚，从事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222934_comment'></div>曰原，朝奉郎、通判抚州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222934_comment'></div>皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222934_comment'></div>曰石，今为通直郎、知常州武进县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222934_comment'></div>女二人，嫁承议郎吕必强、显谟阁待制吕益柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222934_comment'></div>孙男女合八人，曰冲、曰凝、曰沆、曰沇、曰汜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222934_comment'></div>冲今为承议郎、知平江府常熟县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222934_comment'></div>而朝散郎曾纶、朝奉郎莫伯舆、承务郎章奎文者，其女之所适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222934_comment'></div>公清约廉平，胸中乐易，平生未尝以喜怒加人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222934_comment'></div>初，公被诬而复为使者也，陆佃给事中，格其除书不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222934_comment'></div>洎公奉使淮南，佃适为郡守，隶焉，佃不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222934_comment'></div>公至，则释怨与交欢，且阴佐其政事之不及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222934_comment'></div>既殁，佃哭之恸曰：「此公真不可以意量者，世岂复有斯人耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222934_comment'></div>乡闾寒隽，汲引尽诚，不进不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222934_comment'></div>故卒之日，知与不知，皆为之出涕，可谓厚德君子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222934_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1222934'>自古盛世，必多名卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222934_comment'></div>典刑百年，如见老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222934_comment'></div>熙宁有为，公适逢世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222934_comment'></div>以材结知，终始三帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222934_comment'></div>惟始受学，得其师承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222934_comment'></div>摅而及民，久乃济登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222934_comment'></div>出乘轺车，入秉丹笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222934_comment'></div>为邦持平，断以经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222934_comment'></div>心本忠恕，辅之敏明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222934_comment'></div>谳书满旁，为汝得生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222934_comment'></div>雷霆或愆，必犯颜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222934_comment'></div>谆谆靡回，帝屡旰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222934_comment'></div>白首三尺，跻荣近臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222934_comment'></div>能使四海，岁无冤民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222934_comment'></div>矧夫持躬，清约直谅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222934_comment'></div>不名一体，当世师仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222934_comment'></div>归閟窀穸，今兹几时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222934_comment'></div>封木岑蔚，子孙似之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222934_comment'></div>于、张之仁，天岂忘报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222934_comment'></div>镵词于阡，来者是告。</div><div id='poem_sentence_91_1222934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在徽州，为苏颂之季子携作墓志铭。作品：故徽猷阁待制致仕苏公墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222926' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222926' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故徽猷阁待制致仕苏公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222926")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222926'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222926'>苏氏自唐许公，世有人，其后分居闽之泉山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222926_comment'></div>真宗时，有讳仲昌，负文武材，召试贤良方正，属六科罢，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222926_comment'></div>既策名矣，以小失有司程度，补三班官，非其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222926_comment'></div>仕至左屯卫将军，提点荆湖南路刑狱，历知宣、邵、复三州以殁，赠太师、福国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222926_comment'></div>生绅，复举进士、贤良方正科，入翰林为学士，知河阳，年未五十而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222926_comment'></div>生颂，相哲宗，元祐间守观文殿大学士、太子太保致仕，与翰林皆赠太师、魏国公，始葬润州之丹阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222926_comment'></div>公讳携，字季升，丞相季子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222926_comment'></div>幼庄重，举止如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222926_comment'></div>丞相自开封尹知濠州，赴御史台诏狱，公年十三，随至京师，僦舍御史府前，朝夕入问起居状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222926_comment'></div>间衣举子服，诉其诬于待漏院，宰相吴正肃、王文恭见其警敏，召至前与语，奇之，事由是得白，而公亦以此知名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222926_comment'></div>用父任为瀛州防御推官，调监澶州河北仓草场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222926_comment'></div>既少年得声誉，益亲师友、力学问、为词章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222926_comment'></div>当路交荐之，复辞荐书不受，而请授同僚之贤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222926_comment'></div>故一时名士，皆屈辈行与之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222926_comment'></div>秩满，授武成军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222926_comment'></div>丁内艰，免丧监润州织罗务，会课改宣德郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222926_comment'></div>以丞相春秋高，请閒就养，得管当南京鸿庆宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222926_comment'></div>徽宗皇帝立，转通直郎，赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222926_comment'></div>丞相薨，服除，缘兄入党籍，差监兖州东岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222926_comment'></div>寻除丹阳县丞，会令阙，行令事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222926_comment'></div>陈力二年，如实为令者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222926_comment'></div>徙通判庐州，民便安之，去郡，相与遮留，为之罢市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222926_comment'></div>中丞蒋公猷荐为御史台主簿，迁光禄寺丞，改大宗正丞，尚书仓部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222926_comment'></div>经郊祀恩，赐三品服，擢卫尉少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222926_comment'></div>久之，移光禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222926_comment'></div>靖康初，寇至京师，公昼夜乘城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222926_comment'></div>素羸，不胜暴露，寇退即求去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222926_comment'></div>渊圣皇帝雅知公名，谓执政曰：「如此等人，可使之去朝廷耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222926_comment'></div>命降堂劄留之，非故事也，时以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222926_comment'></div>数月复求去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222926_comment'></div>进直龙图阁、知明州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222926_comment'></div>金人渡江，浙东西皆震，独四明罢乡兵、省科调，民恃以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222926_comment'></div>俄请奉祠而归，寻避地闽中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222926_comment'></div>以坟墓在丹阳，由海道往来闽浙间者数岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222926_comment'></div>绍兴初，召赴行在所，除宗正少卿、中书门下检正诸房公事，皆不拜，复主管临安府洞霄宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222926_comment'></div>起知温州，亦不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222926_comment'></div>召为太常少卿，力辞于朝，不可，则见上以辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222926_comment'></div>翌日，诏权尚书刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222926_comment'></div>居无何，得微疾，上章请老，除徽猷阁待制致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222926_comment'></div>数日，以不起闻，上嗟悼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222926_comment'></div>得年七十六，时绍兴十年正月九日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222926_comment'></div>积官至右朝议大夫，赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222926_comment'></div>公退然如不胜衣，与人言，惟恐伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222926_comment'></div>然刚正敏明，凡事亲、居官、治民、与人交，一出于诚，非今人可及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222926_comment'></div>所至必先问职当如何，见有利害可论，必孜孜建明，不为苟且，而卒归于忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222926_comment'></div>若摧彊去恶，则忘其身为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222926_comment'></div>其发擿奸伏如神，人不能秋毫欺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222926_comment'></div>以此自州县历台省至为侍从，五十馀年，无一事不可纪者，隐然为国名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222926_comment'></div>由嘉祐、治平以来，公卿之后能守家法者，莫公若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222926_comment'></div>官武成时，行县，吏送之郊，顾谓吏曰：「某盗二人，于情于法皆可生，胡不谳」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222926_comment'></div>吏曰：「诺」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222926_comment'></div>及归，守迎谓公曰：「官吏无赖，至擅出人于死，既曰彊盗矣，有可悯者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222926_comment'></div>幸吾二人不预也，亟治之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222926_comment'></div>公曰：「使纾此狱者，某也，某当坐耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222926_comment'></div>且为言其所以生之之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222926_comment'></div>守大怒，将并案公，公不为回，而二人卒不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222926_comment'></div>丹阳当东南舟车之冲，异时高句丽入贡，吏并缘掊取，方数百里骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222926_comment'></div>公为区处于未至前，既去，民不知其使者之尝经由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222926_comment'></div>岁饥，行赈济法，公曰：「循虚文，忘实惠，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222926_comment'></div>乃乞米于有司，有司以为难，请之再三，必得米，则朝夕临视，汲汲然惟恐其不均，虽邻邑之归者，亦受而不辞，所全活以千万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222926_comment'></div>方国家兴学校、新祠庭之时，京口号为多士，又三茅山在其提封，生徒之不逞者，凭藉为非，视州县蔑如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222926_comment'></div>公一切以法绳之，旁观为缩颈而公处之泰然，人知其不可犯也，无不屏息，丹阳大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222926_comment'></div>合肥俗喜告讦，为匿名书，至有窃乘驿以驰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222926_comment'></div>公行州事，得何人书于讼箧中，物色久之，释然悟曰：「此老吏某人所为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222926_comment'></div>立遣人捕之，则已亡去，索于田间，得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222926_comment'></div>叩头首服，寘诸法以徇，由是其书遂绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222926_comment'></div>曲院亡曲数万斤，觉，曲官与狱官通，猥归罪于持衡者，以为私其赢于酒官，因使之亡去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222926_comment'></div>公语曰：「持衡者交私，不过铢两之赢耳，能积而至数万斤乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222926_comment'></div>且负担者几何，人岂无可会之数耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222926_comment'></div>狱官不得对，果曲官纳磨户金而授之虚券，曲材未尝入也，左右大惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222926_comment'></div>仓部尝请于朝，岁漕冬初不至者，监司若州县官皆坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222926_comment'></div>吏持符请书，公袖符见长贰曰：「今兹漕至者未半也，吾符一下，坐者无虑数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222926_comment'></div>禋祀止数十日间，士大夫当得恩数者皆阁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222926_comment'></div>若稍引一两月之期，俟礼成而下，则彼将何辞」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222926_comment'></div>长贰从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222926_comment'></div>士大夫欢传曰：「苏季升仁人之言也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222926_comment'></div>建炎赦至，明州戍卒数百人还，据地求卸甲钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222926_comment'></div>公大怒，叱去，而阴勒牙兵为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222926_comment'></div>未及门，果噪而还，趋库授甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222926_comment'></div>公不为动，徐禽为首者数人戮之，而置其馀不问，一州为之肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1222926_comment'></div>盖公之过人者，类皆如此，难以一二记也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1222926_comment'></div>公虽精于吏事，而未尝一日去书不观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1222926_comment'></div>有文集五卷，尤长于诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1222926_comment'></div>韩驹、崔鶠，以诗名者，每读公诗，曰：「苏季升未尝言诗也，每一篇出，高妙敷腴，吾不能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1222926_comment'></div>古人不以多为贵者，其谓是乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1222926_comment'></div>初娶元氏，章简公绛之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1222926_comment'></div>次娶曾氏，资政殿学士孝序之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1222926_comment'></div>继室复以其妹，相敬如宾，四十馀年，后公月馀卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1222926_comment'></div>皆封恭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1222926_comment'></div>子孟容，右修职郎、两浙路转运司干办公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1222926_comment'></div>孙箴，登仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1222926_comment'></div>公卒之五月，孟容奉公葬于镇江府丹阳县长冈之原，以曾恭人祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1222926_comment'></div>藻从公游最久，得公之典刑名理非一，会孟容来速铭，义不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1222926_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_1222926'>苏氏胙许，繇唐迄今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1222926_comment'></div>蝉联再兴，实始翰林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1222926_comment'></div>绵庆既远，乃生魏公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1222926_comment'></div>辅佐泰陵，功名始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1222926_comment'></div>帝想风烈，聿求其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1222926_comment'></div>曰汝是似，为吾近臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1222926_comment'></div>似之伊何，忠孝直清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1222926_comment'></div>流辈尽矣，岿然老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1222926_comment'></div>入侍禁严，于祢有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1222926_comment'></div>年及黄发，祉非不长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1222926_comment'></div>无缺亏者，人胡叹嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1222926_comment'></div>岂德之厚，报犹未遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1222926_comment'></div>大江西来，龟筮叶占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1222926_comment'></div>万古之宅，先茔是瞻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_106_1222926_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　在徽州，封新安郡侯，上谢表。作品：谢除授新安郡侯表。<div id='poem_1222663' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222663' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222663?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢授新安郡侯表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222663")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222663_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222663'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222663'>臣藻言：准告命，伏蒙圣恩，以宗祀赦文授臣新安郡开国侯，加食邑三百户者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222663_comment'></div>礼洽中天，庆覃外服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222663_comment'></div>猥奉十行之诏，就加五等之封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222663_comment'></div>伏念臣积冒恩私，寖踰分愿，昨投閒于异县，蒙起废于偏城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222663_comment'></div>久客还家，方憩南飞之鹊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222663_comment'></div>通侯授印，忽成左顾之龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222663_comment'></div>虽渗漉以维均，何遭逢之独异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222663_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下调和万类，藩饰群工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222663_comment'></div>属宣室之受釐，罄寰区而蒙福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222663_comment'></div>臣适临本郡，仍胙乡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222663_comment'></div>宋人洴澼以得封，望胡及此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222663_comment'></div>汉将银黄而誇里，荣乃过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222663_comment'></div>宠既逮于子孙，忠敢移于生死？</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1222663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222663'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三二，《唐宋元名表》卷下之二，《新安文献志》卷四○，《文章辨体汇选》卷一三八，弘治《徽州府志》卷一一，《宋四六选》卷八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222663_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年</a>　守徽期间，有诗。作品：徽州班春古岩寺呈诸僚友。<div id='poem_528269' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528269' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528269?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽州班春古岩寺呈诸僚友</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528269")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528269_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528269'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528269'>揆日奉明诏，班春出孤城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528269'>和风递鼓鼙，细雨迷旆旌。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528269'>渺渺度阡陌，溪山照人明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528269'>幽花不孤芳，好鸟相应鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528269'>陇麦已争秀，畦秧亦微萌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528269'>食新知有期，及我凋瘵氓。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528269'>古寺依绝壁，林端列飞甍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528269'>残僧四五人，静若无所营。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528269'>石室广百肘，嵌空自天成。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528269'>泉甘与茶宜，就挹岩下清。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528269'>伏槛肆遐瞩，归云入檐楹。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528269'>数农前致辞，貌野意则诚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_528269'>兹幸枉冠盖，使君岂无情。<div id='poem_sentence_12_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_528269'>频年苦饥虚，奚用恤此生。<div id='poem_sentence_13_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_528269'>守昔在闾里，先畴每躬耕。<div id='poem_sentence_14_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_528269'>起家三绝馀，谬忝符竹荣。<div id='poem_sentence_15_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_528269'>无术布宽大，低头愧鳏茕。<div id='poem_sentence_16_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_528269'>愿言同抚绥，永绝愁叹声。<div id='poem_sentence_17_528269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_528269'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_528269_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年7月11日</a>　在徽州。汪藻上启贺秦桧加少保。作品：贺秦少保启。<div id='poem_1222842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺秦少保启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年7月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222842")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222842'>伏颁明诏，登用大儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222842_comment'></div>疏荣三少之班，正位百官之上，生成所及，鼓舞斯同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222842_comment'></div>恭以某官言合六经，学包万古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222842_comment'></div>由周公传之孔子，独承师友之渊源；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222842_comment'></div>惟尹躬暨于成汤，迩应君臣之期会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222842_comment'></div>久借本兵之重，多输纳诲之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222842_comment'></div>方功名未究于经纶，举中外皆形之叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222842_comment'></div>盖文物于斯为盛，欲平治舍公其谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222842_comment'></div>故除书甫降于九天，而和气遂化于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222842_comment'></div>某辱邀知遇，叨被使令，逢恩宠之鼎新，预生灵之均播。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222842_comment'></div>虽官联在远，莫能陪多士之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222842_comment'></div>然谣俗至公，当播作《烝民》之雅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222842_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
福州
-----detail
