-----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c8f59362c5214402a3c45d8225c43d3c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c8f59362c5214402a3c45d8225c43d3c");'><span id='c8f59362c5214402a3c45d8225c43d3c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>，65岁</div><div id='c8f59362c5214402a3c45d8225c43d3c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年10月21日</a>　提举江州太平兴国宫，永州居住。上谢表。作品：谢谪永州居住表。<div id='poem_1222680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢谪永州居住表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年10月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222680")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222680'>孱愚冒宠，久仰日月之光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222680_comment'></div>盈满挻灾，自处雷霆之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222680_comment'></div>蒙圣恩之宽大，与善地以生全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222680_comment'></div>罪大心寒，感深涕落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222680_comment'></div>伏念臣初无称道，积有悔尤，所当退养于疲癃，乃复寖成于老悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222680_comment'></div>忽闻威命，适在穷途，冒风雪以疾驰，越江湖而跧伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222680_comment'></div>非恃冕旒之察，难逃鈇钺之诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222680_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下刚健法天，聪明稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222680_comment'></div>干戈不用，再臻全胜之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222680_comment'></div>刑赏何心，一付至公之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222680_comment'></div>而臣靡思兢慎，仰负函容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222680_comment'></div>瓶居井眉，虽有措身之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222680_comment'></div>孤正丘首，未知归骨之期。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1222680_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1222680'><span class='label'>按：</span>《浮溪集》卷五。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷三三，《唐宋元名表》卷下之二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1222680_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　冒风雪前往永州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　本年，为陈兖作墓志铭。作品：右中奉大夫直徽猷阁知潭州陈君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222927' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222927' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222927?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右中奉大夫直徽猷阁知潭州陈君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十三年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222927")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222927_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222927'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222927'>君讳兖，字景渊，姓陈氏，世家阆中，昭陵宰相文惠公尧佐之曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222927_comment'></div>文惠事具国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222927_comment'></div>生述古，为正议大夫，赠少师，于君为祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222927_comment'></div>生知祥，为朝奉大夫、知德州，赠宣奉大夫，于君为父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222927_comment'></div>君少英发机警，方事纷糅，诸老生未能言之时，已洞然了其微处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222927_comment'></div>及出语，人皆厌服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222927_comment'></div>以父任为陈州商水县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222927_comment'></div>知隆德府潞城县，县胥为奸利，持前令短长告郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222927_comment'></div>郡守惑之，君调护令使善去，而寘胥于法，闻者快之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222927_comment'></div>以亲嫌，移滑州韦城县，改宣教郎、通判常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222927_comment'></div>盗发清溪，浙西诸郡皆震，常当其冲，君亲属夫增陴浚隍，盗知有备不敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222927_comment'></div>宣抚司上其状，迁承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222927_comment'></div>坐小法免，起主管西外宗室财用，提举福建路市舶，通判大原府漳州，皆不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222927_comment'></div>寻通判泗州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222927_comment'></div>时金人寇京师，泗居东南咽喉地，邮传不通者百馀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222927_comment'></div>盗王嗣拥众数万将及城，君白守收民入保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222927_comment'></div>民玩安不知兵，坌入君舍，谋为乱，君正色折之，众逡巡引去，而围亦解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222927_comment'></div>顷之，淮桥戍卒与李丞相纲所留兵无虑万五千人，寓城中，守以无储，懔懔然欲亡去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222927_comment'></div>君请五日除其忧，即夙夜营度，如其所须饷之，逮元帅府檄书至，乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222927_comment'></div>擢尚书膳部员外郎，积劳至朝散大夫、知通州，迁朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222927_comment'></div>通既远行朝，守兵单外无援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222927_comment'></div>金大帅引兵十馀万环之，君先士卒捍城，至食水藻四十馀日，卒使不能近城而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222927_comment'></div>通人德之，家绘君像以祠，饮食必祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222927_comment'></div>后数年复过之，则父老迎君境上，罗拜马前十馀里不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222927_comment'></div>未几，宣抚使周望提兵屯姑苏，与通夹江而军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222927_comment'></div>江北人岁以薪贸江南米，至是宣抚司遮之不得渡，淮人大饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222927_comment'></div>君请会籴于福山，且籍城中能食者日给之，通人滋以为德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222927_comment'></div>擢直秘阁、淮南路转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222927_comment'></div>以分镇，请宫祠，得主管江州太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222927_comment'></div>除广南西路转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222927_comment'></div>会宣谕使明橐询民间利病，君请罢州之为寨者四，置栅者三，废栅者二，并请置检察官以收鬻盐之利，罢免丁钱以招材武之人，毁七星寨以防敌人对垒之奸，岭南人便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222927_comment'></div>复主管江州太平观，改差两浙西路安抚大使司参谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222927_comment'></div>大使司罢，召赴行在者再，迁朝议大夫、三京等路招抚处置使参谋，迁右中奉大夫，除淮南东路转运使，进直敷文阁、知扬州，赐紫衣金鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222927_comment'></div>君至维扬，帑庾无一钱一缕一粒之储，而负公私逋者万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222927_comment'></div>居无何，两朝议和，邻使往来相属，太母奉梓宫还阙，当供亿者复万计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222927_comment'></div>君不请于朝，不取于民，上下充给，流民之归者亦数万口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222927_comment'></div>异时典方面而长于理财者，皆推君之为，自以为不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222927_comment'></div>进直徽猷阁、知潭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222927_comment'></div>君之得长沙也，训词甚宠，思所以报上者，将种种加意，一路八州之人，亦想见其风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222927_comment'></div>然到官而君病矣，一日视事如平时，忽持脉曰：「吾其不起乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222927_comment'></div>以绍兴十三年七月丁卯，卒于官，年五十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222927_comment'></div>君精明勤俭，居官有大过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222927_comment'></div>凡陈请于朝，必为可久无穷之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222927_comment'></div>不媮安于目前，不规合于时好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222927_comment'></div>善任人，明于财计，下有奸伏，发之如神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222927_comment'></div>故数经艰危，及当大事，无不谈笑而办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222927_comment'></div>加以持己廉平，经宗祀恩，不任其孙而任其从兄之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222927_comment'></div>丞相杜充守建康，金人猝至，其属陈兴宗以金一箧委君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222927_comment'></div>已而兴宗陷敌中，君辗转贼间，宁舍己橐而保兴宗之金，访其子归之，人以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222927_comment'></div>娶胡氏，文恭公宿之曾孙，封令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222927_comment'></div>二男四女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222927_comment'></div>男曰兴祖，右从事郎，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222927_comment'></div>曰绍祖，右迪功郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222927_comment'></div>君为帅时，皆以恩书写机宜文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222927_comment'></div>女适迪功郎王拯，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222927_comment'></div>一孙曰注，未官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222927_comment'></div>绍祖以其年十月壬寅，葬君衡州衡阳县慕石乡石门里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222927_comment'></div>藻与君游最旧，且君无恙时，若欲得余文传之不朽者，会绍祖来乞铭，不得而辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222927_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1222927'>土之发身，惟志与才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222927_comment'></div>得时得年，又奚足哀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222927_comment'></div>呜呼景渊，有是三者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222927_comment'></div>独于其年，天不之假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222927_comment'></div>在昔文惠，克勤王家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222927_comment'></div>再传及君，大振厥华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222927_comment'></div>少而激昂，晚益精敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222927_comment'></div>如临霜空，忽见孤隼，盘错必用，所临有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222927_comment'></div>凡今立朝，谁踰仲卿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222927_comment'></div>精神折冲，未老而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222927_comment'></div>君何存亡，哀此人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222927_comment'></div>奄宅异县，祝融之峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222927_comment'></div>后人过之，尚式其封。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1222927_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　本年，为侄汪恺作墓志铭。作品：左朝请大夫知全州汪君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左朝请大夫知全州汪君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十三年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1143年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222937")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222937'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222937'>新安汪氏，见于隋末唐初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222937_comment'></div>五季之乱，有自黄墩徙婺源者，以赀雄饶、歙间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222937_comment'></div>数世而至君之高祖讳某，擢进士第，起家为秘书丞，赠光禄少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222937_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，官至尚书都官员外郎，赠中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222937_comment'></div>祖讳某，官至奉议郎，赠少傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222937_comment'></div>三世踵相蹑登进士第，世有清德，为江南闻家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222937_comment'></div>皇考讳槃，少傅长子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222937_comment'></div>以少傅春秋高，就养左右不求仕，而纵其弟藻于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222937_comment'></div>藻复与君连取科第，里人荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222937_comment'></div>皇考以君赠大中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222937_comment'></div>君讳恺，字伯强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222937_comment'></div>少奇颖浑厚，甫冠，为有司所推，入太学为诸生，有能文声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222937_comment'></div>绍圣四年，解褐调常州晋陵县主簿，用荐者升通仕郎、为宣州太平县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222937_comment'></div>坐小法免，授岳州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222937_comment'></div>丁大中忧，服除监泗州军资库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222937_comment'></div>会盐筴兴，朝廷选君监泰州海安镇盐场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222937_comment'></div>课最，改宣义郎、知淮阳军宿迁、宣州宁国县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222937_comment'></div>丁太硕人王氏忧，服除添差通判饶州，除知常州、汉阳军、吉州，未行，移处州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222937_comment'></div>到官未几，复移知抚州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222937_comment'></div>期年请奉祠，得主管江州太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222937_comment'></div>秩满，起知袁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222937_comment'></div>于是资政殿学士叶梦得、给事中胡交修以十科善治财赋荐君，擢提举两浙东路盐香、江南西路转运判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222937_comment'></div>莅事两月，除知江州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222937_comment'></div>请奉祠，得主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222937_comment'></div>久之，起知全州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222937_comment'></div>君之官簿如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222937_comment'></div>岳州平江民以竞渡斗死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222937_comment'></div>狱上于州，守恶令，欲深探其狱，株连数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222937_comment'></div>时大暑，牢户皆满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222937_comment'></div>君止系其当罪者数人，馀悉平反出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222937_comment'></div>守大怒，君引法力争，守不能屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222937_comment'></div>太平有为五斗米道者，相传能致雷雨，迕者立死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222937_comment'></div>县檄尉捕，尉辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222937_comment'></div>君不俟众，躬造其庐，人为君惧，卒禽之置于法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222937_comment'></div>靖康初，朝廷诏令未通，饶州酒官郝升者，出军伍，怙勇挟奸，持郡短长，郡守不能制而深怨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222937_comment'></div>会盗侵旁郡，举城皆奔，升之子亦佩剑出城，为关吏所录，守即诬以叛，并共械于狱，将斩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222937_comment'></div>君曰：「急装时以刀剑自卫，人情也，可尽诛乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222937_comment'></div>持之数日，升与其子皆免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222937_comment'></div>君之将如处州也，敌已至会稽，人皆劝君毋行，君不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222937_comment'></div>既而溃兵四集，君求所以绥驭之术，至不解衣而寝者两月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222937_comment'></div>寻移抚州，未行间，王𤫉、马俊兵入属邑，州之南北数百里皆震，新守入境不敢行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222937_comment'></div>民挽留君，君曰：「此吾心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222937_comment'></div>乃调护其众，使出疆，而民初不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222937_comment'></div>未一月，盗宫仪焚处州，于是人人思君，至于感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222937_comment'></div>抚州民许以女归其邻久矣，既而悔之，一日白官，女死于兵半年，请公署为异日之信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222937_comment'></div>君立械其人于狱，僚属愕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222937_comment'></div>君笑曰：「女诚死，不白官也，必女家不良，其父欲盗吾判耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222937_comment'></div>请为诸君致其女」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222937_comment'></div>明日而女果出，人以为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222937_comment'></div>绍兴十二年八月某甲子，以疾卒于饶州德兴县所居之第，春秋七十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222937_comment'></div>积官至左朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222937_comment'></div>君刻意学问，欲直造作者之域，而不乐为科举之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222937_comment'></div>未第时，见秦少游于括苍，少游奇其文，以手书勉之，然未尝引以自名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222937_comment'></div>平居孝友清修，日以慕古人、追前辈为事，循循然有德君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222937_comment'></div>及守官临民，则精明刚正，人不能欺，亦不能夺，而卒归于忠厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222937_comment'></div>方大中无恙时，承数世清德之后，家贫不能自如，君之所以养志周旋者，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222937_comment'></div>时二妹未行，大中以为忧，君继纳两妇，皆公卿大家，乃尽举其嫁时衣珥分遣之，不名一钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222937_comment'></div>及官至五品，遇恩当任子，而首任其弟，人以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222937_comment'></div>先是君恬于进取，数免稀迁，居閒之日多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222937_comment'></div>洎大中与太硕人弃诸孤，家徒四壁立，无置锥可耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222937_comment'></div>君合兄弟数房，同食其所得之俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222937_comment'></div>他人见之，若不堪其忧，而君绝甘分少，于长幼亲疏必均，未尝以一介取诸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222937_comment'></div>客至，饭蔬相对，清淡终日，出于至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222937_comment'></div>乃并其家仆隶儿童，亦怡然无不满之色，可谓贤也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222937_comment'></div>故卒之日，无不出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222937_comment'></div>凡三娶：初室吕氏，次蒋氏，次李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222937_comment'></div>朝散郎、赠通奉大夫吕全、宣德郎蒋珍、中散大夫李演之女，而观文殿学士蒋之奇、枢密使李咨之孙也，皆封宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222937_comment'></div>三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222937_comment'></div>曰尧举，右迪功郎、铸钱司催纲官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222937_comment'></div>曰舜举，右修职郎、漳州龙岩县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222937_comment'></div>曰仲举，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222937_comment'></div>一女，适进士俞允恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1222937_comment'></div>尧举等以十三年十二月丁酉，奉君葬饶州德兴县龙溪源少傅墓南三里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1222937_comment'></div>藻虽于君为诸父，而少君九岁，少同学，长同仕也，是宜为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1222937_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1222937'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1222937_comment'></div>人皆乐其所忧，而君独忧其所乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1222937_comment'></div>人皆丰其所约，而君独约其所丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1222937_comment'></div>以孝友纯诚懋其本，以康宁寿祺赍其终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1222937_comment'></div>故所居人慕之，所莅民思之，无秋毫愧怍于其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1222937_comment'></div>盖古之德人，今之循吏也，尚千万年，勿毁其宫。</div><div id='poem_sentence_79_1222937_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f7d22c4427b545a2a4a8a3ac81d73552_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f7d22c4427b545a2a4a8a3ac81d73552");'><span id='f7d22c4427b545a2a4a8a3ac81d73552_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1154')">1144-1154年</a>，66-76岁</div><div id='f7d22c4427b545a2a4a8a3ac81d73552' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　春，抵达永州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　李正民有诗慰之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在永州，为谭章作墓志铭。作品：谭章墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谭章墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十四年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222952")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222952'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222952'>长沙有隐君子，行义如古人，生子为国忠臣，飨耆龄而终，曰右朝奉大夫致仕谭君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222952_comment'></div>讳章，字焕之，其先衡阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222952_comment'></div>四世祖徙家洞庭，过长沙昭潭而爱之，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222952_comment'></div>曾祖裕、祖映、父盛，三世居乡，称善人长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222952_comment'></div>盛用子恩，赠朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222952_comment'></div>君隐居昭潭六十馀年，专以求志为事，孝于亲，诚于物，视听起居，必依于礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222952_comment'></div>故修之身而家齐，家齐而人化其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222952_comment'></div>平居读书，大而六经，小而诸子百家，与夫天文、地理、星历、山经、释老氏之学，无不周览而求其义之所归，不为诸生循诵习传而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222952_comment'></div>故历代治乱兴衰之所由，人材善恶忠邪之所判，祖宗以来因革罢行之所纪，悉贯穿商榷，亹亹牙颊间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222952_comment'></div>稠人广众，纵谈极辩，听者忘倦，倾其坐人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222952_comment'></div>发为诗文，高古精深，根于义理，无补于世者，未尝落笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222952_comment'></div>于是方数百里间，有识者君教之使学，有材者君养之使成，不能仰事俯育者，君振之使给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222952_comment'></div>所施之博，至不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222952_comment'></div>邻里之讼有不能决者，不之官府而之君，人尊仰之，甚于父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222952_comment'></div>有老人黄升贷君钱百万，行而遇盗，尽亡之，归谢于君，君曰：「几累吾故人，今生还幸矣，尚何言」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222952_comment'></div>升感之，为文纪其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222952_comment'></div>君少时儆敏，人莫能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222952_comment'></div>为文立成，视取科第若摘髭拾芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222952_comment'></div>然一旦以亲老不可远游，尽以所得之学付其子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222952_comment'></div>由是弟申、子世绩，皆擢进士第，显于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222952_comment'></div>中遭靖康之变，君恸哭，一目为丧明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222952_comment'></div>时世绩为尚书礼部侍郎，数以书勉其忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222952_comment'></div>故世绩当僭伪时，力起之，不从，至不食，幽愤而死，朝廷嘉之，赠延康殿学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222952_comment'></div>讣闻，君叹曰：「吾子得死所矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222952_comment'></div>不胜父子之情者，一己之私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222952_comment'></div>为国尽节死者，天下之公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222952_comment'></div>吾安得舍此取彼哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222952_comment'></div>昔蔺相如、廉颇死向千载，凛凛然尚有生气；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222952_comment'></div>曹㻌、李志虽无恙，奄奄如九原下人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222952_comment'></div>重轻知所处矣，吾何恨哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222952_comment'></div>乃雪涕欣然自庆，不复戚戚于怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222952_comment'></div>后延康之殁十有八年，寿八十六，无疾而终，寔绍兴十四年四月某甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222952_comment'></div>君以世绩恩，累封至右朝奉大夫，赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222952_comment'></div>妻龚氏，亦儒家女，有贤行，封宜人，前君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222952_comment'></div>子二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222952_comment'></div>曰世绩，延康君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222952_comment'></div>曰世南，未冠而夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222952_comment'></div>女一人，适进士胡扩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222952_comment'></div>孙二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222952_comment'></div>曰知古，右承事郎、荆湖南路安抚司干办公事，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222952_comment'></div>曰知默，右宣义郎、守太府寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222952_comment'></div>曾孙四人，曰式祖、曰述祖、曰企祖、曰昭祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222952_comment'></div>式祖，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222952_comment'></div>君卒之若干日，得十月甲申，合葬君于其县潭子冈龚宜人之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222952_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1222952'>衡山峻极连潇湘，中有君子潜德光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222952_comment'></div>闭关求志闻四方，群书万卷胸次藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222952_comment'></div>上谈羲农下汉唐，诸儒结舌莫敢当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222952_comment'></div>遭时天地纷低昂，有子夙在人主旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222952_comment'></div>浩然之气大且刚，节义凛凛明秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222952_comment'></div>杀身成仁圣所臧，庆门万古传芬芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222952_comment'></div>天相吉人宜寿康，庞眉岁举春酒觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222952_comment'></div>归安窀穸川之阳，潭流要与兹川长。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1222952_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在永州，为刘峤作墓志铭。作品：左朝散大夫直徽猷阁刘君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222929' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222929' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222929?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左朝散大夫直徽猷阁刘君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴八年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1144年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222929")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222929_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222929'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222929'>君讳峤，字仲高，吴兴刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222929_comment'></div>吴兴之刘，其传盖远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222929_comment'></div>熙宁间有讳述、知御史杂事者，正色立朝，与宰相争是非，宰相盛怒，至欲逮治之，不为屈，卒夺御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222929_comment'></div>司马温公称其道胜名立，东坡苏公为之赋《吴兴丈人》之诗，一时名士，慕而宗之，所谓刘孝叔是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222929_comment'></div>于是吴兴之刘闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222929_comment'></div>卒官尚书吏部郎中，累赠金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222929_comment'></div>中兴，又特授秘阁修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222929_comment'></div>生握，为朝请大夫，赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222929_comment'></div>通议生钦止，为承务郎，赠通奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222929_comment'></div>生君，皆世其家而有贤子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222929_comment'></div>君少以文名，端方厚重，不妄交游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222929_comment'></div>范忠宣之子正平，凛然有二父风，君从之数年，尽得其学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222929_comment'></div>由是操修益进，贤于人益远，为乡里所尊，闻其行于朝，擢政和五年上舍高弟，除陈州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222929_comment'></div>丁内艰，免丧调监尉氏税，非其好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222929_comment'></div>会徽猷阁待制赵公鼎臣镇邓，闻君名，辟司仪曹事，一府高其文，部使者交荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222929_comment'></div>居无何，争进者比而谗君，君推其能于人，一不之校，人皆服君长者，而谗者反愧谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222929_comment'></div>君迁宣教郎、睦亲广亲南北宅大教授，历开封府仪曹少监、少府少监、尚书比部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222929_comment'></div>君为郎六年，阅辈流登台省者无虑数百人，未尝以荣滞关怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222929_comment'></div>当国者贤之，擢大理少卿、枢密院检详诸房文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222929_comment'></div>出，提点福建路刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222929_comment'></div>君内为廷尉，外为绣衣直指，于决谳重轻必平反曲折，得其情而后已，不以爰书诿吏，故中外翕然称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222929_comment'></div>使闽时，尉诬民为盗，帅幸尉迁，力主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222929_comment'></div>君知其冤，引囚物色非是，释囚而黜尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222929_comment'></div>帅，贵人也，不悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222929_comment'></div>会贵人还朝，君知其憾不释，力丐奉祠，得提点洪州玉隆观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222929_comment'></div>居数年，以疾请老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222929_comment'></div>卒，年六十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222929_comment'></div>积官至左朝散大夫、直徽猷阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222929_comment'></div>时绍兴八年三月某甲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222929_comment'></div>初室信安郑氏，继室开封朱氏，皆封恭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222929_comment'></div>二男子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222929_comment'></div>曰坰，右迪功郎、怀宁县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222929_comment'></div>曰瀼，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222929_comment'></div>一女子，未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222929_comment'></div>一孙，曰某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222929_comment'></div>坰等以其年八月某甲子，葬乌程县某乡某山之原，以郑恭人祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222929_comment'></div>君同产三人，长曰崧伯高，仲即君，其季前吏部侍郎岑季高也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222929_comment'></div>君事伯高如父，而季高又以君之所以事伯高者事君，兄弟之懿，士大夫谈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222929_comment'></div>伯高少旷达，不以世务经心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222929_comment'></div>通奉公早世，母夫人嫠居而贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222929_comment'></div>君于内外干蛊之责，与郑恭人分任之，而遂伯高于閒适，以宽太夫人之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222929_comment'></div>及伯高疾废，药必亲尝，饮食必亲馈，以终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222929_comment'></div>故君之卒，季高哭之，过时而哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222929_comment'></div>既葬，季高知君与藻善也，来求铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222929_comment'></div>会藻以语言得罪，斥居南荒三千里潇水之上，焚笔砚不复为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222929_comment'></div>而季高每书必以铭为言，諰諰然惟恐君之不得其传也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222929_comment'></div>藻于是为之太息曰：嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222929_comment'></div>季高尽诚于君，固今人所无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222929_comment'></div>然能使季高不能忘君如此，则君平日所以处兄弟之间者于此见矣，铭其可已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222929_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1222929'>嗟仲高，名一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222929_comment'></div>学精深，行尤异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222929_comment'></div>位九卿，非不试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222929_comment'></div>车方驰，忽思税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222929_comment'></div>归里闾，友兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222929_comment'></div>合埙篪，为乐地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222929_comment'></div>谓当还，以经侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222929_comment'></div>甲子周，奄然蜕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222929_comment'></div>相山川，考龟筮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222929_comment'></div>望先茔，窆于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222929_comment'></div>刻幽堂，诏来裔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1222929_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年1月1日</a>　元旦，上贺表。作品：绍兴十五年元会贺表。<div id='poem_1222628' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222628' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222628?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绍兴十五年元会贺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222628")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222628_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222628'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222628'>接千岁之统，方启昌期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222628_comment'></div>盛九宾之仪，大朝献岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222628_comment'></div>会簪缨于率土，瞻旒扆于中天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222628_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下，道冠群伦，泽流亿世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222628_comment'></div>天休滋至，知受命之惟新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222628_comment'></div>治具毕张，见修文之益备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222628_comment'></div>臣久尘法从，叨领真祠，闻盛典之复行，与群情而交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222628_comment'></div>受四海之籍，遥企于垂衣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222628_comment'></div>奉万年之觞，莫陪于舞手。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1222628_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　有吴国太夫人赞。<div id='poem_1222915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴国太夫人赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222915")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222915'>宝文阁直学士贾谠母，吴国太夫人王氏者，秦王审琦五世孙，而显恭皇后之姑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222915_comment'></div>精修乐施，终身如一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222915_comment'></div>建炎二年，随谠至金陵，薨焉，菆于城北正觉寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222915_comment'></div>会有司以其地为元懿太子坟堧，谠欲举夫人葬零陵，不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222915_comment'></div>绍兴十五年，始得请启菆，棺衾腐败，巾屦杯圈，触之埃散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222915_comment'></div>独夫人面如生，肩而下异蔓覆之若铢衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222915_comment'></div>及易棺衾，香闻数十步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222915_comment'></div>金陵倾国都而出，焚香作礼，曰：「善哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222915_comment'></div>非夫人愿力所成不及此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222915_comment'></div>于是藻为之赞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1222915'>夫人生王家，具足诸福慧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222915_comment'></div>珍宝千百亿，视之如微尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222915_comment'></div>倾以饭伊蒲，了无留吝色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222915_comment'></div>用檀波罗蜜，精进终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222915_comment'></div>窆于给孤园，经十八寒暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222915_comment'></div>彼物皆朽坏，而吾面如生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222915_comment'></div>爪眉齿发肤，以至脂泽等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222915_comment'></div>光润柔软相，与生亦无殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222915_comment'></div>宝花绸缪之，芬馥世希有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222915_comment'></div>坐遣诸草木，悉成旃檀林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222915_comment'></div>云何劫灰馀，有此殊胜事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222915_comment'></div>谁非幻泡影，独现金刚身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222915_comment'></div>一时生信心，见者及闻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222915_comment'></div>极无边无量，数等恒河沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222915_comment'></div>由兹證菩提，是名为说法。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1222915_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　居永州期间，自肆于山水，遍访柳宗元遗迹。撰《永州柳先生祠堂记》<div id='poem_1222895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永州柳先生祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222895")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222895'>先生以永贞元年冬，自尚书郎出为邵州刺史，道贬永州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222895_comment'></div>至元和九年十二月，诏追赴都，复出为柳州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222895_comment'></div>盖先生居零陵者将十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222895_comment'></div>至今言先生者，必曰零陵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222895_comment'></div>言零陵者，亦必曰先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222895_comment'></div>零陵去长安四千馀里，极穷陋之区也，而先生辱居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222895_comment'></div>零陵徒以先生居之之故，遂名闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222895_comment'></div>在先生谓不幸可也，而零陵独非幸欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222895_comment'></div>先生始居龙兴寺西序之下，间坐法华西亭，见西山，爱之，命仆夫过潇水，剪薙榛芜，搜奇选胜，自放于山水之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222895_comment'></div>入冉溪二三里，得尤绝者家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222895_comment'></div>因结茅树蔬，为沼沚台榭，目曰「愚溪」，而刻《八愚诗》于溪石之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222895_comment'></div>其谓之钴鉧潭西小丘、小石潭者，循愚溪而出也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222895_comment'></div>其谓之南涧、朝阳岩、袁家渴、芜江、百家濑者，溯潇水而上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222895_comment'></div>皆在愚溪数里间，为先生杖履徜徉之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222895_comment'></div>惟黄溪为最远，去郡城七十馀里，游者未尝到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222895_comment'></div>则岂先生好奇如谢康乐，伐木开径，穷山水之趣，而亦游之不数耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222895_comment'></div>绍兴十四年，予来零陵，距先生三百馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222895_comment'></div>求先生遗迹，如愚溪、钴鉧潭、南涧、朝阳岩之类皆在，独龙兴寺并先生故居曰「愚堂」、「愚亭」者，已湮芜不可复识，《八愚诗》石亦访之无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222895_comment'></div>黄溪则为峒獠侵耕，嶝危径塞，无自而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222895_comment'></div>郡人指高山寺口，此法华亭故处，而龙兴者，今太平寺西瞰大江者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222895_comment'></div>其果然欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222895_comment'></div>周衰，言文章之盛者，莫如汉唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222895_comment'></div>贾谊驰骋于孝文之初，时汉兴才三十馀年耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222895_comment'></div>其谈治道、述骚辞，已追还三代之风如此，自是踵相蹑有之，末而至于刘向、扬雄，益精深不可及，去古未远故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222895_comment'></div>唐承贞观、开元习治之馀，以文章显者，如陈子昂、萧颍士、李邕、燕、许之徒，固不为无人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222895_comment'></div>东汉以来，猥井之气未除也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222895_comment'></div>至元和，始粹然一返于正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222895_comment'></div>其所以臻此者，非先生及昌黎韩公之力欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222895_comment'></div>故以唐三百年世所推尊者，曰韩、柳而已，岂非盛哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222895_comment'></div>先生虽坐贞元党，与刘梦得同，梦得会昌时犹尊显于朝，先生未及为时君所省，而遽殁于元和之世，事业遂不大见于时，可深惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222895_comment'></div>然零陵一泉石、一草木经先生品题者，莫不为后世所慕，想见其风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222895_comment'></div>而先生之文载集中，凡瑰奇绝特者，皆居零陵时所作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222895_comment'></div>则予所谓幸不幸者，岂不然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222895_comment'></div>零陵之祠先生于学、于愚溪之上，更郡守不知其几，而莫之敢废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222895_comment'></div>顾未有求其遗迹而纪之者，余于是采先生之集与刘梦得之诗可见者，书而置之祠中，附《零陵图志》之末，庶几来者有考焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1222895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　居永州期间，常与知永州熊彦诗游。汪藻有文。作品：熊叔雅砚铭。回永州太守熊郎中启。<div id='poem_1222910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>熊叔雅砚铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222910")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222910'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222910'>禹凿馀，韬瘴岚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222910_comment'></div>安得之？虹贯岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222910_comment'></div>斲为泓，携北南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222910_comment'></div>毛褚陈，其友三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222910_comment'></div>出瑰辞，与古参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222910_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1222910_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1222812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回永州太守熊郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222812")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222812'>里闬相闻，何止十年之旧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222812_comment'></div>朝班并进，幸成数面之亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222812_comment'></div>洎来作于湘累，遂莫陪于郑驲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222812_comment'></div>孰云冯子之埽轨，适遇文翁之剖符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222812_comment'></div>伏惟知府郎中古学精深，天才卓越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222812_comment'></div>嗣韦平之世业，大振厥华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222812_comment'></div>决晁董之贤科，屡为之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222812_comment'></div>碑版流传于四裔，词章凌跨于三都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222812_comment'></div>早跻郎选之高，忽倾使华之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222812_comment'></div>相如入蜀，宣诏旨于蛮夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222812_comment'></div>梦得还朝，寄诗情于草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222812_comment'></div>未荷从臣之橐，姑乘刺史之轓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222812_comment'></div>宁容坐席之温，即有追锋之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222812_comment'></div>惟兹衰朽，久矣飘零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222812_comment'></div>生异贾生，敢临流而吊屈？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222812_comment'></div>情同王粲，方去国以依刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222812_comment'></div>念欲驰笺，遽蒙颁教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222812_comment'></div>望旌麾而倍感，穷笔舌以奚殚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222812_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1222812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　居永州期间，常与知永州熊彦诗游。汪藻有诗多首与之唱和。作品：藻蒙叔雅祠部重九日惠花惠酒惠诗，继为袁家碣钴鉧潭之游，因循不能答，再称佳句见寄，今用来韵率课一篇参陪杖履之胜，幸一笑而去之，以覆酱瓯而作纸绞也。次韵熊使君登楼感秋之作。熊使君次韵见属次韵答之。东安许明府同里之亲任满回家求诗为别即席赋此兼简熊使君。熊使君次韵。熊使君垂和漫兴诗次答四首。次零陵太守竟秀堂韵四首。浴孙日熊叔雅有诗次其韵二首。<div id='poem_528265' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528265' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528265?labeling=true' target='_blank'>藻蒙叔雅祠部重九日惠花惠酒惠诗继为袁家碣钴鉧潭之游因循不能答再承佳句见寄今用来韵率课一篇参陪杖履之胜幸一笑而去之以覆酱瓿而作纸绞也</a><span class='authorDate'>（1145年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528265")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528265_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528265'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528265'>秋风入潇湘，千嶂倚天外。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528265'>使君挽衰翁，行乐秋色界。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528265'>放船下空阔，舒笑凫鹥会。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528265'>永怀愚溪人，千载有遗爱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528265'>延缘访遗迹，佳处时击汰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528265'>飞沈各献状，领略在我辈。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528265'>匆匆莫能数，颇似慰无赖。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528265'>杯行未云半，落日已相对。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528265'>归来有酒所，方省欠诗债。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528265'>朱轓幸停轸，嘉汝山水最。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528265'>金茎峙霄汉，行矣分沆瀣。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528265'>何妨共流转，今古同一概。<div id='poem_sentence_11_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_528265'>非君个中人，孰使此中大。<div id='poem_sentence_12_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_528265'>伊余漂泊者，他日名亦在。<div id='poem_sentence_13_528265_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_528265'>一闻欸乃声，蓬荜忘湫隘。<div
