id='poem_sentence_2_528517_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　永州居住，作赵钧臣墓志铭。作品：承议郎通判润州累赠朝议大夫赵君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>承议郎通判润州累赠朝议大夫赵君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1146年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222948")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222948'>政和二年正月丁丑，承议郎、通判润州赵君讳钧臣，字秉之，年四十五，卒于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222948_comment'></div>宣和五年辛亥，葬君开封府长垣县吕村之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222948_comment'></div>又二十四年，当绍兴十六年，君之子奇为朝请大夫、荆湖北路提点刑狱，以书属其故人汪藻曰：「先人以文学行治，有名崇宁、大观间，不幸不得年以殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222948_comment'></div>既葬而衣冠南渡，幽堂之铭未刻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222948_comment'></div>惟先人平生所以树立者如此，而无传于后，不肖孤惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222948_comment'></div>敢以前著作郎王辟章所书行实一通累夫子，惟夫子哀而赐之铭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222948_comment'></div>藻读其书，曰信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222948_comment'></div>藻与君生并世，虽任之南北，相去数千里，不获从君游，然每至中朝，必闻君名贤士大夫间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222948_comment'></div>今得刻君之藏，幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222948_comment'></div>君滑州韦城人，其先世序绵远，至君之祖讳某，始仕为凤州录事参军，赠金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222948_comment'></div>生皇考，讳称，元祐中尝以河北转运副使，论黄河北流贮堤事，名敢直言，事载国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222948_comment'></div>一时伟人如司马温公、翰林苏公兄弟，皆手书慰勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222948_comment'></div>卒官朝请大夫、尚书吏部郎中，赠正奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222948_comment'></div>君少读书，嗜古文，耻以诸生训诂之学干有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222948_comment'></div>用父任为楚州宝应县主簿，会令缺，摄行令事，有能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222948_comment'></div>部使者庄公岳过之，喜曰：「昔吾以州从事吏部公淮南，观典刑前后，常恨不复见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222948_comment'></div>今君能然，吏部公不亡矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222948_comment'></div>调监雍丘县酒税，县跨汴堤为桥，一夕火作阛阓中张甚，或请断桥以纾火怒，君曰：「雍丘之为邑，以有此桥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222948_comment'></div>今火未至而撤之，万有一夫叫呼于其间，则此十万馀家生灵成胡越矣，幸勿遽，请尽力除君忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222948_comment'></div>即冒郁攸坐桥上，相火所焮，为之区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222948_comment'></div>顷之火熄，而桥卒不毁，邑人德之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222948_comment'></div>崇宁初，预增修永裕陵，以劳迁宣德郎、签书常州判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222948_comment'></div>未行，御史察访河北，请君俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222948_comment'></div>是行也，事有关权倖者，御史难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222948_comment'></div>君曰：「御史坐台，犹许以风闻言事，况专属公，何惮哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222948_comment'></div>亦为吾之所当为者而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222948_comment'></div>御史矍然曰：「公言是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222948_comment'></div>乃具以其实归报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222948_comment'></div>张几仲帅高阳，开幕府，孙协志康、王安中履道、赵鼎臣承之、霍安国子磐实从，皆一时之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222948_comment'></div>一日，几仲谓君之弟承之曰：「今兹佐吾军者，得公等矣，而付之民事，未得其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222948_comment'></div>欲烦秉之重吾府，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222948_comment'></div>即辟君知河间县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222948_comment'></div>君感知己，欣然就职，而孜孜于民俗之所先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222948_comment'></div>每讼至庭，率以片言面折其是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222948_comment'></div>父老至相戒曰：「汝曹毋妄诉人，今令君得人眉睫间，不可欺也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222948_comment'></div>先是河北行夹锡钱，而有司调民卖白金甚急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222948_comment'></div>居无何，钱币改议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222948_comment'></div>议者谓君：「锡钱积之官，粪土耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222948_comment'></div>幸诏下民未周知也，胡不白府，豫以此钱贷为买白金之费乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222948_comment'></div>君愀然曰：「是罔民也，吾曹而忍为此哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222948_comment'></div>言者语塞而去，时大观初也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222948_comment'></div>当是时，朝廷方新法度，信赏以劝从者，而州县吏至一岁屡迁其官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222948_comment'></div>君曰：「吾知逭吾责而已，多赏何为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222948_comment'></div>盖其用心，皆如却锡钱之议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222948_comment'></div>官满，民遮道不得去，则相与守府门，愿复借君数年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222948_comment'></div>擢通判润州，未之官卒，以奇故赠朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222948_comment'></div>君平居澹然，未尝见喜愠之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222948_comment'></div>与人交，初若简严，既久无不敬爱而思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222948_comment'></div>家有田二顷，亲戚之贫者皆从君食，岁以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222948_comment'></div>至自奉则仅免饥寒，不恤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222948_comment'></div>官宝应时，已聚书数千卷，无日不观，归则鬻衣衾载之以从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222948_comment'></div>有诗文百馀篇，合为三卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222948_comment'></div>与承之齐名，而友爱尤笃，平居倡詶赠答，若朋友然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222948_comment'></div>故君之卒，承之哭之，过时而哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222948_comment'></div>取刘氏，封安仁县君，赠恭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222948_comment'></div>四男一女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222948_comment'></div>男曰奕、曰京、曰奇、曰亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222948_comment'></div>奕，通直郎、主管登州盐事，与京、亮皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222948_comment'></div>奇，则大夫君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222948_comment'></div>女适承事郎永静军司录事韩承胄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222948_comment'></div>孙曰如圭、曰如川、曰畴，而如圭、如川亦前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222948_comment'></div>曾孙曰祖寿，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1222948_comment'></div>大夫清修而文，复有盛名于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1222948_comment'></div>而大夫之子如川资尤隽敏，年二十馀，以右迪功郎取进士高第，未及策试于庭而卒，士大夫惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1222948_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1222948_comment'></div>君家其世有人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1222948_comment'></div>君虽不得年，不用于时，而所以遗子孙者无穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1222948_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_1222948'>先生读书惟古求，悼世俗学非其流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1222948_comment'></div>伯埙仲篪天北陬，合为雅颂来中州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1222948_comment'></div>一官所至民挽留，忽弃华屋归山丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1222948_comment'></div>厥波之馀子则收，彼寿而达谁吾优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1222948_comment'></div>窆于异县龟告犹，耳孙世世祠春秋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_71_1222948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年1月</a>　建永州玩鸥亭，并作记。作品：永州玩鸥亭记。<div id='poem_1222896' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222896' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222896?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永州玩鸥亭记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十七年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222896")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222896_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222896'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222896'>余谪居零陵，得屋数椽潇水之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222896_comment'></div>既名为僇人，人罕与之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222896_comment'></div>又地承凋瘵之馀，无可游者，故一年而病，二年而苏，三年而心乐之，四年而视我如人，视人如物，休休焉不知忧乐之所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222896_comment'></div>屋临大川，愚溪之水注焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222896_comment'></div>因结茅茨为亭，面愚溪之口，有群鸥日驯其下，名之曰「玩鸥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222896_comment'></div>客有过而问焉者，曰：「玩鸥之说，闻之旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222896_comment'></div>今子之鸥，信可玩乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222896_comment'></div>余曰：「我与物同见于天地之间者以形，而我之知物、物之知我者以心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222896_comment'></div>使吾以心有以胜物，则李广之石可使为虎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222896_comment'></div>使吾为物所胜，则乐令之弓亦能为蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222896_comment'></div>是二者，无情之木石也，徒以人心之故，使之若出于有情如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222896_comment'></div>苟吾心反如木石而无所示焉，则鸥莫得而窥矣，何为而不可玩哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222896_comment'></div>余少迂疏狷介，自知于世无一相宜者，颇欲全生养性于麋鹿之群，以终其天年，而遂吾平生独往之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222896_comment'></div>盖漫仕二十馀年，虽三仕三已，而人不吾嫉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222896_comment'></div>无何，脱下泽之鞅，入承明之庐，佩会稽之章，则几微见于言面者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222896_comment'></div>故近者聚而尤之，远者趋而和之，一斥而置之三千里之外，此正群鸥舞而不下之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222896_comment'></div>吾于是杜门息交，朝饭一盂，夕饮一尊，日取古今人书数卷读之，怠则枕书而睡，睡起而日出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222896_comment'></div>幸无疾病，则复饭饮读书如初，此外无一毫入于胸中，颓然不知天地之大而环堵之隘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222896_comment'></div>庶几所谓心如木石者，则鸥之驯也固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222896_comment'></div>然俛而啄，仰而四顾，物之常情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222896_comment'></div>今鸥忘其常情，而与吾相从于此，固乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222896_comment'></div>安知他日无欲取鸥而玩之者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222896_comment'></div>幸鸥无忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222896_comment'></div>客笑曰：「书之壁以告来者，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222896_comment'></div>余唯唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222896_comment'></div>绍兴丁卯正月，新安汪藻记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1222896_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　为邢敦夫《呻吟集》作序。作品：呻吟集序。<div id='poem_1222867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>呻吟集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222867")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222867'>造物者轻与人以富贵寿考，而重与人以令名，自古富贵未尝一日无人，久生而长世者亦每每有之，率逌然与草木俱腐，世初不知其尝有是人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222867_comment'></div>以童乌也而夭，以王辅嗣、卫叔宝也而夭，以李元宾、李长吉也而夭，是数子皆天才卓超，非偶然而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222867_comment'></div>游戏须臾之间，已暴白于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222867_comment'></div>如此较之，久生长世者，大都不过数十年之顷耳，彼今安在哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222867_comment'></div>而贻声名以资说士者，炳然至今，虽垂之无穷可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222867_comment'></div>使数子复生，肯以此易彼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222867_comment'></div>元祐初，异人辈出，盖本朝文物全盛之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222867_comment'></div>邢敦夫于是时，以童子游诸公间，为苏东坡之客，黄鲁直、张文潜、秦少游、晁无咎之友，鲜于大受、陈无己、李文叔皆屈辈行与之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222867_comment'></div>虽不幸短年，而东坡以为足以藉手见古人，鲁直以为足以不朽，无咎以为足以追逐古人，今《呻吟集》是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222867_comment'></div>敦夫卒六十馀年，而其侄总出此书，于是敦夫之诗文盛行于时，与黄、秦、晁、张并传，信诸公许可为知言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222867_comment'></div>呜呼，敦夫尚何求哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222867_comment'></div>得此，不悼不幸于土中矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　作庄安常墓志铭。作品：左朝请大夫主管台州崇道观庄君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左朝请大夫主管台州崇道观庄君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十七年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1147年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222940")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222940'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222940'>君姓庄氏，讳安常，字子尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222940_comment'></div>曾祖曰允明，世家广陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222940_comment'></div>祖询，始徙宜兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222940_comment'></div>宜兴之庄，逮君三世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222940_comment'></div>皇考曰徽，以进士起家，事永祐陵为通奉大夫、徽猷阁待制，赠少师，谥僖简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222940_comment'></div>而君之祖，亦赠通议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222940_comment'></div>僖简于时为名臣，君世其家学，入太学，为英俊所推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222940_comment'></div>僖简任子次及君，君不愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222940_comment'></div>政和二年，赐上舍第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222940_comment'></div>胪传庭中，徽宗识之曰：「是庄徽子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222940_comment'></div>搢绅荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222940_comment'></div>调青州益都县主簿，改监惠民局，擢广亲宅宗子学正、太学录、太学博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222940_comment'></div>时朝廷以三舍法颁天下，学官号一时人物之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222940_comment'></div>又择老成厚重者使诸路，黜陟勤惰，以广上意，首用君提举京西南路学事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222940_comment'></div>遭僖简公忧，免丧知南剑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222940_comment'></div>靖康初，金人犯阙，诸道兵戍京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222940_comment'></div>福州军行不满意，戕其帅，道将出南剑，部使者莫知所为，厚糗粮金缯幸其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222940_comment'></div>君移书显责之曰：「王室方艰，日夜望天下兵至，今此军甫授甲，已无顾忌如此，尚敢望其冒万死为朝廷用乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222940_comment'></div>不痛惩艾诛，其人将悉效尤而起，祸有不胜言者，公等忍坐视其乱耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222940_comment'></div>不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222940_comment'></div>贼鼓行而来，所过残蹂，南剑空一城皆欲亡去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222940_comment'></div>君豫有以镇抚之，而阴为之备，贼顿城下，出丑语摇城中，君不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222940_comment'></div>至留月馀，秋毫无所得，反虞君袭之，则来告曰：「首乱者，某人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222940_comment'></div>愿执于公，假道以行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222940_comment'></div>于是缚二十馀人来献，君率僚属坐溪上受之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222940_comment'></div>君既得罪人，即遣其馀出疆，悉以手加额而去，无一人敢哗者，繇是闽之八州皆安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222940_comment'></div>无何，南剑受代，交印符，而代者以忧去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222940_comment'></div>适建州兵乱，州人挽君不得行，乃相与乞部使者留君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222940_comment'></div>君不得已，复留三月，阖境无犬吠之警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222940_comment'></div>南剑人德君，歌思至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222940_comment'></div>久之，知处州，处州大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222940_comment'></div>请外祠，得主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222940_comment'></div>起知抚州，寻辞之，复食崇道之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222940_comment'></div>绍兴十六年十二月己亥，卒于镇江府金坛县其子之官舍，得年七十五，积官至朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222940_comment'></div>初室张氏，继室石氏，皆封宜人，石氏亦先君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222940_comment'></div>六男子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222940_comment'></div>曰璹，右宣教郎、知镇江府金坛县，后君逾年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222940_comment'></div>曰琯，监潭州南岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222940_comment'></div>曰玙，婺州兰溪县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222940_comment'></div>皆迪功郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222940_comment'></div>曰玠、曰璋、曰璠，皆将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222940_comment'></div>四女子，右承务郎蒋庆祖、左奉议郎仲并、右从政郎王直谅，其婿也，季未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222940_comment'></div>君浑厚疏通，于经术得其指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222940_comment'></div>与人交，一于至诚，未尝用趋舍为疏数缓急轻重厚薄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222940_comment'></div>平居笑语呴呴，若儒生于世事不经意者，及变出非常，关豺狼之口而夺之气，虽久临方面而老于应变者不能为，人以是服君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222940_comment'></div>君自南剑归，翛然自放于溪山之间，日从诸子质问经义，口未尝挂除书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222940_comment'></div>虽暂出，不旋踵而归，然享静退清康之乐者二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222940_comment'></div>自渡江，士大夫终始无愧，少君比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222940_comment'></div>十七年三月乙亥，诸孤奉君葬宜兴县君山乡紫花坞，以石宜人祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222940_comment'></div>玙等来乞铭，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1222940'>德本于诚，学本于经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222940_comment'></div>隐然振其家声，为后学之师承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222940_comment'></div>遭变而得豺虺之情，立谈而弭一方之惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222940_comment'></div>早休而与世无营，享黄发庞眉之龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222940_comment'></div>所遗子孙者非满籯也，君之后其皆有成乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1222940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　在永州，有启陈情于宰相秦桧，望归家养老。作品：永州上宰相陈情启。<div id='poem_1222797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永州上宰相陈情启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222797")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222797'>遐徼省愆，屡优游而卒岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222797_comment'></div>久生成赘，终疾痛以呼天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222797_comment'></div>夙蒙知己之恩，敢布休骸之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222797_comment'></div>伏念藻偶陪多士，获齿周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222797_comment'></div>永祐龙飞，早赐胪传之第；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222797_comment'></div>建炎岳狩，首为扈从之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222797_comment'></div>蒙亲擢于稠人，几遍誇于清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222797_comment'></div>专司宸綍，遂直禁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222797_comment'></div>西清联三品之班，南国领六州之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222797_comment'></div>升高指顶，知难久于英躔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222797_comment'></div>擿埴索涂，果自投于宪网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222797_comment'></div>言章继上，威命趣行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222797_comment'></div>望丘墓以长辞，挈囊衣而遄迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222797_comment'></div>三湖五岭，问程知在于天涯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222797_comment'></div>一女二男，哭别相持于道侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222797_comment'></div>勉策四肢之惫，殆更两月之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222797_comment'></div>仅存桑榆，获御魑魅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222797_comment'></div>剑拄颐而冒宠，一旦累然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222797_comment'></div>箭贯耳以惧威，五年居此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222797_comment'></div>湘水有飞鸮之集舍，衡阳无过雁之传书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222797_comment'></div>惊骨肉之凋残，叹亲朋之杜绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222797_comment'></div>加以甫里百弓之别墅，岁与江通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222797_comment'></div>善和千卷之赐书，日为鱼蠹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222797_comment'></div>幸洪钧之未弃，明朽质之无他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222797_comment'></div>寘诸善地，而免瘴疠之侵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222797_comment'></div>续以奉祠，而纾饥寒之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222797_comment'></div>然齿衰病至，福过灾生，徒将数子以落南，未见一人之丰下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222797_comment'></div>深惧先茔之不返，欲持孤骨以安归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222797_comment'></div>故虽荐易于炎凉，曾不暂忘于朝夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222797_comment'></div>历历数还家之行店，漂漂羡归土之偶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222797_comment'></div>伏望某官既成万世之王功，俯及一时之士类，省三千里门墙之旧物，怜五十年学校之诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222797_comment'></div>适当引年之期，许为归老之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222797_comment'></div>附之密启，赐以生还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222797_comment'></div>稍刊刑部之章，使拭逐臣之泪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222797_comment'></div>锢人圣世，宜大君子之兴哀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222797_comment'></div>学稼老农，或小丈夫之得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222797_comment'></div>冒输微恳，仰叩深仁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1222797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　在永州，作王夫人墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王夫人墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十八年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222957")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222957'>夫人王氏，营丘人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222957_comment'></div>父师敏，卒官太仆寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222957_comment'></div>母赵氏，丞相清宪公挺之之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222957_comment'></div>为同郡从事郎、晋江县令张君讳应辰之妻，中奉大夫讳纯之子妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222957_comment'></div>中奉、寺丞，同里闬相好也，两家子弟日过从，寺丞与赵夫人贤晋江之为，故夫人甫十八，归于张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222957_comment'></div>夫人智识明辨，有贤士大夫所不能及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222957_comment'></div>靖康末，山东乱，士大夫流离，率鬻田宅去乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222957_comment'></div>或请于夫人，夫人曰：「舅姑在远而我鬻其本业，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222957_comment'></div>且谓吾夫何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222957_comment'></div>不如听之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222957_comment'></div>晋江闻之，喜曰：「真吾妻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222957_comment'></div>晋江为莱州推官，一日其守出，夫人自牖窥之，谓晋江曰：「人不忌其上，鲜不为患者，今卒骄矣，盍白守为备乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222957_comment'></div>守不听，数日而乱作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222957_comment'></div>乱定，人悉玩安不能去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222957_comment'></div>夫人独曰：「是不可留也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222957_comment'></div>晋江以中奉在商于，道阻不通，议所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222957_comment'></div>夫人曰：「东南天子在焉，尚何问」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222957_comment'></div>遂渡江，居金陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222957_comment'></div>不旋踵莱州陷，仕族无脱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222957_comment'></div>已而过湖湘，向商于，中涂遇盗，囊衣一空，夫人夜取敝衣纫缝，为之达旦不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222957_comment'></div>未旬日，举家衣履皆完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222957_comment'></div>其共艰难如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222957_comment'></div>晋江属疾，药非夫人所尝不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222957_comment'></div>洎殁，有欲以赙襚之赢谋生者，夫人正色却之曰：「于窀穸无憾足矣，此何为者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222957_comment'></div>既葬，四壁萧然，人皆以非晋江之清，无以见夫人之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222957_comment'></div>然自是家益穷空，夫人奉养益薄，诸子有忧色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222957_comment'></div>夫人语之曰：「而祖而父，以廉居官，以贫为乐，吾习而安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222957_comment'></div>汝等忘先人之训，虽日致四方之珍，吾不乐也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222957_comment'></div>平时勉诸子以学，戒诸女以顺，于是婚嫁甫毕，而夫人病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222957_comment'></div>绍兴十八年十一月癸巳，卒于其子栋之官舍，得年五十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222957_comment'></div>子五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222957_comment'></div>曰林，右从政郎、南州剑浦县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222957_comment'></div>曰材，右迪功郎、湖州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222957_comment'></div>曰栋，右迪功郎、泉州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222957_comment'></div>曰野，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222957_comment'></div>女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222957_comment'></div>长嫁宣教郎赵善究，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222957_comment'></div>次嫁右迪功郎向士皙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222957_comment'></div>孙男女合十三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222957_comment'></div>以卒之十六日戊申，合葬于晋江之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222957_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1222957'>嗟夫人，出华胄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222957_comment'></div>资敏明，自其幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222957_comment'></div>适名家，媲廉茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222957_comment'></div>遭百罹，谋必售。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222957_comment'></div>脱危机，如夙授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222957_comment'></div>老而从，甘俭陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222957_comment'></div>子诜诜，咸孝秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222957_comment'></div>各以能，为亲寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222957_comment'></div>方燕安，飨遐祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222957_comment'></div>曷倾之，人莫究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222957_comment'></div>窆闽山，祔夫右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222957_comment'></div>尚旋归，昌厥后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1222957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　在永州，作施氏墓志铭。作品：令人施氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>令人施氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十八年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1148年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222960")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222960'>令人毗陵施氏，朝奉郎、知临安军、赠少师讳辨之子，赠殿中丞讳洵之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222960_comment'></div>归同郡孙氏，为朝请郎致仕、赠中奉大夫讳庭臣之继室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222960_comment'></div>以夫封县君者二，以子封宜人、恭人、令人者三，以年赐冠帔者一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222960_comment'></div>群从同居五世，合庖二千指，男女十五人，孙若曾孙、玄孙六十馀人，寿九十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222960_comment'></div>东南士大夫治家教子，以令人为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222960_comment'></div>其寿考康宁，子孙蕃衍，闺门雍睦，兼诸福有之，则自宋兴二百年间，如令人者殆一二见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222960_comment'></div>令人在父母家，即以孝友聪明闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222960_comment'></div>年十七，适胡氏，逾年而嫠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222960_comment'></div>会中奉求继室，遍国中莫如令人之贤，少师亦以非中奉无足当令人者，乃彊夺其志归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222960_comment'></div>令人入孙氏，及其姑广陵郡君刘氏之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222960_comment'></div>广陵性高严，少降接，独令人怡声气奉之，凡岁时祭祀，率诸姒与其诸妇，夙兴视涤濯惟谨，羹胾菹臡，非手烹调之不荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222960_comment'></div>广陵微疾，自官居数百里晨夜驰省之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222960_comment'></div>广陵喜其诚，恨得令人之晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222960_comment'></div>中奉元配王氏，有子数人，令人专其家政六十八年，养生送死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222960_comment'></div>冠婚宾祭之用，尊卑长幼之序，皆有成规，非其财一毫不私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222960_comment'></div>计岁之赢，则储之以待族姻之不足者，予取予求不少厌，宁衣浣濯无所择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222960_comment'></div>于是族侄孙、外姻孤甥若孙甥与宾客之女，受其嫁遣者十一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222960_comment'></div>专以勤俭孝谨为训，上下化之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222960_comment'></div>入其门，弦诵相闻，恂恂然如在庠序；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222960_comment'></div>干蛊相先，整整然如在官府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222960_comment'></div>令人少喜读书，老而不衰，六经孔孟之书，略通其大旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222960_comment'></div>闻士大夫之贤者，必使子孙见而亲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222960_comment'></div>未笄，从少师官洛时，耆旧诸公皆在，得嘉言善行非一，历历能记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222960_comment'></div>晚传司马温公《家范》，乃并以授其子孙，或不如训者，引《家范》切责之，故子孙皆有前辈风，迢以文行擢进士第，薖亦通籍于朝，而长孙瑰博学好古，为诸儒所称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222960_comment'></div>诸女习于礼法，所嫁必为夫家之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222960_comment'></div>郡人敷文阁待制张宧等请表其闾，上之尚书，未报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222960_comment'></div>绍兴十八年八月，忽告其诸妇曰：「吾馀日再浃辰耳，将与而等别矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222960_comment'></div>至期，精爽不乱，视子孙无恋嫪之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222960_comment'></div>以九月某甲子，奄然而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222960_comment'></div>男曰邈，通仕郎、监泗州军资库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222960_comment'></div>曰𨑖、曰迥、曰迨，皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222960_comment'></div>曰蘧，右迪功郎、前清远军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222960_comment'></div>曰迢，左从事郎、监潭州南岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222960_comment'></div>曰薖，右奉议郎、主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222960_comment'></div>女适进士詹直文、李殊、文林郎张彦、右承事郎蔡载、进士刁楶、俞简廉、右朝请大夫应处仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222960_comment'></div>孙曰瑰、曰珂、曰琯、曰玿、曰瑑、曰珵、曰璞、曰琎、曰珌、曰琏、曰迥、曰璂，而琬、琰、琥亦皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222960_comment'></div>孙女十六人，皆为士大夫妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222960_comment'></div>曾孙二十六人，玄孙七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222960_comment'></div>蘧等以其年十二月壬申，奉令人之柩葬晋陵县定西乡浮塘桥中奉公之兆，以令人弟左中大夫大伦之状来请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1222960_comment'></div>藻观诗人载诸侯大夫母妻者多矣，《閟宫》颂鲁僖，而终之以令妻寿母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1222960_comment'></div>僖公，鲁之贤君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1222960_comment'></div>成风，春秋之贤母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1222960_comment'></div>能使国人祝其君，曰：「寿而臧，寿而昌」，「万有千岁，眉寿无有害」，并及其母，则闺门之积累，必有大过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1222960_comment'></div>孙氏自广陵君历年之多，春秋九十一而终，令人继之，至九十四，令人之冢妇葛氏亦九十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1222960_comment'></div>比三世皆寿考百年，孙氏之积累何其厚耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1222960_comment'></div>是宜为铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1222960_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1222960'>施本系鲁，惠公始殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1222960_comment'></div>常事孔子，雠为汉儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1222960_comment'></div>唐有士丐，其家在吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1222960_comment'></div>令人之先，世佩左符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1222960_comment'></div>是生柔明，天锡百祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1222960_comment'></div>来嫔于孙，黄发在堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1222960_comment'></div>五世同本，条支日昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1222960_comment'></div>孝谨属属，执经雁行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1222960_comment'></div>或第于庭，或跻于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1222960_comment'></div>恩锡显号，壸仪屡昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1222960_comment'></div>金蘤锦韬，翟衣步摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1222960_comment'></div>奉祠春秋，燕及庙祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1222960_comment'></div>云胡多休，阅此永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1222960_comment'></div>曰仁是常，如一日然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1222960_comment'></div>祔公而藏，京兆之阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1222960_comment'></div>刻铭于石，以永厥传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1222960_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　友人朱翌自韶州寄灵寿杖并诗，汪藻在永州次韵答之。作品：朱新仲自韶州寄灵寿杖并诗次韵答之。<div id='poem_528412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱新仲自韶州寄灵寿杖并诗次韵答之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528412")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528412'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528412'>苔渍岚侵几百秋，诗仙寄我海南州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528412'>携来应自滇池国，得处还因博望侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528412'>吹烛会寻延阁老，挂钱肯学饮家流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528412'>杖兮莫便为龙去，扶取衰翁老故丘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528412_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528412'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　在永州，得再任宫祠，上谢表。作品：谢永州再任宫祠表三篇。<div id='poem_1222681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢永州再任宫祠表<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222681")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222681'>六年循省，敢逃司败之诛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222681_comment'></div>一札哀矜，复予奉祠之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222681_comment'></div>孤大恩而莫报，雪衰涕以何言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222681_comment'></div>伏念臣承学无闻，饕荣最久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222681_comment'></div>徒幸冒升于班序，不思祇畏于简书，自取颠隮，合从窜殛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222681_comment'></div>蒙亏除于大戾，止投畀于遐方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222681_comment'></div>未绵历于岁时，已续颁于稍廪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222681_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下励精庶政，加惠微臣，虽云原贷之已多，亦复弃捐而未忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222681_comment'></div>今于徙所，拜此恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222681_comment'></div>捧诏天涯，如获望威颜于咫尺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222681_comment'></div>铭诗座右，以明复玷缺之艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222681_comment'></div>誓策疲癃，终期糜殒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222681_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1222682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222682?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222682'>间关百舍，敢怀故国之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222682_comment'></div>循省六年，复窃真祠之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222682_comment'></div>圣恩加厚，衰零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222682_comment'></div>伏念臣推数奇穷，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1222682", 1222682, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>负愆</span>深重，扪心无可言者，擢发皆自取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222682_comment'></div>惟弃置以是宜，何矜怜之敢望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222682_comment'></div>冒陈微恳，遽奉俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222682_comment'></div>如丝如纶，耸九夷之观听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222682_comment'></div>继粟继肉，宽百指之饥寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222682_comment'></div>仰戴生成之私，未知糜殒之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222682_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下至仁恻怛，大造鸿濛，谓尝陪文石之班，且久在细旃之上，怜此愚戆，老于颠隮，姑安处于遐荒，使长沾于温饱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222682_comment'></div>蘼当盛夏而槁，虽隔南讹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222682_comment'></div>葵见太阳而倾，敢忘东向？</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222682_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1222683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222683?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222683'>自求口实，辄贡于危衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222683_comment'></div>下遂物宜，亟颁于俞旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222683_comment'></div>既切竿摩之惧，又增尸素之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222683_comment'></div>伏念臣顷从远方，入冠法从，久无裨于毫发，居殆类于赘疣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222683_comment'></div>福过生菑，志壹动气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222683_comment'></div>甫一麾而出守，凛百病之交攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222683_comment'></div>力丐奉祠，庶几救死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222683_comment'></div>𦮕然疲役，虽幸得以息肩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222683_comment'></div>僒若囚拘，其何施而报国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222683_comment'></div>徒苟延于馀息，益有负于初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222683_comment'></div>岂谓隆宽，复容因任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222683_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下至仁普诩，大智有临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222683_comment'></div>设官分职之甚严，控名责实之惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222683_comment'></div>然而疾必使之有养，禄或加于无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222683_comment'></div>如臣所蒙，其比尤少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222683_comment'></div>盖平日皆繇于忝冒，而晚途荐赐以优閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222683_comment'></div>臣获此便安，敢云暇佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222683_comment'></div>虽筋骸之非昔，尊足者存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222683_comment'></div>顾年岁之几何，修身以俟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1222683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　在永州，得再任宫祠，上谢丞相启。作品：宫祠谢丞相启。<div id='poem_1222863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宫祠谢丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222863")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222863'>黜居善地，方依蛮服之民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222863_comment'></div>收预洪钧，复予祠庭之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222863_comment'></div>扪心知感，零涕何言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222863_comment'></div>伏念某初乏技能，久污班序，但欲追参于簪绂，靡思退服于田庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222863_comment'></div>果速烦言，甘婴显戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222863_comment'></div>蒙止从于轻比，始屏处于遐方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222863_comment'></div>龙钟七十之年，踯躅三千之里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222863_comment'></div>念孰兴哀于缓急，唯当沥恳于生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222863_comment'></div>爰继颁粟之使，思遂叩阍之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222863_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官学超今古，威耸华夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222863_comment'></div>致君泽民，孟子本六经之旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222863_comment'></div>制礼作乐，周公识万世之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222863_comment'></div>诵歌既被于管弦，人物皆归于陶冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222863_comment'></div>有如孤迹，早辱误知，幸平日甄收，当曲借笔端之润；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222863_comment'></div>乃晚途颠沛，反重为门下之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222863_comment'></div>逮兹抆拭之难，尚尔矜怜之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222863_comment'></div>某敢不潜深伏隩，补劓息黥！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222863_comment'></div>饱粗粝于南烹，已安分愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222863_comment'></div>望英贤于东阁，徒企光尘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1222863_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1149')">1149年</a>　在永州，为侄女汪氏作墓志铭。作品：安人汪氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222954' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222954' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222954?labeling=true' target='_blank'>安人汪氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴十九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1149年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222954")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222954'>安人汪氏，世家新安，余伯兄大中大夫槃之女也，为邑人武节郎俞积之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222954_comment'></div>武节之父曰翚，字彦升，知书喜事，从一时贤士大夫游如不及，以大中长者，尤归心焉，请安人为其子妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222954_comment'></div>安人入俞氏，无几何时，而舅姑皆殁，家累千金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222954_comment'></div>安人资警敏，辅佐其夫，奉烝尝、持门户，有健丈夫所不能为者，而武节、安人之年未冠未笄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222954_comment'></div>不数年间，阃之内外，绳绳秩秩然，贤于彦升无恙时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222954_comment'></div>乃勉武节于学，使与胜己者周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222954_comment'></div>客至，安人举中馈之职，酒殽声伎之奉，咄嗟如其所须，必乐饮极欢而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222954_comment'></div>由是武节三十年间，无秋毫不满意者，以安人之贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222954_comment'></div>武节艺成，再以名上礼部，不报，得武功爵而后归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222954_comment'></div>安人相敬如宾，交游日广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222954_comment'></div>再锡命书，封曰安人，仍赐冠帔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222954_comment'></div>武节先安人十五年殁，安人抚其孤，恩意周尽，虽邻里族姻，莫知非其所生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222954_comment'></div>当是时，安人母兄全州府君老矣，安人奉之如父，岁时温凊，礼无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222954_comment'></div>既卒，哭之过时而哀，言及辄声与涕俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222954_comment'></div>凡父党夫党，无亲疏小大，称其力调护之，一以至诚，始终无少异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222954_comment'></div>安人以绍兴十八年八月某甲子遇微疾，终于家，得年六十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222954_comment'></div>一邑之人，讲闻安人之贤者，莫不为之叹息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222954_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，尚书都官员外郎，赠中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222954_comment'></div>祖讳某，奉议郎，赠少傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222954_comment'></div>子三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222954_comment'></div>曰允中，承节郎、徽州黟县尉，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222954_comment'></div>曰允若，登仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222954_comment'></div>曰允恭，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222954_comment'></div>孙男女合若干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222954_comment'></div>男曰某、曰某，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222954_comment'></div>女适迪功郎、饶州府鄱阳县东尉徐琰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222954_comment'></div>十九年某月某甲子，允若、允恭奉安人之柩，合葬于婺源县何村武节之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222954_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1222954'>家溯而盈，莫见其缺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222954_comment'></div>子孚而成，莫见其别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222954_comment'></div>以未亡之身，屹然立俞氏之门，曰女之烈而非妇之哲也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1222954_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年7月20日</a>　在永州，赋诗五首以抒幽愤。作品：庚午岁屏居零陵七月二十日以门掩候虫秋为韵五首。<div id='poem_528292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庚午岁屏居零陵七月二十日以门掩候虫秋为韵赋五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年7月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528292")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528292'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528292'>幽人独夜时，潮落西川根。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528292'>渡口橹声急，一江烟雨昏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528292'>城头短长更，不寐听谯门。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528292'>趺坐数千息，焚香待朝暾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528292_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528292'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528292_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_528293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528293?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年7月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528293'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528293'>暑退潦亦收，潇湘净如染。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528293'>时观自跳鱼，冲破青琬琰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528293'>纤纤初弦月，不受薄云掩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528293'>近村<span class='inlineComment2'>（遗集作林）</span>应渐寒，已有鸦数点。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528293'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528293_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_528294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528294?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年7月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528294'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528294'>人生几聪明，日夜隙驹骤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528294'>才经花信风，又过麦秋候。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528294'>吾非金石坚，与世相邂逅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528294'>胡为闻钟鸣，更历路傍堠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528294'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528294_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_528295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528295?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年7月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528295'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528295'>家山在何许，渺渺彭蠡东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528295'>人来数月程，衣敝补道中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528295'>昨宵青灯花，似坠钗头虫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528295'>儿饥女沈绵，岁晚书未通。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528295_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528295'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528295_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_528296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528296?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年7月20日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528296'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528296'>人言间阔者，一日如三秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528296'>孤臣昔放逐，七见天星周。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528296'>早污高门地，姓名记前旒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528296'>如何<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_528296", 528296, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>天鸡</span>星，不照湘南州<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《浮溪集》卷二九）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528296'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在永州，为程克一作墓志铭。作品：判官程克一墓志铭。<div id='poem_1222944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222944?labeling=true' target='_blank'>判官程克一墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1150年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222944")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222944'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222944'>公讳克一，字贯之，衢州开化人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222944_comment'></div>曾祖寿、祖昭、考玑，皆隐德不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222944_comment'></div>程氏之先，见于诗书，其后解散流衍，布满南北，各自为族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222944_comment'></div>公之上世，口相传授，以为黄巢之乱，自徽州之黄墩徙焉，不知徽州之程何别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222944_comment'></div>至公始推究本末，谱而第之，于是知其为程忠庄公灵洗之后，今其丘墓尚在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222944_comment'></div>自黄墩之徙凡八世，公之兄宠始以经学应书，公与弟允若皆从受教焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222944_comment'></div>三人相继贡于乡，而允若以政和八年赐进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222944_comment'></div>未几，兄弟皆蚤世，公岿然独存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222944_comment'></div>公仪表魁硕，语声如钟，性厚重谨悫，孝于亲，友于兄弟，信于邻里乡党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222944_comment'></div>其弟没于京师，犯大寒奔走脩途，取其柩以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222944_comment'></div>伤兄弟之蚤世，凡所以恤嫠拊孤，恩意周浃，调胹里外，一无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222944_comment'></div>靖康、建炎间，盗起邻境，柝声相闻，人惴惴不自坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222944_comment'></div>公纠合庐井，以相保卫，无敢后先，讫赖以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222944_comment'></div>平居言语确讱，人以其可否为轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222944_comment'></div>间有阋讼不能平者，往往得公一语即定，盖所以信服之者旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222944_comment'></div>议者谓公祖考之积行，兄弟之力学，皆不克施，意者其有待于公乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222944_comment'></div>然且偃蹇不偶，绍兴八年，乃以特奏名，考中乙等，补京府助教，年五十馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222944_comment'></div>太夫人在堂，公不忍舍去，求便于养，以右迪功郎监西中岳庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222944_comment'></div>太夫人没，既卒丧，乃调澧州军事判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222944_comment'></div>公不以老故自任而薄其官，事无纤悉，皆亲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222944_comment'></div>析疑发伏，多出人意表，于是又知公之敏于事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222944_comment'></div>部使者仰其才，符檄狎至，不遑宁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222944_comment'></div>公素有足疾，至是寖剧，十有九年九月十七日卒于官，年六十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222944_comment'></div>既而命下，以右承奉郎致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222944_comment'></div>娶江氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222944_comment'></div>子男三人，曰知训、知谦、知谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1222944_comment'></div>女三人，长归进士刘翰，次未缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1222944_comment'></div>孙三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1222944_comment'></div>越明年二月十有一日，祔公于开化之某乡裴源先茔之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1222944_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1222944_comment'></div>世所以望于公者已矣，而曰或在其子孙乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1222944_comment'></div>虽然，孔子曰「惟孝友于兄弟，施于有政，是亦为政」，公何憾焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1222944_comment'></div>公之兄子刚中，幼鞠于公，念无以报罔极之德，则疏公之行事，以来请余铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1222944_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1222944'>开化之程，其来自歙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1222944_comment'></div>至公弟兄，始事儒业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1222944_comment'></div>公于其间，天假之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1222944_comment'></div>谓将显庸，而又不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1222944_comment'></div>惟孝且友，是亦为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1222944_comment'></div>子孙其承，所谓馀庆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1222944_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1150&endYear=1150')">1150年</a>　在永州，感风痹，乞致仕，不许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年3月</a>　在永州，为《东原集序》题跋。作品：跋《东原集序》<div id='poem_1222873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋东原集序<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十一年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222873")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222873'>嘉祐六年，先人为泰兴令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222873_comment'></div>岁大水，民田与江通，无从得食，转运使督秋输不少贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222873_comment'></div>诸县皇恐听命，独先人哀其穷，悉蠲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222873_comment'></div>转运使大怒，文移如星火，先人处之自如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222873_comment'></div>其冬事闻，诏起居舍人、同知谏院龚公鼎臣安抚淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222873_comment'></div>至泰州，部使者皆从公立诸县令庭下，数之曰：「人饥不能自存，而汝必得租，为民父母，当如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222873_comment'></div>泰兴令可尚也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222873_comment'></div>乃会部使者、郡守食堂上，泰兴令预焉，且使交章荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222873_comment'></div>藻为儿童时，记先人之言如此，恨不知龚公出处之详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222873_comment'></div>后六十年，至零陵，得学易先生所书集序读之，叹曰：龚公千载人也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222873_comment'></div>因知士欲行其志，非得大君子无所知名，反获戾焉者有之，况交荐之幸哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222873_comment'></div>公于是能举直错诸枉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222873_comment'></div>绍兴二十一年三月，男藻书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1222873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年4月</a>　在永州，有《靖州营造记》<div id='poem_1222893' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222893' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222893?labeling=true' target='_blank'>靖州营造记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十一年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1151年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222893")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222893_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222893'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222893'>国家承六世积累之馀，开拓土疆，过成周广轮之数，于是极楚越之南陬，皆列为郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222893_comment'></div>熙宁九年，增筑唐之城州为渠阳军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222893_comment'></div>建中靖国二年，又移军于渠阳江之西，赐名靖州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222893_comment'></div>初，夷人散居溪谷间，各为酋长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222893_comment'></div>及上版图职方氏，为王民，与彼之山川壤比疆连，犬牙相入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222893_comment'></div>虽岁久声教所覃，去椎结之俗而饰冠巾，转侏离之音而通字画，奉官吏约束，一如中州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222893_comment'></div>然此州实初郡，新民庶事，漫无纪律，重以连遭饥馑之灾，斗米千钱，弄兵之民，乘时抢攘，五十年间，凡六七作，发卒击之而后定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222893_comment'></div>为民上者，救过不给，间于忧虑，则趣办目前而已，遑暇及市朝道巷门渠之制哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222893_comment'></div>绍兴十九年，大梁刘侯临是州，营丘王侯为通守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222893_comment'></div>二侯，今之材吏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222893_comment'></div>相与戮力，不鄙夷其民，有惠有威，抚善良如赤子，去奸慝如稂莠，州人翕然信服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222893_comment'></div>渠阳旧为茇舍板屋，虽官居帑庾亦然，侯一新之，聚材瓦于场，募工于市，又以三者非渠阳所出，经营于数百里之外，其勤可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222893_comment'></div>绍兴己巳孟冬，遂甓州之通衢七百馀丈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222893_comment'></div>行者免于崎岖沮洳之艰，而望之绳直，循之砥平，为无穷之利，咸欣然相告曰：自有此州，阅府守丞不知其几，莫克为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222893_comment'></div>今一朝谈笑而成，非二侯之泽欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222893_comment'></div>且是役也，不期年毕工，其费出于二侯唱始之俸，与四方乐输之金，无秋毫及民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222893_comment'></div>集其事者，进士陈大有、僧世遂、祖能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222893_comment'></div>尝谓天下事无大小，如不萌苟且之心，鲜不成者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222893_comment'></div>鲁叔孙昭子所馆，虽一日必葺其墙屋，去之日如始至，《春秋》称其贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222893_comment'></div>况分符竹为州，有社稷人民之寄，师旅之屯，宾客之奉，而通衢者憧憧往来之会，肩摩毂击，朝夕是由，其可漠然不加之意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222893_comment'></div>故薛惠为彭城令，桥梁邮亭不修，兄宣知其不能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222893_comment'></div>陈道茀不可行，单襄公知其必亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222893_comment'></div>政之能否，国之存亡，皆于此而见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1222893_comment'></div>则二侯经渠阳者，其泽岂不远哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1222893_comment'></div>后人求营造之因，当有所稽考，盖不可以不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1222893_comment'></div>绍兴二十一年四月，左大中大夫、提举江州太平兴国宫汪藻记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1222893_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1151&endYear=1151')">1151年</a>　在永州，为绹瓬作墓志铭。作品：朝请郎绹君墓志铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年3月8日</a>　程瑀卒，汪藻在永州有诗挽之。作品：哭尚书龙学程公。<div id='poem_528449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭尚书龙学程公<span class='inlineComment2'>（名瑀）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年3月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528449")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_528449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528449'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528449'>江左推人物，时清得俊髦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528449'>肺肝倾耿介，头角长英豪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528449'>乡郡宾兴最，贤关誉望高。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528449'>万夫争射鹄，一举独连鳌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528449'>经术争儒馆，词章重省曹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528449'>主忧俄旰食，邦祸始秋毫。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528449'>彊寇来侵逼，敷天遍绎骚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528449'>奋身摅愤懑，衔命何腥臊<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作涉尘嚣，据聚珍本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_528449'>深入边亭隧，坚持汉节毛。<div id='poem_sentence_8_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_528449'>道途千里隔，忠义寸心牢。<div id='poem_sentence_9_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_528449'>归报龙颜喜，亲闻凤诏褒。<div id='poem_sentence_10_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_528449'>功成侔李郭，政合付伊皋。<div id='poem_sentence_11_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_528449'>超擢升青琐，谋谟拱赭袍。<div id='poem_sentence_12_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_528449'>百官瞻矩矱，八座次甄陶。<div id='poem_sentence_13_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_528449'>晚岁犹持橐，邻州暂梦刀。<div id='poem_sentence_14_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_528449'>台星方两两，逝水忽滔滔。<div id='poem_sentence_15_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_528449'>上意长图旧，朝廷未闵劳。<div id='poem_sentence_16_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_528449'>谢安几一起，秦失却三号。<div id='poem_sentence_17_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_528449'>伊昔身遐谪，公时首屡搔。<div id='poem_sentence_18_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_528449'>交情如骨肉，仕路正风涛。<div id='poem_sentence_19_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_528449'>里闬期重会，泉台恨莫逃。<div id='poem_sentence_20_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_528449'>终天吁永诀，雨泪滴香醪。<div id='poem_sentence_21_528449_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_528449'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_528449_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年7月28日</a>　在永州，有文祭张徽猷。作品：祭张徽猷文。<div id='poem_1222964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭张徽猷文<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年7月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222964")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222964'>维绍兴二十二年，岁次壬申，七月甲午朔，二十八日辛酉，左大中大夫、提举江州太平兴国宫汪藻，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于故提宫徽猷张公之灵曰：公出西蜀，大儒大家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222964_comment'></div>逢时中兴，大振厥华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222964_comment'></div>干国利器，深藏莫邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222964_comment'></div>扬于丹墀，天子叹嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222964_comment'></div>进直延阁，恩光日加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222964_comment'></div>西清近班，唾手可拿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222964_comment'></div>一日去国，君门遂赊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222964_comment'></div>甘心外庸，两郡拜嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222964_comment'></div>吏畏民爱，声闻迩遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222964_comment'></div>惟公有常，不陋不奢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222964_comment'></div>晚复静退，䌷书五车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222964_comment'></div>圭璋粹温，无可摘瑕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222964_comment'></div>游戏翰墨，如锥画沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222964_comment'></div>丛林饱参，诸障莫遮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222964_comment'></div>心法照了，谈馀雨花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222964_comment'></div>中年养生，彊健靡他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222964_comment'></div>云何鵩飞，庚子日斜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222964_comment'></div>重到旧治，岁方及瓜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222964_comment'></div>士林宗师，谁借齿牙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222964_comment'></div>行哭相吊，堂空绛纱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222964_comment'></div>藻久叨游从，敢并等差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222964_comment'></div>一觞永诀，哀岂有涯！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1222964_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1222964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年7月28日</a>　在永州，又有诗祭张徽猷。作品：张徽猷挽诗二首。<div id='poem_528437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张徽猷挽诗二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年7月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528437")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528437'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528437'>家有平津旧学传，人材嘉祐至和前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528437'>运筹惯倚将军树，画诺频分刺史天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528437'>字得钟王真楷法，心超粲可祖师禅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528437'>零陵宴寝公重到，父老追思静治年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528437_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528437'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528437_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_528438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528438?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1152年7月28日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528438'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528438'>天与精忠伯仲间，功成公独拂衣闲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528438'>专城早应贤侯选，延阁荣联近侍班。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528438'>去国久违龙尾道，思乡长梦鹿头关。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528438'>谈经尽日抠衣处，学子相逢泪雨潸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528438'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528438_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　居永州期间，有文多篇。作品：永州太平寺钟铭。回永州太守孙吏部启。回永州秋试举人启。<div id='poem_1222902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222902?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永州太平寺钟铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222902")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1222902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222902'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222902'>起空寂中，无间断者，非雷非霆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1222902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1222902'>一刹那间，遍满大千，非声非形。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1222902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1222902'>以悉檀成，以慈悲撞，以欢喜听。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1222902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1222902'>从无始来，如瞑而寤，如醉而醒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1222902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1222902'>九疑之西，潇湘之会，梵释之庭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1222902_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1222902'>绍兴庚午，春再浃辰，散吏是铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1222902_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1222811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回永州太守孙吏部启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222811")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222811'>自收朝迹，久阔英游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222811_comment'></div>如鲁灵光岿然，今谁存者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222811_comment'></div>闻暴公子旧矣，敢望见之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222811_comment'></div>忽传千骑之来，首拜百函之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222811_comment'></div>伏以知府郎中文高当世，气盖诸公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222811_comment'></div>珥笔中台，应郎官之列宿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222811_comment'></div>剖符名郡，分刺史之二天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222811_comment'></div>行闻中诏之颁，宁俟外庸之讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222811_comment'></div>退惟屏迹，方托提封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222811_comment'></div>怀长者之忧，虽乖于曩志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222811_comment'></div>吊逐臣之邑，幸遇于贤侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222811_comment'></div>大旆遄驱，先声蔼布，愿精加于调护，用深副于倾驰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1222811_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1222813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回永州秋试举人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222813")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222813'>伏审远偕计吏，荣诣太常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222813_comment'></div>词场推较艺之公，乡举有得人之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222813_comment'></div>解元才华俊发，学术精深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222813_comment'></div>万选钱中，气已吞于馀子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222813_comment'></div>三条烛下，名伫冠于群英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222813_comment'></div>猥记衰残，尝参耆旧，既俯临于蓬荜，仍请贽于琼瑰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222813_comment'></div>悚感兼深，敷宣罔既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1222813_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　居永州期间，有诗多篇。作品：观秋江捕鱼图。和家叔春日。<div id='poem_528305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观秋江捕鱼图</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528305")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_528305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528305'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528305'>霜飙落木潇湘秋，黄芦飒飒秋江头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528305'>渔翁短棹摇轻舟，夕阳斜照寒波流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528305'>篷蓑箬笠兴夷犹，得鱼沽酒更劝酬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528305'>生涯一叶水上浮，市朝利病不相谋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528305'>青山绿水得鱼游，此乐未必饶公侯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_528305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_528305'>画图忽见清两眸，恍疑身在沧浪洲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_528305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_528305'>年来萍梗叹滞留，拟欲与子为朋俦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_528305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_528305'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_528305_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_528416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_528416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/528416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和家叔春日</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_528416")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_528416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_528416'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_528416'>晓看春水满方塘，静掩柴扉白日长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_528416'>花意风光空烂漫，客愁山色对苍茫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_528416'>扬州歌吹今何在，陶令田园亦就荒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_528416'>试问南来米贵贱，欲随春浪过潇湘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_528416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_528416'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_528416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　在永州，为鲍慎由之诗集作序。作品：鲍吏部集序。<div id='poem_1222866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1222866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1222866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲍吏部集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1153年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28543, "宋", "汪藻", "poem_title_1222866")'>汪藻</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1222866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1222866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1222866'>括苍鲍钦止既卒若干年，其子延祖始裒钦止之诗，为小集若干卷，属藻序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1222866_comment'></div>藻为之言曰：古之作者，无意于文也，理至而文则随之，如印印泥，如风行水上，纵横错综，灿然而成者，夫岂待绳削而后合哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1222866_comment'></div>六经之书，皆是物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1222866_comment'></div>逮左氏传《春秋》，屈原作《离骚》，始以文自成为一家而稍与经分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1222866_comment'></div>汉公孙弘、董仲舒、萧望之、匡衡，以经术显者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1222866_comment'></div>司马迁、相如、枚乘、王褒，以文章著者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1222866_comment'></div>当是时已不能合而为一，况凌夷至于后世，流别而为六七，靡靡然入于流连光景之文哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1222866_comment'></div>其去经也远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1222866_comment'></div>本朝自熙宁、元丰，士以谈经相高，而黜雕虫篆刻之习，庶几其复古矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1222866_comment'></div>然学者用意太过，文章之气日衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1222866_comment'></div>钦止少从王氏学，又尝见眉山苏公，故其文汪洋闳肆，粹然一本于经，而笔力豪放，自见于驰骋之间，深入墨客骚人之域，于二者可谓兼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1222866_comment'></div>自黄鲁直、张文潜没，钦止之诗文独行于世，而诗尤高妙清新，每一篇出，士大夫口相传以熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1222866_comment'></div>余尝恨未见其全书，晚得此集读之，曰：「嗟乎，钦止于斯文，可谓毫发无遗憾矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1222866_comment'></div>钦止讳慎由，钦止其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1222866_comment'></div>风度凝远，如晋、宋间人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1222866_comment'></div>谈笑风生，坐者皆屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1222866_comment'></div>家藏书万馀卷，率手下雌黄，非雠得其真不止，故当时诸公交口称誉且论荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1222866_comment'></div>崇宁中，天子召见者数人，上独伟视钦止，即日除尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1222866_comment'></div>居无何，不合去，出为郡守、部使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1222866_comment'></div>久之，方向用钦止，而钦止以疾废于家矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1222866_comment'></div>故士大夫莫不惜其才不克施，而见于世者，特诗文而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1222866_comment'></div>故录钦止之生平大槩而并见之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1222866_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1153')">1153年</a>　通显三十年，无屋庐以居。博极群书，老不释卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1154&endYear=1154')">1154年6月1日</a>　卒于永州。<br /></div>
-----end
